[kakawin sumanasāntaka,

*Awiǥnamāstu*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:1:\:1:\:1:. saŋ hyaŋ hyaŋ pinakādidèwa ni karas para kawi makatattwa ŋ akṣara,
saŋ saṅkan paran iŋ palambaŋ atiduṙllaƀa kahanan ira n kawīśwara,
saŋ sūkṣmè kukus iŋ tanaḥ kinikiṙ iŋ kuku ri sĕḍĕŋ iŋ aṅṛĕgĕp laṅö,
māyākāra winimba nitya sinamāđi manurunana caṇḍi pustaka*

:2:\:1:\:2:. sambanđanya k aṅaṙccanè pada nirāhyun ajaṙ ajara milwa riŋ kawi,
yèkī kāraṇa ni ṅhulun praṇata ƀakti ri sira magawè namaskṛti,
luṅgaḥ niŋ kalaṅön sapuṅgĕl asĕkaṙ kakawin inupaṛĕṅgan iŋ laṅö,
puṣpāñjalya ri jöŋ nira n sumanasāntaka caritakĕnāstu sanmatan*

:3:\:1:\:3:. pūṙwwapraṣtuti niŋ kaŧā hana sira dwija taruṇa suśīla subrata,
śiṣyāgastya sira prakāśa kaṛĕṅö kasutapan ira nora tan ‌wruha,
ꝁyātīŋ rāt tṛṇawindu nāma pinakèsi niŋ ujaṙ ujaṙ iŋ kadèwatan,
sakwèḥ niŋ hyaŋ anaṅśayè hyuna nirāṅadĕha ri paṅadĕg surāđipa*

:4:\:1:\:4:. ndan saŋ hyaŋ suranāŧa muꝁya pinakādi niŋ awĕdi manaṅśayè hati,
lwiṙ tan duhꝁa sira ndan i twas awiwèka riŋ aṅĕnana dè niŋ olaha,
gūḋākāra nira n wikalpa kadi tan hana panaha nahā nirālaha,
prāyè saŋ suyaśa n tĕka ŋ ƀaya sakèŋ musuḥ awĕdi kaciṙyyanāwĕdi*

:5:\:1:\:5:. wwantĕn rakwa warāpsarī linĕwiḥ iŋ sa haripada wagĕd wicakṣaṇa,
prajña dyaḥ hariṇīṅaranya tuwi waṅśaja wĕka wĕka dèwaputrikā,
sākṣāt hrū nikaŋ indracāpa suƀagèṅid iṅidan i hayunya dug siṅī,
Aṅhiŋ sāra hiḍĕp hyaŋ Indra śaraṇāśraya paṅalaha śakti niŋ tapa*

:6:\:1:\:6:. yèkī rakwa kinon hyaŋ Indra maṛĕkāṅucap ucapa rahasya riŋ taman,
śīǥrānĕmbaḥ acum wulat nika sinuṅṣuŋ iŋ ujaṙ amanis priyambada,
Om putrī saŋ anĕmwa kāṣṭaguṇan aṅhilaṅakĕna kaśaktin iŋ tapa,
Aṅhiŋ māsku sinamƀawāsiha paṅöbana niŋ aśaraṇèŋ kadèwatan*

:7:\:1:\:7:. wwantĕn brāhmaṇa sidđiśakti magawè tapa katĕka tĕkèŋ surālaya,
maṅdè saṅśaya ni ṅhulun‌ ndan alĕmĕḥ katĕṅĕra ri wikalpa niŋ hati,
saṅkṣèpanya lumampahānaku mamañcana maṅĕnĕsa tan parowaṅa,
Èñjiŋ māsku lumakwa wörakĕna riŋ hima sumiliba tan hana ‌wruha*

:8:\:1:\:8:. nāhan dè nira mojaṙ aśru paṅutus nira lumariṣa tan ‌wruḥ iŋ ƀaya,
kèpwan dyaḥ hariṇī katon gĕgĕḥ i suṅṣut ira yadin apakṣa laṅǥana,
ṛĕs lāwan pagĕḥ iŋ kaƀaktin ika kāraṇa niki n uƀaya n lumampaha,
paṅgil paṅhwata janma liṅnya sĕḍĕṅanya karahatana riŋ pamañcanan*

:9:\:1:\:9:. mantuk dyaḥ hariṇī manĕmbaḥ i surèndra ri wijila nikā madandana,
Èñjiŋ maṅkat akañcugādarupa ƀūṣaṇa nika pinasaṅnya tūt hĕnū,
tan kwāmbĕknya lumampa lampaḥ aṅĕliḥ kasusu laku nikāṅhadè hadè,
dènyāđaṙmma ri dè nirāṅutus amiǥnanana tapa tatan hanāṅṙwwaṅi*

:10:\:1:\:10:. ṅūni n pamwit i jöŋ surèndra mamĕgĕŋ taṅis inimuṙ imuṙ kinölakĕn,
maṅkè n sāmpun adoḥ lakunya wĕnaŋ aṅlĕpasakĕna taṅisnya riŋ hawan,
lagy ānambatakĕn laranya kasihan pati sĕsĕl anĕsĕl purākṛta,
tūt māṙggāmbara luhnya tan papĕgatan drawa kadi titis iŋ maṇik bañu*

:11:\:1:\:11:. kāṅĕn dènya katuhwan iŋ giṇa mamiǥnani tapa wipaŧāgawè hala,
yadyastun kawaśā pira ŋ suꝁa tĕmun yan amuhara hala ndya don ikā,
mwaŋ yan tan kawaśā katon tĕtĕp i śāpa nira paṅawaśanya tan wuruŋ,
kodāsīnan irèka ta pwa pinalaṙ palaṙ ika siha saŋ hyaŋ Īśwara*

:12:\:1:\:12:. mampĕḥ mātra laranya luhnya pinakèmbuḥ i manis i matanya yan wulat,
luṅṣuṙ luṅṣuṙ ikaŋ tapiḥ pinakatambĕḥ i raras i tĕṅaḥ nikālaris,
hṛĕknyālwan ya samaṙ samaṙ tuna tunāmuwuhi manis i dè nikāṅucap,
Aśrī waṙṇna nikāṅĕliḥ wĕnĕs ikāṅhalĕpi kadi wĕnĕs niŋ abrata*

:13:\:1:\:13:. luṅhā lampaḥ ikānĕlat ri hiṛĕŋ iŋ gagana hanan awās hanan samar,
ṛĕp mukṣānusup iŋ ṛĕmĕŋ kadi wulan lumaku kasaputan lamad lamad,
lwiṙ wintaŋ sumurup katonan ika riŋ wĕkasan asĕmu maṙmmakè kapö,
ṛĕm niŋ mèǥa tinūtakĕnya manicip nicipi jawuḥ awaṙṇna cātaka*

:14:\:1:\:14:. ramyanya n pamĕgat laṅit lĕpas adoḥ tĕka ri sadawatā nikaŋ limut,
Agyā dè ni panas hyaŋ aṙka karaṇanya n alisuḥ atawĕŋ tawĕŋ hima,
prāpta ŋ truḥ sumaput praƀāwa ni lakunya wahu mari huyaṅnya kāṅinan,
tūt gaṅgāhawan indracāpa tumurun lari nika suꝁa mampiṙ iŋ wukir*

:15:\:1:\:15:. watw ānuṅgul amaṙwwatāhrit aguhātupis atiba tiban latāṅkura,
ṅkā tèka n dumunuŋ lukaṙ ni darupanya pinahayu lugas siniṅṣĕtan,
tistis tan hana tīṙŧayātra wiku śakty atapa katĕmu śūnya kèwala,
Aṅhiŋ handiwa handiwāgarawalan katĕmu maṛĕk anuṅṣuŋ iŋ guyu*

:16:\:1:\:16:. priṅgātyanta ruhuṙṇnya mānuṣa paran wĕnaṅa mara ri dohnya duṙggama,
ṅhiŋ saŋ paṇḍita saŋ huwus tumĕmu ŋ aṣṭaguṇa sira wĕnaŋ marèrika,
hètu dyaḥ hariṇī wĕnaŋ mara kajanman ika saꝑala dèwakanyakā,
lĕṙ dènya n tumurun sawaŋ garagatī tumurun ahawan antiḥ antihan*

:17:\:1:\:17:. tiṅhalnyābayaṅan mamèt i patapan saŋ atapa parananya bañcanan,
riŋ winđyācala rīndrakīla salĕbak wukiṙ ika pinaran katuṅkulan,
mwaŋ riŋ rèwatakāgra ganđamadanādri masamun apa tan hanātapa,
hètunya n ƀramitāpĕgākuliliṅan kadi pakalaṅan iŋ niśākara*

:18:\:1:\:18:. lambuŋ niŋ himawān kidul hana ta paṙwwata śuci patapan hañaṙ katon,
tumraŋ tèja nika praƀāwa nira saŋ sutapa tilaka niŋ jitèndriya,
Aṅlīlāṅililan pahoman ira söḥ kukus ika maṅadĕg nirantara,
lwīṙ oṅkāra mawindunāda kadi hĕnwa nira hĕlĕm anĕmwa śūnyatā*

:19:\:1:\:19:. budđi dyaḥ hariṇī tumiṅhal irikaŋ patapan asĕmu haṙṣa niścaya,
byaktāwās tṛṇawindu ta pwa makapājaran iki liŋ ikānĕhĕṙ maṛĕk,
līlāṅambaḥ i hambal iŋ jalada saṅṣaya samaṙ asamun hibĕk jawuḥ,
miṅṣoṙ lwīṙ ahawan turun turunan iŋ gupura suꝁa hanan kadīnulur*

:20:\:1:\:20:. prāptèŋ paṙwwata śūnya kaywan ika pakṣa wukiṙ asĕgĕḥ iŋ hañaṙ ḍatĕŋ,
haṙyyan mwaŋ hujuṅan sakèŋ pisaŋ alasnya rumaraṣaḥ amèt kalālatā,
sakwèḥ niŋ wulakan sumaṅgraha bañunya walahaṙ ika pakṣa sāgara,
jaṅgāṅambĕki pakṣa kasturi waṅinya hinaturakĕn iŋ dṛĕs iŋ barat*

:21:\:1:\:21:. wahw āron anak iŋ pakis haji katon sukĕt i pasusupanya duṙggama,
sakwèḥ niŋ kayu nora tan pagati dè niŋ anila tĕka riŋ tṛṇāṅkura,
ndan trāṣāsĕpi tan paron kapanasan paḍa ragas amalaṙ malaṙ jawuḥ,
waṅkal sèṅwan alīt alīt bataŋ agöṅa hĕlĕm i paṅadĕgnya riŋ juraŋ*

:22:\:1:\:22:. lwiṙ tan pahyaŋ ikāŋ alas hana giraṅnya wahu linawad iŋ warāpsarī,
tapwan maṙmma dahat panuṅṣuŋ ika kèwala kusuma yayā mawèḥ suꝁa,
lumrākwèḥ tumibèŋ gĕluŋ kadi tinap sawaŋ aṅit aṅitan sĕkaṙ taji,
kady āṅĕmbaŋ akon aṅantya pakamaṅgala nika tanĕmĕn ya dèwatī*

:23:\:1:\:23:. lĕṅlĕŋ niŋ talagānamaṙ tasik anak tuna tuna kawi nora maṅlĕṅĕŋ,
paṅgaŋ wwadnya kakumbaḥ iŋ bañu suluṙṇnya wahu mĕtu satuṅtuŋ iŋ tanaḥ,
I groŋ groŋ i pasiṙ pasiṙṇnya mawatu dyan aniru niru piṇḍa niŋ karas,
līlāṅanti darā putihnya kadi śaṅꝁa maduluṙ aṅurambat iŋ hĕnī*

:24:\:1:\:24:. ṅkā ta dyaḥ hariṇī marādyus amĕḍaṙ tĕṅaḥ abuṅaḥ amawwahan gaḍiŋ,
māliḥ ṣaṭpada niŋ saroruha maliwran i wĕtis ika kèsisan tapiḥ,
romanyāwilĕtan marè susu nikāniru niru rakĕt iŋ lumut lumut,
kĕmbaŋ niŋ kumudāṅliliṙ kadi tinaṅhi winulatan ikāṅdadak mĕkar*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:25:\:2:\:1:. ri sāmpun ika mĕntas aṅliga ligā kadi taman aśarīra dèwatī,
titis titis ikaŋ wĕhaŋ satitis iŋ bañu wulakan anumbĕṙ iŋ paras,
lumöŋ amiluluk gaḍiŋ kahudanan susu nika kasarambahan bañu,
sirat ni bañu niŋ gĕluŋ kinirab aṅhiribi kukus i sāri niŋ puḍak*

:26:\:2:\:2:. titis ni mađu niŋ mađubrata baṅun lĕṅa waṅi humaḍaŋ hanèŋ śilā,
pawitra hana tīṙŧa niṙmmala sumaṅgraha ri haṛĕp awaṙṇna pahyasan,
hṛĕbuk hṛĕbuk i kĕmbaŋ iŋ saraṣijāsĕmu hawu hawu muṅgu riŋ cupu,
hiṛĕŋ ni kucup iŋ trikañcu sumĕlat kadi sipat awawan puḍak puḍak*

:27:\:2:\:3:. lumampaḥ aṅĕliḥ kaṅèlan apa tan tahu mahās ahas iŋ wanāśrama,
sĕkaṙ niŋ asanāmayuŋ kuniŋ apiṇḍa mamayuṅana kāla niŋ panas,
paḍāṅṛĕs atatā ŋ wuluḥ kadi haṛĕp tĕkĕnakĕna tan intaṙ aṅhaḍaŋ,
gaḍuŋ kadi kamāsihĕn paḍa lumuŋ baṅun ahaṛĕp anuntunèŋ hĕnū*

:28:\:2:\:4:. huwus tĕka riŋ āśramāṅiṅĕt iṅĕt ry ulaha nika mĕnè n panĕmbaha,
nĕhĕṙ lumaku muṅgaḥ iŋ gupura saṅśaya manaha nahā marè dalĕm,
Aluṅguḥ irikaŋ bukuṙ paṅaraṅanya nĕhĕṙ asidĕhāṅurè gĕluŋ,
cĕcĕk masahuran sakè wuri pinakpak ika pinakadūta niŋ hala*

<nawahaṙṣa> ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓

:29:\:3:\:1:. ƀagawān tṛṇawindu sĕḍĕŋ ajapa nitya śiwasmaraṇa,
Asamāđi kumöl katĕmu hĕniŋ i budđi nira n humĕnĕŋ,
dwija śukla suśīla sira pinakadaṙśana riŋ patapan,
kadi waiṣṇawawimba pawulatan ira n pamutĕṙ guduha*

:30:\:3:\:2:. I rarè nira ṅūni hati nira hibĕk sukĕt aṅrahabi,
Inĕnö ni rajaḥ tamaḥ ira karaṇanya n aron asĕwö,
Atuha pwa sira ‌wruḥ aṅaji guṇa niŋ guru nora kari,
hana sattwaguṇāmaṅani sukĕt i budđi nira n patapa*

:31:\:3:\:3:. wijayèŋ patapan dwijawara makasāđana yoga nira,
Anukūla ri jöŋ nira sahana niŋ indriya nora wani,
Aṇimā laǥimādi kakaratala dè ni samāđi nira,
kamumukṣuhan aṅhaḍa maṛĕk akĕliṙ swaśarīra nira*

:32:\:3:\:4:. ri huwus ni samāđi nira linĕsu rakwa haṛĕp mijila,
Anĕlat rarab iŋ ṛĕṛĕb aṅuraṅi tan panĕlĕs haṛĕpan,
larap iŋ kilat iŋ gagana kadi dinĕmwan aganti lumöŋ,
paṅapö ni gĕṛĕhnya kadi mamisiki n hana wāhu ḍatĕŋ*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:33:\:4:\:1:. mijil muniwarāhawan hĕniŋ i budđi nira laku nirāṅhadè hadè,
pijĕṙ mulat i posik iŋ jalađi ramya tĕpi nika katuṅku tuṅkulan,
ri tiṅhal ira riŋ bukuṙ saŋ araras winulatan ira maṅligā ligā,
ya kāraṇa nira n parāgarawalan saŋ ahayu tumuluy madan tapiḥ*

:34:\:4:\:2:. saŋ ugratapa niṙwwikāra tamuyan wĕkas iŋ ahayu riŋ kadèwatan,
salaḥ sĕmu manis manis nira baṅun manis iŋ anĕmu mitra riŋ hĕnū,
dudū suꝁa nira n mulat paḍa lawan suꝁa niŋ atamuyan kadaŋ kadaŋ,
Ikaŋ turida rāga sāmpun amatĕḥ milu milu mamiratyakĕn manaḥ*

:35:\:4:\:3:. Aniṅṣĕti hĕniŋ ni budđi nira śudđa ni basahan ira n siniṅṣĕtan,
subadđa daluwaŋ siṅī pinakabadđa nira pamađa riŋ rajaḥ tamaḥ,
samaṙ tura turaḥ ni ƀasma nira paṅgĕsĕŋ ira wiṣayātĕmaḥ hawu,
jamaŋ kadi mahā taraṅtaṅĕn i sampĕt ira huwus anampĕtīndriya*

:36:\:4:\:4:. maṛĕk sira sulakṣaṇādara maṅakṣama kamĕna nira n paluṅguha,
katon upaśamātalaṅkup aṅagĕm kayu kanaka supattralèpana,
tamuy nira masèwa đaṙmma pakatonan i manaḥ ika ƀakti kèwala,
praṣidđa guru śiṣya rūpa nira kāliḥ i papupul irèrikaŋ bukur*

:37:\:4:\:5:. Anĕmbaḥ ikaŋ apsarī mĕtu raraṣnya tan asarag aṅambĕk ambĕki,
lĕmĕs ni luṅayanya kāliḥ ajajaṙ kadi pĕpĕsa kahambĕŋ iŋ susu,
laris ni jarijinya sāmpun atalaṅkup inayat inamĕṙ marèŋ muꝁa,
Amatyakĕn i raśmi raśmi ni liriṅnya n api miṅay aṅīrakĕn wulat*

:38:\:4:\:6:. lanāṅiṅĕt iṅĕt dwijèśwara tumon hayu nika winiwèka riŋ hati,
tulis kanaka wahw inuṅkaban aṅāśraya ri buṅaḥ ika n paƀūṣaṇa,
Ahadyan ahĕnĕŋ nĕhĕṙ masidĕhāsĕmu taruban i kāla niŋ gawè,
yadin haliwatèŋ saƀā tan alaraŋ halĕpakĕna maḍampa mās tatur*

:39:\:4:\:7:. sinaṅśaya nirālumāluñuta mađya nika kulayĕn iŋ pasaṅgaman,
susunya winaliŋ nirèmwa gamĕlĕn ri kahiḍĕpan ikôṇḍuḥ oṇḍuhan,
wĕtisnya kadi maṙwwi maṅgarita paṅkwakĕna kahiḍĕpanya dè nira,
muꝁanya gumawaŋ ya rakwa tinahālwaṅa hilaṅa ri kāla niŋ tilĕm*

:40:\:4:\:8:. hyaŋ iŋ nagara kālasan pawulatanya n anuruni rikaŋ wanāśrama,
mađubrata baṅun pinañjiṅan ikāṅidĕri salaga mĕtta riŋ sĕkar,
puḍak kadi panĕmpa nĕmpahan ikāsĕmu maniliha lambay iŋ ṭikā,
Amānuṣa hayunya kènaka nikāmulaṅunakĕna riŋ jitèndriya*

:41:\:4:\:9:. kayogyan iŋ apiṇḍa ratna liniṅiṙ saparana nika ta pwa hĕmbanĕn,
hadè kumĕḍapa n wulat yan aṅadĕg tĕhĕṙ aṅadĕga tan paluṅguha,
yadin lukara kènya tan ‌wruḥ amahāywa kahalĕp ika dènya n aṅligā,
sawaŋ sawaŋ iŋ aṅhĕmū guyu kapantĕs ika pamapaganya riŋ wulat*

<basantatilaka> – – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓

:42:\:5:\:1:. Āścaṙyya budđi ƀagawān tṛṇawindu dènya,
ndātan hana hyun ira mātra sumöṅa riŋ twas,
kèwalya susŧira manaḥ nira tan prapañca,
maswāgatāmanis ujaṙ nira sāṙjjawātwaŋ*

:43:\:5:\:2:. rakryan‌ kṣamākĕna kamību paran kitāri,
strī tan ‌wruḥ iŋ ƀaya ri duṙggama niŋ wanādri,
Aṅhiŋ katon kita wĕnaŋ mara niṙwwikāra,
prāptāṅĕnĕs maniluman baṅun indrajāla*

:44:\:5:\:3:. Āsĕṅka ni ṅhulun i māsku tĕkanta maṅko,
strī niŋ wiśèṣapuruṣa praƀu cakrawaṙtti,
tan saḥ kinuṇḍaŋ i sĕḍĕŋ niŋ abuṙwwa buṙwwan,
ndā ṅkè n katĕmwa samayanta lawan priyanta*

:45:\:5:\:4:. strī tan pađaṙmma ta kunaŋ kita kāri śoka,
swāminta tan pahamĕṅan kawi tan pawasŧa,
Ambĕkta wikwa manusup nusupèŋ alas göŋ,
sambin hiḍĕpta wulikĕn palaṛĕn katĕmwa*

:46:\:5:\:5:. Anwam kunaŋ kita katuṅhapan iŋ bapèbu,
muṅgw iŋ kadaŋ maṅupapīra mawèḥ larāmbĕk,
māṙgganta lampus aṅusiṙ wanadèśa śūnya,
Ahyun lumakwa wiku kilya rarā wiratya*

:47:\:5:\:6:. hyaŋ hyaŋ niŋ āśrama kunaŋ kita diwyacakṣuḥ,
‌wruḥ riŋ jitèndriya sadābrata tan kĕnèŋ‌ strī,
budđinta moǥa mawĕlas mulat iŋ daridra,
prāptānurun paran ikā paṅanugrahanta*

:48:\:5:\:7:. rakryan hiḍĕpku ri hayunta sakèŋ wanādri,
Ambĕt ni sinwam iŋ aśoka marè tĕṅahta,
molaḥ kadīnĕluk ĕluk luŋ ikaŋ gaḍuŋ mrik,
tan saḥ katon i luṅayanta lĕmĕs lĕmĕsnya*

:49:\:5:\:8:. Amraŋ baŋ iŋ katiraḥ aṙjja hanè laṭinta,
tuñjuŋ birū mĕkaṙ aluṙww akusū suganđa,
māliḥ lurunya mamanis kawawè matanta,
mimbāmarāśraya tikĕlnya hanè halista*

:50:\:5:\:9:. polaḥ nikaŋ kusumasāri hanè wiwalta,
maṅgiṣṭa wāhu rinĕmĕk tumibè kĕcapta,
paṅhṛĕŋ nikaŋ ƀramara muṅgw i taṅis taṅista,
hīs niŋ tusāra rumarab makajanma luhta*

:51:\:5:\:10:. sandèha budđi mami dè ni halĕpta māsku,
dūra n manuṣya kita kèwala dèwaputrī,
dè niŋ manaṙka ri ḍatĕṅta mahāpraƀāwa,
saṅkè hyaŋ Indra mapa donta waraḥ kamību*

:52:\:5:\:11:. nāhan panaṙka nira maṙmma dahat raṣanya,
mambö tilam kadi huwus ‌wruḥ i rumrum iŋ‌ strī,
śṛṅgāra dèwaduhitā kawĕlad hatinya,
maṅgĕḥ ri budđi ƀagawān kĕna bañcananya*

<A> kind of/ Akṛti ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:53:\:6:\:1:. suraputrikā sumahuṙ ādara mulat awiraŋ tumuṅkul anaṅis,
ƀagawān ṛĕṅön pawaraḥ i ṅhulun aṅusiṙ aṅāśrayè kadi kita,
taha tan sakè surapati n ḍatĕŋ aṅĕnĕs amèt pradèśa wĕgilĕn,
mwaŋ asamƀawa n hyaṅa niŋ āśrama panaha nahā dwijèśwara hadè*

:54:\:6:\:2:. tuwi tan manuṣya maniwi praƀu maduluṙ abuṙwwa buṙwwa riŋ alas,
hayu ni ṅhulun taha tan antuk iŋ aṅalap alap sakèŋ giriwana,
riŋ apa n rarāhaṛĕpa wikwa manusupa manĕmbahèŋ wiku talun,
pisaniṅw ajalwa kawi mūṙcꞓita layat alaṅö manambaŋ anadin*

:55:\:6:\:3:. ƀagawān manĕhta huniṅan humulunakĕn awaknya tan patĕbusan,
tuwi hètu niŋ mara ri jöŋ dwija taruṇa ƀaṭāra đaṙmma maṅutus,
I ratĕŋ nikaŋ brata samāđi kakawaśa tĕkapta sāmpun amatĕḥ,
mĕtu tan pasaṅkan inucap wulatana tariman‌ ṅhulun ꝑala nika*

:56:\:6:\:4:. hyaṅĕn i ṅhulun ri pada saŋ dwija taruṇa kaśudđyanôtus utusĕn,
pisanīṅw anĕṅgaha mĕnè n pasuruhana sĕkaṙ lawan bañu damu,
maṛĕkèŋ patuṙwwan aṅisapwakĕna suku munīndra riŋ pakasutan,
tan asamƀawa n hulun anaṅhuluna yan apuyĕŋ dwijaṙṣi majapa*

:57:\:6:\:5:. Aṛĕnaḥ tĕkapnya n aṅucap kama riŋ ujaṙ amiǥnani brata tapa,
mata mèsi luḥ saha taṅis winulatakĕn ikā winèḥ amanisa,
Ajajaṙ pasaṅgraha nikā susu waṅi ni pipinya lāgi sumaji,
kadi pādapāṅliḥ alaris tĕṅaḥ ika pasĕnāha ri dwijawara*

:58:\:6:\:6:. Umĕnĕŋ dwijaṙṣi rumasè wacana nika tĕkā waśāṅhamu hamu,
smaradūta kèwala manisnya n aṅucap ataṅis lanāmĕlas aṛĕp,
wĕkasan dwijèndra wihikan ry aƀimata nika yan pamiǥnani tapa,
mĕtu kadwijātyan ira nora kawĕdi nira sāhasānapaŧani*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:59:\:7:\:1:. Aḍā wipaŧa ko pakojaṙ iku đūṙtta tan ahaṛĕp i haywa niŋ tapa,
huwus ‌wruḥ aku yan pakona suranāŧa karaṇamu ḍatĕŋ mamañcana,
Ikaŋ hala gawèmu tan wuruŋ amaṅṣulana malĕsanèri ko mĕnè,
manuṣya tĕmahāmwa tan waluya riŋ surapada wĕkasamwa dèwatī*

:60:\:7:\:2:. yadin śatasahaśraƀāgan i suꝁaṅku n ataki taki niṣparigraha,
taŧāpi kapana n samaṅkana suꝁaṅkwa k aṅusira suꝁèŋ surālaya,
hana pwa suꝁa niŋ manuṣya masamāgama mapa ta gawè nikāđama,
lĕhĕŋ juga ŋ anĕmwa pātaka sakèŋ katuduhana kabañcanātapa*

:61:\:7:\:3:. nahan liŋ ira sāhasāṅḍawuhi śāpa nĕhĕṙ anudiṅī kiwāṅdĕlö,
prapañca surakanyakā kahilaṅan hurip apĕga ri tan siḥ iŋ wiđi,
ri doṣa nika rāga rāga n aṅusiṙ sutapa pisaniṅūn kabañcana,
Alum kadi gaḍuŋ pinuṅgĕl aṅayuḥ sĕkaṙ iŋ asana tan wuruŋ pĕjaḥ*

:62:\:7:\:4:. tumuṅkul i haṛĕp dwijaṙṣi makacāmana rarab i lĕbū ni jöŋ nira,
hanan kadi waśāṅdĕlö nĕhĕṙ aminta winaluyakĕn iŋ surālaya,
mĕhāḥ salahasātĕpak jaja manĕmbaḥ aḍĕkuḥ amalaṙ kasanmata,
Apan haṛĕp iŋ antaśāpa karaṇanya n aṅucap amanis maṅañjali*

:63:\:7:\:5:. dwijaṙṣi huripĕn‌ ṅhulun titisanāmṛta waluyakĕnèŋ kadèwatan,
Ĕmās maṇik anèkawastu kĕta ŋ ènaka panĕbusa ni ṅhulun hurip,
ṅhulun pwa kasihan muwaḥ syapa pamètana pirak i rikaŋ tapowana,
mataṅnya k anaṅis panĕmbaha ri jöṅta panĕbusa ri jīwa ni ṅhulun*

:64:\:7:\:6:. tuhanku ƀagawānku hāḥ sipi lalista wulatana manĕhta kāsy asiḥ,
haṛĕp muliha tan wĕnaŋ muliḥ aṅantya ri kita kita mèlik i ṅhulun,
Unĕŋ niŋ abapèbu tiṅhalana dènta mapa karika hètu niŋ hĕnĕŋ,
kĕdö haṛĕp anona māti kĕna śāpa karika kita tan ‌wruḥ iŋ wĕlas*

:65:\:7:\:7:. Ahā mpu wihikan‌ ṅhulun ri wuyuṅanta kalalarana śudđa niŋ tapa,
kṣamākĕna manĕhta tan tugĕtananta sakasalaḥ i śīla ni ṅhulun,
praṣidđa kita paṇḍitānumata riŋ wiguṇa wipaŧa tan ‌wruḥ iŋ krama,
si sĕmbaḥ ika jampya niŋ kadi kita n lumĕkasa wuyuŋ iŋ kadi ṅhulun*

:66:\:7:\:8:. kucup niŋ asanāluru ndan amalaṙ kaririṣana ri taṅgal iŋ kapat,
gaḍuŋ lumay aṅolakĕn tawaŋ aluṅluṅan amalaṙ anĕmwa rambatan,
hĕlaŋ midĕṙ anambayaŋ saha taṅis kapanasan amalaṙ dṛĕs iŋ jawuḥ,
ṅhulun pwa kalaran mataṅnya k amalaṙ turunana wara dè dwijèśwara*

:67:\:7:\:9:. Ahā pahalawö ta koŋ awakana ŋ kapalaŋ alaŋ i dèmu n apsarī,
kadaŋ kadaṅa dè bapèbu pĕkulĕmwa paḍa kari sirèŋ kadèwatan,
pĕjaḥ ṅaran iki syapèka ta taṅis taṅisana mulatāsihèri ko,
wĕlasku ri hayunya sis mapa tikī hamĕṅana niki yan pĕjaḥ mĕnè*

:68:\:7:\:10:. ƀaṭāra suranāŧa tiṅhalana dè nṛpati kasiḥ aṛĕp patik haji,
huwus kalĕmahān śināpa kapana n maluya muwaḥ i pāda saŋ praƀu,
hilaŋ manĕ manĕḥ surāđipati tan wuruṅa pĕjaha riŋ pamañcanan,
riŋ āśrama wĕkas ni jīwita patik haji wiꝑala pakon surāđipa*

:69:\:7:\:11:. praƀu praƀu ṛĕṅön taṅis ni hariṇī kapĕgan aputĕk aṅhiḍĕp lara,
pĕjaḥ pinatiwaṙ kinonakĕn i tan kawĕnaŋ ika gawè dinohakĕn,
Ikaŋ gati śināpa sis ya katahā ya katĕmu tuluṅĕn patik haji,
pati pwa balik iŋ hurip lara lalis pwa balika ni wĕlas surāđipa*

:70:\:7:\:12:. wijil sahana saŋ hyaŋ iŋ kusuma wāhu sumalaga nihan lawad‌ ṅhulun,
hurip gĕlisa ni ṅhulun ya palakunta ri yatiwara haywa tāsuwè,
kunaŋ yan agĕgĕḥ dwijaṙṣi palalun sawuyuŋ ira sadènya saṅkulĕn,
tuhun kita lumĕṇḍwa lĕṇḍwa ri śawaṅku gĕsĕṅĕn i pañaṇḍi niŋ wuṅū*

:71:\:7:\:13:. manis ni mata ni ṅhulun labuhĕn iŋ jalađi luḥ irikaŋ tasik mađu,
raras ni waja ni ṅhulun hañutĕn iŋ śrigaḍiŋ i pucak iŋ gunuŋ gula,
lĕmĕs ni lĕṅĕn i ṅhulun lĕpasĕn iŋ gaḍuŋ aṅĕliḥ aṅolakĕn tawaŋ,
laris ni wĕtis i ṅhulun kĕkĕsananta kĕmitana ni dèwa niŋ puḍak*

:72:\:7:\:14:. kĕlab ni tapiḥ i ṅhulun suji ya tèki pupulakĕn i posik iŋ sĕkar,
pataṅkis i giriṅṣiŋ i ṅhulun aṅantya ri lĕṅĕŋ i kiriñciŋ iŋ bañu,
pĕnĕd ni laku ni ṅhulun tan asarag waluyakĕna ri lampaḥ iŋ liman,
pĕpö ni panaṅisku tan kahuniṅā ḍawuhakĕna ri śabda niŋ cucur*

:73:\:7:\:15:. Amèta maṅunĕŋ galuḥ kita pamorana ni kusut i roma ni ṅhulun,
ri mimba ni taman ta paṅlĕpasananta ri ṛĕṅu ni halisku yan tikĕl,
gĕmuḥ ni susu ni ṅhulun wahu mijil tuhañaṅakĕna riŋ pucaŋ gaḍiŋ,
wĕnĕs ni muꝁa ni ṅhulun hañutĕn iŋ wulan inĕmukan iŋ lamad lamad*

:74:\:7:\:16:. pamādapa ni mađya ni ṅhulun aros kirimakĕn iŋ aśokapādapa,
Ĕbun hana ri tuṅtuŋ iŋ tṛṇalatāṅkura patuwawanè luḥ i ṅhulun,
lawan pañurigènunus ni paṅawakku rakĕtakĕna dènta riŋ tulis,
luṅid ni kuku ni ṅhulun turuŋ aṅanya ri jaja jajaṙ iŋ sĕkaṙ taji*

:75:\:7:\:17:. nahan śruti ni dè nikānaṅis atuṅtuŋ ucapan amĕlas mĕlas haṛĕp,
samasta para dèwa sūkṣma humĕnĕŋ tinaṅisan ika tan hanāṅlawad,
Aṛĕs hawa hawākĕnāwĕdi kumöl ‌wruḥ i gĕgĕḥ i wuyuŋ dwijèśwara,
paḍāṅṛĕs anaṅis naṅis taṅis ikā piniturun ika muṅgu riŋ wanèḥ*

:76:\:7:\:18:. taṅis taṅis i dèwa niŋ kusuma sūkṣma tinaṅisakĕn iŋ mađubrata,
taṅis niŋ amarāśrayèŋ wulan awā tinaṅisakĕn i śabda niŋ cucur,
taṅis taṅis i dèwa niŋ jalada cātaka manaṅisakĕn hanèŋ tawaŋ,
taṅis taṅis i dèwa niŋ masa kapat tinaṅisakĕn i gĕntĕṙ iŋ patĕr*

:77:\:7:\:19:. muwaḥ dyaḥ anu mojaṙ asṛĕt ucapanya tuna tuna sinambaṅan taṅis,
mpu ḍaŋ hyaŋ apa tāḥ inanti ni manĕhta paṅuṣađa ri duhꝁa ni ṅhulun,
yatan hana hinèṙ manĕḥ dwijawarāṣiha humuripana ŋ huwus pĕjaḥ,
kṣamākĕna magöŋ‌ ṅhulun‌ mpu warahĕn duga duga mara tan haṛĕp haṛĕp*

:78:\:7:\:20:. nahan raṣa ni dè nikānaṅis aminta winaluyakĕn iŋ kadèwatan,
Uđāni ƀagawān paṅa‌wruhana dè nira mulat amanis wawaŋ lipur,
Apuy siniram iŋ jawuḥ paḍa ni suṅṣut ira tan agĕgĕḥ wawaŋ paḍĕm,
sĕṛĕḥ waṅi lawan duḥ iŋ wwaḥ aramĕs ri waja paḍa ni dè nirāṅucap*

:79:\:7:\:21:. paran karika tan sihaṅkwa ri kitānaku kita karikāpan uttama,
manuṣya tuwi sāwakanya yan atön mara mara hiniḍĕp kadaŋ kadaŋ,
kunaŋ saŋ agawè laranta paramāṙŧa nira sira ƀaṭāra śaṅkara,
lukat ni kapalaŋ nikaŋ sukṛta māṙgga ni kapalaŋ i dènta dèwatī*

:80:\:7:\:22:. priyanta riŋ anādijanma dadi mānuṣa lituhayu sūṙyyawaṅśaja,
narèndra raǥu rakwa mānak aniru prakaśita suƀagèŋ purāntara,
Apañjy Aja đanuṙdđarānwam isi niŋ raǥunagara turuŋ‌ smarātura,
tuhun kita dinè ƀaṭāra yugalanya muwaḥ akuṛĕnāsihè kita*

:81:\:7:\:23:. kunaŋ pwa siha ni ṅhulun ri kita tan kalawasana dadinta mānuṣa,
Aṅālihana kapraƀun kita lawan saŋ Aja suꝁa sarājya tuṅgalĕn,
tuhun pamĕkasanta wīja sawijīrika kita maluyèŋ kadèwatan,
sĕkaṙ sumanasāntakanta ya tikāmĕgatakĕna ri śāpa ni ṅhulun*

:82:\:7:\:24:. huwus pwa kita mantuk iŋ surapadānaku katĕka tĕkèŋ wwaluŋ tahun,
samaṅkana narèndra saŋ kawĕkas iŋ nagara muliha riŋ kadèwatan,
Apaṅgiha muwaḥ lawan kita tumĕmwakĕna ꝑala nikaŋ kadigjayan,
mataṅnya pahayun manahta suꝁamāṙgga matĕmahāna rājaputrikā*

:83:\:7:\:25:. nahan raṣa ni dè nirāmĕgati śāpa nira tĕhĕṙ ajaṙ satoraṣiḥ,
ri mūla ni dadinya lèn tĕmahānanya tinalataḥ irāgalaṙ taṅan,
kunaŋ pwa wĕkasan hiḍĕpnya ri kaśāpa nika kadi winèḥ anugraha,
Unĕṅnya matĕmaḥ luḥ adṛĕs i kapö lara turida nikātĕmaḥ taṅis*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:84:\:8:\:1:. hāḥ saŋ mukṣa ri luhku tan pahamĕṅan namu namu pĕjaḥ iŋ pasaṅgaman,
maṅkè pwāmbĕka niŋ prahāsana bisāṅhari hariḥ iŋ aṛĕs pinaṅkwakĕn,
ṅūni n hyaŋ kita riŋ surālaya manĕhta milu matĕmahān warāpsarī,
maṅkè pwāṅdadi rājaputra kita hèṙ ṅhulun atĕmahā rājaputrikā*

:85:\:8:\:2:. hāḥ swāmiṅku dudut‌ ṅhulun ri juraŋ iŋ lĕpihan alal aṅölakĕn laṅö,
hĕmban riŋ wwat aśokapādapa tĕṅahku pagamĕlana luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,
suṅṣuŋ riŋ maṅunĕŋ galuḥ lulut unĕṅku ri kita kaka tan wĕnaŋ kinas,
riŋ paṇḍan haḍaṅĕn‌ ṅhulun lumaku śoka laku laku ṭikāhawan puḍak*

:86:\:8:\:3:. nāhan ṅṛĕs ṅṛĕs i samba sambat ika kāsihan alal apasaḥ lawan priya,
tan siḥ niŋ wiđi moǥa tan patuluṅan karaṇa nika manĕmwakĕn lara,
dè niŋ gyānya tumĕmwa janma saŋ aniṅgalakĕn iriya riŋ kadèwatan,
Amwit matya manĕmbaḥ iŋ dwijawarānĕhĕṙ aṅusapi luhnya riŋ sabuk*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:87:\:9:\:1:. huwus praṇata ƀakti tan paśaraṇāśraya mati lumaḥ iŋ pamañcanan,
humuŋ taṅis i sundarī nikaŋ alas hinariwuwu ni śabda niŋ gaguŋ,
ṛĕṛĕb kusumasāri tan papĕgatan kĕtug i tĕḍun iŋ èṙttalīŋ juraŋ,
luŋ iŋ gaḍuŋ aṅindracāpa humaḍaŋ hawana nika madadya mānuṣa*

:88:\:9:\:2:. hyaŋ Agni hana riŋ śarīra mijil aṅgĕsĕṅi śawa nikāgilaŋ gilaŋ,
kasidđyan ira saŋ dwijaṙṣi gumawè dilaḥ ika karaṇanya n ujwala,
bukuṙ pamiḍaran‌ ndatan milu gĕsĕŋ kadi jalada rinĕṅgan iŋ kilat,
samantaji paḍĕm tuhun hana kukusnya kari sakukus iŋ damaṙ pĕjaḥ*

:89:\:9:\:3:. hayunya milu ƀasmiƀūta tĕka riŋ gĕluŋ ahawuk amiṇḍa riŋ kukus,
lumöŋ wa nikaŋ asŧi mātra kadi śèṣa ni luru ni matanya yan wulat,
baṅun tura turaḥ nikaŋ sipat ikaŋ latu latu tumibā paḍāhiṛĕŋ,
hilaŋ siniriṙ iŋ samīraṇa hawunya tumuluy anarīra riŋ hṛĕbuk*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:90:\:10:\:1:. saŋ hyaŋ niŋ suraloka tan pahamĕṅan namu namu pĕjaḥ iŋ pamañcanan,
sūkṣmāṅjanma marèŋ widaṙƀanagarī sira ta pinakasāri niŋ sarāt,
putrī śrī kraŧakèśikèśwara nĕhĕṙ hayu nira kadi ṅūni n apsarī,
ꝁyāti śrīndumatī panaṅgaḥ i sira n pamuꝁa kadi śaśaṅka pūṙṇnama*

:91:\:10:\:2:. lwīṙ iŋ swapna wijil nirādƀuta kaṛĕṅwan i wali nira riŋ kadèwatan,
ṛĕmṛĕm taŋ daśadèśa dè ni sahab iŋ jaladakusuma muṅgu riŋ tawaŋ,
lĕṅlĕŋ dè ni gĕṛĕhnya ṣaṭpada maliwran apupul irikaŋ limut hṛĕbuk,
sumyuk taŋ mađupuṣpawaṙṣa maduluṙ jaya jaya ri jayā nṛpātmajā*

:92:\:10:\:3:. ṅūni n tuṅgal anak narèśwara lawö manaḥ ira ri wijil nṛpātmajā,
ndātan pèmbuḥ ikaŋ suꝁè sira baṅun bañu humidĕŋ aṅanti riŋ ranu,
maṅkè n pèmbuḥ anak nirāhayu sinamƀawa maṅadĕha lakṣmi niŋ purī,
Èmbuḥ göŋ kadi sāgara rwab amĕpĕk suꝁa nira ri wijil nṛpātmajā*

:93:\:10:\:4:. rakryan saŋ pinakèña rakwa kulawaṅśa wĕka wĕka kadaŋ kadaŋ haji,
Aśrī waṙṇna nirāraras kadi saroja kinĕlabakĕn iŋ ryak iŋ bañu,
dè niŋ mĕñcuḥ aṅambĕk ambĕki saƀāwa nira tĕka hiṛĕŋ kinèriṅan,
suswan bāhwan agasyak aṅhalĕpakĕn ‌wruḥ iŋ aṅinakanè tuhan tuhan*

:94:\:10:\:5:. lāwan towi nirāhalĕp maṛĕka hadyana kunaŋ asawaŋ priyambada,
ndan paṙṇnaḥ kaka dè nirèña nira kaṙwwa sira paḍa suśīla wīṙyyawan,
kāliḥ kāliḥ irāṅharis haris anuswani rahina wĕṅī suputrikā,
saṅkèŋ swaṙgga hulun tuhāṅgĕḥ ira ṅūni ri hana nira riŋ kadèwatan*

:95:\:10:\:6:. wwaŋ ri jro juru niŋ mĕṅĕs pinaṛĕk iŋ wagĕd amirit i hatwik iŋ manis,
sakwan sèlwan atūt manahnya kalawan kabayan iŋ aṛĕjèŋ kaguṇḍikan,
tuṅgal riŋ katĕkāsihan lawan ikaŋ pinuji pinakagusti riŋ raras,
rūm rakryan nṛpaputrikā mawa hayunya tuhu ratu ni raśmi niŋ prajā*

:96:\:10:\:7:. strī māwak caturaṅga saƀya tan aŧāni panagara tĕkāhawan raŧa,
prāyāpāmbĕkan aśwasañcari lakunya wagĕd aniru lampaḥ iŋ liman,
nistanya n wiparīta rūpa nika tan kasaḥ i pada narèndraputrikā,
himpĕṙ pèka minantṙyyakĕn huwus aƀūṣaṇa hinalĕpakĕn yayāhala*

:97:\:10:\:8:. rakryan rājasutānwam èṅgal atuhāṅiṅĕt iṅĕtakĕn aṅdĕlö tawaŋ,
Aṅliṅliŋ kinahaṙṣan iŋ kaka  kakāmwaṅi sira rinĕbut pinaṅkwakĕn,
kahyun hyun kumuṛĕb kuṛĕb kumĕdal aśriŋ aniru niru putra niŋ pĕñu,
wahw āhuntw aputiḥ katon sĕḍĕŋ irāṣĕmu guyu baṅun aṅhĕmū mĕnur*

:98:\:10:\:9:. solaḥ ƀāwa nirāmaṅun siḥ aṅĕwaḥ bapa bapa juga dè nirāṅucap,
yan paṅjaṅkaḥ aṅaṅguḥ aṅguhi gumoḥ lumaris asĕmu lĕmbu kanyakā,
mogāhyaŋ sira yan maluṅguḥ araṛĕm tumiru tiru paluṅguḥ iŋ gaṇa,
yan sorè mulat iŋ wulan ‌wruḥ awawā wulan anuduhi wimba niŋ wulan*

:99:\:10:\:10:. Èndaḥ budđi nikaŋ wanèḥ mamitaṅis mitaṅis i sira haṙṣa riŋ taṅis,
Èṅgal maṙyy anaṅis pinakpak amanis wulat ira sinawè pinaṅkwakĕn,
lèn tèkaŋ haṛĕp iŋ halāhala halan mamalaku hala hāsyakāraṇa,
maṅkin tībra raras narèndratanayāhayu ri huwus ira n pawèḥ ala*

:100:\:10:\:11:. Anwam tapwan apāsarik hayu nirān inaṅĕtan apupuk ri wunbunan,
tan paṅdè hala tambĕḥ iŋ hayu bajaŋ bajaŋ ira mata niŋ lawak bulu,
pantĕs yan pagĕlaŋ lawè wĕnaŋ i kāla nira kapĕjahan rarè bajaŋ,
tambā niŋ sĕgu tuṅtuŋ iŋ sĕṛĕḥ aṅimbuhi manis ira yan hanè rahi*

:101:\:10:\:12:. ndi nyū danta paḍā mĕnè n lĕwiha yan maṛĕk i sira sĕḍĕŋ pinaṅkwakĕn,
lāwan kètaka dūra n aṅhiriba nista nika n inupaṛĕṅgan iŋ ṭikā,
sakwèḥ niŋ kusumāwĕnĕs pinakataṇḍiŋ ira wawaŋ alum sakèŋ taṅan,
maṅgĕḥ dè niŋ anuswanī sira dudū lawan anak anakan sinuswakĕn*

:102:\:10:\:13:. Èṅgal ‌wruḥ tinitaḥ bisātaratayan wĕgig aṅadĕg adĕg wawaŋ tibā,
guywan ‌wruḥ makukuk bayan tinañakĕn kahanan ira bisātukup mata,
sorèṣuk malĕbū lĕbū cala kinon ahuwusana ya saṅkan iŋ taṅis,
haṙṣānon gigiṛĕn sirāṅgyat anĕpak bisu bisu nĕhĕṙ aṅgigiṙ gigir*

:103:\:10:\:14:. dudw aṅkĕn wĕṅi dè nira n ‌wruḥ aṅucap mari bisu bisu saṅṣayābĕnĕr,
sāmpun rakwa sirāpupak pinakapūṙwwaka nira n aṅajī munīśwara,
prajña ‌wruḥ ri kalīṅa niŋ pada kadi ‌wruḥ alawas anulus wicakṣaṇa,
Èṅgal paŧya ri kaprayogan i ruṣit niŋ aji kadi tĕmaḥ saraṣwatī*

:104:\:10:\:15:. Umwat śīǥra tuwuḥ nirāhayu sawaŋ salaga niŋ asanāṅṛĕṅö gĕṛĕḥ,
tapwan ‌wruḥ riŋ iraŋ dahat kalukaran tapiḥ awuda wudāgĕlaŋ  gĕlaŋ,
tan pèndaḥ lĕṅĕŋ iŋ wuluḥ gaḍiŋ i kāla ni pamilĕt i luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,
mambĕt mađya nirāwĕlū buṅaḥ i waṙṇna nika kadi giliŋ giliŋ kuñit*

:105:\:10:\:16:. niṙwwā tan paguṇa ŋ pupuṙ pinakapahyas ira tĕwas awèḥ kram iŋ muꝁa,
dūrāṅhaywana tan padon sipat irāṅlĕtuhi ri hĕniŋ iŋ matābiru,
lāwan taŋ paṅĕluk lĕṅĕn wiꝑala yèka karaṇa ni halis nira n tikĕl,
wyaṙŧāŋ tūlahanānukĕṙ nukĕri tan wuruŋ amaṅunakĕn sṛĕt iŋ susu*

:106:\:10:\:17:. sumraŋ śraŋ mata wahw atön ri lĕṅĕŋ iŋ gĕṛĕḥ aṅirim irim lawan riris,
Aṅlūd ry ambĕk ira n rimaŋ taṅis ikaŋ ƀramara kalilipĕn saḍĕk hṛĕbuk,
yan sorè ri huwus nirāhawu hawu ‌wruḥ amawa kalaṅön irèŋ natar,
Aṅhĕmban karas èsi ƀāṣa pinakānak anakan ira tan saḥ iŋ tanaḥ*

:107:\:10:\:18:. piṇḍa dwādaśawaṙṣa kāla ni wijil nira rumara rara n hanè dalĕm,
yan paṅhyas hyasi moǥa tan kawanĕhan tiniru tiru sadè nirāṅhyasi,
sotan ta ŋ hyaŋ iŋ Indraloka kapana n tan apĕnĕda tĕmahnya mānuṣa,
lakṣmī niŋ nagarāhulap mulat i rūpa nira n ahayu katwaŋ iŋ tulis*

:108:\:10:\:19:. miṅkil tapwan agöŋ payođara nirāṅlĕwihi buṅaḥ i tuṅtuŋ iŋ gaḍiŋ,
hyaŋ hiŋ tāman aṅiṇḍarat sĕmu ni rūpa nira n ahayu muṅgu riŋ taman,
tistis lālana tan hanāṅiriṅakĕn laku nira kadi tan tuhan tuhan,
molaḥ sumpiŋ irāṣanālum awĕnĕs baṅun awĕdi ri luñcip iŋ mata*

:109:\:10:\:20:. paṅrāt niŋ kalaṅön tinuṙwwakĕn irèŋ watu karaŋ aṅilo wway iŋ ranu,
tan śoƀā humiriŋ lumaḥ makakaraŋ hulu lĕṅĕn ira mūṙcꞓitāṅligā,
paṇḍan raṅkaŋ aṅöbi tan panisi mātra ri sira n apulaŋ lawan hṛĕbuk,
Amṛĕm kaṙwwa karas lĕṅĕŋ kadi ṭikā piniturun inamĕṙ sakèŋ puḍak*

:110:\:10:\:21:. maṅkin maṙmma narèndra māsiḥ anĕkāni samaṅinakanè manaḥ nira,
budđi śrī paramèśwarī suꝁa makānak i sira samanaḥ nirènariḥ,
maṅkè n tan hana wahw atakwan ahiḍĕp nṛpati tĕka sirāṅhĕmū guyu,
maṅgĕḥ budđi nirājajaṙ lawan anak nira baṅun aṅabèhi jīwita*

:111:\:10:\:22:. saŋ ƀojānak irātuhāpagĕḥ ikaŋ guṇa ri sira paṅa‌wruḥ iŋ ratu,
sākṣāt prāṇawa īśwara nṛĕpati kāsiḥ ira sira suśīla nītimān,
Aṅhiŋ rakwa pakö narèśwara ri ƀūmi nira sira sadā janapriya,
maṅgĕḥ rowaŋ irāṅadĕg ri hiḍĕp iŋ mulat i suꝁa nira n paḍāpagĕḥ*

:112:\:10:\:23:. ndan griŋ saŋ praƀu saṅṣayābwat atĕlĕb maṅinak inaki tan tulus waras,
tĕṅrān iŋ hurip iŋ śarīra paḍa rūkṣa mawaraḥ i tĕkā nikaŋ pati,
yèkā hètu nirāṅutus maṛĕka riŋ dwijawara ṛṣi śaiwa sogata,
mwaŋ mantrī winĕkas wĕkas nira n anak nira sumiliha ratwa haywa lèn*

:113:\:10:\:24:. sakwèḥ saŋ winĕkas wĕkas paḍa tĕñuḥ twas ira kahĕnĕṅan mulat juga,
dè niŋ duhꝁa tumon i kāsy asiḥ i saŋ kawĕkas ira dumèḥ sirāṣiha,
mojaṙ mātra pĕgat pĕgat wĕkasan amriḥ asayut amĕlas mĕlas haṛĕp,
luḥ lāwan sĕkĕl iŋ taṅis duluṙ i dè nira sumahuṙ i śabda saŋ praƀu*

:114:\:10:\:25:. hè nāŧaṅku huwus kapaṅku wacana nṛĕpati raṣa nirāwĕkas wĕkas,
An saŋ ƀoja gumantya ratwakĕna yadyapi pĕjaha mĕnè narèśwara,
ndan lwiṙ wyaṙŧa ḍawuḥ ni śabda naranāŧa ri sama maṛĕk aṅlawad lawad,
Āpan‌ ṅhiŋ sira kèṅĕ kèṅĕt alawas kumalilirana kapraƀun haji*

:115:\:10:\:26:. śaktin dè naranāŧa haywa lĕsu saŋ praƀu tahapana wèdya kinkinĕn,
śrī dèwīndumatī katoliha katon uwuḥ uwuha nira n katiṅgala,
mwaŋ saŋ ƀoja sirānwam aṙdđa kapalaŋ wĕkasakĕna narèndra riŋ prajā,
ndān amriḥ mriha saŋ praƀu syapa parāśrayana sama maṛĕk mĕnè n kari*

:116:\:10:\:27:. nāhan liŋ sama maṅlawad lawad i saŋ praƀu lara nira mèmbuḥ aṅlarè,
wahw āṅlumpuhi saṅṣayāmaṅĕti roga nira wawaŋ alum sirāwĕnĕs,
tan polaḥ sira tan kĕḍap ṅuni ṅuni n paṅucapa sira kèwalāturū,
ṅhiŋ maṅguḥ kalawan miṅĕl sahuṙ ira n tinaña tañan i dè nirālara*

:117:\:10:\:28:. satya śrī paramèśwarī tan awĕdīŋ pati tumuta ri līna saŋ praƀu,
ndan dèwīndumatī tinoliḥ ira kāsy asiha nira mĕnè n katiṅgala,
mwaŋ saŋ ƀoja paḍānwam anwam anaṅis paḍa wihikan i tībra saŋ praƀu,
kāliḥ kāliḥ irāpupul tinaṅisan pinĕkul ira nĕhĕṙ sinuṅkĕman*

:118:\:10:\:29:. Ꜽ ƀojaṅku wĕkaṅku haywa tan asiḥ kita bapa riy arinta kāsihan,
putrīṅkwi indumatīṅku ƀaktya ri kakanta kita sarika samƀawāsiha,
Anwam kāri tuhanku dèṅku kawĕkas riŋ iña lawan uwāmalaṙ tuha,
himpĕṙ hantiga niŋ manuk taḍahasiḥ sy anaku tinuwawākĕn iŋ wanèḥ*

:119:\:10:\:30:. wuṅṣw amwīta bibinta matya tumutè kapati saŋ ahulun‌ ṅhulun tuhan,
lwāmbĕk māsku saŋ aprihèŋ ƀuwana sĕmbahĕn iŋ amawa rāt kitānaku,
Ꜽ putrīndumatīṅku māsku t ahurup tapiḥ alaḥ ibu kènku kènakĕn,
soṅṣoṅaṅkwa tapihta kaṙwwana lawan haji lĕpasa mamukṣa mukṣana*

:120:\:10:\:31:. sĕmbaḥ ni ṅhulun alpađaṙmma ri padadwaya paramawiśèṣapaṇḍita,
pun dèwīndumatī kayatnakĕna dè wiwuđapati bapèbwa māsiha,
mwaŋ saŋ ƀoja muwaḥ wuruk wurukĕn iŋ nagara palaṙ aniṙwwa saŋ praƀu,
waṙṣājñāna parāđipaṇḍita dumadyakĕna kawijayanya riŋ prajā*

:121:\:10:\:32:. nāhan liŋ paramèśwarī tucapa saŋ praƀu kasiḥ aṛĕp aṅhiḍĕp lara,
saŋ hyaŋ jīwa hanè gulū nira lawan kĕtĕ kĕtĕg ira saṅṣayāsamun,
sāmpun kāku pasāra sāra ni waraḥ yatiwara rinĕgĕp narèśwara,
tan simpaŋ kadi dè nirāṅayatakĕn panaḥ aṅĕnani dè nirāṅhiḍĕp*

:122:\:10:\:33:. tṛṣṇābanđana riŋ śarīra pinĕgat nira manaḥ ira kèwalāhĕniŋ,
sadyotkranti linakṣyakĕn pataṅananya tumutupana simpaŋ iŋ hĕnū,
lāwan mantra nikā ndatan dwa sira saŋ praƀu wiƀu riŋ awak wawaŋ mĕsat,
kèwalyāśraya sūkṣma māri kahiḍĕp mamaṛĕṅi śiwamāṙgga dug mĕṅā*

:123:\:10:\:34:. sāmpun māti narèśwarātri sakaḍatwan anaṅisi pĕjaḥ nirālara,
śrī dèwīndumatī muwaḥ tinaṅisan kapati lumay awak nirāwĕnĕs,
mādan śrī paramèśwarī maṛĕk anĕmbaḥ i śawa haji satya sādara,
mājaṙ yan sira milwa matya pawaraḥ nira karaṇa ni luḥ niŋ aṅṛĕṅö*

:124:\:10:\:35:. hè nāŧaṅku nihan‌ ṅhulun praṇata ƀakti tumuta saparanta tan saha,
yadyastun kita dèwatāŧawa manuṣya huluna pakĕnaṅkwa dè haji,
putrī putra rarā sĕḍĕŋ mĕṛĕ mĕṛĕḥ kaŧamapi tan ikā katoliha,
patṛĕmta praƀu yèki haṇḍĕmana ni ṅhulun amaḥ aku suṅṣuŋ iŋ hĕnū*

:125:\:10:\:36:. nā liŋ śrī paramèśwarī nĕhĕṙ apatṛĕm amĕkasi hurip sirāṣĕgu,
himpĕṙ waṙṣa tibā nikaŋ luḥ i widaṙƀanagara humilī mawaḥ wahan,
sambat sambat ikaŋ sarājya gumĕṛĕḥ kadi kĕtĕṙ i gĕṛĕḥ niŋ ampuhan,
tawwan riŋ kusumāṅjraḥ iŋ masa kapat paḍa ni taṅis ikā n rinĕṅwakĕn*

:126:\:10:\:37:. prāpta ŋ truḥ kadi sĕmbu sĕmbuṙ i jajāṅawara ri gĕmuḥ iŋ payođara,
waṙṇnākāra nikaŋ kuwuŋ kuwuŋ apiṇḍa pupuk i rahi kèṅgutan halis,
polaḥ niŋ kilat iŋ tawaŋ kadi kĕḍap niŋ asamaya kapaṅgihèŋ taman,
his hīs niŋ bañu muṅgu riŋ taṛĕtĕpan kadi luḥ iŋ anaṅis pinaṅkwakĕn*

:127:\:10:\:38:. muṅgw iŋ maṇḍyusa kāli kāliḥ ira moǥa kadi kinasut iŋ pasaṅgaman,
kèṅĕṙ mātra gulū narèndramahiṣī kadi cala cala tan panūt kinol,
piṅgiṙ niŋ kanin iŋ jajāsĕmu miraḥ kadi karagĕt i tuṅtuŋ iŋ kuku,
rāhĕn siñjaŋ ira n lumè miṅay awaṙṇna wahu kawawa dè narèśwara*

:128:\:10:\:39:. śrī dèwīndumatī lĕwĕs lara nira n panaṅis asidĕhāṅurè gĕluŋ,
mambĕt mađya nirāṅgaluṅgaŋ araras tĕṅaḥ ira sumawè ri saŋ pĕjaḥ,
tan kèwran lukaṙ iŋ tapiḥ wijil i luḥ nira tan inusapan hanè muꝁa,
sambat sambat irāṅṛĕmĕk hati raṣanya karaṇa ni taṅis niŋ aṅṛĕṅö*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:129:\:11:\:1:. Ahā bibi haji ndi sihta winaliṅku ta kita tulusāsihè ṅhulun,
muwaḥ bapa haji ndi sihta palakunkwa tulusa ni wĕlasta ri ṅhulun,
Ujaṙtta kita ṅūni kāsihana niŋ jagat anaku sadā pakāśrayan,
jagat karika māsihèṙyy aku kita pwa paḍa tan awĕlas maṅaṙyyakĕn*

:130:\:11:\:2:. praƀuṅku kita kāliḥ ĕndi parananta pawuṅu sakaṛĕŋ waraḥ ṅhulun,
yan iŋ śiwapadāŧawèŋ haripadāŧawa lĕpasa kunaŋ sakèrikā,
ṅhulun tumuturāpa don iŋ ahurip wiꝑala yan apasaḥ lawan kita,
patiṅku hawanaṅkwa muṅṣiṙ i padanta bapa tañakĕnèŋ kadèwatan*

:131:\:11:\:3:. pulahta humĕnĕŋ diṅaṙyyan asagaṙ ndi kari culu culuhta ri ṅhulun,
nihan‌ ṅhulun anakta paṅkwakĕn aḍātiśaya bapa kita n huwus pĕjaḥ,
prayojana ni dèṅkw asambat akusā baribinana kita n paḍāturū,
palaṙ palaṙ awuṅwa dè ni panaṅisku nĕhĕṙ ajara māsku cĕp tuhan*

:132:\:11:\:4:. nihan tĕtĕlakĕn hatiṅku bibi muṅgaḥ akĕsĕl ahĕnĕk tĕkè jaja,
muwaḥ priḥ i mataṅku tīsana rahup rahupana bibi bawwa bawwana,
pilī  piliṅan i ṅhulun dumadak aṅhĕlu pupukana tulya tulyana,
guluṅku kadi mèḥ kahötana raṣanya n anaṅis i patinta sĕmbuṛĕn*

:133:\:11:\:5:. ri kāla ni huripta ṅūni bibi sāhasa kita sahasāṅabĕt‌ ṅhulun,
hasiḥ bapa hajī ṅhulun tĕka sirānuluŋ aṅusapi luḥ mamaṅkwakĕn,
mataŋ ya bibi maḥ palu ṅhulun alaḥ pawuṅu sakahaṛĕp‌ ṅhulun habĕt,
ndya sī yan anuluŋ muwaḥ bapa hajī ṅhulun atĕhĕṙ ataṅguhè kita*

:134:\:11:\:6:. syapèka śaraṇāśrayaṅkwa ri pĕjahta bapa haji nihan dudut‌ ṅhulun,
Apan kaka turuŋ wĕnaŋ śaraṇa ni ṅhulun apituwin anwam iŋ wayaḥ,
kadaŋ kadaŋ adoḥ sirāṣiḥ alĕbāmihutaṅanana sī kadi ṅhulun,
mataŋ yan anakanta riŋ suruwayan‌ ṅhulun alaḥ alapĕn maran pĕjaḥ*

:135:\:11:\:7:. Aḍā hyaŋ aparan ta koŋ wiđi ṅaranmu tan awĕlas adĕṅky anon suꝁa,
bapaṅku sira māti dèmu mapa doṣa nira huwus akīṙtti riŋ jagat,
lawan bibi tumūt praṣidđa tika ko muwaḥ amĕjahi tan pakāraṇa,
mataŋ ya wĕtu ko rwa sānak aku patyani saha bala dèmu hĕntyakĕn*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:136:\:12:\:1:. nāhan sambat irānaṅis kaḍĕḍĕtan lara hati nira tan wĕnaŋ kinöl,
simsim wāhu hilaŋ maṇiknya kalĕbū paḍa paḍa nira niṣpraƀākucĕm,
dady ātèja katonan iŋ rahina tan parawi wĕṅi tiniṅgal iŋ wulan,
saṅkè rūpa nirāṣawaŋ kaṛĕbahan gunuŋ alara ri līna saŋ praƀu*

:137:\:12:\:2:. paṅdè niŋ wiđi tan wĕnaŋ winađa tiṅhalana kasiḥ aṛĕp suputrikā,
kāṙyy anwam ri pĕjaḥ narèśwara samaṇḍyusa sira kalawan narèśwarī,
dè niŋ duhꝁa kĕdö sirāmalaku milwa maṅatigana maṇḍyusè dalĕm,
patṛĕm wahw inunus nirènayatakĕn ri jaja kaka kakākrak aṅṛĕbut*

:138:\:12:\:3:. maṅkin ǥūṙṇnita śabda niŋ wwaŋ anaṅis wĕdi kaluputanèŋ nṛpātmajā,
Āpan budđi nirāṅhuwus huwus apakṣa pĕjaha tumutè narèśwara,
göŋ tṛṣṇāsiḥ arāma rèna kapĕgan kapati pati sirālarānaṅis,
drāk sidđānĕmu duhꝁa niŋ dadi manuṣya paṅawaśa ni śāpa saŋ‌ ṛṣi*

:139:\:12:\:4:. saŋ ƀoja prihati n tumon kasiḥ aṛĕp ny awak ira kari dè narèśwara,
kady agriŋ sira dè ni duhꝁa nira tan saḥ anaṅis i dagan narāđipa,
Āśāƀūta marambĕhan wĕtu ni luḥ nira mulat i narèndrakanyakā,
maṙmmāmaṅku pĕgat pĕgat sapitutuṙ nira tuna tuna dè nikaŋ taṅis*

:140:\:12:\:5:. rakryan haywa wiraṅṙwwaŋ induŋ ĕnĕbĕn ta pamanas i laranta tīsakĕn,
riŋ swaṙggasŧa narèndra sāmpun atuhāpituwi huwus akīṙtti riŋ jagat,
pakṣa kṣatriya rāka rakryan apagĕḥ wĕnaṅa śaraṇa rakryan iŋ hayu,
ṅhiŋ yan māti kakanta mamriḥ iŋ ayun kita pĕjaha tumūta ri ṅhulun*

:141:\:12:\:6:. haywāśālara duhꝁa yan bapa haji mwaŋ ibu haji pĕjaḥ sirādulur,
yāwat janma ṅaranya tan hana tuwuḥ watu kaluputa saṅka riŋ pati,
tan pèndaḥ kadi cakra niŋ raŧa tĕka ŋ dadi niyata midĕṙ puriḥ nika,
saṅkèŋ mṛtyu tĕka ŋ hurip kunĕŋ ikaŋ pati niyata mijil sakèŋ hurip*

:142:\:12:\:7:. māyākāra hanèŋ cṛĕmin paḍa nikaŋ dadi sahana hananya tan‌ sŧiti,
himpĕṙ pādapa tan wuruŋ manirarāmĕkasi tuha tuwuhnya tan lanā,
tiṅkaḥ niŋ hurip iŋ manuṣya juti tattwa nika tan alawas wawaŋ hilaŋ,
kintw īkaŋ pati jāti tattwa nika tan‌ kṣaṇika pinakađaṙmma niŋ dadi*

:143:\:12:\:8:. Èman ṅwaŋ lumĕkas mamèt pati sakèŋ lumĕkasa ri kapètan iŋ hurip,
pöṅpöṅĕn ta huripta yogya dadahanta makahuluna dè munīśwara,
Āpan yan ‌wruḥ i ƀèda saŋ rwa kalawan ‌wruha ri pasamudāya niŋ tiga,
Icꞓā nora kasaṅśayèŋ hala lawan hayu niyata luput sakèrika*

<wisaṙjjita> – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓

:144:\:13:\:1:. kumwa kunaŋ liṅa rakryan apa hayu nikaŋ hayu yan gawayĕn,
ri ‌wruḥ i saŋ rwa ƀinèda lawan i sira saŋ tri tinuṅgalakĕn,
kumwa kunaŋ liṅa rakryan apa hala nikaŋ hala yan gawayĕn,
ri ‌wruḥ i saŋ rwa ƀinèda lawan i sira saŋ tri tinuṅgalakĕn*

:145:\:13:\:2:. siṅgiḥ ujaṙtta ri saŋ kṛtasamaya wiśèṣa paṅa‌wruḥ ira,
kwèḥ nira riŋ nagarèŋ acala paḍa tikā pinakoṅgwan ira,
ndin rakĕta ŋ suꝁaduhꝁa ri sira satatābrata tan palabuḥ,
lokaparāśraya kāraṇa nira magawè hayu tan wipaŧa*

:146:\:13:\:3:. saŋ ‌wruḥ i saŋ wĕkas iŋ samaya winuni dè paramādiguru,
kèwala śudđa manaḥ nira linĕtu lĕtuḥ kapanālĕtuha,
wāhyaśarīra pinucꞓa nira ri tĕka niŋ pati tan ginĕgö,
jñāna wiśèṣa śarīra nira taya śarīra nirèŋ wĕkasan*

:147:\:13:\:4:. wwaŋ magawè hayu yan ‌wruḥ i sira saŋ amukti gawènya hayu,
tan dadi tan luput iŋ hayu hayu ni gawè nika tan wiꝑala,
wwaŋ magawè hala yan ‌wruḥ i sira saŋ amukti gawènya hala,
tan dadi tan luput iŋ hala hala ni gawè nika tan wiꝑala*

:148:\:13:\:5:. wwaŋ magawè hayu tan ‌wruḥ i sira saŋ amukti gawènya hayu,
tan dadi tan tumĕmu ŋ hayu hayu ni gawènya tumūt maṅiriŋ,
wwaŋ magawè hala tan ‌wruḥ i sira saŋ amukti gawènya hala,
tan dadi tan tumĕmu ŋ hala hala ni gawènya tumūt maṅiriŋ*

:149:\:13:\:6:. saŋ wiku gūḋa nihan wulatana mamaṅan tĕḍa riŋ pahĕhan,
tan tĕḍa tan śuci ta pwa sahana hana niŋ pinaṅan liŋ ira,
hètu nirāmbĕk alokika winulatan ajṛĕm apiṇḍa kasop,
śudđa nikaŋ pratipatti makalarapan uttama niŋ samaya*

:150:\:13:\:7:. māsku mataṅnyan ikaŋ hayu gawayakĕnanta sĕḍĕŋ mahurip,
paṇḍita towi yayā sira maṅulahakĕn brata tan kaluṣa,
budđy ahĕniŋ brata yoga tapa taki takinta maran kawaśa,
gĕgwana rakryan anĕmwakĕna wara waraḥ paramādiguru*

<giriṣa> ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:151:\:14:\:1:. Anĕmu nĕmu kĕtèkā saŋ sāmpun kṛtasamaya,
wihikan i raṣa saŋ hyaŋ tattwajñāna kalĕpasĕn,
tan uliḥ uliḥ iŋ aṅdoḥ saṅkèŋ pāda muniwara,
Uliḥ iŋ asaṅu tasyan ƀaktīŋ paṇḍita matuha*

:152:\:14:\:2:. Aṅinak inaka taŋ wwaŋ yāwat‌ jñāna pinakadon,
syapa ta sira mamaṅgiḥ tattwajñāna dudu gawè,
hana satata masèwā tan byaktanya pinihanan,
sukṛta juga maṅintè lāwan duṣkṛta maṅiriŋ*

:153:\:14:\:3:. hana sira guruputrānak niŋ paṇḍita nagara,
sahana nira ta rakwādṛwya ŋ‌ jñāna pakagurun,
taha tan ika panidđan wèt niŋ paṇḍita matuha,
Amilihi juga saŋ hyaŋ tattwèŋ uṅgwana rahayu*

:154:\:14:\:4:. Anak iŋ apirak akwèḥ ṅūnī nwamnya paḍa suꝁa,
sahana nika ta rakwāniṙww akwèḥ apirak ika,
taha tan ika panidđan wèt niŋ śrèṣṫa panariman,
Amilihi juga saŋ hyaŋ śrī tan siŋ kahanan ira*

:155:\:14:\:5:. kita yayi sĕḍĕŋ anwam priḥ saŋ hyaŋ raṣa kawikun,
pira karika musuḥ niŋ wikw aṅhiŋ nĕm ikaŋ akas,
Alahakĕn i dalĕm twas pèt siŋ soṅgwan ika raraḥ,
Alaha pĕjaha rakryan yèki swaṙgga ṅaran ika*

<basantatilaka> – – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓

:156:\:15:\:1:. nā dè nirāwara waraḥ ri narèndraputrī,
tapwan tĕtĕs tinuna sanđi nikaŋ prayoga,
Anwam suśīla guṇamanta kṛtopadèśa,
saṅkè paṅajyan ira ka‌wruḥ irāđiguhya*

:157:\:15:\:2:. śrī putrikā kapĕnĕtan humĕnĕŋ tumuṅkul,
sāmpun ƀinasmi śawa saŋ praƀu dè munīndra,
muṅgw ī taman sira cinaṇḍi lawan sudèwī,
sampūṙṇna bapra nira ratna mahāpraƀāwa*

:158:\:15:\:3:. saŋ ƀoja sāmpun aṅadĕg ri widaṙƀarājya,
swasŧā saƀūmi nira ƀakty anukūla sāđu,
mawwat paḍāmarahakĕn ri suꝁanya rakwa,
Anwam muwaḥ nṛpati liṅnya muwaḥ manĕmbaḥ*

:159:\:15:\:4:. sāmpun sirāyugala ratna wiśèṣaputrī,
rājāṅkurāwilĕt ikaŋ pakuṛĕn sawanđu,
soluṙ lulut sahati lĕṅlĕŋ aluṅluṅan kuŋ,
saśrī sakĕmbaŋ alaṅö sakurā sawīja*

:160:\:15:\:5:. kaywan ragas paḍa nikaŋ nagarī widaṙƀa,
riŋ wṛdđarūpa haji dèwata lahru sākṣāt,
maṅkè n praṣidđa kadi kaywan aron akĕmbaŋ,
śrī ƀoja maṅdani sirānwam apiṇḍa ṛĕṅṛĕŋ*

:161:\:15:\:6:. wèt niŋ kṛtā ri paṅadĕg haji nora duṣṭa,
ramya ŋ hĕnū tĕgal ayun tĕka riŋ wanādri,
wāni ŋ wwaŋ aṅhaliwatīriya tuṅga tuṅgal,
Aṅhiŋ gaḍuŋ luŋ ika maṅhabĕt aśriŋ oliḥ*

:162:\:15:\:7:. mantrī nirātuha tuha dwija śaiwa bodđa,
kāsiḥ kapaṙccaya narèndra wĕnaŋ marè jro,
prajñèṅgitajña ginulaŋ halu riŋ wiwèka,
sojaṙ niŋ āgama tinūt nira tan wimāṙgga*

:163:\:15:\:8:. söḥ śāla đaṙmma kuṭi kīṙtti narèndra riŋ rāt,
wwaŋ śrèṣṫi đaṙmma ginawè nira sāri sāri,
wwaŋ duṣṭa moǥa kapitūt milu đaṙmmabudđi,
solaḥ swaƀāwa haji tan dadi tan tinūtnya*

:164:\:15:\:9:. śrī ƀoja sāmpun apagĕḥ siniwīŋ kaḍatwan,
Okĕṙ tumiṅhal i saŋ Indumatī hanè jro,
Āpan samāsa niŋ akaṙmma wayaḥ nirāgöŋ,
Aṅhiŋ swayĕmbarakĕnèṅĕt iṅĕt narèndra*

:165:\:15:\:10:. nā dè nirāṅiṅĕt iṅĕt kalawan sudèwī,
sāmpun wināhyakĕn irè kulawanđu ri jro,
riŋ saṙwwasidđi tuwin amṛĕtayoga tĕmbè,
höman hajīnarahakĕn para taṇḍa mantrī*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓

:166:\:16:\:1:. Èñjiŋ śrīndumatī kinon maṛĕka kāliḥ saŋ sunandāṅiriŋ,
lāgy āmūṙṇnama mopawāsa ya ta maṅdè suṅkawā niŋ hati,
tistis mèḥ tumibā ŋ ḍawuḥ wwalu lumampaḥ tan kwa dè niŋ harip,
mukṣa lwīṙ amarāśrayè muꝁa nira śrī niŋ wulan tan lumöŋ*

:167:\:16:\:2:. sāmpun prāpta sirè dalĕm praṇata maṙmmātwaŋ ri jöŋ saŋ praƀu,
lāwan śrī paramèśwarī sira sinambaḥ māsiḥ aṅliŋ ṛĕsĕp,
Om rakryan pada nīlakaṇṫa kinaƀaktyantāstu dīṙǥāyuṣa,
swasŧā tuṅgalĕn iŋ manuṅgali jagat māskw ību nā liŋ nira*

:168:\:16:\:3:. mojaṙ saŋ praƀu māsku tan tugĕta niŋ twastān inundaŋ mami,
rākanta prihati n haṛĕp mamituhè māsku ndan èwĕḥ juga,
saŋ ratw āsiha lèn sasamƀawa muwaḥ yèkī pinèt ni ṅhulun,
kady amrat mrati mās juga ṅwaŋ amagantākĕn puriḥ niŋ dadi*

:169:\:16:\:4:. yāwat đaṙmma ṅaranya riŋ dadi manuṣyāwās hiwĕḥ yan pinèt,
lwiṙ sūkṣmā maganal ƀaṭāra gumawè tiṅkahnya yan maṅkana,
yadyastun jalu jalw amèta sawawanyèŋ janma haywāsali,
byaktèwĕḥ niki kimpunaḥ kita yan iŋ‌ strī strī n mamèta priya*

:170:\:16:\:5:. saṅkṣèpanya kita swayĕmbarakĕnaṅkwānugrahaṅkwè kita,
sakwèḥ saŋ ratu hundaṅĕn pilihanantāsiŋ sayogyè hati,
yadyan hyaŋ palakunta māsku yugalantāmriḥ mrihaṅkwāṅhyaṅa,
Aṅhiŋ yan hyaŋ Anaṅga kahyuna hadè tan pāwak èwĕḥ pinèt*

:171:\:16:\:6:. nājñā saŋ praƀu yogya paṅkwakĕna dè saŋ mās maṇik niŋ purī,
Āpan māsa nira n prapañca saputĕn riŋ rāga dè hyaŋ‌ smara,
tan ‌wruḥ riŋ sahurāwiraŋ mata sira n paṅyogyanè saŋ praƀu,
tan maṅguḥ sira tan miṅĕl kadi liṅiṙ mās aṙcca paṅhyaŋ hyaṅan*

:172:\:16:\:7:. tan saṅkèŋ awalèpa kāraṇa nira n lwiṙ tuhwa monabrata,
kèpwan budđi nirātĕgĕg maṅucap agyā gyān haṛĕp mantuka,
wahw ādandan anĕmbahè nṛpati mojaṙ saŋ sunandāṅjawil,
Om yan om huwusĕn huwus liṅa ni māskw ālaḥ tuhan mājara*

:173:\:16:\:8:. tan kèwö pitutuṙṇnya dè nṛpasutā mantuk sirèŋ pamṛĕman,
strī strī mājaṙ ajaṙ gumanti humatuṙ prāptèñjiŋ akwèḥ maṛĕk,
moliḥ tīṙŧa binuṅbuṅan winalun iŋ handoŋ sakèŋ paṙwwata,
maṅdè śudđa ri budđi saŋ praƀu suꝁā sāmpun sirācāmana*

<puṣpacāpa> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| – ⏓

:174:\:17:\:1:. prāṣāda sꝑaṭikālaṅö ri tĕṅaḥ iŋ nūsāraras pañcuranya,
strī stṙyy āmaṅku puḍak winimba makaranya lwiṙ lĕṅĕŋ dè ni kuṅnya,
kady ahyunn amahāywa luṅṣuṙ i tapihnya n maṅligā yan hana wwaŋ,
lāgy ānaṅga susunya saṅka ri pacuṙ niŋ wwai ya tāṅdè ṅĕlihnya*

:175:\:17:\:2:. ri prāṣāda hanāṙcca ratna ri dalĕm‌ ndān aṙdđanārīśwarāhyaŋ,
wimba śrī naranāŧa dèwata lawan dèwī nirārok śarīra,
ṅkā saŋ ƀoja maṅaṙccana pratidināṅaƀyāsa ri swasŧa niŋ rāt,
kady āmakpak aṅastwakĕn ri jayaśatṙwwa śrī narèndra n pamūjā*

:176:\:17:\:3:. saŋ ƀoja ‌wruḥ i tattwa niŋ japasamāđi n đāraṇa đyānapūṙwwa,
mwaŋ tiṅkaḥ niŋ adèhaśudđi pinakānuṣṫāna yan rècakādi,
sāmpun kālap ulaḥ dwijèśwara mamūjā paŧya riŋ brāhmamantra,
saŋ hyaŋ kūṭarahasyamantra jinapākĕn dè nirātūt gaṇitri*

:177:\:17:\:4:. tatkāla nṛĕpati n paṅuccaraṇakĕn mantra stutī saŋ hyaŋ aṙcca,
tan polaḥ wiṣayāṅhiḍĕp ri sira saṅyogānta riŋ yogya yogan,
maṅgā tan lĕpara ŋ japastawa sĕḍĕŋ niŋ‌ jñāna n ènak tĕtĕpnya,
simpaŋ niŋ hati yèki kāraṇa nirānaṅhāra saŋ hyaŋ śiwātma*

<giriṣa> ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:178:\:18:\:1:. ri huwus ira mamūjā līlā śudđa manaḥ ira,
Aṅusapi muꝁa saśrī dè niŋ candana karakĕt,
mijil aṅinaŋ aṅicꞓā riŋ wwai niŋ ranu maṅilo,
nĕhĕṙ anisigi dantè tuṅtuŋ niŋ gagaŋ inapi*

:179:\:18:\:2:. tucapa ta para mantrī śaiwa brāhmaṇa sugata,
paṛĕŋ apupul asèwa ṅkānè jro paḍa humatur,
nṛpati sira maluṅguḥ riŋ siṅhāsana kanaka,
Aṅiṅĕt iṅĕt i sidđā niŋ kāṙyya n gawayakĕna*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:180:\:19:\:1:. ndin kāṙyyèwĕha riŋ wicakṣaṇa sujanma lituhayu kawi priyambada,
ƀaktīŋ hyaŋ praƀu śakti đaiṙyya saha wānđawa saha bala kośawāhana,
yadyan sāgara tambakĕn satakĕnāŧawa wukiṙ alihĕn ratākĕna,
byaktāwās kawaśanya dè nira saŋ uttamapuruṣa wiśèṣa riŋ jagat*

:181:\:19:\:2:. śrī ƀoja pwa sira n praṣidđa guṇamanta saꝑala sira ƀūmipālaka,
prajñā śāstrawit iṅgita ‌wruḥ iŋ apālapan aṅinaki budđi niŋ maṛĕk,
Akwèḥ dṛwya nirāpramèya kadi sāgara papupulan iŋ wway iŋ nadī,
wany ānindita riŋ parākrama yan iŋ naya kadi ƀagawān wṛhaspati*

:182:\:19:\:3:. maṅkè pwa n hana rājakāṙyya gawayĕn kakaratala tĕkap narèśwara,
śrī dèwīndumatī swayĕmbarakĕnāmiliha  ratu sasamƀawè sira,
sāmpun saŋ praƀu motusan maminaṅè para ratu samayogya hundaṅĕn,
lāwan saŋ haja milwa winwitakĕn iŋ nṛpati raǥu katon tĕkā nira*

:183:\:19:\:4:. sāmpun höman irèrikā ta para taṇḍa sama sama samāṅhaṛĕp  gawè,
sorèṣuk gumĕṛĕḥ makakṛĕtug abaṇḍuŋ asahuran aganti loṙ kidul,
lèn taŋ wwaŋ maṅusuŋ lakaṙ lakaṙ ikā winaca wuhaya dè nikaŋ mulat,
Akwèḥ wwaŋ ka gĕrāḥ aṛĕp mulata wāhu mĕtu sinurakan muliḥ pacĕḥ*

:184:\:19:\:5:. Abwat hajyan ikaŋ humuŋ saha garantuŋ atabĕ tabĕhan paḍāsĕlur,
Agyā lagy aṅuhuḥ sirè haṛĕp alaḥ laku laku liŋ ikaŋ hanè wuri,
tuṅgul paṅhaṛĕp osik akṛĕp asinaŋ kumuliliŋ anamaṙ kuwuŋ kuwuŋ,
lwiṙ guntuṙ kamaṛĕkṛĕkĕn kayu pĕtuŋ priŋ asalĕsĕk agĕṇṭaḥ iŋ lĕbuḥ*

:185:\:19:\:6:. Èwĕṙ nora lĕgāŋ apaṇḍay anulis para lukis asipĕt mwaŋ aṅjahit,
sakwèḥ niŋ ginĕlaṙ ‌wruhāṅanam anam ‌wruḥ i suruhan ikā siliḥ tuluŋ,
solaḥ niŋ tama tan hanātaña ṅaranya huwus adu kabèḥ dinadyakĕn,
paprāṣan winaṅun paḍācarita paṙwwa piniturun atuṅgalan kaŧā*

<widyutkara> – – – |⏑⏑– |⏑– ⏑|⏑⏑– |⏑⏑⏑|⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑|⏓

:186:\:20:\:1:. Èmbuḥ ƀūṣaṇa niŋ tĕkĕn wuwuŋ apūṙwwa karacanan ikā tĕkèŋ pamanisan,
lāwan tiṅkaḥ ikaŋ paṅastṙyyanan apaṙppat ahalĕp akilā paḍāhayu hayu,
dè niŋ mās pinakopacāra sinisik pĕñu pinakawuwuṅnya kumram asinaŋ,
lwiṙ digdāha riŋ astapaṙwwata sĕnö nika murub apadĕlwan iŋ‌ kṣititala*

:187:\:20:\:2:. Aśrī ramya ni dè nirāmahāyu rājya kaliliran apūṙwwa kādƀuta dahat,
miṅgaṙ bapra nikè dalĕm watu hitĕm kuṭa nikaŋ i yawā lumaṅkuŋ ahiṛĕŋ,
kulwan wètan agopurātiśaya loṙ kidul agupura piṇḍa maṙppat aruhur,
kṛṣṇākāra paḍāṅlunaŋ kadi gunuŋ kumukus i sĕḍĕŋ iŋ darāwṛĕg aputiḥ*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:188:\:21:\:1:. luṅhā ŋ wṛtta ri kāṙyya saŋ praƀu paḍādƀuta sahana nikaŋ wwaŋ ṅṛĕṅö,
wwaŋ wwaŋ pora ḍusun ḍusun paḍa haṛĕp wihikana mulatèŋ swayambara,
tan samwas raray aṅhwan iŋ tĕgal atakwan i tĕka ni gawè narèśwara,
salwiṙ niŋ baṇijèŋ pĕkĕn taliṅa lintaḥ anaḍaḥ ucapan gawè nika*

:189:\:21:\:2:. sāmpun prāpta samotusan humatuṙ iŋ nṛpati sĕḍĕŋ irān hanèŋ saƀā,
Ènak budđi narèndra dè ni panuwal para ratu raṣa tan wuruŋ tĕkā,
lumrā ŋ wṛtta tĕkè dalĕm ri ḍatĕṅāṙyya raǥusuta marèŋ swayambara,
twas niŋ‌ strī sakaḍatwan aṅdadak aluŋ turida paḍa rumūpakè sira*

:190:\:21:\:3:. strī strī haṙṣa pinöm pinañjiṅakĕn iŋ nagara ri pamihaṅnya riŋ yayaḥ,
tan haṙṣèŋ kawi rakwa rèna nika monaguṇa pisaniṅūn tumiṅhala,
ndan rakwèki hinuṙṇnya matya saka riŋ tuluyakĕna susatya riŋ priya,
liṅnya n kèwala tan hinanti ni papaṅgiha nika pĕjahèŋ panambaṅan*

:191:\:21:\:4:. tapwan māri taṅis taṅisnya n inalap hinaturakĕn i jöŋ suputrikā,
wrā niŋ roma maṅèkadèśa ri piliŋ piliṅan ika baṅun pamèṙ i luḥ,
Ènak riŋ wĕkasan manahnya mamalaṙ malaṙ i pada narèndraputrikā,
Āpan swāmi nikā kaṛĕṅwan i paṛĕknya ri saŋ Aja tĕwĕk nikāpasaḥ*

:192:\:21:\:5:. Antuk saŋ priya maṅdawākĕn inalĕm para kawi sumĕnāha riŋ kajaŋ,
yèki n rakwa kinonya kady aṅucapāmaḥ aku tuhan alap waca ṅhulun,
moǥa nyan ya kinonakĕn wacan ikā ri pamaca nika maṅdadak lumuḥ,
swāminyādadi pustakānuturakĕn hiḍĕp ika pinapagnya riŋ taṅis*

:193:\:21:\:6:. ṅūnī kāla nika n turuŋ maṛĕk i jöŋ nira ṅaran ika kèn mađūdakā,
saŋ mambaŋ mađusūdana priya nikā kawi taruṇa maṛĕk ri jöŋ haji,
wiđy āmiđyani kāraṇanya wirahènalapan alara luhnya tan pĕgat,
ndaḥ rakryan jayawaspa tèki wĕkasan ṅaran ika satĕwĕk nikā maṛĕk*

<A> kind of/ Aƀikṛti ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:194:\:22:\:1:. para praƀu kaḍaṅhanan turida rāga nira sinaput iŋ‌ smarāmulaṅuni,
huwus katĕka kuŋ nirāhawan ujaṙ tuhun amĕlas aṛĕp riniptakĕn ira,
lawan punagi kèsy anambaha ri jöŋ nṛpawaraduhitā hana hyuna nira,
Akiṅkiŋ aṅalap kasoṙ paḍa tan apraƀu sahana nirāṛĕbut kahulunan*

:195:\:22:\:2:. wawaŋ nṛpatiputrikā rinĕbut iŋ hiḍĕp inaṅĕn aṅĕn raras raras ira,
hanan kahiḍĕp iŋ mađubrata ṛĕṅiḥ ṛĕṅiha nira n aṛĕs kapaṅkwa haraṣĕn,
lĕyĕp hayu nira n linaṅwakĕn amūṙtti kakawin inapus winèḥ amanisa,
hanè hati kinubđa kady apĕga kāraṇa nira mijil iŋ puḍak dadi ṭikā*

:196:\:22:\:3:. Adandan asĕnāha sañjata para praƀu ḍatĕṅa marè widaṙƀanagara,
lanāṅiṅĕt iṅĕt ri pahyasan irāṅinakana ri manaḥ narèndratanayā,
hanāṅdadak anat śarīra manahap nahap ahaṛĕp alantasa n winulatan,
paḍāṅalap alap sipat jĕnu mĕnuŋ hawu karaṇa suputrikā n ahaṛĕpa*

:197:\:22:\:4:. muwaḥ saŋ Aja sāmpun aṙppat akirè lumariṣa makamaṅgala dwijawara,
sahaśraśatakoṭi wīra winiđi nṛĕpati tumuta śakti sāmpun ayaśa,
pĕnuḥ sahana niŋ lĕbuḥ tĕkap i sañjata nika kumaluŋ pinañjĕṙ aṅadĕg,
Ikaŋ nagara dènya kady akalaṅan wihaga saŋ Aja moliha praƀusutā*

:198:\:22:\:5:. mijil sira śinaṅꝁapāṇyan i karaŋ ni patiga niŋ aśoka wahw asalaga,
Ikaŋ ƀramara haṙṣa riŋ kusuma muṅgw i taṅan ira marāṅisĕp tan awĕliŋ,
laki stṙyy aliwĕran hañaṙ hañaṙ apaṅgiḥ aduluṙ akaraŋ karaŋ sĕkaṙ arūm,
katampwan i kucuṙ nikaŋ wway atawiŋ tawiŋ i lawĕ lawö nikaŋ saraṣija*

:199:\:22:\:6:. I sāmpun i kaśaṅꝁapāṇyan ira mañjiŋ i dalĕm aduluṙ lawan dwijawara,
Anambaḥ aṅusap ri jöŋ nṛpati mamwit i ḍatĕṅa nirèŋ widaṙƀanagara,
sinuṅṣuŋ iŋ ujaṙ prahāsana nĕhĕṙ jumaya jaya jayā nirè paran ira,
Aum hanaku saŋ pakolihĕn i tiṅhal iŋ ahayu dumĕlwa jalwa raṣika*

:200:\:22:\:7:. kunaŋ pawĕkasaṅkwa haywa ta bapaṅku tan apĕnĕd iŋ ambĕk iŋ para paran,
rarè mara kita ndatan raraya dè niŋ amawa manaḥ atwaṅèŋ wwaŋ atuha,
Inuttama đanuṙdđarānaku taŧāpi tan ika paṅayāya riŋ kadi kita,
Ikaŋ guṇa ya tan paraṅkĕpana maṙyyada rahayu lawö hananya kapalaŋ*

:201:\:22:\:8:. Ikaŋ sakahawan ri ƀūmi ni bapaṅku pahayu kita rakṣakāṅanumata,
sapawwat ika hantusākĕna sasamƀawa haturakĕnanya māsku tariman,
Ujaṙku pituhunta haywa kita sāhasa maṅalapa wastu mūlya tinĕṅĕt,
praṣidđa kadaŋ iŋ jagat kita dumadyakĕna suꝁa nikā mataṅnya pahayu*

:202:\:22:\:9:. pamitran alawas ṛĕsĕp karaṇa niŋ wĕnaŋ aṅalapa wastu tan pamalaku,
yan iŋ wiṣayarāmajātaka purihnya karaṇa niŋ anĕmwa mās pirak ika,
karāṣikaguṇan ya kāraṇa niŋ oliha raras i manaḥ niŋ adyaḥ araras,
kaśaktin aƀimāna kāraṇa niŋ aṅraraḥ aṅalapa rājya niŋ ripukula*

:203:\:22:\:10:. sirat sirat i dè narèndra raǥu mojaṙ amanis amađaṙmmakĕn ri saŋ Aja,
minuṣṭi pinakādidèwa hiniḍĕp raṣa nika kinayogyakĕn pinituhu,
putus niŋ ađamā tan ahyuna rumĕṅwakĕna ri pitutuṙ nirāhayu dahat,
ya kāraṇa narèndraputra makacāmana rarab i lĕbū ni jöŋ narapati*

:204:\:22:\:11:. ri sāmpun ira mamwit iŋ nṛpati saṙwwi laku nira marè narèndramahiṣī,
hanāṅhaḍaŋ awèḥ sĕṛĕḥ saha taṅis wagĕd ahayu hinĕmban iŋ kaka kaka,
kataṅgamaŋ awèḥ sĕpaḥ nṛpatiputra nĕhĕṙ amuhun amriḥ aṅhari hari,
tapiḥ saŋ araras pininta nira mūlya basahan ira raṇḍi paṅhurup ira*

:205:\:22:\:12:. byatīta ri huwus nirāṅucap ucap tĕka sira ri taman narèndramahiṣī,
lĕṅĕŋ kadi kadèwatan halĕp ikāpan ajuraŋ awukiṙ mapājaṙ ajaran,
maèṙttali pinañcuran jinalatuṇḍa tinalaga ri soṙṇnya kādƀuta dahat,
Ikaŋ kaka kakānwam adyus anĕṅaḥ lawan anak anakanya kètaka miṅiŋ*

<kilayu> Anĕḍĕŋ – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:206:\:23:\:1:. kalpadruma taruwara pārijāta winaṅun bwat asana sakapat,
Aƀrāṣinaŋ asĕmu sakèŋ kadèwatan ululnya kanaka pinahat,
jinriṅjriŋ iŋ anak anakan maṇik cinaturaṅga lumarap amiraḥ,
mās jaṅga katiraḥ awilĕt pralĕmba nika riŋ taṛĕtĕpan alaṅö*

:207:\:23:\:2:. ṅkānā nṛpatisuta maṛĕk ri rèna nira sādara satiru tirun,
Amwit lumariṣa ḍatĕṅèŋ widaṙƀanagarī bibi nira wihikan,
maṙmmāsiḥ awĕlas asĕgĕḥ mamakpak amapag riŋ ucapan amanis,
niṙwwiǥna kita bapa jayèŋ swayambara sadāṅalahakĕna ratu*

:208:\:23:\:3:. rakryān aṅinaṅa tanayaṅku māsku mapa hètu niŋ awak akuru,
Agriŋ karika kita lawan wanèḥ brata kunaŋ karaṇa niŋ awĕnĕs,
haywānaku kaluṣa kitāhyun iŋ kajayaśatṙwwan anuta ri haṛĕp,
Akwèḥ ꝑala nika kaki saṙwwawiǥna niyatanya hilaŋ alaradan*

:209:\:23:\:4:. ndan rakwa kadamĕlan ikaŋ swayambara kahop riŋ anakĕbi rara,
sakwèḥ para ratu pininaŋ ya tèka pilihĕn sakahaṛĕp alapĕn,
dè ni ṅhulun ahiḍĕp i budđi saŋ rara kapan haṛĕpa riŋ atuha,
ṅhiŋ kahyuna nika ratu cakrawaṙttitanayāguṇa kawi taruṇa*

:210:\:23:\:5:. rakryan pwa saꝑala wĕka cakrawaṙtti tuwi śakti wihikan aṅaji,
siṅhākṛti tuhu tuhu siṅhaputra wĕnaŋ uṅṣiṛĕn iŋ aśaraṇa,
byaktānaku mamĕnaṅa riŋ swayambaraṣaƀāṅalahakĕna ratu,
tan sĕṅgahĕn aṅalĕm anak syapèka kadi māsku lituhayu wani*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:211:\:24:\:1:. tatkālè paṅucap narèndramahiṣī tucapa ta para ratnakanyakā,
Osik tan pakawanwan agyaŋ i ḍatĕŋ saŋ Aja kadi hañaṙ hañaṙ mulat,
tan pātmā kamatĕṅgĕṅĕn kalukaran gĕluŋ asidĕha tan hanāṅucap,
kady āhöm turidanya n osaḥ akĕcap lwiṙ anicipi manis nṛpātmaja*

:212:\:24:\:2:. wwantĕn lwiṙ śaśiwimba wāhu mijil aṅḍaḍari hayu nikānwam iŋ wayaḥ,
Aṅgöŋ mabrata śuklapakṣa nika paṅlwaŋ i manaḥ ika tan wĕnaŋ licin,
rāganya n dadakan tumaṅgal i ḍatĕŋ nṛpasuta kadi tambwaŋ iŋ wulan,
kṛṣṇākāra tĕṅahnya dè ni tapak iŋ suḥ asĕmu  sĕmu rāhw añumbana*

:213:\:24:\:3:. lèn taŋ lwiṙ pranitādagaŋ kira kiranya sumikĕpa wĕkas nṛpātmaja,
kapraŋ rwèpu kataṇḍĕgan turida tan patahĕnan aṅagĕm pralāpita,
toḥ toḥ nyān iŋ agĕgwan ambĕk apagĕḥ mapa tiki n alaḥ aṅgĕgö smara,
Aṅlampwāṅusirè padadwaya nirān panikĕlakĕna tuṙ humaṇḍĕma*

:214:\:24:\:4:. strī saṅṣāra sarāga mohita sawaŋ wana gahana kalahṙwwan iŋ kapat,
trāṣa twasnya kakiṅkiṅan ginĕsĕṅan pinarawaśa tinunwan iŋ‌ smara,
norānīsi manahnya kèwala panasbaran alisuḥ aṅölakĕn lara,
maṅkè pwa n kaṛĕṅö gĕṛĕḥ saŋ Aja mañjiŋ aluŋ asĕmi kuŋ nikāsĕwö*

:215:\:24:\:5:. Èndaḥ budđi nikaŋ wanèḥ tĕkap ikāmawa turida luput linakṣaṇan,
muṅkuṙ tan huniṅè ḍatĕŋ saŋ Aja mañjiŋ asila ri haṛĕp narèśwarī,
ndan dènyāhyas apahyasan dudu dudū hiniraṅakĕn ikè nṛpātmaja,
sūkṣmākāra ni raśmi raśmi ni wulatnya n araras apadĕlwan iŋ cṛĕmin*

:216:\:24:\:6:. kanyā rwaŋ siki ramya kāliḥ aṅisapwakĕn anak anakanya kètaka,
tuṅgal mājaṙ i putra putran ika māsku saŋ Aja sira rakwa maṅkata,
ndan haywākilayū tuhanku niyata ṅhulun inucap ujaṙ nikākalib,
maṙmmanyāpasaḥ ambĕk èṅgal apadudwan aṅuwahi pamitran aṅdadak*

:217:\:24:\:7:. strī strī sukṣĕka wahw agātra turidanya mijil i wijil iŋ payođara,
tan saḥ riŋ salukat gawè nṛpatiputra sinalukatakĕnya tan humuŋ,
ramyārūm kaṛĕṅö manisnya sinamèni pamawan ika riṅraŋ iŋ hati,
tan samwas ginarut garutnya hiniḍĕpnya saŋ Aja sahasāṅisapwakĕn*

:218:\:24:\:8:. sakwèḥ niŋ kumĕmit prapañca ni hatinya kumĕkĕsi taṅisnya riŋ karas,
Āpan budđi narèndraputra kadi tan tulusa duga dugāṅhalimbaṅa,
ƀakty ānĕmbaḥ i jöŋ ni rèna nira mĕṅgĕp amanis agawè wulat maliŋ,
luṅhā tan pracurānĕhĕṙ nĕhĕrakĕn manaḥ iŋ ahayu kāri sukṣĕka*

<A> kind of/ Aƀikṛti ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:219:\:25:\:1:. mijil saŋ Aja kādƀutāƀinawa rūpa saŋ aṅiriŋ apan paḍāhyaŋ ahalĕp,
Ikaŋ gaja raŧāśwa sañjata saƀūṣaṇa nika dumilaḥ kasĕnwan aruṇa,
sumaṅgraha humèrakĕn wiđi nira n lumariṣa kumisik pasaṅǥa niŋ ujar,
baṅun jalada tan pakāla gumĕṛĕḥ ri taya niŋ aṅin aṅḍapuṙ saha kilat*

:220:\:25:\:2:. payuŋ  payuṅan iŋ lĕbuḥ kadi sĕkaṙ sinawuŋ apan anèkawaṙṇna sumĕkar,
Ikaŋ paṅuṅaṅan huwus winalunan wĕḍihan inupaṛĕṅga riŋ tulis ĕmās,
rarānwam inĕgĕḥ paṛĕŋ mijil amaṅguŋ asĕmu sĕmu lakṣmi niŋ masa kapat,
paḍālal asĕnāha tiṅhal amanis wulatakĕna ri raśmi raśmi saŋ Aja*

:221:\:25:\:3:. hanèŋ gupura tan wawaŋ sira lumampaḥ ataña ri gĕnĕp ni sañjata nira,
samāsila hanèŋ lĕmaḥ muni manuk marahakĕn i wijilnya tan hana kari,
sirèŋ palukayan kinon ira kumona ri para juru yan lumakwa rumuhun,
samaṅkana sira n lumampaḥ aḍarat haṛĕp iŋ ulaḥ awās yayanyan ahalĕp*

:222:\:25:\:4:. ri lampaḥ ira ǥūṙṇnita ŋ paḍahi paṅhaṛĕp ira kumisik maṅèṙttali tibā,
saru swara nikābaruŋ binaruṅan tabĕ tabĕhan agĕnturan kadi gĕṛĕḥ,
humandaru tibā gubaṙ kumĕtug aśriŋ aniru kĕtug iŋ hudan wahu ḍawuḥ,
Arūm uni ni ǥaṇṭa niŋ liman aṅuṅkaŋ asahuran i paṅhrik iŋ kuda bisir*

:223:\:25:\:5:. dwijāti ṛṣi śaiwa bodđa śuci sojaṙ ira maṅaƀiwāda muṅgu ri haṛĕp,
yaŧākrama paḍādarāhalĕp agöŋ i wĕtĕŋ ira lawan huwan riŋ atuha,
lumampaḥ alaris malaḥ ya tan arampaka ri sadawatā nikaŋ lĕbuḥ agöŋ,
humuŋ tĕkap ira n paṅuccaraṇa mantra kadi mađukarāṅisis humaliwat*

:224:\:25:\:6:. kĕliŋ wani wanīŋ usāna pamarakṣa nira mamawa ƀindiwāla palaga,
baṅun rinawisan wĕhaṅnya kalawan ḍaḍa nika paḍa wok tĕkèŋ suku wulun,
hibĕk tatu rujit rujit kadi tinambalan awak ika waṙṇna bĕntaṙ inawĕt,
Agöŋ paḍa kaƀīma ƀīma kadi dānawa muꝁa muꝁa daitya piṇḍa cawiri*

:225:\:25:\:7:. Ikaŋ maṛĕk i jöŋ narèndratanayānwam aguṇa paḍa daṙśanīya taruṇa,
titik nagara nora tan ‌wruha n anak wĕsi haji tuwi mūlya kawwaṅan ika,
watĕk madana maṅdadi wwaŋ ujaṙ iŋ mulat i lituhayunya n ahyaŋ araras,
kunaŋ saŋ Aja kāmadèwa sakalānurun ucapan ikaŋ kapūhan i sira*

:226:\:25:\:8:. samaṅkana nikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan haṅu haṅun aṛĕbut mulat ri saŋ Aja,
hanan kadi haṛĕp siliḥ galaha riŋ susu manĕwĕka riŋ naꝁākas aluṅid,
paḍākira kirākĕkĕs mata maliŋ maliŋ aṅiriṅi kāladèśa sumilib,
katon kadi siliḥ praṅèŋ halis aṛĕṅw inayat ayatakĕnya maṅkin araras*

:227:\:25:\:9:. Ikāŋ amawa pawwahan lituhayu prakaśita kawi mambaŋ uttama rarè,
hañaṙ tĕka sakèŋ widaṙƀanagarī layat inalapan aṅhañaŋ hañaṅakĕn,
rarānya kawĕkas pinañjiṅakĕn iŋ nagara maṛĕk i jöŋ narèndratanayā,
ya kāraṇa ni luhnya mantĕn amalaṙ malaṙ i saŋ Aja molihè sira hĕlĕm*

:228:\:25:\:10:. manis ni kakawinya mūla ni papaṅgiḥ ika lawan ikaŋ rinudđa winalat,
pinèt pĕjahanāsĕnötan i kadaṅnya winuni karaṇanya yan lĕpas adoḥ,
paḍāpalaraṣan lawan jaruman amriḥ aṅaliḥ ahawan wĕṅīŋ awa wulan,
tinūt i paṅaran ṅaranya kawidoṣa wĕkasan i ḍatĕṅnya riŋ nṛpasuta*

:229:\:25:\:11:. ya tīka tan adoḥ ginĕgwan ira bāhu nika winisikan tinakwanan ira,
syapèka paḍa saŋ swayĕmbarakĕna prakaśita pinakādi niŋ wwaŋ ahayu,
Ikaŋ wwaŋ aṅuṅaŋ bwat indrawanitāhyas ika pahawasĕn ta ya n sama hirib,
kĕcapnya n aṅĕsaḥ miṅĕl ya pawarahnya ri saŋ Aja wawaŋ ṛĕmĕk hati nira*

:230:\:25:\:12:. hanāṅuṅaŋ anuṅga  nuṅgal aṅisapwakĕn anak anakanya kètaka miṅiŋ,
mahāṅjĕlagakĕn hayunya makapaṅhaḍa buṅaḥ i muꝁanya tan patalutuḥ,
ri kāla saŋ Ajāṅinaŋ winulatanya ri wulat ira löṙ matanya lumiriŋ,
baṅun hañaṙ anūt haṛĕp sĕpaḥ awĕdy aṅucapa tumiliŋ miṅè kadi cala*

:231:\:25:\:13:. rarānwam akirè wulat dudu dudū saŋ aṅĕsaḥ i kisapwan iŋ kaka kaka,
tupis tupis i dè nirāṅĕnahakĕn manaḥ ira tumibè narèndratanaya,
wagĕd wagĕd aniṙwwa niṙwwakĕn i dè nira gamĕl inamĕṙ nirè taṅan ira,
tĕkāsiḥ atabĕḥ sĕṛĕḥ saha pucaŋ nika dalihan irāṅawè ri saŋ Aja*

:232:\:25:\:14:. I soṙ niŋ asanāsĕkaṙ hana sirāṅuṅaŋ araras aliṇḍuṅan kaka kaka,
ṅĕliḥ ṅĕliḥ iŋ èkacitta ri narèndraṣuta ṅĕliḥ irāhuyaŋ pinĕpĕtan,
sawaŋ sawaŋ i dènirāmawa wulat wulat iŋ asamayāwĕdi n katĕṅĕra,
mulat pwa saŋ Ajāṅdadak sira miṅè sĕmu niŋ awarahè katĕmwana nira*

:233:\:25:\:15:. muwaḥ wwaya sirāhalĕp rara sujanma pinawulaṅakĕn hanèŋ paṅuṅaṅan,
gaḍiŋ pinakaputra putran ira tan saḥ inaṛĕk aṛĕkan sakè nṛpasuta,
ya tèka tumurun hinĕmban iŋ iñāmawa sĕṛĕḥ aṛĕnaḥ maṛĕk ri saŋ Aja,
bapāṅinaṅa rakwa liŋ ra bibi liŋ nikaŋ aṅujarakĕn waśāsĕmu guyu*

:234:\:25:\:16:. pratāpa naranāŧaputra kumutug pracalita kadi paṙwwatāgni dumilaḥ,
Ikaŋ wwaŋ aṅuṅaŋ baṅun kusuma sālas anĕḍĕŋ ika kāri tan papĕgatan,
manahnya ginĕsĕŋ tĕkèŋ turida rāga nika paḍa hilaŋ syuḥ aṅdadi hawu,
ya tèka hinañutnya riŋ nṛpatiputra sakala sira pöḥ niŋ aṙṇnawa mađu*

:235:\:25:\:17:. manis niŋ ucapan kaka dyaḥ ari liṅnya sinĕpuhan i raśmi niŋ wulat arūm,
ya tèka kinabèhan iŋ wwaŋ aṅuṅaŋ mṛdu lalita raṣanya rāgakaraṇa,
raras raras i dènya miṅgĕk aṅĕnāni n aṅucap api tan ‌wruhĕn hana mulat,
halisnya minahānya molaḥ amaṅun gĕt unĕŋ aṛĕṅu maṅlarè ri saŋ Aja*

<Indrabajra> – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓

:236:\:26:\:1:. strī stṙyy āṅucap sojaṙ ikā yinuktyan,
liṅnyè narèndrātmaja mūḋabudđi,
Akwèḥ sira ṅkè nagarī ry Ayođyā,
sāmantaputrī paḍa yogya yogyan.

:237:\:26:\:2:. yadyan tĕkā dlāha sirè widaṙƀa,
tan suṅṣuṅĕn riŋ kakawin wilāpa,
tan kèwwa riŋ rāga tĕkap suputrī,
ƀagnapratijñā mulihèraŋ èraŋ*

:238:\:26:\:3:. nāhan wuwusnyè naranāŧaputra,
ndan rakwa paṙṇnaḥ jaruman gatinya,
wwantĕn suputrī paṅadunya yogya,
maṙmmanya duhꝁè saŋ Aja n tan ahyun*

:239:\:26:\:4:. paṙṇnaḥ kakanyāśrak atuṅga yôjar,
Antĕn hadè dènta tĕkôjaṙ apyak,
putrī paran tan haṛĕpè tuhanku,
hyaŋ niŋ purī towi yayā sirāhyun*

:240:\:26:\:5:. maṅko n marè śrī naranāŧa ƀoja,
Ambĕk nira śrīndumatī pakādin,
ǥārāpan atyanta wiśèṣaputrī,
sāmantaputrī sira tā maṅadyaḥ*

:241:\:26:\:6:. nāhan sahuṙṇnyè paṅucap ny arinya,
ƀāwanya miṅgĕk tumikĕl halisnya,
koŋ aṅdĕlö solaḥ ikā n asĕṅhit,
göŋ krođa sojaṙ nika kaṙṇnaśūla*

:242:\:26:\:7:. wwantĕn kili wṛĕdđa sahuṙ nirātwaŋ,
sajñèbu ni ṅwaŋ‌ kṣama ta ṅhulun dyaḥ,
budđinta kèwalya sumorakĕn saŋ,
sāmantaputrīndumatī wiśèṣa*

:243:\:26:\:8:. tan soṙ sirèŋ janma karājaputṙyyan,
riŋ wīṙyya siṅgiḥ sira tan paḍāḍaḥ,
ndan yogya ǥārāpa hiwaŋ nirèbu,
mūlya n minūlyan krama niŋ dadi wwaŋ*

:244:\:26:\:9:. nāhan sahuṙ saŋ wiku wṛdđarūpa,
mĕṅgĕp pratuhw āsĕmu pakṣapāta,
milw āhadènī sira yan lumampaḥ,
rowaŋ nirāgoṣṫi wulatnya hèwa*

<nawahaṙṣa> ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓

:245:\:27:\:1:. tucapa ŋ wwaŋ i paṅguŋ ika kadi wayaŋ jinajaṙ kinudaŋ,
sakunaŋ kunaŋ iŋ taliṅa larap i hintĕn ika n kumĕñar,
hana tāṅadĕg an hayu nika kahiḍĕp kadi modahita,
I kasiṅkab i kènya hana kadi gibaḥ winuluŋ sinurat*

:246:\:27:\:2:. paḍa tan humĕnĕŋ sahana niŋ aṅuṅaŋ mawagĕd wagĕdan,
Amanis manisan mata nĕhĕṙ araṅin raṅinan paṅawak,
Arupit rupitan susu nĕhĕṙ alĕmĕs lĕmĕsan luṅayan,
sira saŋ sinajinya saŋ Aja juga nora muwaḥ kinirè*

:247:\:27:\:3:. nṛpaputra sĕḍĕŋ sapawulatan awèḥ lĕṅĕṅèŋ aṅuṅaŋ,
tadanantara mèḥ lĕpasa laku nira wĕkas iŋ nagara,
Amanis kadi tan pĕgata wulat irè salawaŋ salawaŋ,
Amalaṙ hana niŋ wwaŋ ahaliṅana kori mĕṅā sasisiḥ*

:248:\:27:\:4:. Araras rinasan patĕmu nira wulat raṣa tan lĕpara,
kalawan saŋ akūŋ alawas i sira kady awaṛĕg waṛĕgan,
Apatūtan unĕŋ kasiḥ aṛĕp inatīta tiniṅgalakĕn,
I layat nira kāri saŋ ahayu wulatnya tinambaŋ ira*

:249:\:27:\:5:. nda atīta sira n kajĕnĕkan akuṛĕn wulat èsy akadi,
Asalin wiṣaya n lĕpas i muꝁa nikaŋ lĕbuḥ iŋ nagara,
kuṭi śāla lumaṅkuŋ i tĕpi niŋ ayun tiriṣanya pĕnuḥ,
panĕḍĕŋ ni wuṅūnya mamituturi rāga nirèŋ aṅuṅaŋ*

:250:\:27:\:6:. kadi waḥ suraṣinđu bala saŋ Aja kātatakut gumuruḥ,
raŧa ṛĕṅga padāti kadi parahu söḥ aduluṙ humilī,
gajaḥ aṅgala ǥūṙṇnita piraŋ iwu kady asibū gumuluŋ,
sagĕḍaŋ kahilī gaḍiŋ ika tulalènya lumintaḥ awās*

:251:\:27:\:7:. paḍa ƀakti hĕnū nira sakalihatan paḍa tan humĕnĕŋ,
walahaṙṇnya lawan pahatan asaji mīna sayub cumaḍaŋ,
Amapag waṅi niŋ kusuma winawa niŋ pawana mrik arūm,
ƀramarāṣĕmu maṅhaturakĕn i gawènya kiduŋ ri sira*

:252:\:27:\:8:. kadi maṇḍala ramya ni papupul ikaŋ kayu kayw asĕkar,
waṅunanya wuṅū sĕḍĕŋ asinaŋ añaṇḍi minèṙww aruhur,
humilī wulakanya paḍa caluṅanèka katon humaḍaŋ,
hulu kĕmbaŋ ikaŋ gaḍuŋ anĕpĕrakĕn ri narèndraṣuta*

:253:\:27:\:9:. patapan kĕna rāga kayu manis ikā sinĕpĕṙ sĕpĕran,
Amapag mata jāti ni mata ni wuluḥ nika tan wriŋ iraŋ,
Aḍahĕm haḍawanya rumara rara haṙṣaja dènya mulat,
pajajaṙ ni pabañwan ika kapahiriŋ milu kady aṅaraŋ*

<giriṣa> ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:254:\:28:\:1:. saŋ Aja sira kaṅèlan muṅgaḥ riŋ raŧa wĕkasan,
saŋ agajaḥ aturaṅgānuṅgaŋ saƀya ciha ciha,
mwaŋ agiliṅan arampak wwaŋ sāmānya tan ahalĕp,
saŋ aḍarat alarèraŋ kagṛĕk gṛĕk magarawalan*

:255:\:28:\:2:. nṛpasuta lĕpas èṅgal prāptèŋ ŧāni kuluwutan,
satĕka tĕka ni lampaḥ niŋ wadwānamun adulur,
I haṛĕp i wuri lumrānĕṅkw āyun manasa nasar,
hawan arupĕk inambaḥ mèmbuḥ lwā kadi tinĕpa*

:256:\:28:\:3:. wukiṙ ajajaṙ ahaṇḍap haṇḍap śūnya maṅililan,
kadi kukusan amuñjuŋ puñcaknyāṙṇnĕb inululan,
hana talaga riŋ agra ndan wwainyāhaṅĕt ahasin,
pinara paran iŋ adyus baṙyyan landĕp awukiran*

:257:\:28:\:4:. suku suku nika duṙggātyantèwĕḥ nika pinaran,
pinĕga tinĕpa dè niŋ molaḥ ṅūni riŋ alawas,
sahaja maliwat i jro ṅkān līlāmĕkasi parab,
dadali nika laki strī prāptānambĕṙ asahuran*

:258:\:28:\:5:. lura luraḥ apaṛĕk lwaḥ guṅguŋ wwainya ḍinawuhan,
papupulan ikaŋ aṅhwan ramyāḍöm aṅariŋ ariŋ,
paḍa maṛĕk adum uṅgwan yan wwaŋ śrèṣṫi humaliwat,
Asila sila ri piṅgiṙ niŋ māṙggāmalaku sĕṛĕḥ*

:259:\:28:\:6:. Umaḥ atiśaya dènyāporaŋ mĕṅgĕp aṅililan,
wwaŋ ika paḍa humöt riŋ budđy ālumbuŋ alit alit,
tĕka ri sapi nikālit norākral kral amĕḍusi,
talaga nika jugālwāṅlaṅhuy laṅhuyakĕn agöŋ*

:260:\:28:\:7:. hana ta baṅun amèt wwaŋ doṣa n krūra lĕkas ikā,
Amawa tali lawan kris pamraŋ mraṅnya habalaṅan,
sapi nika sinikĕpnyāṅṛĕñcal maṅlawan agalak,
ri huwus ika katalyan kèṇḍit dinwal iŋ aṅulaŋ*

:261:\:28:\:8:. nṛpatisuta kaluṅhādoḥ śīǥra n saha śakaṭa,
karaṇa nira n araṙyyan mwaŋ sakwèḥ ni bala nira,
Amaṛĕki pĕkĕn alwā ŧāny āgöŋ pakulĕmana,
pira ta puluḥ i dūwanyākwèḥ söḥ paḍa winĕgil*

:262:\:28:\:9:. saŋ Aja kadi hanè jro rājyāpan sira kinĕmit,
sahana hana nikaŋ saṙwwāstra lwiṙ pinakapagĕr,
raŧa turaga tiniṅkaḥ baprāṅrakṣa sana sini,
makagupura halĕp niŋ mātaṅgāruhuṙ ajajar*

:263:\:28:\:10:. tucapa para kadūwan tuṣṭa n paṅhinĕpan ira,
sahana hana ri dèśanyānèka ŋ paḍa pamapag,
nṛpasuta sira muṅguḥ muṅgw iŋ bwat halu tĕpi lor,
sama humatuṙ aṅantī soṙ niŋ wāṇḍira magĕlar*

:264:\:28:\:11:. wiku haji jĕnĕk aṅhèṙ iŋ śūnyālawas amarāt,
‌wruḥ aṅaji sira santoṣāṅdo dohi narapati,
nĕhĕṙ amarahi sāmpun wṛdđāṅgöŋ ulaḥ alaṅö,
Atuha tuha kadi bṛĕm santĕn kāku manis ira*

:265:\:28:\:12:. sira ta maṛĕk aluṅguḥ milw iŋ dāyaka humatur,
kinasĕgĕhan apan ‌wruḥ ṅūnīŋ rājya sira kabèḥ,
Apituwi paḍa rowaŋ rowaŋ niŋ maṅikĕt ikĕt,
muꝁa niŋ aṅucap aśrī dè niŋ mojaṙ akakawin*

:266:\:28:\:13:. kṣamakĕna bapa pawwat niŋ grāmyāđama kaluṣa,
padapa hima lawan cèntĕn mèpālpa lihatana,
sama duwĕga ri rakryan yan twak haywa hali halin,
pinakabañu bañu ṅkè ṅhiŋ yan lèn juga yan ikā*

:267:\:28:\:14:. wulatana kakudèśanyāŧānī gĕgĕṙ asĕpi,
ya tuna tuna sĕṛĕḥ wwaḥ tĕkwan tan hana dinadak,
palapat alas agaṙyyaŋ gaṙyyaŋ tan sawĕgilana,
linĕṅĕṅakĕn iŋ ambĕk maṙmmanya n ṛĕsĕp alaṅö*

:268:\:28:\:15:. Aluru wahu kalahṙwwan kaywanya n śrawaṇamasa,
Asĕpa humuraŋ awyaŋ ruṙwwan ronya kapawanan,
Analukati tĕlā wwad niŋ saṙwwatṛĕṇa riŋ ayun,
pĕjaḥ amĕkasi kiṅkiŋ luŋ niŋ jaṅga kapanasan*

:269:\:28:\:16:. tĕwĕk i ragas i kaywanya n kaṙwwāraras alaṅö,
tĕṅaḥ i tal ika mambĕt mambĕt kāṅinan aṅĕliḥ,
manis i lahaŋ ikāṅhiŋ panraŋ nraŋ wulat amanis,
tiniru tiru niŋ ahyas ronyāṙjjāpataḥ akiris*

:270:\:28:\:17:. sĕḍĕŋ iŋ asujimāsātyantèŋ kaṣṭa gataraṣa,
karikil ika kumĕṇḍĕŋ tūt māṙggāmacĕki suku,
saha panas i hĕnunyādoḥ wwè nora pinalaku,
tuhun amuhara ramyā sakwèḥ niŋ wwaŋ ika jĕnĕk*

:271:\:28:\:18:. jalada kadi pĕtĕŋ yan tĕmbè niŋ kapat alaṅö,
jawuḥ amĕkasakĕn ṛĕm riŋ kaywan hañaṙ asĕmi,
wahu mari panaṅis niŋ kālaṅkyaŋ suꝁa sumayab,
Asiga kadi tinambaŋ wahw īnantukan agiraŋ*

:272:\:28:\:19:. tṛṇa taru paḍa mĕltik wījanya n masa kalima,
wawaŋ aluru kapiṅṛĕs tūt māṙggāṅĕliḥ alumè,
linaran i kĕñaṙ iŋ wai yan luṅhā ŋ ṛĕmĕŋ anisiḥ,
kadi pamanas i kuŋ niŋ kanyā dūra n atĕlĕba*

:273:\:28:\:20:. hañaṙ abañu tĕgalnya n kānĕm tapwan acaṛĕcĕḥ,
kadi sinipatan apriḥ māṙgganyāracĕk abĕnĕr,
turaḥ i wĕṛĕḥ ikaŋ waṙṣāsat kāri kasarakat,
Asĕmu pupuṙ arèḥ tūt piṅgiṙ niŋ halis inamĕr*

:274:\:28:\:21:. brata nika ri sĕḍĕŋ niŋ māǥādyus rahina wĕṅi,
jawuḥ aṅapitu tan pāntyādṛĕs maṅkin akĕcĕhan,
Aṅura ṅuraṅi tèja hyaŋ candrāṙka kaginĕman,
suꝁa salabuḥ ikaŋ luṅlūṅan māri kapiṅĕliḥ*

:275:\:28:\:22:. lĕbug i palĕmahānyājro riŋ ꝑālguna puraci,
patuna tunahan iŋ lĕmbw āsaṅṣiŋ tahi papuṅĕn,
dwijawara sira baṙyyan ṛĕṅṛĕŋ moǥa humaliwat,
sumĕpĕṙ anasi pöhan maṙmmanya n śuci wĕkasan*

:276:\:28:\:23:. masa kasaṅa tĕka traŋ‌ ndan mātrānĕlani jawuḥ,
ya karaṇa ni latĕknyātiṅgaṙ wahw asat anisiḥ,
sapapikatana göṅĕn tĕmbè niŋ manuk agalak,
tuhun asĕpi hĕnūnya lwīṙ agriŋ paḍa caciṅĕn*

:277:\:28:\:24:. kusuma sahana māywan yan waiśāꝁa paḍa wijaḥ,
sĕkaṙ iŋ asana kantun kady ahyun kalarakĕna,
paṅirim irim ikaŋ waṙṣāhèṙ wèḥ ayu ḍumawuḥ,
kadi jaruman aṅintè rāgānīs amawa taṅis*

:278:\:28:\:25:. muwaḥ asĕkaṙ alasnya jyèṣṫāmiṅṙwwani sahapit,
tuhun aṅuraṅi ruṙwwan dè niŋ waṙṣa wahu muliḥ,
tura turaḥ i gĕṛĕhnyāgupyan mèḥ amĕkasana,
tuna tuna kadi pamwit niŋ haṙṣāmĕkasi taṅis*

:279:\:28:\:26:. Analahasa laṅönyèŋ āṣāđāṅlarani kawi,
paḍa gumigil aṅinkin tiṅhalnyāniliṅi tawaŋ,
kamaḍiḍiṅĕn aṅèpw ī roganyāṅgĕgĕs aṅĕsaḥ,
kadi kahapit aṅunṅun muṅgw iŋ śūnya kakilatan*

:280:\:28:\:27:. nahan ucapan ira mpuṅkw aṅdè haṙṣa ri saŋ Aja,
wĕṅi mara sakamantyan prāptānèka taḍaḥ ira,
dwijawara sira māliḥ muṅgw iŋ bwat halu tĕpi lor,
para wiku juga kāṙyy āgoṣṫi mwaŋ nṛpatanaya*

:281:\:28:\:28:. paḍahi maṛĕk agupyan śabdanyāmanis inamĕr,
kadi paṅucap ucap niŋ muṅgw i jro jinĕm akulè,
Apituwi sinamènīŋ gīta śrī nṛpatanaya,
raṣa nika winiwèkānèka ŋ pālapan amanis*

:282:\:28:\:29:. tucapa bala nirākwèḥ ƀāwanya n paṅinum inum,
Aṅigĕl aṅiduŋ aśraŋ twaknyākwèḥ kadi humilī,
paḍahi nika gumĕntĕṙ sinraŋ niŋ tabĕ tabĕhan,
kadi baribina saŋ hyaŋ riŋ swaṙggātukupa kapö*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:283:\:29:\:1:. luṅhā ŋ māsa piliḥ tĕṅaḥ wĕṅi tiḍĕm sahana niŋ aṅinum paḍāturū,
tistis nora mumik tuhun saŋ Aja tan mṛĕm amaṅu maṅu tan kĕnèŋ turū,
Aṅhiŋ ramya rinĕṅwakĕn panalimuṙ nalimuṙ ira ri kiṅkiŋ iŋ hati,
gĕṇḍiŋ walyan arūm swaranya kaṛĕṅö sawĕṅi kiniduṅan kiduŋ buwun*

:284:\:29:\:2:. loṙ wètan pamalantĕnan kapaṛĕk iŋ lwaḥ adalĕm asamīpa paṅdyunan,
wwaṅnyāwuṅw amasaŋ damaṙ ‌wruḥ i masanya n amalu malu mèḥ tibā ŋ ĕnĕm,
tan paśrī swara niŋ palu dyun asarag tĕwas amaribini ŋ wwaŋ aṅṛĕṅö,
Èndaḥ mwaŋ palu wastra ramya kadi dè niŋ amalu daluwaŋ rinĕṅwakĕn*

:285:\:29:\:3:. Aṅdyun kaṙwwa rabinya tan padiwasāwiḍiṅan awurahan siliḥ cacad,
nitya ŋ śabda paḍèṅgal aśrak amalĕs hinalan uliḥ ikāgawè ǥaṭa,
strīnyāmèt parihāra tan wĕdi kadūṣana n ahala gawè nikā paṭa,
kahyun hyun kadi śaiwa sogata mapaṅǥaṭapaṭa juga hètu niŋ humuŋ*

:286:\:29:\:4:. sakwèḥ niŋ baṇijèŋ tĕpas paḍa sumambutakĕn i sagawè nikālawas,
norāpĕk paḍa loƀa lāƀa kahaṛĕpnya n akuṭa kaṭikan paḍādamar,
saṅkĕp dwalnya huwus ratĕŋ paḍa sumaṅgraha wijila niki n marèŋ pĕkĕn,
Asyaŋ syaŋ kaṛĕṅö humuŋ saṅa saṅanya sĕmu niŋ ahaṛĕp katumbasa*

:287:\:29:\:5:. Èñjiŋ wāhu huwus ḍawuḥ pitu muni ŋ paḍahi baṅun akon adandana,
sakwèḥ niŋ prajurit paḍāmuṅu ri paṅhawin ika kamĕnanya maṅkata,
Aṙdđèñjiŋ pwa hiḍĕpnya tĕkwan apuyĕŋ ya ta karaṇa nikāturū muwaḥ,
ṅhiŋ maṅkat saŋ Ajākĕmul kĕmul alañciṅan aṅarahakĕn sakèŋ raŧa*

:288:\:29:\:6:. saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa tan wĕnaŋ adoḥ ri sira maṛĕk amaṅku pawwahan,
prajñā tan kasilib ri tiṅkaḥ iŋ asèwaka maṅinakanèŋ tuhan tuhan,
‌wruḥ riŋ yogya kahĕnwa dè nira tinūt sapawaraḥ ika ramya tūt gĕgĕr,
yèkā rakwa hĕnūnya ṅūni n aṅaliḥ saha jaruman ikāmĕgat gunuŋ*

:289:\:29:\:7:. śūnyāporaŋ ikaŋ gĕgĕṙ hana guhā ṛĕbaḥ adalĕm aṛĕs twas iŋ mulat,
tan pātmā ŋ aṅuṅaŋ hanan kadi hanāṅduhuṅakĕna tĕkā sakèŋ wuri,
tistis nora marāṅlĕṅĕŋ ri pataninya paḍa kadi sinaṅgan iŋ kawi,
ṅhiŋ raṅṝö gumĕṛĕḥ tinūb niŋ aṅin adṛĕs aniru gĕṛĕḥ iŋ labuḥ kapat*

:290:\:29:\:8:. ṅkānè lĕmbaḥ ikālaṅö pamaḍĕkan wwaŋ ika wija wijaḥ paḍāṅayar,
lumrākwèḥ aputiḥ wuyahnya kasawuṙ sumaraṣaḥ anamaṙ wway iŋ jawuḥ,
Awrā tampĕṙ ikāgĕlaṙ kasarakat sarakat asĕmu sāri niŋ puḍak,
haṙṣāmbĕk saŋ Aja n tĕkāwuya wuyaḥ mata tuwin aharip kadīnusap*

:291:\:29:\:9:. tambak tambak akaṇḍa loṙ kidul i pomahān ika kadi piṇḍa niŋ sawaḥ,
wwaṅnyārampak amèt wĕlut kadi pucaŋ pucaṅan iŋ aṅurit katiṅhalan,
pakṣinyāgĕŋ agĕŋ humuŋ kadi kĕbo paṅulaḥ awurahan siliḥ buru,
yan kawṛĕg paḍa möṙ gumĕntĕṙ anamaṙ gĕṛĕḥ iŋ adurugan paḍāwĕṝö*

:292:\:29:\:10:. Aƀrā lwiṙ sĕkaṙ iŋ laṅit braja katon pamĕwĕḥ i supit iŋ sahiŋ sahiŋ,
Aṅjraḥ tan kahanan lĕwas pasuŋ ikāsira sira kadi kĕmbaŋ iŋ karaŋ,
lwiṙ luŋ niŋ katiraḥ miraḥ ni suṅut iŋ huraŋ aṅariŋ ariŋ marèŋ lumut,
tūt māṙggāhaṛĕmis pĕjaḥ kadi mĕnuṙ saka salawĕ lawö sumamburat*

<basantatilaka> – – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓

:293:\:30:\:1:. sāmpun lĕpas raŧa narèndraṣutāpan adṛĕs,
saŋ brāhmaṇè wuri lawan ṛĕṣi śaiwa bodđa,
Agyā paḍānututi tan hana kāṙyy araṙyyan,
muṅgw iŋ gajāśwa raŧa maśraŋ alumba lumba*

:294:\:30:\:2:. lwaḥ naṙmmadā katĕmu dè naranāŧaputra,
saŋ brāhmaṇāsaƀa saƀā ri ya sāri sāri,
Atyanta niṙmmala paṅa‌wruhanè śucinya,
maṙmmanya n uttama wijilnya sakèŋ śaśāṅka*

:295:\:30:\:3:. söḥ puṣpa laywan iŋ atīṙŧa hanè hĕnīnya,
kuntul paḍāṅadĕg adĕg ri pacaṙ pacaṙṇnya,
līlā ḍarā ri kalakānya wijaḥ paḍādyus,
Akwèḥ mayūra maṅigĕl ri pasiṙ pasiṙṇnya*

:296:\:30:\:4:. ṅkāna n paraṙyyan arahup naranāŧaputra,
muṅgw iŋ aśoka sira tan mari śokacitta,
nyū danta mèdi ri manaḥ nira kèṅin èṅin,
kāṅgĕk sirānĕmu puḍak maṅuḍoḍa riŋ wwai*

:297:\:30:\:5:. nya ŋ cakrawāka paḍa ramya mahimya himyan,
ṅkānè saroruha wĕkasnya lawan priyanya,
manda swaranya kaṛĕṅö nira tan sꝑuṭārūm,
winṛĕg nirāpa ta kalīṅa ni dè nirāmṛĕg*

:298:\:30:\:6:. haṅśāputiḥ ri tĕṅaḥ adyus aṅumbaŋ umbaŋ,
kombak tinūb iŋ aṅin adṛĕs aṅiṅgĕk iṅgĕk,
mogāraras raras arūm kaṛĕṅö swaranya,
kady āwaraḥ yan alaṅö ri hananya riŋ wwai*

:299:\:30:\:7:. wadwā nirāduluṙ i piṅgiṙ aḍanta ḍanta,
Akwèḥ lĕpas paḍa kahañjuṙ adoḥ lakunya,
maṅṣul muwaḥ saha padāti tinuṇḍa pājar,
Āpan kinonakĕn aṅantya makuwwa  kuwwa*

:300:\:30:\:8:. śīǥrāgawè gṛhalatā mrik arūm sĕkaṙṇnya,
norākawö paḍa wicakṣaṇa riŋ kalaṅwan,
Andul wuṅū mwaŋ asanāṅjraḥ i piṅgiṙ iŋ lwaḥ,
ramyālaṅö pinaṛĕkanya hanan pamaṅguŋ*

:301:\:30:\:9:. ndaḥ riŋ samantaji hanādƀuta mūṙtti niŋ hyaŋ,
mātaṅgarūpa pinakāṙggaḍa riŋ wanādri,
siṅhāṅḍapuṙ wĕdi manambaḥ aṛĕs tumon ya,
Airāwaṇānurun ujaṙ niŋ anaṙka naṙka*

:302:\:30:\:10:. ri lwaḥ saƀānya sĕḍĕŋ adyus ahilya hilyan,
nora ŋ ƀayèriya putus wuhayāluṅāṅlwaŋ,
Aṅlaṅhuy adṛĕs anamaṙ gajamīna mĕtta,
himpĕṙ karaŋ liman i kāla nikāṅalimpuŋ*

:303:\:30:\:11:. Ambö ni mèda ni gajaḥ naranāŧaputra,
sākṣāt inambuŋ ika hètu nika ƀramanta,
Abyūran iŋ lwaḥ alĕtuḥ kakĕbuṙ bañunya,
wit niŋ saroja kadahut kalawan sĕkaṙṇnya*

:304:\:30:\:12:. mĕntas pwa yāṅadĕg aṅuṅgul i tīra niŋ lwaḥ,
gaṅgĕŋ lawan saraṣijāṅhibĕki ry awaknya,
mĕttāwĕṝö nĕhĕṙ asumpiŋ aǥaṇṭa kambaŋ,
Aƀrā katiṅhalan ikā kadi nāgapuṣpa*

:305:\:30:\:13:. mèww īwu saṅꝁya ni gajaḥ naranāŧaputra,
ndātan pamaṙppati ri göṅnya lawan guṇanya,
Awṛĕg sakè taṅan alaḥ ḍyam api n rinukrak,
Āpan swaƀāwa niŋ alit juga ta n tinaṅgĕl*

:306:\:30:\:14:. strī strī paḍāṅhili lawan raray anwam anwam,
Adṛĕs lakunya karikil kawĕdinya ṅūni,
maṅkè n tĕkèŋ ƀaya sukĕt rwi yayān inambaḥ,
wèt niŋ takut pati susup susupīŋ alas göŋ*

:307:\:30:\:15:. Akwèḥ marèŋ tahĕn anuṅtuŋ amèt upāya,
watw īnuluṙṇnya sagĕnuk sawaluḥ salumpaŋ,
tĕṇḍas nikaŋ liman awās tinujunya tan lèn,
tog toṙ ndatan dwa katibān dan ikaŋ śilā syuḥ*

:308:\:30:\:16:. krođa ŋ liman mata nikāṅdṛĕŋ anon wwaŋ akwèḥ,
riŋ kāywan aṅhabalaŋ iŋ kayu kayw aganti,
yèka n tumandaŋ aṅayuḥ paŋ agöŋ katuṅkul,
syāk pok ṛĕbaḥ ri walakaṅnya baṅun rinĕṅgan*

:309:\:30:\:17:. wadwā nṛpātmaja masĕṅhit asiṅhanāda,
sārākusāra śaraṇāśraya wāni riŋ praŋ,
krūrākihal kihal agöŋ karawalya timbul,
śūrabratāsira siran paḍa tan dadi jriḥ*

:310:\:30:\:18:. yèkāṅlawan paḍa maṛĕk pinupul sĕmutnya,
kwèhnyāpramāṇa satasik ya ta paṅhaḍanya,
Ambĕk nikaŋ gaja mamatyana nora wāni,
göṅnyāpramèya sagunuŋ ya ta paṅgajahnya*

:311:\:30:\:19:. māsö hanèŋ raŧa narèndraṣutāṅagĕm hrū,
laṅkap hanè kiwa huwus pinasaŋ talinya,
sāmpun minantran inayat saha hastiśikṣā,
saṙ cĕb tibāṅĕnani kumƀa nikaŋ gajèndra*

:312:\:30:\:20:. sāmpun kĕnāmriḥ aṅusī pulihan tumandaŋ,
ndan saṙwwasanđi ni śarīra nikāgraḥ aṅṛĕs,
yèka n paṅohan aṅadĕg mati tan pasāra,
goṙ ƀoḥ tibā kadi śilādri ṛĕbaḥ kaliṇḍwan*

:313:\:30:\:21:. waṅkènya sakṣaṇa hananya kadīŋ paṅipyan,
tèja prakīṙṇna dumilaḥ tĕka tan pasaṅkan,
widyāđarāhalĕp adĕṇḍa hanè tĕṅahnya,
Utpatti niŋ dwirada māti mahāpraƀāwa*

:314:\:30:\:22:. kalpadruma mrik inalapnya pamuṙṣitanya,
lwiṙ puṣpawaṙṣa tumibè naranāŧaputra,
Āścaṙyya budđi nira sādara dè nirāṅliŋ,
hyaŋ hyaŋ paran kari kita syapa tā ṅaranta*

<waṅśasŧa> ⏑– ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏑⏓

:315:\:31:\:1:. kĕnoḥ patakwanta ri tiṅkaḥ i ṅhulun,
ṅhulun kasaṅꝁya n maṅaran priyambada,
swaputra saŋ citraraŧa prakāśita,
sirādiganđaṙwwapatī kadèwatan*

:316:\:31:\:2:. ṅhulun sakèŋ swaṙgga wiśāta lālana,
Anuṅga nuṅgal mahās iŋ wanāntara,
tĕkèŋ pasiṙ tan hana tan kalaṅlaṅan,
laṅö niŋ ambĕk saparan tinūtakĕn*

<basantatilaka> – – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓

:317:\:32:\:1:. ṅkè naṙmmadā ṅhulun acaṅkrama sāri sāri,
kañcit kapaṅgiḥ aṅadĕg ƀagawān pataṅga,
pakṣādyusāpatĕlĕsan tumuluy marèŋ lwaḥ,
moǥa ṅhulun tumurun aṅruhurī sirādyus*

:318:\:32:\:2:. göŋ krođa wākcala sira n panibāni śāpa,
Oyuḥ gajaḥ tĕmahānamwa maran mari hyaŋ,
ṅkè tôṅgwanamwa tan adoḥ ya sakèrikiŋ lwaḥ,
nāhan wĕkas ni paṅucap nira kaṙṇnaśūla*

:319:\:32:\:3:. tan miŧya ri ṅhulun ikaŋ gajamĕttarūpa,
byaktān asaṇḍuta ŋ ujaṙ yan anĕṅgaḥ alwā,
saṅkèŋ amaṅgiḥ i wuyuŋ ƀagawān pataṅga,
tapwan śināpa tumuluy matĕmaḥ gajèndra*

:320:\:32:\:4:. An maṅkana bwat i wuyuŋ ƀagawān pataṅga,
kāruṇya budđi nira riŋ wĕkasan sirāṣiḥ,
Āpan‌ ṅhulun maṛĕk anĕmbaḥ apinta kāsiḥ,
maṅhyaŋ ry anugraha nirè rikaŋ antaśāpa*

:321:\:32:\:5:. mojaṙ sirāṣĕmu manis tĕkap iŋ tumiṅhal,
Om haywa saṅśaya ri sidđa niŋ antaśāpa,
tan lupta yan tĕka hĕlĕm saŋ Ajāhawan‌ ṅkè,
tuṅtuŋ ni sañjata nikā hawananta mantuk*

:322:\:32:\:6:. sāmpun sirāmĕkasakĕn wacanāntaśāpa,
luṅhā sira ṅhulun aṅanti humèṙ tĕkanta,
sowènta tan tĕka ya kāraṇa niŋ ƀramanta,
mĕttāwĕṝö pira piraŋ tahunĕn byamoha*

:323:\:32:\:7:. maṅkè n ḍatĕŋ kita sahāśwa sahaśra saṅꝁya,
ṅkè naṙmmadāwija wijaḥ sawatĕk watĕkta,
mātĕṅga papraŋ aṅiriŋ paḍa sāra śūra,
