mawṛĕg ṛĕbaḥ binuru ni ṅhulun iŋ paḍöman*

:324:\:32:\:8:. Aṅhiŋ kitāmanaḥ anuṅṣuŋ iŋ astra tīkṣṇa,
syuḥ kumƀa ni ṅhulun ikā tinut iŋ paratra,
ndātan paniṣꝑala wawaŋ maluyādadi hyaŋ,
sākṣāt kitāmṛta wijil nikaŋ antaśāpa*

:325:\:32:\:9:. Atyanta göŋ ni hutaŋ i ṅhulun apramāṇa,
saṅmohana ŋ pamalĕsè kita diwyaśastra,
ganđaṙwwaśastra pinajöŋ hyaŋ asañjatèka,
jñānanta maṅlĕpasakĕn saha mantra sidđi*

:326:\:32:\:10:. Atyanta yogya yan ajinta ya ka‌wruhanta,
kārāđananya saha mantra sahèndikanya,
pöṅpöŋ‌ ṅhulun ‌wruḥ i wĕkas ni ruṣit ruṣitnya,
śaktinya ka‌wruhan anambĕhanè guṇanta*

:327:\:32:\:11:. ndātan pamatyani guṇanya yadin guṇanta,
śatṙww āđamāpituwi tan mati dènya mūṙcꞓa,
moǥāturū sahana niŋ ripu tan wri rātnya,
nistanya maṅkana yayā kita yan jayèŋ praŋ*

:328:\:32:\:12:. hè saŋ priyambada kita n paṅutus paṅajya,
moǥāwiraŋ hulun apan gumawè laranta,
ṅūnī sĕḍĕṅta matĕmaḥ gajamattarūpa,
tan lèn‌ ṅhulun kaṅaranan karaṇanta māti*

:329:\:32:\:13:. hā hāḥ hadè saŋ Aja dènta manaṅgaḥ èraŋ,
An sāhasāmĕjahi ri ṅhulunĕn gajèndra,
Āpan praṣidđa kita maṅhwatakĕn kajanman,
Atyanta göŋ i hutaŋ i ṅhulunĕn maluy hyaŋ*

:330:\:32:\:14:. yadyan saƀūṙ ƀuwaḥ ikaŋ guṇa ka‌wruhanta,
tātan sadoṣa yan atambĕha wīṙyya saswaḥ,
ndā maṅkanā kita n aṅajya wimohanāstra,
taṅgap nihan hila hila ŋ tumulak pawèwèḥ*

:331:\:32:\:15:. An saŋ priyambada kĕdö maṅutus maṅajya,
maṙyy āwiraŋ saŋ Aja sāmpun atiṅkaḥ uṅgwan,
loṙ saŋ priyambada kidul saŋ Ajātalaṅkup,
saṅmohanènaji nirèṅgal apan widagđa*

:332:\:32:\:16:. sanđinya kāku saha śakti ni dèwatanya,
saṅyoga niŋ śarawara mwaŋ ikā tujunya,
sāmpun tama stuti nikā saha kūṭamantra,
saṅhāramantra paḍa ka‌wruḥ ira praƀèda*

:333:\:32:\:17:. ‌wruḥ saŋ priyambada ri haṙṣa narèndraputra,
An pèmbuḥ astra śara sūkṣma mahāpraƀāwa,
tiṅkaḥ niŋ apraŋ inucap nira moǥa jambat,
Amwit sirāṣĕmu manis baśa dè niŋ ojar*

:334:\:32:\:18:. hè mitra mantuka kakanta lumaṙyya maṅkè,
sidđā ŋ prayojana kita n ḍatĕṅèŋ widaṙƀa,
nāhan wuwus nira nĕhĕṙ maṅagĕm sĕṛĕḥ wwaḥ,
luṅhāhawan gagana mĕltuk apan sira hyaŋ*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:335:\:33:\:1:. sāmpun prāpta sirèŋ surālaya wicitraraŧa paḍa suꝁa n tumon sira,
ndan saŋ kāri kamānuṣan hĕla hĕlāṅucap ucap i sĕḍĕŋ nirāpupul,
nistanya n tama dè nirāṅaji taŧāpi salahasa ri saŋ priyambada,
yan tĕṅhā kadi tan tumuṅkula sawèt ni karakĕtan irāṅdĕlö tawaŋ*

:336:\:33:\:2:. sanđyākāla pasaŋ damaṙ nṛpatiputra manaḍaḥ i huwus nirājapa,
Èñjiŋ pūṙwwaka saŋ priyambada ginoṣṫi nira mahuwusan tĕṅaḥ wĕṅi,
wahw amṛĕm tumuluy tinaṅhi sira maṅkat asalĕsĕk i tīra niŋ nadī,
gĕntĕṙ ni grit ikaŋ raŧāmĕkarakĕn kucup iŋ asana ramya tūt hĕnū*

:337:\:33:\:3:. Èñjiŋ kāla nira n tĕkèŋ pasiṙ alasnya pĕtĕŋ asĕmu śèṣa niŋ wĕṅi,
lwiṙ haṙṣā gaganāsĕgĕḥ pawulatanya gĕṛĕḥ ika kadi priyambada,
moǥāśrī kumĕḍap kilatnya nĕhĕṙ aṅluru luru kadi mèdi maṅdu lor,
kady ānĕmbahakĕn sĕkaṙ niŋ asanānisi huyaŋ i riris nikāṅdadak*

:338:\:33:\:4:. mambö sāgara ramya niŋ laṅit awaṙṇna tali hurut urutnya tan pĕgat,
kālaṅkyaṅnya baṅun jukuŋ niŋ amayaŋ lĕyĕp i lari nikāmaḍĕm ḍarat,
kuntul möṙ kadi tuṇḍan iŋ banawa kāri tan ilu kajahat lanālayar,
saŋ hyaŋ candra baṅun bahitra ḍatĕŋ iŋ kulĕm amawa śaśā marè jawa*

:339:\:33:\:5:. mèǥa lwiṙ karaŋ iŋ laṅit kadi wĕṛĕḥ limut ika ri sarè nikāputiḥ,
wahw āmīt i kuwuŋ kuwuṅnya sawanèḥ kaṛĕṛĕban akucĕm pĕgat pĕgat,
gĕntĕṙṇnyāwurahan humuŋ kadi katunwan i larap i kilat nikā murub,
runtuḥ piṅgiṙ ikātĕmaḥ jawuḥ anūtakĕn aṅin alaṅö tibānisiḥ*

:340:\:33:\:6:. ramya lwiṙ siluman karaŋ ri muꝁa niŋ muhara paḍa paḍāṅhapit bañu,
Alwā tiṅkaḥ i mèꝁalanya ri tĕṅaḥ paṅadĕg adĕgan iŋ marāṅlĕṅĕŋ,
kaṙwwānuṅgul apāntaran sapaṅuhuḥ kadi gupura śīwak sakèŋ adoḥ,
lwiṙ hambal sꝑaṭikāŋ alun turunan iŋ kawi pĕjaḥ atuhāṅhañut laṅö*

:341:\:33:\:7:. priṅgāhrit tĕpi niŋ samudra kadi paṅhinĕpan i lĕṅĕŋ iŋ labuḥ kapat,
lwiṙ prāṣāda pukaḥ karaŋ ni paraṅanya hana kadi siluṅluŋ iŋ kawi,
Aiṙttambaṅnya baṅun wwit iŋ truḥ asĕwö kilat awilĕt alūŋ awaṅkawa,
lumrāwaṙṇna ṛĕṅit kukusnya sinawat sawat inidĕran iŋ guruṇḍaya*

:342:\:33:\:8:. miṅgut piṇḍa nikaŋ karaŋ liman anuṅkuli paraṅan i piṅgiṙ iŋ tasik,
lwiṙ molaḥ tulalè nikāmijilakĕn bañu kadi paṅanak niŋ èṙttali,
kahyun hyun kumucuṙ paṛĕŋ rwa tumĕḍun lĕṅĕŋ aṅĕnani tiṅhas iŋ karaŋ,
ṛĕmpū syuḥ amĕniṙ mĕniṙ kadi tinapyan iŋ aṅin aputiḥ sumamburat*

:343:\:33:\:9:. paṇḍan māti lĕṅĕŋ sumuṇḍay akaraŋ hulu karaŋ i sarè nikaŋ pasir,
sakwèḥ niŋ ƀramarānaṅis paḍa sumuṅkĕm aṅaṛĕki sĕkaṙ huwus lĕwas,
dinyūs iŋ truḥ i saṅhub iŋ jalađi saṅṣaya lĕṅĕŋ arurub rurub limut,
hèmanyānwam arūm puḍak nika tumūt pĕjaḥ i turuŋ ikātulis ṭikā*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓

:344:\:34:\:1:. nyū dantāsĕpi tuṅga tuṅgal aṅadĕg muṅgw ī ṛĕṅat niŋ tṛĕbis,
lĕṅlĕṅnya n hana riŋ pasiṙ siliḥ awè lāwan ryak iŋ sāgara,
tan ‌wruḥ yan tinulis parab sahana niŋ wwahnyākĕmul nīrada,
dè niŋ laṅw anaput katuṅkul i laṅö niŋ nūsa mukṣa n ṛĕṛĕb*

<śiꝁariṇī> ⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓

:345:\:35:\:1:. mahāntĕn sāk riñcuŋ lĕṅĕŋ i tĕpi niŋ sāgara lĕyĕp,
palambaṅnyākwèḥ nora wĕnaṅa wacan śīṙṇna lamukĕn,
tulisnyānuṅgal wikw acĕpuḥ atalaṅkup katuruhan,
tumuṅkul ƀāwanyāḍĕku ḍĕkuḥ apiṇḍānasi hatĕp*

:346:\:35:\:2:. Ikaŋ prāṣāda syuḥ karahan apa tèkāmarikala,
tibè piṅgiṙ niŋ sāgara kasiḥ aṛĕp hyaŋ gaṇapati,
katampwan dè niŋ ryak mata nira kumĕmbĕŋ kadi lumuḥ,
mulat kady ahyun wuṅwakĕna sira yan kāla hasila*

:347:\:35:\:3:. karaŋ sawwaŋ muṅgw iŋ jalađi mapa mūlanya ta kunaŋ,
wilĕt niŋ mèǥa ry āwak ika sagibaḥ tan pinahuwus,
winaswās kady ānabraṅa sĕmu nikāṅlaṅhwiy anĕṅaḥ,
baṅun ƀrāntāmaṅgiḥ pasiṙ ahaṛĕp aṅlimbaṅa laṅö*

<giriṣa> ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:348:\:36:\:1:. banawa kajahat iŋ lod biṅkas dè niŋ alun agöŋ,
tihaŋ ika gumalaṅgaŋ muṅgw iŋ tuṇḍan ika maṛĕk,
kadi ta pamĕkulanya n māsiḥ tan wĕnaŋ apasaḥ,
sapati sahuripa ṅwaŋ līṅanya n ‌wruḥ aṅucapa*

:349:\:36:\:2:. wukiṙ anak anĕlat riŋ wwai niŋ sāgara ri tĕṅaḥ,
kadi sakadaṅa lāwan wwaŋ mūṙcꞓā kawi pasisi,
sĕmu sĕmu nika sānak lāwan ryak jĕnĕk aharas,
pili piliḥ abapènduŋ truḥ truḥ māṙgga nika lĕṅĕŋ*

:350:\:36:\:3:. layaṙ iŋ amayaŋ akwèḥ ṅkānè soṙṇnya humaliwat,
karahan aburu maṙmmanya n kèdĕṙ nĕhĕṙ awĕlaḥ,
đwatala rayuŋ ikānraŋ lumrā söḥ paṅanan ika,
bañak aṅidĕri nūsā kāraṅnya n midĕṙ alaṅö*

:351:\:36:\:4:. patani kadi jamuṙ syuŋ rūpanyāmanis atulis,
kalimutan i siluk niŋ groŋ groŋ iŋ paraṅan aṛĕs,
kakawin ika palambaŋ riŋ lambaŋ cinacahakĕn,
cĕcĕk ika hana tan saḥ muny aśriŋ baṅun amaca*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:352:\:37:\:1:. māṙyy āmèt lĕṅĕŋ iŋ pasiṙ nṛpatiputra lumaris ahawan gunuŋ gunuŋ,
Ambö niŋ pakis ĕṇḍaḥ iŋ walahaṙ aṅlĕwihi waṅi ni ganđa niŋ pupur,
moǥārūm sirarā nikaŋ kayu ragas kadi hulĕs apulaŋ lawan burat,
sakwèḥ niŋ kahalintaṅan rumimaŋ ambĕk ira winulatan paḍālaṅö*

:353:\:37:\:2:. paṇḍan suṇḍay asoŋ latāṅkura paranti para kawi mahās lanāpikat,
paŋ niŋ campaka śudđi guṇḍik aṅilo ri haṛĕp ika maṅuṅkul uṅkuli,
luṅlūṅanya tikĕl tikĕl katitihan papikatan agĕnĕt hibĕk hĕlar,
tan śoƀa ŋ kitiran jaraḥ pili piliḥ luput alara kasambĕt iŋ habĕt*

:354:\:37:\:3:. wwantĕn ramya kadèwaguṙwwan aṅuṅaŋ jalađi kadi kalaṅwan iŋ tulis,
saŋ muṅgw īriya tan wĕnaŋ lumaganīndriya nira kawĕnaŋ binañcana,
paṅliṅgāna sawaŋ sawaŋ ni hayu nīdĕman ira sĕmu niŋ warāpsarī,
kady āṅanti ri sampunanya n apatūtan aniliba marèŋ surālaya*

:355:\:37:\:4:. ṅkānèŋ bwat halu sāk durènya kahanan nṛpatanaya tumiṅhal iŋ tulis,
hèman waṙṇna nikāsamun katuruhan lutuṙ asamun inambaḥ iŋ cĕcĕk,
ṅhiŋ dèwī kawĕkas lawan kili paḍāṅadĕg adĕg abĕbĕd bĕbĕd hati,
kady āminta tumūta rūpa nika budđi saŋ Aja hiḍĕpan kamānuṣan*

:356:\:37:\:5:. ṅkānè ṛĕmbaṅan iŋ juraŋ‌ mpu tapa ramya mamuluku katuṅku tuṅkulan,
wuṅkal kèdĕran aṅjĕlag sadĕdĕg iŋ sapi kapaṛĕk i piṅgiṙ iŋ galĕŋ,
lĕmbunyān ahĕlè hĕli n palayanan pawulatan ika dè nikaŋ watu,
Aśrak waṅṣulan iŋ kiyātṛĕt alaṅö lĕṅĕŋ araras aniṙwwa niṙwwakĕn*

:357:\:37:\:6:. nyāsa lwiṙ minahā gunuŋ pinakapājaran aṅadĕg i mađya niŋ juraŋ,
lwīṙ apwī kumukus miraḥ ni kayu tèja nika kasaputan himāputiḥ,
wwai saṅkèŋ paraṅan ya kadṛĕsan aṅin kadi siniramakĕn sumamburat,
saŋ wṛdđaṙṣi katon iŋ agra sawaŋ aṙcca lamukĕn alaṅö kasaṅhuban*

:358:\:37:\:7:. siṅgiḥ kottaman iŋ wanāśrama saƀā saŋ ataki taki niṣparigraha,
kaywanyā‌wruḥ acandanāpriḥ atĕṅö jawa huwi kusumāṅjraḥ iŋ talun,
kālaṅkyaṅnya lĕyĕp wiśāta baṅun ahyun atapa riŋ aṅin huwus lĕpas,
saŋ hyaŋ lèk sumĕnö prakāśa śuci śukla pinakasuluḥ iŋ hanèŋ wukir*

:359:\:37:\:8:. tan saḥ riŋ daluwaŋ kukap nika subadđa sĕkaṙ ikaŋ uluṙ paḍājaṭā,
wrènyāṅalwaŋ ikaŋ warāha wana tan parabi suꝁa manambi riŋ tahĕn,
mwaŋ saṙppātapa tāpan abrata lanāṅaluṣa puyuḥ ikākipū kipū,
niṙdđūma ŋ balĕman lumöŋ baṛĕbĕk iŋ kayu pinaṅan ika n hanèŋ alas*

<kilayu> Anĕḍĕŋ – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:360:\:38:\:1:. budđi nṛĕpatisuta jĕnĕk ya kāraṇa nirāṅṛĕwĕŋ alas akulĕm,
sakwèḥ nira saŋ ajaṙ ajaṙ maṛĕk saha kilaŋ hinaturakĕn ira,
ramyāṅucap i sakahaṛĕp nirèŋ ꝑala nikaŋ tapa ginawayakĕn,
Èñjiŋ sira tumurun atūt alas wahu tinoṙ pinakapatalĕsan*

:361:\:38:\:2:. dèśāsĕpi hawan ira kālasan sipi kaniṣṫa nika gataraṣa,
Aṅluḥ wwaŋ ika pinanasan ḍinaṇḍa sinipat layat apalaraṣan,
Akwèḥ pahutaṅan i sawaḥ gaganya paḍa tan hana maṅinak inak,
lumbuṅnya kasiḥ aṛĕp aninya ya n milu katuṅkĕb alawas aṅariŋ*

:362:\:38:\:3:. Akwèḥ wray anusup anukĕt nukĕt baṅun amèt kayu paṛĕŋ adulur,
ḍaṅḍaṅnya lumĕkas aṅatĕṙ sĕsĕḥ kaṅĕlihan sawaŋ aṅipil ipil,
pakṣinya palatuk amaduŋ maduŋ kahiḍĕpanya n amahāyu kuwuŋ,
wwaḥ niŋ kamalagi tumatiŋ katon kadi caluk niŋ anutu nutuhi*

:363:\:38:\:4:. kācāṙyyan alawas inatīta śīṙṇna pamicāran ika katuruhan,
riñcuŋ saka nika sasisiḥ siliḥ jaga murantak aṅĕmuki parab,
norākṣara kakawin i paṅlarinya paḍa tan hana katĕmu lĕbur,
ṅhiŋ candana kasirat agātra mātra ri tawiṅnya kari kadi panu*

:364:\:38:\:5:. jöŋ niŋ giri gahana kadèwaguṙwwan ahalĕp lura luraḥ aṛĕnĕb,
strī strī dwijakula śuci śudđa saŋ pinakamaṅgala niŋ anaruka,
tūs niŋ wulakan aṅali mèkalanya śatapattra nika mĕkaṙ arūm,
sakwèḥ niŋ amaṅan i lumutnya rakwa cinacad puru puru katalu*

<śiꝁariṇī> ⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓

:365:\:39:\:1:. byatītan mèḥ prāptèŋ nagara saŋ Ajāṅèl bala nira,
Araṙyyan‌ ṅkānè jro kuṭi katĕmu sakwèḥ para wiku,
tinamwī tamwī riŋ sĕḍĕṅan amanis dè nira mulat,
Apan prāya ŋ wastw alpa maṅinaki yan riŋ sĕḍĕŋ aṅèl*

:366:\:39:\:2:. wiwakṣan sakwèḥ saŋ para ratu hinundaŋ paḍa tĕka,
paḍākuṇḍaŋ gĕṇḍiŋ gumĕṛĕḥ asĕluṙ tan papĕgatan,
tuwin paṅhrik niŋ tuṅgaṅan asahuran lāgi kaṛĕṅö,
Ikaŋ sattwālöŋ śabda nika baṅun asyaŋ syaŋ aṅuhuḥ*

:367:\:39:\:3:. kaḍatwan saŋ ƀojātiśaya mara göṅnyāparamita,
yayāhöt maṅkè kāṙyya nira ri ḍatĕŋ saŋ para ratu,
pĕnuḥ tamwī tamwī sahana para taṇḍālana ṅiwö,
tĕkèŋ māṙggāgöŋ nora pinakapahidwan paḍa hibĕk*

:368:\:39:\:4:. Ikaŋ rājya lwiṙ sāgara kahibĕkan wwaŋ kadi bañu,
karaŋ mātaṅgākāra ni liman ikānèka majajar,
baṅun ryak polaḥ niŋ đwaja kagurilap kadṛĕsan aṅin,
curik wahwas patṛĕm lumarap asĕmu praŋ praŋ agalak*

:369:\:39:\:5:. sanistanya n tan waspada wiṣaya niŋ śabda kaṛĕṅö,
tĕkap niŋ gĕṇḍiŋ mwaŋ gṛĕbĕg i laku niŋ wwaŋ mapapagan,
yayātaḥ wṛtta śrī raǥusuta kaṛĕṅw an sira tĕka,
wulat hèṛĕn taŋ wwaŋ sanagara paḍālaḥ ṛĕṅĕ ṛĕṅön*

:370:\:39:\:6:. lumampaḥ saŋ ƀojāmapag i saŋ Ajāpan sira tĕka,
kasuṅṣuŋ riŋ māṙggāṅucap ucap aluṅguḥ paḍa suꝁa,
paṛĕŋ maṅkat ramyāduluṙ iniriŋ iŋ wwaŋ sanagara,
Ikaŋ rājya lwiṙ bĕntara muꝁa nikān aṙdđa marupĕk*

:371:\:39:\:7:. Umaḥ niŋ taṇḍāgöŋ pinakapasĕnāhè nṛpasuta,
kulĕm saŋ hyaŋ sanđyā diwasa niŋ amūjājapa japa,
tĕka ŋ pamyāpārè sira wijil ikaŋ sāgara wukir,
ndatan waṙṇnan tiṅkaḥ ni panaḍaḥ irākwèḥ cinarita*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:372:\:40:\:1:. tiṅkaḥ śrīndumatī n kapiŋ tiga nira n piniḍuḍuk i dalĕm kaŧākĕna,
Akwèḥ pañcabalè ri wiṅkiṅan ikaŋ pamiḍuḍukan i soṙ huwus hibĕk,
dè niŋ‌ strī paḍa hinyasan cumurigènunus awak ika waṙṇna sañjata,
byaktākūṅa kalĕṅgakèŋ panulisan puḍak ikaŋ anulad raras nika*

:373:\:40:\:2:. twas niŋ mèǥa dinadyakĕn waṅunan uttama pinahuwus iŋ labuḥ kapat,
tumpaŋ pitw aruhuṙ sinaptaƀuwanāparimita kalaṅönya riŋ tawaŋ,
truḥ truḥ mwaŋ larap iŋ kilat hatĕp ikā karaṇa nika lanākuwuŋ kuwuŋ,
gĕntĕṙṇnyāṅdadi kumbaŋ èdran anaṅis hana lĕṅĕŋ aṅurambat iŋ tĕtö*

:374:\:40:\:3:. ryak niŋ tīṙŧa sinṛṣṭi wastra tinulis pinakatiba tibān linaṅwakĕn,
tustus niŋ maṇi sūṙyyakānta dumilaḥ rahina wĕṅi dinadyakĕn damar,
kĕmbaŋ niŋ cirapattra kalpatarupuṣpa sadĕdĕg aṅadĕg tigaŋ siki,
māyā niŋ wulan iŋ samudra mađu śudđa saꝑala ginawè laṅit laṅit*

:375:\:40:\:4:. byaktābyakta nikaŋ tulis wuwuḥ i kādƀuta nika tulis iŋ huwus tama,
yan kĕmbaŋ kadi mambwa rūmnya kadi molaha winilĕt i luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,
mwaŋ yan wwaŋ wwaṅan aṙjja kady aṅucapāsĕmu sĕmu guyu dè nikā mulat,
wimba hyaŋ‌ smara śudđi dè niŋ anulis lwiṙ amanaha manaḥ nṛpātmajā*

:376:\:40:\:5:. ṅkā tôṅgwan nṛpatiputrikā piniḍuḍuk tuhu tuhu sira janma dèwatī,
tan sāmānya mahāpraƀāwa tĕka riŋ kaka kaka kadi dèwakanyakā,
Aśrī pahyas ira bwat/ Indrawanitāmuwuhi halĕp ira n hanèŋ saƀā,
ḍaŋ saṅǥāguñĕpan ƀaṭāra karikāṅrakĕt ujaṙ ira yan tumon sira*

:377:\:40:\:6:. sakwèḥ kwèḥ nira saŋ kadaŋ haji huwus kili maṛĕk atatā paḍātuha,
mambö paṙwwata pājaran halĕp i dè nira humalĕpakĕn suputrikā,
Èndaḥ mwaŋ sira saŋ rarè hañaṙ ataṅkil ahayu hayu wahw amèꝁala,
mambö maṇḍala riŋ saƀā paṅupaṛĕṅga ni halĕp ira riŋ nṛpātmajā*

:378:\:40:\:7:. strī strī wāhu cumampakāsĕmu hijo pamulu nika pinantĕs iŋ saƀā,
sampiṙṇnyèŋ jaja tan paniṣꝑala hananya muwuhi halĕp iŋ wulaŋ tatur,
tuṅgal dènya mawāmbĕk abwat atuhan ri paṛĕk ika ri jöŋ nṛpātmajā,
lwiṙ dèwī humatuṙ sakèŋ surapadānrahakĕna halĕp iŋ surālaya*

<kilayu> Anĕḍĕŋ – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:379:\:41:\:1:. praḥ praḥ nṛpawaraduhitā ri guṇḍik ira lèn i kaka kaka nira,
yan ‌wruḥ ‌wruḥ agamĕl aṅiduŋ lawan ‌wruḥ aṅawat ya linĕṅĕnan ira,
Èmbuḥ pwa guṇa nika siniṅhĕlan kinaluṅan ya kinalĕwihakĕn,
sāmpun pwa ya kawi paḍa kāku siŋ guṇa samaṅkana ya kinarahan*

:380:\:41:\:2:. sakwèhnya paḍa maṛĕk anaṇḍaŋ anwam araras rara rahayu wagĕd,
saƀyāmanis aṅucap ikāŋ asiṅhĕl akaluŋ wahu kawi kakawin,
ndan rwaŋ puluḥ ikaŋ akaraḥ jitākṣara wicakṣaṇa naṭakagiṇa,
ṅhiŋ dyaḥ jayaluḥ ikaŋ inuttamāsisik ĕmās maṇi nĕhĕṙ amawa*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:381:\:42:\:1:. prāpta ŋ rātri yayan katon hayu ni waṙṇna nira ri wijil iŋ niśākara,
hyaŋ hyaŋ niŋ mađumāsa rūpa nira yan kasaṅa kasapuluḥ tiniṅhalan,
maṅkè n māsa kapat hyaŋ iŋ masa kapat kahiḍĕpan ira dè nikaŋ mulat,
cañco strī liṅa niŋ tumon sira mĕnè n huwus atĕmu lawan nṛpātmaja*

:382:\:42:\:2:. lumrāmintaŋ ahöm ri bāhu lumarap jĕnu nira kanakāṅhulap hulap,
Èmbuḥ söŋ ni tutup gĕluŋ nira murub maṇik ika kadi motaṙ otaran,
dè niŋ kostuƀa nīla kādƀuta sĕkaṙ taji nira sumĕnö kapañjutan,
Ūṙṇnā śudđa huwus hanèŋ rahi nirāṣĕmu paṅawaka tĕṅran iŋ hurip*

:383:\:42:\:3:. ndin‌ ṅgānya ŋ wwaŋ anĕmwa rūpa kadi rūpa nira n ahayu rājaputrikā,
wwaŋ riŋ rājya yayan kapūhan aṅalĕm ri sira kadi hañaṙ hañaṙ mulat,
Aśrī waṙṇna nira n tuhan saꝑala yogya n adĕgakĕna ratwa niŋ tulis,
tan samwas lawaŋ iŋ kaḍatwan inucap milu milu kawĕṅān tiniṅhalan*

:384:\:42:\:4:. paṅkun mèsya ṭikā kayogyan i wĕtis nira damarana tèja niŋ wulan,
pantĕs yan makasumpiṅĕn kikiṛĕn iŋ kuku kuku nira kosapèŋ laṭi,
rèꝁan riŋ kakawin wilāpa kahalĕp ni susu nira parantya niŋ parab,
tan sāhèŋ ratu śakti kènaka ni soca nira yan ikĕtĕn sĕkaṙ taji*

:385:\:42:\:5:. Èkĕl roma nirāraras kadi katona rumaraba sakèŋ gĕluŋ lukar,
Akwèḥ mahyun aṅuḍwa dè nira yan ahyas anisigi wajāṅhĕmū guyu,
yogyāsaṅkan aṅin dumadyakĕna polaḥ i tikĕl i halis nira n cala,
byaktāgatgat ataṅhya taṅhya manaḥ iŋ mulat i muꝁa nira n pasaŋ damar*

:386:\:42:\:6:. ndin putṙyy āhayu  hayw amaṅpaṅa hayunya ri hayu nira n ahyas aṅḍiri,
sakwèḥ niŋ wwaŋ ahadyan akṙyyan asawaŋ hinayu maṛĕk i jöŋ nirālawas,
pahyas niŋ para pora maṅhiribi pahyas ira hinayu cihna niŋ manūt,
Èkacꞓattra raras raras nira paṅöban iŋ ahayu sujanmakanyakā*

:387:\:42:\:7:. sakwèḥ saŋ ratu tan wĕnaŋ sahasa kèwala humĕnĕŋ aṅantyakĕn pariḥ,
Aṅlampū sumĕsĕl śarīra nira tan wĕnaŋ anĕkani sènakè hati,
mogānaṅgĕl aṛĕs rumĕṅwakĕn i kādƀuta ni hayu narèndraputrikā,
mawwat rāga wilāpa cihna niŋ akūŋ alaḥ alĕḥ akirim kirim ṭikā*

:388:\:42:\:8:. Akwèḥ pahyas irāṛĕbut kahulunan kahiḍĕpan ira dè nikaŋ maṛĕk,
roṙww aŋ campaka ramya māyun ayunan ri jaja nira n amaṅya maṅyani,
lāwan pādapa tan wĕnaŋ saḥ i sirāmĕpĕti gaway ika n sĕḥ iŋ gĕluŋ,
tañjuŋ muṅgw i kapö nira n mrik inaṅit maṛĕk araras anulya nulyani*

:389:\:42:\:9:. prāptôliḥ kalaṅön ikāŋ asana ramya pinakakalasā nirāturū,
mwaŋ roṇḍonya tinap rinūpaka tilam sinalinan i sĕḍĕŋ nikāluñut,
maṅgā sĕmpalĕn aṅkĕn èñjiŋ alapĕn humatura śayanā nira n rimaŋ,
swaṙgga n māti kakiṅkiṅan huwus akīṙtty amihutaṅi laṅö ri jöŋ nira*

:390:\:42:\:10:. moliḥ waṙṣa sipat nirārahat i solaḥ ika tĕka hiṛĕŋ hanè mata,
kālanya n kahĕmū sĕpaḥ nira baṅun pinakaliḍaḥ ira n hanè tutuk,
kāsiḥ kāsiḥ irālawas karika puṇḍutan ira kasĕlap hanè hati,
ṅhiŋ kĕṇḍit nira mās tumūt i parahasyan ira wahu maṛĕk sinanmata*

:391:\:42:\:11:. tambè rakwa sira n swayambarakĕnāmiliha sakahaṛĕp nira praƀu,
ndān ambĕk nira kèwalāwiraŋ i līṅa niŋ umulat anĕṅgahāhaṅan,
Āpan tan hana ṅūni kèwala sirāmuṅari pinakakabwatan hañar,
yèkā hètu nirāwiwèka kalawan kaka kaka wihikan riŋ iṅgita*

:392:\:42:\:12:. ndātan kaṙkaśa dè nirāṅucap ucap ri pasĕluṙ iŋ ujaṙ sirāṅucap,
ndi ŋ paṙwwa ndi kitāṅṛĕṅö n hana kadi ṅhulun amiliha jalwa riŋ saƀā,
yadyastun hana maṅkanā niyata ta pwa wiraŋ ika kadīraŋ i ṅhulun,
saṅkṣèpanya huwus katon wiđi narèśwara dinuluṙ i tan siḥ iŋ wiđi*

:393:\:42:\:13:. Āpan kènaka niŋ kadi ṅhulun aṅanti ri kaka haji yan sirāṣiha,
hèṙ hèṛĕn palaṛĕn hanāsiha ƀaṭāra tumĕkakĕna đaṙmma ni ṅhulun,
prāptānomahā yogya liŋ nṛpati samƀawa kahaṛĕpa ni ṅhulun muwaḥ,
yadyastun layata ṅhulun pi tawanĕn ry uƀaya haji paran kasaṅśaya*

:394:\:42:\:14:. lāwan yan hana ratw anomahā marā ta sira humaturè narèśwara,
ndātan kahyuna ni ṅhulun sira tuhun kaka haji sira kèwalāhaṛĕp,
haywāmiđyani ta pwa siḥ siha nirāmawaṛĕṅĕha ri budđya ni ṅhulun,
ndak ton duhꝁa nikaŋ kinĕdwakĕn apaṅgiha wiꝑala yan tan paḍāhaṛĕp*

:395:\:42:\:15:. yan kāṅĕn suꝁa niŋ licin dumadak ahyun adaluwaṅa haṙṣa riŋ jamaŋ,
dènya n kilya rarā makāśraya narèśwara kumĕmita kāla niŋ rarè,
yan wṛdđājara đaṙmma riŋ giriwanāmagĕhakĕna ri đaṙmma saŋ wiku,
ramya ŋ waŋ guru loka saṙwwa tĕka yan lumaku laku rinampak iŋ kili*

:396:\:42:\:16:. maṅkè pwa n ḍumawuḥ wiđi nṛĕpati tan pamawaṛĕṅĕḥ i budđi ni ṅhulun,
ṅwaŋ dūra n wĕnaṅājñalaṅǥana tuhun raṣa pĕjaha tibèŋ paluṅguhan,
Èwĕḥ tan kahiḍĕp kalīṅa ni manaḥ nira yan ahaṛĕp iŋ swayambara,
maṅgāṅdadya limut‌ ṅhulun ri wiraŋ i ṅhulun amiliha jalwa riŋ saƀā*

<nawahaṙṣa> ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓

:397:\:43:\:1:. tuhan i ṅhulun akṣamakĕna paṅucap ni manĕhta ṛĕṅön,
wiđi saŋ praƀu samƀawa kĕkĕsakĕnè hati yogya dahat,
dumadak pwa hadè n katĕkana rinasan ri manahta tuhan,
pira haywa nikāṅucapa n ahala yan hiniḍĕp mahāla*

:398:\:43:\:2:. pituhun wiđi saŋ praƀu tuhan anipis kawiraṅta hadè,
paḍa wāhu ḍatĕŋ sahana hana nikaŋ pariwāra maṛĕk,
Amahuṙ hurakĕn ri para ratu pinètnya sirèŋ wĕgilĕn,
sira saŋ kinabèhan inalĕm ika ṛĕṅwakĕnanta tuhan*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:399:\:44:\:1:. saŋ nāŧèŋ magađa praƀāwa nira tan patĕpi kadi laṅit maṅambara,
lwiṙ widyāđara daṙśanīya pakatonan i bala nira śūra dug siṅī,
Ahyaŋ solaḥ irāmanis kawadi dè nira lituhayu tan pasiṅṣiṅan,
sākṣāt/ Indra sakèŋ surālaya kawèni tumuta mijilèŋ swayambara*

:400:\:44:\:2:. krūrākāra saŋ Aṅganāŧa sanirukti sira yan aruhuṙ sulakṣaṇa,
saƀyāmbĕk nira tan rinakwa sira yan praƀu lituhayu sādarāṅucap,
śakty ānindya mahāpraƀāwa kumutug bala nira paḍa śūra suśrama,
tan pèndaḥ kadi saŋ hyaŋ Agni mijil amralayakĕna rumampaka ŋ jagat*

:401:\:44:\:3:. siṅhāmbĕk saŋ Awantināŧa kadi saŋ yama guṇa nira lokapālaka,
norāđaṙmma ṅaranya rakwa yan i ƀūmi nira paḍa suꝁāgawè hayu,
söḥ wadwā nira piṇḍa kiṅkarabalāmawa curiga gadāyuđāpupul,
sākṣāt mṛtyu curik nirākas aluṅid baṅun aṅayam ayam parāṅmuꝁa*

:402:\:44:\:4:. tan pèndaḥ baruṇānurun saŋ Anupāđipati suyaśa ƀūmipālaka,
himpĕṙ sāgara kāṅinan bala nirāṅṙwwabi nagara hibĕk tĕkè dalĕm,
tĕkwan lwiṙ nira riŋ raṅin đwaja wĕlaŋ wĕlaŋ aputiḥ arok lawan hiṛĕŋ,
rāhu mwaŋ śaśiwimba rūpa nika kāraṇa ni musuḥ irātabĕḥ titir*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:403:\:45:\:1:. siŋ solaḥ saŋ susènā pracalita kadi saŋ bāyu riŋ budđi madṛĕs,
wadwā wadwā riŋ ambĕk lituhayu katĕṅĕṙ yan prawīrāpriḥ iŋ praŋ,
himpĕṙ sèḍuŋ kaṛĕsṛĕs bala nira kumisik lwiṙ gĕlap holiḥ aśriŋ,
byakta syūha ŋ musuḥ dè nira n asĕmu hudan sañjatāwoṙ halisyus*

:404:\:45:\:2:. ṅhiŋ saŋ hèmāṅgadātyanta sugiḥ ira hibĕk mās maṇik rājayogya,
līlācum somya saŋ waiśrawana paḍa nira n ǥorarūpādawāgöŋ,
norānaṇḍaŋ yatan mās bala nira satĕgal kāla niŋ hanyan aṅjraḥ,
sakwèḥ niŋ śatru śīṙṇnākuniṅa wulat ikā dè nirāpan waḥ iŋ mās*

:405:\:45:\:3:. Aśrī saŋ pāṇḍya śudđākṛti nira satirun paṇḍitānwam widagđa,
tan kāsy asiḥ tuhun tan haṛĕp iŋ ulaḥ agasyak yayan sopacāra,
saŋ hyāŋ Īśāna sākṣāt paḍa nira n ahalĕp riŋ saƀā nora tan ‌wruḥ,
Atyantèŋ yoga ka‌wruḥ nira karaṇa nira n katwaŋ iŋ śatru śakti*

:406:\:45:\:4:. wwantĕn saṅkèṙyy Ayođyā lituhayu dahatĕn rājaputrādwitīya,
ndan rakwānak mahārāja raǥu saŋ Aja saṅjñā nirèŋ rāt prakāśa,
saŋ saptāđikṛĕtātyanta halĕp ira kabèḥ soṙ kagöṅan pratāpa,
himpĕṙ candrākucĕm tan wani mulat i narèndrātmaja lwiṙ hyaŋ aṙka*

:407:\:45:\:5:. saŋ hyaŋ brahmāgawè rūpa nira kadi paran riŋ raras māṙ manisnya,
yadyan ganđaṙwwa widyāđara niyata nikāsora riŋ rūpa kāliḥ,
Aṅhiŋ hyaŋ kāma saŋ samƀawa mapaga raras rūm nirèŋ maṙttyaloka,
sāmpun pwāṅāśrayè citta nira masuruhan rāga kuŋ don irāṅhèr*

:408:\:45:\:6:. ndān ambĕk ni ṅhulun‌ ṅhiŋ sira juga kadĕlö n kāptya rakryan suputrī,
Anwam pūṙṇnèŋ paṅa‌wruḥ lituhayu taruṇāpālapan‌ kṣatriyāṅśa,
jaṅgāṅuṅṣiṙ kapat ramya nira winulatan dlāha yadyan patĕmwa,
Āpan tuṅgal sirèŋ rūm kadi wulan aṅilo wimba niŋ candrakānta*

<wisaṙjjita> – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓

:409:\:46:\:1:. nāhan ujaṙṇnya paḍāsĕluṙ awara waraḥ kinatuṅgalakĕn,
söŋ i manahnya katon sĕmu sèmu niŋ akuŋ ri narèndraṣuta,
ṅhiŋ kakĕna priḥ ikā sira wiṣaya ni goṣṫi nika n paṅucap,
rūpa nira sŧiti ri twas ika sinamudāya lawan turida*

:410:\:46:\:2:. śrīndumatī suꝁa māṙ hati nira rumĕṅö ry ucapanya ṛĕsĕp,
yan tan awĕdya sirèŋ wwaŋ atuha hana budđi nirāmĕpĕra,
rāga nirè saŋ Ajāwĕtu taṅis inamĕṙ wĕdi ka‌wruhana,
liŋ nira moǥa lumuḥ yan aharip araras parihāra nira*

:411:\:46:\:3:. mojaṙ ikaŋ rinahasyan ira wacana liṅnya ṛĕṅön ta tuhan,
saŋ ratu tan hana tan lituhayu kadi dèwata rakwa sira,
ndan paḍa soṙ sira dè saŋ Aja saꝑala putra narèndra raǥu,
hīṅan ira n sira yogya kahaṛĕpana digjaya rūpa nira*

:412:\:46:\:4:. śrīndumatī kĕna rāga tuhun api hadè kadi tan malara,
dè nira mojaṙ apèt silib amarani lokika budđi nira,
haywa wawaŋ pinisiṅgiḥ ujaṙ ika tuhun hiḍĕpĕn sakaṛĕŋ,
Āpan ikaŋ dadi janma sakahaṛĕp ikā kaka moǥa dudū*

:413:\:46:\:5:. nista nikān apadudwan ibu kahaṛĕp iŋ dadi janma kabèḥ,
yan kinatuṅgalakĕn‌ ndya tika hala nikā tuhanĕn pituhun,
māsku mataṅnya kakūṅana saŋ Aja tuwin wwaŋ anakta sira,
haywa kĕdö liŋ ira ndan asĕmu sĕmu haṙṣa nĕhĕṙ gumuyu*

:414:\:46:\:6:. ndaḥ paḍa bindaṙ ikaŋ maṛĕk i sira kapèṅin ajalwa muwaḥ,
moǥa girahyasĕn ambĕk ika katanĕhan turidāṅlarani,
Asyaŋ i rowaŋ ikāṅucap ucapa kinonya maṛĕk maṛĕka,
liṅnya nihan sanu saŋ ratu pili pilihan dumĕn i ṅwaŋ ari*

:415:\:46:\:7:. wwaŋ wwaŋ ahadwan agatgat anagu nagu mĕṅgĕp atĕṅw ahĕniŋ,
ƀāwa nika n kĕna rāga hanan asidĕhālupa tan paṅinaŋ,
wyaṙŧa sĕṛĕhnya hanè taṅan inagĕm agĕm tuhu tuhw alaṅö,
ƀrānta rumūpaka saŋ suṅana sĕṛĕḥ asūṅa sĕpaḥ ri waja*

:416:\:46:\:8:. lèn taŋ agoṣṫi ri gīta saŋ Aja ginawènya hañaṙ katĕka,
dudw aṅalĕm ri palambaŋ ira mamaranī manis iŋ paṅikĕt,
śrīndumatī kawĕlad hati nira rumĕṅö ri raṣanya lĕṅĕŋ,
lwiṙ jaruman saŋ Ajāmisiki hiḍĕp irāśriŋ akon mijila*

:417:\:46:\:9:. saŋ wwaŋ inuttama sāmpun adaluwaŋ adoḥ sira riŋ wiṣaya,
milw atuhāmbĕk irāraṛĕm aṛĕja suśīla lanāsiḍakĕp,
tan ṛĕṅu tan lumiriŋ duga duga pakatonan i tiṅhal ira,
yan paṅucap sira tan paṅucap ucapa lèn saka riŋ kawikun*

:418:\:46:\:10:. strī sĕḍĕŋ iŋ wiṣayānwam ahaṅan apasabraṅan ambĕk ika,
mwaŋ sira saŋ wiku wṛdđa maṛĕk aṅipi nāga milĕt ri sira,
yan wulat aṅdu matanya dinuluṙ i halisnya tikĕl minahā,
maṙmma manisnya paḍāṅucapakĕn i kahaṙṣa nikā kaṛĕṅö*

<nawahaṙṣa> ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓

:419:\:47:\:1:. wiku rājya kawi ‌wruḥ aṅaji kahaṛĕpku siwiṅkwa sanu,
kakawinya palaṙ piguṇana ri paṛĕknya ri jöŋ nṛpati,
Ulaḥ iŋ paḍa kāsy asiḥ aṅapi laṅö hiḍĕpĕṅkwa suꝁa,
kĕmulaṅkwa jajanya taṅan ika saput saputaṅkwa susu*

:420:\:47:\:2:. Agaḍuḥ kawi kāpti mami sanu wĕnaŋ pasaƀā pawukir,
wijil iŋ pihutaŋ pawadal inani rowaŋ ikānuꝁani,
kalawan kalaṅönya wĕnaŋ anigakĕn manaḥ iŋ prihatin,
yadin aṅlĕṅĕṅādulura maṅusirè tṛĕbis iŋ paraṅan*

:421:\:47:\:3:. Atitiḥ kahaṛĕp mami sanu wĕka niŋ pihutaŋ hutaṅan,
‌wruha tèŋ kakawin kiduŋ ulaḥ ulaḥ iŋ wahu wāhu kawi,
saparanya pamaṅkwakĕna lĕpihan amriḥ amèta laṅö,
sumĕpĕṙ sĕpĕrèŋ papihutaṅan i saṇḍiŋ ikaŋ pasisi*

:422:\:47:\:4:. kahaṛĕpkw alawas‌ ṅhiŋ abasana wicakṣaṇa riŋ kalaṅön,
niyatāraraṣĕn maṛĕk anigi nigī pamabaṙṇnya tapiḥ,
paṅapusnya hatiṅku laris i paṅawaknya katon adadar,
prawalanya marèŋ papasaṅan ika ta n kahaṛĕpku sanu*

:423:\:47:\:5:. puhawaŋ wahu wahw amṛti mṛti katönku siwiṅku sanu,
turidaṅku kaḍaṇḍa n alawas ahaṛĕp wwatĕn iŋ banawa,
Aputĕk hati niŋ kasarapuŋ alaṅö mulat iŋ pasisi,
kaputĕṙ hati ni ṅhulun alal ahaṛĕp tumutèŋ alayar*

:424:\:47:\:6:. Anak iŋ prajurit mĕtu pajurit ikaŋ kahaṛĕpku sanu,
lĕwu ramya niki n katĕkana lurugan ri huwuskw atĕmu,
hawinĕṅkwa curiknya saha raṅin ikā payuṅaṅkwa tumūt,
tan aṛĕs yak umilwa sĕḍĕṅa nika kèṇḍita riŋ palagan*

<giriṣa> ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:425:\:48:\:1:. ya ta tĕmahāna tiṅluṙ dènya n śaiwa sira siwin,
Ikaŋ apalaran anwam ‌wruḥ tèŋ śāstra wiku haji,
lilu tumakula lampūn dan yan paṇḍita nagara,
Atuha tuha bagañjiŋ byaktāṅhöbi yan inusir*

:426:\:48:\:2:. kunaŋ amuhara kiṅkiŋ yan bot swan sipi mararas,
wiku miraḥ aguṇāśrī maṅgĕḥ wikwa narapati,
sira ta siwin ahaṙyyan santoṣāmalara dĕmak,
palumutana yan anwam yan wṛdđāpuput anadi*

:427:\:48:\:3:. taha sanu yan i rantĕntāṅhiŋ tyāga juga siwin,
sipi raras iŋ ataṇḍaŋ dèśādoḥ mahās alaṅö,
lĕwu suꝁa niŋ akaṙwwan soṅṣoŋ yan jamaŋ anipis,
pakararas ika paṅkun gantin mwaŋ palu daluwaŋ*

:428:\:48:\:4:. tuhu marika wuwusta ndan son moǥa salaḥ ilè,
tĕka turida kĕna priḥ dè saŋ brāhmaṇa siniwi,
mulat iŋ awĕka mambaŋ prajñā prāya jitasaƀā,
ṅhiŋ amuhara wiraṅroŋ hèman đūṙtta cala nika*

:429:\:48:\:5:. kunaŋ amuwuhi rāgī riŋ twas ni ṅhulun alawas,
wĕka wĕka capaŋ apriḥ riŋ praŋ wāni panagara,
Aṅawayuha saliŋ liṅnya n sāmpun ṅwaŋ apatutan,
Ikaŋ ujaṙ ibu rakryan kadi asyaŋ maṅiṅin iṅin*

:430:\:48:\:6:. nahan ucapan ikaŋ‌ strī tĕmbènyānĕmu turida,
tan awuni ri manahnya n ƀrāntākuŋ managu nagu,
hana ta titiṙ anambut wèhan milw aṅucap ucap,
mawara waraḥ i rumrūm niŋ sāminya tan awiraŋ*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:431:\:49:\:1:. rarè mĕṛĕ mĕṛĕḥ pajātyan agĕlo winara warahan iŋ pasaṅgaman,
mapaŋ kumĕtĕṙ aṅgamĕl susu taṅanya saha kĕtĕ kĕtĕg sumamburat,
Uliḥ niŋ amuruk muruk tinaṅanan ri pataṅanan i sanđi niŋ pṛĕman,
huwus pwa ya tamāhaṛĕp wayuha tan ṛĕṇa kadi manaḥ iŋ tamèŋ aji*

:432:\:49:\:2:. dudū sanu lawan huwus pracacaḥ aśriŋ arabi siniwi priyambada,
huwus tama karāṣikanya kadi waḥ mađu raṣa nika riŋ giṇāmanis,
Amakpak aṅucap tuhan tinikĕlan halis i sĕḍĕŋ ikāṅgamĕl tapiḥ,
baṅun pĕjaha riŋ karaŋ hulu taṅan ṅwaŋ i paṅamĕṙ ikāṅalap hati*

:433:\:49:\:3:. Ikaŋ kawi ñamut laṅönya rinasan saha kakawin araśmi riŋ tilam,
Ikaŋ jariji moǥa kèlu ginamĕlnya kinuku hiniḍĕp hiḍĕp tanaḥ,
lanānipati pèt manis kawawa kèlu kadi lĕkas ikānulis karas,
kiduṅnya panurū nurūnya sahajāṅgamĕli susu nĕhĕṙ kinaṅṣyakĕn*

:434:\:49:\:4:. prawīra siniwi priyambada tuhun kawatĕk ulaḥ ika n wanīŋ raṇa,
Añumbu kadi dè nika n paṅalawaŋ raṅin i sĕḍĕŋ ika n paṅolakĕn,
Anaṅtaŋ amapag wulat nĕhĕṙ aminta linawanan anūt mamaṅkwakĕn,
marèŋ susu taṅanya moǥa hiniḍĕp nika ḍuka ḍuka niŋ curik siṅī*

:435:\:49:\:5:. lawan lawanan i ṅhulun wiku miraḥ lituhayu pinakèsi niŋ kuṭi,
manisnya kadi poḥ apādapa tiki n mamaragi gula gaṇṭi dug siṅī,
liriṅnya pinarantyan i ṅhulun iŋ ambyan iŋ umaḥ i sĕḍĕŋ nikānasi,
dudū swara nikè karinya kaṛĕṅö panamaya nika yan parè ṅhulun*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:436:\:50:\:1:. nāhan dè nika goṣṫi sènak i manahnya panalimuṙ ikāharip mata,
tan tuṅgal rumĕṅö ry ujaṙṇnya hana hèwa hana sĕmu pacĕḥ mĕṅĕn mĕṅĕn,
strī kṙyyan kṙyyan paḍa mūla mūla rabi niŋ kawi muwaḥ aṅucap samaṅkana,
tan doṣāsiŋ ujaṙṇnya moǥa minanis manisan ika tinuṅtuṅan laṅö*

:437:\:50:\:2:. rakryan kènaka niŋ manuṣya sararā wĕṛĕ wĕṛĕha yayan papaṅgiha,
Ambĕk nāgarika ‌wruhāṅikĕta ƀāṣa sakuraṣa sawīja riŋ laṅö,
yan pāywan kakawin maṅaṙwwana wilaḥ kakawin ika palambaŋ iŋ yaśa,
yèkā kāma ratī ṅaranya n araras paḍa kawi sawawānak iŋ maṅö*

:438:\:50:\:3:. luṅhāṅdoha marèŋ pasiṙ kahalĕpanya n amaṛĕṅana māsa kāṙtttika,
sakwan sèlwan ahimya himyana manumpaka ri walakaŋ iŋ karaŋ liman,
ramyātuntunanèŋ hĕnī ri surud iŋ rwab i tĕpi tĕpi saṅṣayāḍakè,
līlāmèta huraŋ tanaḥ nĕhĕṙ asumpiŋ asaṅu saṅu saṅwa niŋ maṅö*

:439:\:50:\:4:. ndak ton haṙṣa nika n parambakana riŋ bañu tuna tuna mombak ombakan,
kāliḥ kāliḥ ikāduluṙ paḍa girahyasĕn anĕmu laṅö lĕyĕp dahat,
strīnyāmiṅkasakĕn tapiḥ jĕnĕk amèt uwuṙ uwuṙ agĕlaṙ marèŋ tĕpi,
byaktālūma kaköma riŋ bañu hasin wĕtis ika panahā nikaŋ mulat*

:440:\:50:\:5:. rūpanya n mahāsèŋ pasiṙ kadi katona mahāsa ri samudra niŋ tulis,
Āpan dè ni lĕyĕp lĕyĕp ni patĕmunya kadi tasik awoṙ lawan laṅit,
yadyastun yan aṅumbaṅèŋ jalađi ka‌wruhan i pamilĕt iŋ kuwuŋ kuwuŋ,
sākṣāt dèwata dèwatī mahās ahas lĕṅĕŋ aṭika ṭikan sakèŋ tawaŋ*

:441:\:50:\:6:. budđinya n wahu wahw acaṅkrama marèŋ pasisi wahu mahās lawan priya,
maṅgā n tan muliha n panon paduluṙ iŋ layaṙ asĕmu matuntunan taṅan,
solihnya n pakaraŋ karaŋ winawanan taṅan ulaḥ ulaḥ iŋ hañaṙ hañar,
Apwī niŋ hiliran ya sāđana nikākĕla kĕlana ri piṅgiṙ iŋ tasik*

:442:\:50:\:7:. piṅgiṙ niŋ paraṅan gihā watu sumoŋ pinakapasaji riŋ marāṅlĕṅĕŋ,
priṅgāṛĕs tinataṙ hĕnū nika sumĕṅka tumurun atupis ṛĕṅat ṛĕṅat,
paṙṇnaḥ loṙ maṅuṅaŋ tasik muꝁa nikā dunuṅan i kĕñaṙ iŋ niśākara,
ṅkāna n paṅhinĕpāmaḍaŋ wulana yadyan aharipa suꝁa n paḍāmṛĕma*

:443:\:50:\:8:. tĕkwan pwèki n anak wĕsi nṛĕpati kawwaṅan ika wĕka niŋ sinanmata,
yadyastun kilalan tĕkap saŋ ahulun pawĕkasakĕna riŋ marèŋ pasir,
byakta n mantuka moliḥ oliḥ alaṅö haturakĕna ri jöŋ narèśwara,
cihnanya n kawi kaṙwwa kāsiḥ ika wāhu wihikan asaƀā saƀāmasir*

:444:\:50:\:9:. nāhan wastu ni dènya mojaṙ api doḥ ndan aƀimata nikè suputrikā,
śrī dèwīndumatī huwus ‌wruḥ iŋ apa n kasiliba riŋ ujaṙ samaṅkana,
kālap budđi nirèniriŋ winawa riŋ lĕṅĕŋ amasiṙ ahimya himyana,
ndan mogāpi hadè sahuṙ nira paṅa‌wruhana panalimuṙ manaḥ rimaŋ*

:445:\:50:\:10:. siṅgiḥ ṅgānya wuwusta ramya ŋ akuṛĕn sarara wĕṛĕ wĕṛĕḥ paḍāraras,
luṅhāsaṅwa karas tanahnya mahāsèŋ pasiṙ aduluṙ ahimya himyana,
tan waŋ mātra kasiṅya mātra manaḥ i ṅhulun irikaŋ ulaḥ samaṅkana,
ndak ton kèwran ikaŋ giṇāniwi taṅèḥ mamaḍana raras iŋ wujaŋ wujaŋ*

:446:\:50:\:11:. tĕkwan tan hana haṙṣa ni ṅhulun ataṇḍaṅa pasisi huwus tama ṅhulun,
pora wwaŋ nika tan ‌wruḥ iŋ puruṣaƀèda hiliran amukĕt hanāmayaŋ,
moǥèraŋ ṅwaŋ isin maṅambila karaŋ karaṅan i pasurak niŋ ampuhan,
Aṅhiŋ ryaknya maṅaṅkul aṅkul ajajaṙ baṅun asĕgĕḥ anĕmbaḥ iŋ maṅö*

:447:\:50:\:12:. Ambĕk ni ṅhulun iŋ wukiṙ tĕka ṛĕsĕp mwaŋ aṅalĕwihakĕn sakèŋ pasir,
dè niŋ kwèḥ nira paṇḍitātapa ri paṙśwa nika kumuliliŋ tĕkè ruhur,
yadyastun ṅwaŋ atiṅgalèŋ nagara wikwa rara maṅusirè munīśwara,
ramya ŋ pakṣa wukiṙ yayan ku n aṅuṅaŋ ry aƀimata saŋ apakṣa sāgara*

:448:\:50:\:13:. wöṅīŋ māsa kapat‌ ṅhulun milu ri jöŋ nṛpati mahās ahas mariŋ wukir,
saŋ hyaŋ lèk i surup hyaŋ aṙka mijil aṅḍaḍari kadi maṅumbaŋ iŋ pasir,
tūban mwaŋ gĕṛĕḥ iŋ patĕṙ tan asarag đwani nika lalitānurū nurū,
Èñjiŋ mèḥ tumibā ŋ ḍawuḥ pitu samaṅkana mawuṅu tinaṅhi niŋ cucur*

:449:\:50:\:14:. Aƀrā kaywan ikaŋ wukiṙ wijaḥ arūm kadi pinisalinan sĕkaṙ miṅiŋ,
lèn taŋ saṙwwalatāwilĕt samaṙ arok baṅun ahurupa luṅgu luṅguhan,
sakwèḥ niŋ kayu mās lawan kayu puriŋ paḍa paḍa masuṅut wĕlas haṛĕp,
ṅkānè piṅgiṙ ikaŋ juraŋ pĕtuŋ ikā paḍa kadi pinituṅtuṅan limut*

:450:\:50:\:15:. sorè ry ampĕḥ ikaŋ jawuḥ kari gĕṛĕhnya muni pinakaramya niŋ wukir,
lāwan mèǥa marantayan tura turahnya siniriṙ iŋ aṅin pĕgat pĕgat,
miṅṣoṙ miṇḍuhuṙ aṅlayaŋ kadi dinĕmwan añawĕli kukus carik carik,
himpĕṙ siñjaŋ iŋ apsarī kasarakat ri laris ika sakè pamañcanan*

:451:\:50:\:16:. saṅkṣèpanya katon kasoṙ i lĕṅĕŋ iŋ pasisi tĕkap i ramya niŋ wukir,
tĕkwan wiǥna niŋ aṅlĕṅĕŋ mahāsa riŋ pasisi tarahan aṅhaḍaŋ haḍaŋ,
śudđa ŋ paṙwwata nityaśāsĕmu kadèwatan i hana saŋ ugrapaṇḍita,
ndak gañjaṙ kita yan kitāntuka tasik mamaḍana kapawitran iŋ wukir*

<śiꝁariṇī> ⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓

:452:\:51:\:1:. taham rakryan di ŋ paṙwwata lĕwiha saṅkèŋ jalaniđi,
Anūsāpaṇḍan raṅkaŋ apasiṙ asaṅhub saha kilat,
muwaḥ tan pāntyāntyāmpuhan ika baṅun kāṙtttika sadā,
manuknyāliwran yan wahu mari jawuḥ lwiṙ laru laru*

:453:\:51:\:2:. kumĕmbaŋ tuñjuŋ kāṅinan uwuṙ uwuṙṇnyāṅjraḥ aputiḥ,
layaṙ niŋ baṇyāgānutakĕn aṅin aṅdoḥ kadi limut,
lĕṅĕŋ ryaknya n sanđyāmiraḥ asĕmu mèǥānisik iwak,
laṅit suṅṣaŋ lwiṙṇnya n maśaśađaramāyā makalaṅan*

:454:\:51:\:3:. ƀaṭārī śrī pöḥ niŋ jalađi pinutĕṙ lāwan amṛta,
muwaḥ catrāśwātyanta riŋ aṅupaṛĕṅgè halĕp ira,
tuwin hyaŋ wiṣṇu swāmi nira jĕnĕk i jro jalaniđi,
mataṅnyan mūlya ŋ sāgara karaṇa niŋ paṙwwata sinor*

:455:\:51:\:4:. tuhan putrī tan kèmĕṅan iŋ ucapan yogya sahura,
huwus ‌wruḥ rakwè tiṅkaḥ iŋ acala lèn‌ kṣīrajalađi,
Apan yan mūḋā budđi nira pisaniṅw ānĕmu sahur,
kunaŋ pwāpan prajñā sira sumahuṙ apyak saha guyu*

:456:\:51:\:5:. ndatan moli n hyaŋ śrī winijilakĕn iŋ‌ kṣīrajalađi,
paṛĕŋ lāwan catrāśwa kapat ira tèkīkaŋ amṛta,
Apaṅgiḥ mwaŋ hyaŋ wiṣṇu hana riŋ Anantāsana sadā,
ya hètunya n soṙ liṅta ŋ acala tĕkap niŋ jalaniđi*

:457:\:51:\:6:. kaka ndi n sora ŋ paṙwwata tĕkap i rūm niŋ jalaniđi,
Apan lwiṙ ‌wruḥ riŋ swaṙgga ŋ aṅahasi puñcak niŋ acala,
paran saṅkan saŋ hyaŋ rawi gati niŋ astodayagiri,
Umādèwī sākṣāt mara sira sinaṅguḥ giriṣutā*

:458:\:51:\:7:. sirātèkā duṙggā ṅaran ira kasaṅꝁyèŋ triƀuwana,
wĕkas niŋ‌ strī sidđi syapa ta sira dèwī kadi sira,
huwus limpad riŋ kāṣṭaguṇan atiduṙgga n tiru tirun,
kunaŋ tāpan riŋ bimba ya sira n awās kottaman ira*

:459:\:51:\:8:. ƀaṭāra hyaŋ rudra pwa siniwi nirātūt siliḥ asiḥ,
Apaṅgiḥ ṅkānèŋ mèru sira paḍa sidđapraƀu wiƀu,
mataṅnyan nora hyaŋ kadi sira mahāsidđi dahatĕn,
Anādi n riŋ liṅgodƀawacarita pamyaktana kaka*

:460:\:51:\:9:. sirātèkā tūtĕnkwa lumĕwihakĕn riŋ mahiđara,
sakè sakwèḥ niŋ sāgara mapa ta sī madwa karika,
sahuṙ haywāsowè kaka raṣa raṣāpan kita bisa,
tuhankwi ibw amwītālaha tuhu wuwustāhayu dahat*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:461:\:52:\:1:. nāhan dè nira goṣṫi ramya tadanantara rahina huwus ḍawuḥ pitu,
sakwèḥ niŋ paricārikāṅiriṅa sāmpun anarima dadaṙ paḍāsalin,
lāwan saŋ wwaŋ inuttamāhayu sujanma paḍa sira maṛĕk sumaṅgraha,
śrī dèwīndumatī sirāṅadĕg awaṙṇna ratu ni lĕṅĕŋ iŋ ṭikāṅaraŋ*

:462:\:52:\:2:. strī stṙyy ānèkawiśèṣa pakṣa ḍatĕṅèŋ paṅuṅaṅan aduluṙ hanèŋ lĕbuḥ,
Ahyaŋ waṙṇna nika n hinĕmban araras pinayuṅan iniriŋ ƀinūṣaṇan,
sakwèḥ niŋ kapapag lumiṅṣiṙ awĕdīŋ wwaŋ ahalĕp akĕmul ya riŋ wĕṅi,
pañ̈ñjut sañjata lèn garantuŋ i haṛĕp prakaṭa baṅun akon sumiṅgaha*

:463:\:52:\:3:. Èñjiŋ ramya tiniṅhalan sahana niŋ paṅuṅaṅan atatākatap katap,
dè niŋ pañjut awaṙṇna wintaŋ anulaṙ wĕdi karahinanānusup nusup,
mrik ganđanya huwus kinasturi miṅiŋ rinacana tinulis linaṅwakĕn,
wwaṅnyāpiṇḍa surāpsarī saha wimāna wahu tĕka sakèŋ surālaya*

:464:\:52:\:4:. wastrāƀrā pinakapralamba hana riŋ walikuwaŋ anamaṙ kuwuŋ kuwuŋ,
kram niŋ cawli kukus baṅun truḥ anisiḥ pinakapaṅupaṛĕṅga niŋ hatĕp,
himpĕṙ nīrada citramèǥa nika riŋ haḍa pinakatawiŋ tawiŋ marar,
luṅṣiṙ baŋ pinakoluṙ oluṙ i pucak pucak ika kadi luṅgaḥ iŋ kilat*

:465:\:52:\:5:. saśrī waṙṇna nikaŋ payuŋ payuṅan akṛĕp asĕmu sĕmu paṅjraḥ iŋ jamur,
Akwèḥ waṙṇna nikā hanan dadu hanan pṛĕcik asira siran paḍāṅadĕg,
dè niŋ kwèḥ nira saŋ wĕnaŋ paḍa katon kawĕnaŋ ira mijil samaṅkana,
lèn taŋ biṙyyan amèt sĕkaṙ niŋ asanāniru niru halĕp iŋ payuŋ kuniŋ*

:466:\:52:\:6:. saŋ hyaŋ sūṙyya mijil kamantyan abuṅaḥ pawulatan i saƀā nikaŋ kuwu,
wwaṅnya lwiṙ jaladākĕmul kilat asoŋ hima sahana hananya riŋ lĕbuḥ,
dè niŋ kwèhnya lawan praƀā ni sasinaṇḍaŋ ika lumarap aṅhulap hulap,
śaṅꝁa mwaŋ tarayan mṛdaṅga kumisik mamaji taliṅa niŋ wwaŋ aṅṛĕṅö*

:467:\:52:\:7:. wwaŋ wwaŋ ŧāni paḍāduluṙ wahu tĕkāṅibĕki nagara lèn hanèŋ hĕnū,
tĕkwan riŋ sakuṛĕn hanānak ika pat lima maṛĕk amilĕt milĕt laku,
strīnyāṅĕmban anuntun āmĕtĕŋ apan maṅĕliḥ ika manamby anuswani,
Aprakprākan apan hilaŋ sasiki lūd kakutil awurahan siliḥ daliḥ*

:468:\:52:\:8:. lèn tèkaŋ kaki kaky amèt putu nikā hilaŋ i sĕḍĕŋ ikā siliḥ sĕḍĕk,
liŋ niŋ‌ strīnya mahākas ī kita haṛĕp mulata kita nininya riŋ wanèḥ,
Āpan dè ni uninta lāgi ta kitāmupuḥ i sĕḍĕŋ ikāṅucap kaki,
Iḥ dūrānaṅisāku yan kita midoṣana pĕjahana sĕṅgahĕn bahud*

:469:\:52:\:9:. strī strī wṛdđa huwus tĕkèŋ kabuyutan milu milu mulat iŋ swayĕmbara,
Aṅhĕmban raray anwam akrak anaṅis winaliŋ ika putunya rakwa ya,
mojaṙ swāmi nikā nini syapiku hāpa ya kaki taha tan putunta ya,
hā hāḥ tiṅgalakĕn hadè nini tĕwas kita kabṛkĕkĕ duhꝁa kabwatan*

:470:\:52:\:10:. nāhan liŋ nika hāsyakāraṇa sapolaḥ ika tucapa saŋ para praƀu,
ginyākĕn ḍatĕṅèrikaŋ pagĕlaran paḍa mijila kabèḥ sirèŋ lĕbuḥ,
wīṙyya wīṙyyan amĕtwakĕn hati nirèrikaŋ aṅinakanè wwaŋ iŋ saƀā,
muntab lwiṙ ni halĕp nirāṅarab arab sama sama kadi bahni kāṅinan*

:471:\:52:\:11:. maṅkat śrī magađèśwarātri gumuruḥ paḍahi nira kaṛĕṅw agĕnturan,
sakwèḥ niŋ maṅuṅaŋ kapūhan i halĕp nira paḍa mapipit pipit muꝁa,
kady āṅaṙwwani sumpiŋ èndaḥ araras pinatihakĕn ika n paḍāṅuṅaŋ,
tuṅgal waṙṇna nikābuṅaḥ kadi wulan sasiki pinarawĕñca niŋ‌ smara*

:472:\:52:\:12:. Aśrī waṙṇna saŋ Aṅganāŧa sawatĕk watĕk ira mapupul paḍāhalĕp,
himpĕṙ sāgara lakwa lakwan ira ramya tan asĕpi kapiŋ rwa niŋ laku,
tĕkwan rūpa nirāṣĕḍĕp tan ahañaŋ huwus amuyahi ri twas iŋ rimaŋ,
tan tuṅgal stṙyy aṅaraŋ tumon sira manahnya kalara lara kaṙwwaban laṅö*

:473:\:52:\:13:. lwiṙ guntuṙ saŋ Awantināŧa tĕka gumṛĕbĕg ahalĕp anuṅgaŋ iŋ raŧa,
himpĕṙ truḥ sumaput lĕbū nira mĕlĕk pĕtĕŋ alimunan aṅhudan hawu,
sakwèḥ niŋ maṅuṅaŋ paḍa mṛĕm apĕpĕt mĕpĕti muꝁa ri tuṅtuŋ iŋ sabuk,
Agraḥ rūpa nikaŋ kaḍatwan i kĕtug ni paḍahi nira mapratiđwani*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:474:\:53:\:1:. liṇḍū lwiṙ saŋ hanūpāđipati manaḥ ikaŋ‌ strī mulat ƀrāntacitta,
miṅgut miṅgut halisnyāṛĕṅu ṛĕṅu kadi tan wwaṅnya kèwalya mūṙcꞓā,
katrag santĕnya kègū hati nika kagiwaŋ sāri sāri prapañca,
kady ānumbak jajanya n pasidĕha tĕka riñcuŋ tĕṅahnyāṅgaluṅgaŋ*

:475:\:53:\:2:. wānīŋ praŋ saŋ susènā laku nira lumurug kèsyan ambĕk nirākras,
wadwā wadwān dĕlit niŋ tahu rinĕbut i rūm niŋ mulat riŋ paniñjon,
siṅhākārèŋ saƀā yogya wulatana kasaṅꝁya n đanuṙwwèdaśāstra,
sakwèḥ niŋ‌ stṙyy āmapag tiṅhal ira paḍa kĕnèŋ rāga tībra byamoha*

:476:\:53:\:3:. ṅhiŋ saŋ hèmāṅgadākwèḥ asĕmu gunuŋ mās katraṅan kāla sanđyā,
dè niŋ siṅhĕl kaluŋ mwaŋ karaḥ atip apipit paṅhaṛĕp niŋ lumampaḥ,
tan pèndaḥ puṣpa sālas dadaṙ i bala nirārūm apan saṙwwawastra,
gĕṇḍiŋ tan kaṙkaśālwan ƀramara kahiḍĕpanyāṅisĕp saṙwwasāri*

:477:\:53:\:4:. saŋ pāṇḍyāpiṇḍa dèwālaku laku tuwi saŋ paṅruhun paṇḍitākwèḥ,
tātan pèndaḥ sakèŋ budđapada sahana saŋ bodđapakṣāmpak ampak,
śaiwaṙṣy āwaṙṇna saṅkèŋ śiwapada paḍa sāmpun pĕnuḥ riŋ paṅa‌wruḥ,
sakwèḥ saŋ brāhmaṇāpūṙwwa pawulatan ira lwiṙ sakèŋ brāhmaloka*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:478:\:54:\:1:. maṅkat śrī naranāŧaputra kadi kāṙtttika wahu tĕka dè nira n laku,
luḥ niŋ‌ strī kĕna rāga riŋ paṅuṅaṅan kadi riris inusap sakè muꝁa,
tiṅhalnyādu baṅun kilat lumarap aṅluru luru ri huwus nikaŋ jawuḥ,
sambat sambat ikā ginūḋa kadi mĕtwa maṛĕṅana kalaṅwan iŋ patĕr*

:479:\:54:\:2:. liṅnyè twasnya ƀaṭāra manmaŧa manĕhta kawĕlas aṛĕp aṅhiḍĕp lara,
kiṅkiŋ rāga tĕkānaput prihati māṙ pinuhara nika tan wĕnaŋ kinas,
maṅkè kāla nikaŋ swayambara tĕkāmarupuhi sahasāṅṛĕmĕk hati,
Aṅgyat lwiṙ hudan adṛĕs iŋ katiga tan pakakaraṇa kaṛĕṅwan iŋ gĕṛĕḥ*

:480:\:54:\:3:. t asy āsiḥ siha saŋ hyaŋ i ṅhulun alaḥ sĕpĕrakĕna narèśwarātmaja,
syūhĕn dènta manaḥ nirèŋ lulut unĕŋ kĕtĕrakĕna nĕhĕṙ tĕkākĕna,
Āpan tan hana lèn sakè sira pakāśrayan awĕlasa riŋ griŋ i ṅhulun,
tambā rāga siroṣađa prihati jampi turida pinakāmṛtèŋ rimaŋ*

:481:\:54:\:4:. yadyan laṅǥana tan panūta manaḥ i ṅhulun i sĕḍĕŋ ira n pamaṅkwakĕn,
ndak ton kĕdwa nirānukūlakĕna tan kawaśa hinudanan wulat maliŋ,
Āpan siṅha sirèŋ rahasya niyatāṛĕp aṛĕpan i tan olya kapṛĕma,
byaktāṅrampasa kèn dunuŋ susu kayuḥ tĕṅaḥ anĕkani sènakè hati*

<A> kind of/ Aƀikṛti ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:482:\:55:\:1:. nahan liŋ ika ri twas èpu wihikan ri manaḥ ika yatan sakāra dahatĕn,
ya kāraṇa nikāwuyuŋ ri taliṅanya tĕka ṛĕṅĕ ṛĕṅön i wṛtta saŋ Aja,
halisnya pinisitnya tan duga duga n paṅujiwat i sĕḍĕŋ nira n umaliwat,
matanya dinalihnya duṙjjana hĕnū nira mara ri hatinya tan pamali luḥ*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:483:\:56:\:1:. taṅèḥ yan ucapĕn laranya tali niŋ carita waluyanôcapĕn muwaḥ,
para praƀu huwus tĕkèŋ pagĕlaran mapupul asĕmu hètwa niŋ laya,
Apan gumuruḥ apratiđwani surak ni bala nira ya tāmaṅun ƀaya,
baṅun hana katona digjaya katona pĕjaha ṛĕbutĕn salaḥ siki*

:484:\:56:\:2:. Atuṅgalan umaḥ bwat/ Indranagarājajaṙ asĕmu kaḍatwan iŋ tawaŋ,
para praƀu mahāpraƀāwa sawaŋ aṙcca maṇik inululan hanèŋ saƀā,
paḍāsira siran pratāpa kadi tan hana lĕwiha sakè halĕp nira,
tĕka pwa saŋ Ajākucĕm sira baṅun śaśađara matĕmaḥ kunaŋ kunaŋ*

:485:\:56:\:3:. syapèka tan awĕdya riŋ kadi sirāguṇa wĕka niŋ amĕdyakĕn ratu,
Awaṙṇna mađumāsa kāṙtttika piniṇḍa piniturun adadya mānuṣa,
Ikaŋ wwaŋ ahaṛĕp ‌wruhè sira humuŋ sahana hana nikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ saƀā,
katon pwa sira dènya ṛĕp wĕdi kumĕl humĕnĕŋ asĕmu sinyukan bañu*

:486:\:56:\:4:. rarè saŋ Aja śakti pustaka lĕṅĕn raǥuwĕka wani kawy anuṅgali,
Ikaŋ guṇa hanè sirāgaṇita riŋ kapana kawaśa taṙka niŋ mulat,
praṣidđa sira sūtra niŋ karawiwaṅśan amagĕhakĕn āgamèŋ prajā,
ruṣit niŋ aji ta pwa rūpa nira tan hana ratu wĕnaŋ aṅdĕlö dĕlö*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:487:\:57:\:1:. sāmpun prāpta sirèŋ saƀā pinakamaṅgala ni halĕp ikaŋ swayambara,
śrī dèwīndumatī sirènarahakĕn mijila wahu huwus ƀinūṣaṇan,
muṅgw iŋ ḍampa sirāpĕgāṅĕnĕb ĕnĕb kĕtĕ kĕtĕg ira māṙ sumamburat,
saśṙyy āwaṙṇna tulis ḍinampan awĕnĕs wĕnĕs asĕmu rakĕt kapañjutan*

:488:\:57:\:2:. Èndaḥ ḍampa nirāpĕnĕd kinajaṅan kusumaśara tinap linaṅwakĕn,
ronyèndrāyuđa puṣpacāpa pikulanya mamuꝁa muꝁa nāga campaka,
mās tuṅgal nika puṣpaliṅga niŋ aṅaṙccana ri pada ƀaṭāra manmaŧa,
nāgākāra surat suratnya tinĕtĕs ni luḥ iŋ akuŋ amaṅkwakĕn ṭikā*

:489:\:57:\:3:. Ācārī kalawan karaṇḍan ira saŋ pinituhu ri tatā samāṅiriŋ,
sāmpun muṅgw i haṛĕp sirāhalĕp acum nĕhĕṙ aṅarahakĕn lumampaha,
kĕṇḍaŋ goŋ muni t aṅkat aṅkat atĕṛĕḥ đwani nika kaṛĕṅö sakè yawa,
sakwèḥ niŋ maṅuṅaŋ paḍāṅĕnĕb ĕnĕb raras i hati nika n tumiṅhala*

:490:\:57:\:4:. maṅkat śrīndumatī garantuŋ ira muny asĕmu gula ǥināṣa riŋ waja,
rūm niŋ paṅlima muṅgu riŋ śrigaḍiŋ iŋ masa kalima tinū hanèŋ kapö,
Aṅlaṅwākĕn awaṙṇna kāṙtttika pamatnya gumuruḥ araras rinĕṅwakĕn,
lwiṙ tūban kumusuḥ kaṛĕṅwan i panĕmpuḥ ika kadi panĕmpuḥ iŋ jawuḥ*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:491:\:58:\:1:. rakryan putrī mijil kāƀinawa halĕp irāpūṙwwa saṅkèŋ kaḍatwan,
Aṅlīlāwās katon ƀūṣaṇa nira kumĕñaṙ lwiṙ panoliḥ hyaŋ aṙka,
Aṅhèṙ riŋ gopurāṅṛĕgṛĕg i pasalĕsĕk iŋ paṅhaṛĕp söḥ marampak,
sākṣāt saŋ hyaŋ wulan wāhu mĕtu riŋ udayādrīniriŋ niŋ grahākwèḥ*

:492:\:58:\:2:. mogāhyaŋ dè nirāmèt hayu mamulaṅunī budđi niŋ wwaŋ tumiṅhal,
hyaŋ śrī liṅnyè sirāṅiṇḍarat ahaṛĕp amètāśrayèŋ maṙttyaloka,
lèn tèkaŋ wwaŋ sumĕṅgaḥ ratiḥ i sira sakèŋ swaṙgga lāwan suraṣtrī,
ƀrantānĕṅgaḥ dwicandrāduluṙ i payuŋ irātyanta śudđa rwa sādĕg*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:493:\:59:\:1:. mènmèn rwaŋ siki wāhu rāgawaśa muṅgw i haṛĕp ira maṛĕk manimbaṅi,
hyaŋ niŋ gīta tĕkānurun kahiḍĕpanya ḍatĕŋ iniriŋ iŋ tabaŋ tabaŋ,
siṅhĕlnyāṙjja lawan sawitnya katiraḥ wĕlas aṛĕp awilĕt lawan gaḍuŋ,
tan pèndaḥ kadi nāgapāśa pamanaḥ niŋ Atanu karaṇanya lĕṅlĕṅa*

:494:\:59:\:2:. nyū dantākuniŋ aṅhapit gula gula lwiṙ ikaŋ amawa pawwahan gaḍiŋ,
tapwan wāla dahat rwa sādĕg abĕbĕd niyata kahiriṣan twas iŋ mulat,
tĕṅgĕknyāluŋ apiṇḍa kāṅinana polaḥ ika n asĕmu buṅkaḥ iŋ pupus,
Aṅhiŋ dyaḥ jayawaspa paṅhulu manisnya n anilihi mamaṅku pawwahan*

:495:\:59:\:3:. tan hawwan gati saŋ rarāhawu hawu wwaŋ ahayu tinuras raras nika,
lūd ƀasmāṅkura laṇḍa rakwa sira saŋ tuha tuha nika yan sakèŋ bibi,
solaḥ sèṅĕṙ ikāhaṅan gĕsĕŋ i pāmbĕkan ika tĕkap iŋ‌ smarānala,
yogyā kuṇḍaṅa niŋ manunwani pamiṅgiṙ amĕnĕma kaḍatwan iŋ musuḥ*

:496:\:59:\:4:. mopiḥ wahw amayaŋ mayaŋ ri hati niŋ mulat anĕku nĕku pralāpita,
tapwan rañca hatinya kèwala walĕlwan amagĕhakĕn iŋ kakanyakān,
kāsĕṅkanya piliḥ pucaŋ pucaṅan iŋ‌ smara rumimaṅa budđi niŋ kawi,
yogya n raṅkulĕn iŋ wanīŋ raṇa tĕṅahnya pasuṅakĕna sĕmba sĕmbahan*

:497:\:59:\:5:. tapwan wṛdđa dahat sirèña nira lāwan uwa nira paḍākurug miraḥ,
Èkĕl roma nirāṣĕlat huwan ikaŋ hayu tumalawuṅan turuŋ lĕwas,
luñcip niŋ kuku pantĕs aṅgṛĕmusa lagy aṅuluŋ uluṅi rāga niŋ mulat,
Èdran tiṅhal irèŋ saƀā baṅun anambĕra hinayamakĕn titik maṅö*

:498:\:59:\:6:. putrī niŋ kṙyyan anak wĕsi nṛĕpati rakwa kaka kaka nirānwam iŋ wayaḥ,
pantĕs tan pamikārakĕn hayu ṛĕṅunya muwuhi raras iŋ matāmanis,
lwiṙ hyaŋ hyaŋ tĕka tan hinundaŋ anurun sahana nika paḍāwulaŋ tatur,
kram niŋ sampiṙ i bāhu mās inapi molaḥ asĕmu hĕlaranya n aṅlayaŋ*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:499:\:60:\:1:. Ikaŋ mamawa kaṇḍi kaṇḍi rara wahw agĕluŋ ahayu poṣađan lulut,
lumut  lumut ikaŋ payođara wĕnaŋ paṅuwata sĕḍĕŋ iŋ jajāhĕnĕk,
pupuṙ nika wĕnaŋ paṅoṣađa pilĕg niŋ iruŋ apan arūm sakèŋ kapur,
lukaṙ karika kènya muꝁya pinakādi paṅuwata ri rāga niŋ rimaŋ*

:500:\:60:\:2:. wagĕd wagĕd ikāŋ añāmarani waṙgga pasisi salĕmaḥ lawan wukir,
sawaṙgga kalawan wulan muꝁa nikā kalĕṅĕṅan ika mitra niŋ cucur,
tĕṅahnya wahu wanwa riŋ jriŋ aṅĕliḥ wahu waśa riŋ aśokapādapa,
sasīma kalawan mayūra gĕluṅanya wĕka niŋ asanākadaŋ patĕr*

:501:\:60:\:3:. kunaŋ saŋ apahidwan èṅas ahaṅan pawulatan i manahnya riŋ saƀā,
sĕkaṙ nika pinintakāsihakĕn iŋ kawi huwus aṅikĕt hañaṙ tĕka,
kisapwakĕna riŋ prawīra kahalĕp nika suṅana sĕpaḥ sakè waja,
kayogyan i laṭinya yan kadi duḥ iŋ wwaḥ ika sĕsĕpĕn iŋ priyātalĕḥ*

:502:\:60:\:4:. Anak wĕsi narèndra rakwa raṣikā saŋ amawa curigāraras dahat,
Aroma maṅunĕŋ galuḥ kahiḍĕpanya n apaṅawaka patṛĕm uttama,
Ikaŋ wwaŋ araṅin winèḥ curiga kadga sinĕpuhan apan wagĕd waśi,
wajanya mamiraḥ tĕkè gusi gusinya halis ika tĕkāmraŋ iŋ mulat*

:503:\:60:\:5:. Ikaŋ wwaŋ aṅagĕm curik pinakapaṅruhun aduluṙ aṛĕs twas iŋ mulat,
Asiṅhĕl akaluŋ kṛtāṙŧa riŋ ayun pinakapaṅisi niŋ wanīŋ raṇa,
surakṣaka kaƀīnna ƀīnna baṅun antaka mapupul ahöm aṅiṇḍarat,
winaswas asipattra sālas asĕwö kṛtala curiga tomarāluṅid*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:504:\:61:\:1:. wwaŋ wwaŋ kasturi sāri niŋ kusuma rūpa saŋ aṅiriŋ inuttamāhayu,
mèww iww ātap awaṙṇna kuntul aṅusī pasisi kakilatan hanèŋ tawaŋ,
yadyastun tulisĕn samaṅkana pirāwig awiga nika yan hanèŋ yaśa,
ṅhiŋ ganya n drawanĕn manisnya niyatanya tumuluy atĕmaḥ tasik mađu*

:505:\:61:\:2:. laslāsan ‌wruḥ iŋ iṅgitāṅinakanèŋ mulat ahayu puji n pakawwaṅan,
yan tiṅhal kadi tiṅhal iŋ cala calāṛĕṅu ṛĕṅu sahajāpuput guyu,
nistanya n kadi pāwak iŋ mađu manisnya raras ika kadi ṅṛĕs iŋ hati,
tan paṅgintiṙ i rūm nirāṣĕmu jamuṙ hapa hapa maṛĕk iŋ jamuṙ wulan*

:506:\:61:\:3:. dènyāṅlaṅkahakĕn sukunya kadi tan lĕpasa tĕkap i lon ikaŋ laku,
mĕñcuḥ mĕñcuḥ aṅambĕk ambĕki pupūnya hana bĕnĕṙ adĕgnya pèt ulaḥ,
kahyun hyun laris iŋ wĕtis tan alaris laku nika minahā hinèrakĕn,
Aṅjiṅjiŋ sasisiḥ mĕluk tuṙ ika mātra wagĕd aniru lampaḥ iŋ tulis*

:507:\:61:\:4:. strī strī saƀya wicakṣaṇānagara nora kakuraŋ ika pantĕs iŋ saƀā,
kady ānaṇḍuṅakĕn rwi dè nika lumampaḥ aṛĕṅu sahajāṅhĕmu guyu,
Èñjuḥ prāya nika n wulat riŋ aṅuṅaŋ tan ahulap atawĕŋ tawĕŋ taṅan,
tan pèndaḥ salukat jajaṙ gĕluŋ ikā lukaṙ i jaja tinumbakan susu*

:508:\:61:\:5:. kady aṅrakṣa hayunya rūpa nika dè ni galak i pamatanya yan wulat,
hrū nīruṅnya lanā katon amatitis pamarayaŋ i halisnya lot mayat,
waṙṇnākāra nikaŋ wajākṛĕp asinaŋ gusi gusi nika kèsisan laṭi,
Ahrit wit ni susunya tĕkwan aluṅid paḍa paḍa kadi suṅga niŋ jaja*

<suwaṅśapattra> ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏓

:509:\:62:\:1:. tucapa tikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan wagĕd aṅucap ucap,
liŋ ika suputrikā pinakaratna winuni ri dalĕm,
saŋ Aja sujanma mās kinĕmit iŋ nagara wahu tĕka,
saꝑala sira n humambanakĕnè narapatiduhitā*

:510:\:62:\:2:. nṛpatanayā katon wĕdi nira n mulat i para ratu,
yadin alupa ŋ śarīra sira mūṙcꞓita lumaya kawĕs,
hulĕsana tan bawaŋ jasunanè sĕḍĕŋ ira kapati,
niyata sirāṅliliṙ saŋ Aja saṇḍiṅakĕna ri jaja*

:511:\:62:\:3:. narapatiputrikā n gĕluṅa niŋ wwaŋ anaṅis i ṭikā,
saŋ Aja paṅisya mon sira wirāga sadaka pasaji,
Aŧawa yadin padadyana sipat narapatitanayā,
nṛpasuta dè nira n gagaṅa mon pusuḥ usapa mata*

:512:\:62:\:4:. sĕkara niŋ aṅhiḍĕp‌ smara kunaŋ narapatitanaya,
saꝑala n apallawāmbĕt i tĕṅaḥ narapatiduhitā,
nṛpawaraputrikā n sĕkara dè nira kumuda paḍa,
saŋ Aja niśākarā nira maran patĕmu paḍa lĕṅĕŋ*

:513:\:62:\:5:. para ratu tan padon pisaniṅū sira kahaṛĕpana,
tuhu sira śakti wāni paḍa tan hana kakuraŋ ira,
ndan atiśaya praƀāwa saŋ Ajādƀuta kagiri giri,
Asana lawan wuṅū paḍa nira ndya ta huṛĕn i rika*

:514:\:62:\:6:. nahan ucapanya yan dinuluran ṛĕṅu saha kujiwat,
waja nika tan wĕnaŋ winuni kèṅis amuhara raras,
wĕkasan anagwa nagwakĕn i rowaŋ ika ri saŋ Aja,
cinalukakĕn mahāpicala haṙṣa riŋ ujaṙ ajuwĕt*

:515:\:62:\:7:. hana ta muwaḥ sira kṙyyan apupul pupul ahayu raras,
walu walu saŋ lumaḥ ry anu patibrata lumaku wiku,
paṅawaśa niŋ nwam iŋ wayaḥ agatgat asalaha jamaŋ,
hana sĕmu niŋ manaḥ maru marun mulat i nṛpasuta*

:516:\:62:\:8:. hana wahu wahw anūt karakĕtan siliḥ asiḥ akuṛĕn,
nṛpaduhitā kahèwa nika mĕṅgĕp aṅalĕm aṅupĕt,
tuhu tuhu yan latā paḍa ni budđi nika kadi nadī,
cumulu culuḥ priyanya pamawanya lulut i saŋ Aja*

:517:\:62:\:9:. rara ri widaṙƀarājya makamuꝁya nṛpatitanayā,
paḍa kĕna rāga rāga nika tībra lumuŋ aṅalayan,
humañutakĕn lulut lulut unĕṅnya mara ri saŋ Aja,
bisa sira tan tĕñuḥ rinĕbut iŋ turida sanagara*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:518:\:63:\:1:. Osik budđi nikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan tucapa sira narèndrakanyakā,
sāmpun prāpta ri mađya niŋ pagĕlaran para ratu kĕna rāga dè nira,
Akwèḥ ƀāwa nira n wimūṙcꞓita hanan maṅuwahi makuṭa ndatan tulus,
dudw āƀāwaka kady awèḥ sĕpaḥ aƀāwaka kadi tinĕwĕk miṅè midĕm*

:519:\:63:\:2:. lèn taŋ tībra lulut nirè nṛpasutā humiḍĕp awak irāṅisapwakĕn,
dè niŋ rāgawaśāmarājaya tĕkāmulaṅuni ya tinūtnya yan rimaŋ,
ṅhiŋ kāmīraṣa lot ginoṣṫi nira ramya lawan ikaŋ amaṅku pawwahan,
mogāṅdè tutuṙ iŋ gula drawa kaṛĕṅwan i wacana nirānamaṙ juruḥ*

:520:\:63:\:3:. Ambĕk ni ṅhulun iŋ rarāhayu lawan lituhayu sawawān apaṅgiha,
ndan maṙmmanya n atĕmwa dūta lĕpihan piṛĕsĕpakĕna riŋ pralāpita,
Āpan tan hana raśmi niŋ winaraŋ iŋ wwaŋ atuha tuna dè nikālaṅö,
ṅhiŋ ganđaṙwwawiwāha ramya katigāmawa sĕṛĕḥ amisāta riŋ pasir*

:521:\:63:\:4:. luṅhāhĕmbana putra putran ika gantin aṛĕk aṛĕkanèŋ paraṙyyanan,
liṅlīṅĕn kisapun kudaŋ  kudaṅĕn iŋ kakawin uliḥ iŋ aṅdadak dadak,
yadyan māliha riŋ wukiṙ sipi laṅönya winulatan awikwa wikwana,
Aṅhiŋ gīta panĕmba nĕmbaha nika n huwus inuƀaya mantukèŋ bibi*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓

:522:\:64:\:1:. nāhan liŋ nira n aṅlipuṙ lipurakĕn kiṅkiŋ nirè twas nira,
kāsiḥ kāsiḥ irāṅlawan lawani goṣṫy āpan huwus ‌wruḥ kawi,
wwaŋ śṛṅgāra wicakṣaṇāṅrahati sojaṙṇnyān asiḥ saŋ praƀu,
pèt pèt haṙṣa sahuṙṇnya rāgakaraṇa ‌wruḥ riŋ kasöṅan‌ smara*

:523:\:64:\:2:. yan kanyā ri hiḍĕp patik haji hadè kahyūnanāpan raray,
tonĕn dè nṛpati ndya taŋ mađukarā hānè kucup niŋ sĕkar,
lāwan yan lĕwasa ŋ rarāpa pakĕnanyāpan lĕwas riŋ raras,
paṅliṅganya sĕkaṙ lĕwas pisaniṅū kumbaŋ marāṅambuṅa*

:524:\:64:\:3:. saṅkṣèpanya sĕḍĕŋ rarā bwatana kiṅkiŋ hundaṅĕn riŋ ṭikā,
maṅgĕḥ dè niŋ aṅolakĕn tĕṅaḥ ikā sāmpun pinaṅkw āṅliga,
kady aṅgān i sĕkaṙ nikāŋ asana yan mĕmbaŋ katampwan riris,
ṅkāna ŋ ṣaṭpada miwya yan ƀramara saṅjñānya n jĕnĕk tan midĕr*

:525:\:64:\:4:. nāhan dènya n apèt sahuṙ mĕtu raraṣnya n pāwak iŋ rāṣika,
tambā niŋ rimaŋ aṅlawaŋ lawaṅi kuŋ pèt rāga dènyāṅucap,
lwiṙ truḥ niŋ mađumāsa kāraṇa ni kiṅkiŋ śrī narèndrāṣĕwö,
mambö kèn lukaṙ iŋ tilam sahuṙ irātuṅtuŋ rum iŋ saṅgama*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:526:\:65:\:1:. kanyā liṅta hadè kahaṙṣana paḍanya salaga kapana n kakūṅana,
kuŋ jaṅgāṅalayan taŧāpi kapana n pamilĕta raras iŋ rara n lĕwas,
dṛṣṭāntanya sĕkaṙ lĕwas riŋ apa rakwa wulatana mĕnè n kasumpiṅa,
kiṅkiŋ tībra yan iŋ sĕḍĕŋ rara raraṣnya paḍa paḍa lawan jraḥ iŋ sĕkar*

:527:\:65:\:2:. yèkā tèka hadè paṅa‌wruhana campaka salaga nika n kinahyunan,
yadyan sumpiṅa niŋ maṅālihi hulĕs lĕwu raras ika yan pagantyana,
mambö rūmnya hanèŋ karaŋ hulu taṅan turaḥ ika rumĕsĕp tĕkè hati,
haṙyyan tan hana haṙṣa ni ṅwaŋ i sĕkaṙṇnya puru puru ṛĕmĕk katiṇḍihan*

:528:\:65:\:3:. yan laywan pakasumpiṅĕn hana raraṣnya tuhun asĕpi solaḥ iŋ lĕwas,
tĕkwan rakwa ꝑalanya moǥa pinalaywan asiŋ amupu luṅṣuran sĕkar,
dènya n mantĕna rūmnya yan pakirim iŋ wwaŋ ahayu panuwal nikā ṭikā,
Ambönya n huwus aṅharas pipi ya tāṛĕk aṛĕkana waṅinya kuṇḍaṅĕn*

:529:\:65:\:4:. mwaŋ yan‌ strī hucapĕn raraṣnya paḍa ta pwa kahaṛĕpana tan tayākĕna,
rūmrūm niŋ rara kanyakā kadi saroruha kumuḍu mijil sakèŋ bañu,
himpĕṙ paṅkaja kaṙyyakan wahu mĕkaṙ pamĕwĕḥ i raras iŋ sĕḍĕŋ rara,
tan pèndaḥ śatapattra wāhu lĕwas iŋ talaga hayu nikaŋ rara n lĕwas*

:530:\:65:\:5:. kanyā ta pwa wiśèṣa riŋ pawaraṅan raras ika marumaḥ lawan riris,
Antuk niŋ maṅalap kasoṙ karaṇa niŋ tinarima maṛĕkāṅaras pipi,
riŋ paṅkwan winaraḥ riŋ akṣara manaḥ wahu tama wahu wanwa koluyan,
Āŋ aḥ wus kaka liṅnya moǥa kawatĕk ri sĕḍĕŋ ika kinèwalānukĕr*

:531:\:65:\:6:. yadyan rowaṅa niŋ maṅaṙwwani hĕnū rumasa raṣana ramya niŋ kapat,
byaktālona lakunya sotan ika tan tahu mahās ahas aṅṛĕṅö gĕṛĕḥ,
tapwan wanwa dahat tuhun ṛĕṅu nikāmarahakĕn i haṛĕpnya hĕmbanĕn,
suṇḍaŋ suṇḍaṅĕn iŋ tĕgal payuṅanāsana hari harin iŋ paraṙyyanan*

:532:\:65:\:7:. tan gyā gyākĕna dè nikā lumaku mon kaririṣana ri mađya niŋ tĕgal,
yan paṅdöla paran kunaŋ wĕnaŋ akona pituhun ika yan lumampaha,
solahnyèriṅanāpa tan wuruṅa luhnya patulaka nikā yadin kĕdön,
ṅhiŋ gānya nya lumampaha n hana gĕṛĕḥ maṅarahakĕna kāla niŋ ṛĕmĕŋ*

:533:\:65:\:8:. ndan yan ramya nikaŋ sĕḍĕŋ rara kapiŋ rwa niŋ arabi ṛĕsĕp twas iŋ mulat,
kas kas pādapa kāṅinan kas i tĕṅahnya kinayuḥ aṅĕliḥ wawaŋ tumūt,
mwaŋ twasnyāṅasanāṅṛĕṅö patĕṙ adan mĕkara hinudanan karāṣikan,
kady amṛĕm kalawan puḍak ṅwaŋ aṅisapwakĕn ariṣi kanin ragĕt ragĕt*

:534:\:65:\:9:. yadyan rowaṅa niŋ lumampaḥ anukū sapara paran iŋ aṅraraḥ musuḥ,
śođāta pwa hayunya nora kakuraṅnya mata waja nikā paḍānulus,
mambö wīra raras raraṣnya tĕkap iŋ hañaŋ aṅiriŋ akālihan tapiḥ,
pantĕs pantĕs anuṅgaṅèŋ śakaṭa pamṛĕgakĕna kahalĕpnya riŋ hĕnu*

:535:\:65:\:10:. Aśrī raśmi nikaŋ rarā tuha kapiŋ tiga niŋ arabi mon kapiŋ pata,
prāyāsiḥ wilaja n kinolakĕn anaṅgap i waja nika yan winèḥ sĕpaḥ,
dūrāṅṛĕṅwana yan kisapwakĕna riŋ śayana pisaniṅūn apaṅgila,
Èṅgal wanwa wisik pisan kadi sadoṣa ginupi tumuluy kataṅgama*

:536:\:65:\:11:. yogya n rowaṅa niŋ licin wanawasānusupa ri pasamūha niŋ sĕkar,
kuṇḍaŋ kuṇḍaṅa niŋ mahās mahās atīṙŧa riŋ acala mahārakā gaḍuŋ,
līlānaṇḍaṅa walkalājaṙ ajarānalawaha jawuḥ iŋ labuḥ kapat,
śrī rājādayitā pi yogya ṅaranya n aduluṙ anusup lawan ratu*

:537:\:65:\:12:. nāhan dè nira nāŧa mojaṙ apadudwan ulaḥ ulaḥ ira n paḍālulut,
budđi śrī naranāŧaputra milu rañca ri wulat ira riŋ nṛpātmajā,
mūṙcꞓāpan wahu wahw anon rakĕt aṅiṇḍarat anĕmu ṭikā tĕkālulut,
paŋ niŋ kūŋ asĕwö wilāpa kakawin tinama tama nirè dalĕm hati*

:538:\:65:\:13:. rakryan‌ ṅkè kahananku māsku mapa hètu niŋ asĕmu wiwal salaḥ wulat,
Ahyun suṅṣuṅĕn i ṅhulun karika māsku karaṇa niŋ aṛĕṅwa pèt ulaḥ,
Om om haywa miṅè nihan‌ ṅhulun amaṅkwakĕna ri kita milw aḍampana,
taṅgap māsku sĕpahku sāmpun amiraḥ rumĕsĕpakĕna rāga ni ṅhulun*

:539:\:65:\:14:. dyaḥ saŋ sāgara katruhan luḥ apasiṙ panĕpi saŋ ahĕnī hĕnī pupur,
muṅgw ī jro hati kuṅta māsku kapana n rwaba sumapatanè kuŋ i ṅhulun,
Ambĕk ni ṅhulun amriḥ aṅlayari tan wĕdi kajahata kombakan halis,
swaṙggāku n kaṛĕmèŋ tĕṅahta suꝁa kapṛĕma kapaguta riŋ karaŋ susu*

:540:\:65:\:15:. rakryan saŋ mađu niŋ kaḍatwan uliḥ iŋ hyaŋ amituruni sāri niŋ sĕkar,
lwiṙ tawwan pakatonan iŋ kaka kakāṅrubuŋ ahayu paḍāṅisis wĕtis,
dè niŋ hyunku tumon manista n agĕlaŋ gupura maṇi duwĕg pakolihĕn,
ndak lampū pĕtĕŋ iŋ mulat sakahananta ri dalĕm ibu rohĕn i ṅhulun*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:541:\:66:\:1:. ndaḥ nāhan liŋ narèndrātmaja ri hati nirāpan sira ƀrāntacitta,
rakryan putrī marè śrī magađapati pĕnuḥ wwaŋ manonton marè jro,
Awṛĕg dè saŋ sunandā kadi lanaŋ aṅusī sāhasānĕmbuŋ iŋ hwī,
ramyāwèlā katon riŋ wĕkasan aṅililan śrī suputrī tinonton*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:542:\:67:\:1:. mojaṙ śrī magađāđipè nṛpasutā nihan ibu maṛĕkākisapwana,
socaṅkw ību lawan matanta sakadaŋ paḍa paḍa dadi niŋ gula drawa,
Atyantèbu hayunta tan patatalan tuhu tuhu n awatāra niŋ ratiḥ,
hèman māsku yatan papaṅgiha lawan‌ ṅhulun apan awatāra niŋ‌ smara*

:543:\:67:\:2:. ‌wruḥ ku n tan hana sanmatanta hana duṣṭa maṛĕki ri kitāmadohakĕn,
tonton dènta matanta mĕṅgĕp amanis dumadak aṛĕṅu yan tumon‌ ṅhulun,
paṅron wimba nikuŋ halista n abĕnĕṙ kuṭila milu ri tuṅtuŋ iŋ hiḍĕp,
tan saṅkèŋ hana doṣa kimburu manahta tĕka wiwal apèda ri ṅhulun*

:544:\:67:\:3:. rakryan janma ni janma ni ṅhulun adadyana ratu tumutèŋ swayambara,
ndan rakryan ta muwaḥ swayambarakĕnāmiliha ratu ri mađya niŋ saƀā,
dènya n tan kinasanmatanta palalun sinalahasa ri tan siḥ iŋ wiđi,
ramya ṅwaŋ pinagantakĕn tulusa tan tulusa tuwi yayāpuput raras*

:545:\:67:\:4:. nāhan dè magađèśwarāṅucap arūm amalaṙ i sahura nṛĕpātmajā,
śrī dèwīndumatī tan èṅĕḥ apa tan hana manaḥ ira kèṅĕrè sira,
maṙmma śrī naranāŧa mantĕn aṅucap tĕhĕṙ amaḍĕm ikaŋ‌ smarè hati,
‌wruḥ ri wyaṙŧa ni kuŋ nirè nṛpasutā n kadi wiꝑala niŋ ahyun iŋ tulis*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:546:\:68:\:1:. ndaḥ mojaṙ saŋ sunandā ri narapatisutā liṅnya tiṅhal tuhanku,
nāhan ta śrī mahārāja magađapati saŋ yogya pètĕn siwinta,
yadyastun sidđa rakryan sasisihana hulĕs dlāha lāwan narèndra,
sakwèḥ niŋ‌ strī hanè jro nagara niyata tan sāha saṅkè padanta*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:547:\:69:\:1:. sugyan tan ‌wruha māsku yan śrī magađèśwara sira maṅaran parantapa,
sāmpun śīṙṇna musuḥ nirāwṛĕg i kaḍatwan ika mati ri mađya niŋ raṇa,
Aṅhiŋ pat lima śèṣa niŋ karahatan paḍa kawĕkas anūt marè sira,
saṅkṣèpanya yaŧāṙtta māsku sira yan prakaśita maṅaran parantapa*

:548:\:69:\:2:. yan riŋ wīṙyya lawan guṇa syapa sirāṅlĕwihana sira yan paḍa praƀu,
waḥ riŋ mās maṇik uttama ndya ŋ adagaŋ lumĕwihana sira n đanèśwara,
sāmpun pūṙṇna kadānaśūran ira kaprakaśita tĕka riŋ purāntara,
ṅhiŋ putrī kakuraŋ ni ǥāra nira hètu niŋ aṅadu ri māskw aṅĕdwakĕn*

:549:\:69:\:3:. wwantĕn dèśa lĕṅĕŋ ri puṣpapura ƀūmi nṛpati pasamūhan iŋ kawi,
luḥ niŋ‌ strī kĕna rāga rakwa talaganya pinarigi ri laywan iŋ gĕluŋ,
sambatnya n panaṅis ya tāṅdadi mađubrata hana dadi cātakèŋ tawaŋ,
mambö rūm ni muꝁanya sāmpun atĕmaḥ kumuda mĕkaṙ i tambwaŋ iŋ wulan*

:550:\:69:\:4:. ṅkā tènduŋ parananta māmĕŋ amĕŋ an huwus atĕmu lawan narèśwara,
ƀuktin siḥ nira dènta ramya niŋ atuntunan aduluṙ akālihan payuŋ,
yèkā wīṙyya ṅaranya riŋ kadi kitāhayu pinuji yan amriḥ iŋ priya,
ramyāṅaṙwwana ḍampa riŋ para paran sipi wanĕḥ iŋ akālihan tilam*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– |– ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:551:\:70:\:1:. nāhan liŋ saŋ sunandāmanis araras arūm dè nikākon atĕmwa,
sāmpun kājaṙ pratāpa nṛĕpati lawan ikaŋ wīṙyya sāmpun tiniṅkaḥ,
ndātan mlècꞓā suputrī n inucapan aṅucap lèn sakè saŋ narèndra,
mogāsuṅṣut mĕnè n ahyuna kinĕdĕ kĕdö kèwalādoḥ riŋ ambĕk*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:552:\:71:\:1:. śrī dèwīndumatī katon sĕmu ni budđi nira n alalisè narèśwara,
Āpan tan hana raśmi raśmi ni wulat nira pinaṛĕkakĕn wawaŋ miṅè,
yèkā hètu nira n kinon aṅalihāmwita rumuhun anĕmbahè sira,
mambĕt mađya nirāṅgaluṅgaŋ i panĕmbaḥ ira kadi panĕmbaḥ iŋ tulis*

:553:\:71:\:2:. ry aṅkat śrī nṛpaputrikā śrī magađèśwara kawĕlas aṛĕp kamānuṣan,
maṙyy ātèja sĕpaḥ nirāṣĕpa sigit sigitan ira tibākusèŋ lĕmaḥ,
tan śoƀākilayū wulat nira sĕkaṙ nira maṅaway awè hanèŋ kapö,
tṛṣṇā kūŋ ira tan katoliḥ inatīta nĕhĕṙ inilagan yayan tumūt*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓

:554:\:72:\:1:. śrī dèwīndumatī lumampaḥ aṅĕliḥ prāptè saŋ Aṅgāđipa,
ndātan wany asaƀāhaliŋ haliṅan iŋ cèṭī paḍākwèḥ maṛĕk,
tan saḥ dyaḥ jayawaspa lot linihaṅan bāhunya kaṙwwāwiḍaŋ,
Āpan kāsiḥ irālawas tuwin arūm tan soṙ dahat riŋ hayu*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:555:\:73:\:1:. Agyā ŋ budđi saŋ Aṅganāŧa ri ḍatĕŋ nṛpawaraduhitā marè sira,
mojaṙ tan panahānĕkākĕn i lulut lulut ira ri narèśwarātmajā,
ṅkè rakryan mapa hètu niŋ kadi wiwal mulat ariris apakṣa maṅṣula,
hāḥ wāliṅku tĕkākisapwana kita n tĕka dumadak adoḥ tĕka ŋ tamuy*

:556:\:73:\:2:. Antĕnku n tuna kapwa sihta winaliṅku tumuta saparanku tan saha,
māskwi induŋ‌ ndi wĕkas ni kuṅta palakuṅkwa hurupĕn i lara priḥ i ṅhulun,
rāganta mwaŋ unĕṅku dènya n ahurup tali paṅuwata kiṅkiŋ i ṅhulun,
wèt niŋ tan hana sanmatanta palaṛĕṅkwa karika karaṇanta tan sahur*

:557:\:73:\:3:. dyaḥ saŋ haṙṣa piniṇḍa ratnawanitāṅaraṅa karaṇa niŋ lanā lulut,
saŋ kiṅkiŋ ginawè rarāhayu sujanma karaṇa niŋ akuŋ tumon kita,
saŋ rāgānala maṅdadi wwaŋ amanas manasi hati kita n kinonĕṅan,
saŋ ṛĕs maṅdadi janma rājaduhitāmuhara wĕdi niŋ ahyunè kita*

:558:\:73:\:4:. nāhan dè nira mojaṙ aṅṛĕsi hatīniṅĕt iṅĕt apa tan kinahyunan,
hèman wīṙyya nira mwaŋ uttama ni kapraƀun ira suyaśādƀutèŋ jagat,
riŋ rūpāsĕmu rūpa niŋ‌ smara sawaṙgga lawan asana riŋ labuḥ kapat,
tan kèwö wiꝑalaprayāsa hana tan pinakadi kadi kambaŋ iŋ caru*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓

:559:\:74:\:1:. mantĕn śrī naranāŧa mojaṙ irikā ta dyaḥ sunandāṅucap,
liṅnya dyahku haṛĕp kita ‌wruha ri pāwak niŋ gĕṛĕḥ niŋ kapat,
nāhan māsku saŋ Aṅganāŧa pahawās gĕntĕṙ madadyan ratu,
yogyātĕmwa lawan kitā kita tĕmaḥ niŋ cātakāmèt jawuḥ*

:560:\:74:\:2:. ṅkānè rājya saŋ Aṅganāŧa wĕkas iŋ ramyè huwus niŋ laga,
ry antuk saŋ praƀu maṅlurug saha bala lwiṙ waḥ sakèŋ paṙwwata,
gĕntĕṙ niŋ grit ikaŋ raŧānĕmahākĕn kuŋ ni wwaŋ iŋ kāṙtttika,
luḥ niŋ‌ strī kahañaŋ ri līna ni ratunyāṅdè paḍĕt niŋ lĕbū*

:561:\:74:\:3:. ndan hèman tuna rājalakṣmi satĕwĕknya n rājya niṙddèwatī,
hètu śrī naranāŧa tan‌ sŧiti pijĕṙ luṅhā madèwāśraya,
dè niŋ hyūn ira n aṅhyaṅa ŋ nagara moǥa n kèwĕhan tan hana,
ṅhiŋ rakryan pakarājalakṣmi nira maṙmma dè nirāṅundaṅa*

:562:\:74:\:4:. rakryan yan hana sanmatanta ri sirānambāna kiṅkiŋ nira,
ndak pinta nya sĕkaṙ tajinta pamahugya mwaŋ sĕṛĕḥ riŋ kajaŋ,
taṅgap dènta mĕnè sĕpaḥ nira katon hèman yatan suṅṣuṅĕn,
nya ŋ siṅhāsana kaṙwwananta pakisapwan māskwi i paṅkwan haji*

:563:\:74:\:5:. nāhan dènya n aṅĕdwakĕn nṛpasutāhyun waspadè saŋ praƀu,
mogācūm araṛĕm wulat nira sinuṅṣuŋ riŋ wulat löṙ miṅè,
ndan dūrāhyuna kèwalāwĕdi kumöl ambĕk nirāṅdoḥ aṛĕs,
yan tiṅhal kadi tiṅhal iŋ mulat iŋ aṙccāṅhèṙ iŋ uṅgwan ƀaya*

:564:\:74:\:6:. māliḥ śrīndumatī riniṅriŋ inariḥ dè saŋ sunandāmawa,
Āśāƀūta saŋ Aṅganāŧa ri layad dèwī nĕhĕṙ tan waluy,
dè niŋ ƀrānta nirāṅikĕt raṣa palambaŋ paṅlipuṙ luḥ pinöm,
ṅkānè watwan ikaŋ salö panulisan maṙmmā raṣanyāmanis*

:565:\:74:\:7:. rakryan saŋ maliŋ iŋ matāmatik i rūpaṅkw āṅĕḍap yan wulat,
kālap dènta manahku mĕṅgĕp amanis rūpanta duṣṭèŋ hati,
mukṣa twaskwi i sĕḍĕṅta mūṙ syapa ta lèn saṅkè kitāṅambila,
Èman māsku tuhan tuhan maliŋ atimpuḥ duṙyyaśakṣatriya*

:566:\:74:\:8:. rakryan haywa kita pramāda ri surup niŋ lèk mĕnè riŋ wĕṅi,
prāptāmora kakanta haywa kita tan yatnā ry awaktèŋ jinĕm,
sāk niŋ kèn awanaṅkwa mañjiŋ i parāhasyanta riŋ pamṛĕman,
maṅgā matya matāku pökana kukuṅku n paṅguhā riŋ pupū*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:567:\:75:\:1:. nahan raṣa ni dè nirāhyun amaliŋ maliṅana ri raras suputrikā,
Agöŋ suꝁa nira n tibā manaḥ i saŋ katuduḥ aruṣita pwa riŋ manaḥ,
ri kāpusan ikaŋ‌ smarāpunagi yan waluyana sira dè nṛpātmajā,
lumakwa mapasaŋ pasaŋ wuyaha yan muliḥ iriŋ iriṅĕn marè dalĕm*

:568:\:75:\:2:. Atīta sira saŋ narèndra maṅaraŋ tucapa sira narèndrakanyakā,
sinuṇḍaŋ inamĕṙ kininkin aṅĕliḥ raṣa tumayuṅa kabwatan raras,
tuwin manaḥ ira n prapañca kumĕtĕṙ hati nira mulat iŋ wwaŋ iŋ saƀā,
baṅun lumaku ri wwat èwĕḥ alĕyö maṅamĕṙ amĕṙ i dè nira n laku*

:569:\:75:\:3:. sahaṙṣa saŋ Awantināŧa ri ḍatĕŋ saŋ ahayu pinakahyaŋ iŋ saƀā,
hanan pasiḍakĕp hanan pasidĕhāṅuraḥ ariḥ ulaḥ iŋ girahyasĕn,
waḥ iŋ kapitu tan pahī wĕtu ni rāga nira ri naranāŧaputrikā,
pĕnuḥ maṅarapè tĕkèŋ kaka kakānwam atuha sinarambahan lulut*

:570:\:75:\:4:. I maṅkana ni dè nira n karakĕtan turida sinaput iŋ manoƀawa,
tan ènak aṅinaŋ tan ènak aṅucap humĕnĕŋ apĕga ta n sayāwĕnĕs,
sawèt i pamanas nikaŋ madanabahni ri hati nira maṅkin aṅlarè,
ya kāraṇa nirāṅucap tan awiraŋ sumĕgĕ sĕgĕḥ i saŋ nṛpātmajā*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:571:\:76:\:1:. rakryan ƀāgya kita n ḍatĕŋ nihan aluṅguha yayi ri kisapwan i ṅhulun,
mās lāwan maṇik uttamāṙjja humaḍaŋ pakĕna nika panumbasè kita,
yadyan kapraƀun i ṅhulun suṅakĕnaṅkwa ri kita yayi yan kitāhaṛĕp,
yan praŋ yan kakawin panĕkwa ni kakanta ri kita yayi yann apaṅgiha*

:572:\:76:\:2:. yan riŋ kāṙtttikamāsa ramya masa ni ṅhulun amĕŋ amĕŋ iŋ pasiṙ wukir,
kuṇḍaŋ kuṇḍaṅĕn i ṅhulun kita mulat mulata ri kakawinku riŋ yaśa,
yan māsāsujimāsa ramya masa ni ṅhulun amĕnĕm i rājya niŋ musuḥ,
kuṇḍaŋ kuṇḍaṅa ni ṅhulun kita mulat mulata ri kawaninku riŋ raṇa*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓

:573:\:77:\:1:. nāhan dè naranāŧa mojaṙ araras mambö laṅö niŋ jinĕm,
siṅgiḥ yan pracacaḥ karas waśa ri tuṅtuŋ niŋ tanaḥ riŋ kapö,
siŋ soṅkab ni tutuk nirāwĕtu laṅö kāmīraṣāpèt manis,
pöḥ niŋ haṙṣa pinöm atūt guru laǥunyāṙjjāṅĕnoḥ lambaṅa*

:574:\:77:\:2:. saŋ katwaŋ niŋ awaṙṇna campaka tumiṅhal sakṣaṇè saŋ praƀu,
cèṣṭākāra nirènariḥ winulatan dè saŋ sunandātaña,
māskwi induŋ mapa budđi rakryan i narèndra n swāmya rakryan sira,
yogyāpan kadi mūla tuṅgal apasaḥ maṅkè n tĕmaḥ mānuṣa*

<Upèndrabajra> ⏑– ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓

:575:\:78:\:1:. yadin kitātĕmwa lawan narèndra,
ry Awantidèśātiśayèŋ suƀikṣa,
wwaŋ uttama wwaṅnya kawīṅgitajña,
pacaṅkramānanta pasiṙ wukiṙṇnya*

:576:\:78:\:2:. gunuŋ mahākāla ṅaranya ramya,
kapunpunan dè saŋ Awantināŧa,
I pāṙśwa pāṙśwanya patīṙŧa tīṙŧan,
pĕnuḥ dwijaṙṣy ājaṙ ajaṙ tan imbā*

:577:\:78:\:3:. saƀā ƀaṭārèśwara nityakāla,
śiwāmƀa sakwèḥ ni bañunya śudđa,
kulĕm pwa saŋ hyaŋ tuwi kṛṣṇapakṣa,
yayāpaḍaŋ dè nikaŋ aṙdđacandra*

:578:\:78:\:4:. paran tatan ramya nikā parāna,
pamènanè kāla nikaŋ basanta,
Ikaŋ larāgöŋ mala niŋ śarīra,
Awās hilaŋ māṙyy aṅawèśa dènya*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:579:\:79:\:1:. tāman saŋ nāŧa tan popama halĕp ika sāmpun prakāśādwitīya,
piṅgiṙ niŋ lwaḥ sṛĕp ātis ny aṅin ika humaras ganđa niŋ paṅkaja mrik,
sākṣāt swaṙggātmakāpan sahana hana nikaŋ kĕmbaŋ aṅjraḥ paḍārūm,
hèman yan lèna saṅkè kita śaraṇa ni kādèwatanya n pinūjā*

:580:\:79:\:2:. nāhan dè saŋ sunandāmiṛĕsĕpakĕn i saŋ yogya kaṙmmā sudèwī,
ndān ambĕk śrī suputrī miṅay atimĕs adoḥ tan hana ŋ rāga mātra,
sāmpun ‌wruḥ saŋ sunandā karaṇa nika n akon muṅṣirè saŋ pratīpa,
Asṛĕt lampaḥ nirālon laku laku jaladānūtakĕn mārutālon*

:581:\:79:\:3:. ndan saŋ kāṙyy āṅaraŋ sis kawĕlas aṛĕp irāmèri luḥ tan tinoliḥ,
baṙyyan tiṅhal ri dèwī sira raṣa pĕjahāpan ṛĕmĕk twas nira syuḥ,
limbè limbè sudèwī kadi maṅaway akon milwa ri śrī narèndra,
wèt niŋ ƀrāntāṅikĕt ƀāṣa ri saruṅan ikaŋ patṛĕm aṅṛĕs raṣanya*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:582:\:80:\:1:. ṅhulun yaśana rāga māsku pakađaṙmman ĕnahana raras niŋ aṅṛĕṅiḥ,
hayunta makawāṇḍiranya ya paṅöbana para paranaṅkwa yan rimaŋ,
praṣĕnta ri dalĕm jinĕm titisananta luḥ i lukaṙ i kènta riŋ tilam,
susunta pakasāđananta kalawan pipi katiga tĕṅaḥ maran lĕpas*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:583:\:81:\:1:. nāhan dè śrī narèndrānĕmahākĕn i lulut kuŋ nirāwak wilāpa,
yèkī tan saḥ ri paṅkwan winaca tiniliṅan koŋ rinĕṅwan winaswās,
Adṛĕs luḥ śrī narèndrāṅraṣani raṣa nikāpan katuhwan raṣanya,
yogyāṅantyèŋ mahāntĕn wacan iŋ alaradan kālapan ratnakanyā*

:584:\:81:\:2:. rakryan putrī huwus māliḥ asĕmu paṅaliḥ niŋ sĕkaṙ sālas aṅjraḥ,
kwèḥ niŋ guṇḍik nira mwaŋ kaka kaka rumarāṅasturi mrik waṅinya,
lagy ātaṅkis humuŋ hambuluṅan i tali kènyānamaṙ ṣaṭpada strī,
haṙṣāmbĕk saŋ pratīpāmapag iŋ ujaṙ arūm tustus iŋ laṅwa laṅwan*

<A> kind of kṛti ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– |⏑⏓

:585:\:82:\:1:. Ibu t asy asiḥ kita kadaŋ kadaṅa ri sĕḍĕŋ i ṅhulun rimaŋ,
kita yogya mitra kulabanđw amaraṣana ri rāga ni ṅhulun,
pakawaṙgga ni ṅhulun i paṅkwan asisihana raśmi niŋ pṛĕman,
Aṛĕnaḥ manahkw aṅaku sānak iri kita patĕmwan iŋ jaja*

:586:\:82:\:2:. pakĕnaṅkwa yan maṛĕk i māskw amibikana laṭinta riŋ waja,
lumut iŋ payođara huwus kakiṅan usapanaṅkwa riŋ jaja,
Iruŋ i ṅhulun panutulaṅkwa luḥ i pipi ri pamriḥ iŋ sipat,
lukaṙ iŋ tapiḥ salinanaṅkwa karatala mĕnè n pamaṅkwakĕn*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:587:\:83:\:1:. ndaḥ yèki n liŋ narèndrāraṣa mijila sakèŋ ƀāṣa lāwan palambaŋ,
sotan ta ŋ sāri niŋ rāga piturun i laṅö niŋ kawi ƀrāntacitta,
tan paṅgintiṙ manis niŋ tĕbu sawukiṙ apan tan patuṅtuŋ manisnya,
maṙmmānyuḥ prāṇa rūmnyāsĕmu paṅucapan iŋ wahw amaṅkw āṅdudut kèn*

:588:\:83:\:2:. rakryan putrī mulat riŋ nṛpati kadi wulat niŋ ṭikā riŋ wilāpa,
mojaṙ ta dyaḥ sunandā wwaya ta sira siwin śakty asaṅjñā pratīpa,
sākṣāt swaṙggānurun rūpa ni nagara nira ry ānupa ꝁyāti riŋ rāt,
kumbaŋ kĕmbaŋ papaṅgihta kadi patĕmu niŋ kāṙtttika mwaŋ basanta*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:589:\:84:\:1:. saŋ Aṙjjuna sahaśrabāhu riŋ usāna sira siniwi śakti nītimān,
prakāśa sira saŋ daśānana musuḥ nira huwus ayaśāmatī musuḥ,
taŧāpi kaparājayèŋ raṇa huwus hinuripan alawas pinañjara,
hana pwa sira saŋ pratīpa sira rakwa wĕka nira suśīla digjaya*

:590:\:84:\:2:. paran pwa wĕkas uṅṣiṛĕnta paḍa wastu kita wĕka niŋ uttamapraƀu,
para praƀu kapan paḍāsira lawan sira tĕwas amilĕt milĕt wulat,
Amèta kita lèn muwaḥ tĕwas aṅèl midĕṙ ibu kapana n pamaṅgiha,
mataṅnya sira sĕṅgahĕnta kaka yogya sira manuwalèŋ ujaṙ yayi*

<śiꝁariṇī> ⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓

:591:\:85:\:1:. yadin sidđā rakryan sasisihana rūm niŋ siliḥ asiḥ,
Awās rakryan glānāhuyaŋ apupul i jro pakasutan,
hana lwaḥ ramyālwā prakaśita si rèwā ṅaran ika,
kitādyusa ṅkānèsuḥ isuhana lāwan saŋ ahulun*

:592:\:85:\:2:. raras niŋ kaṙwwa swāmi paran ika rakwāṅlĕwihana,
marā riŋ tāman tan hana maṛĕka līlā ṅwaŋ aṅĕnĕs,
yadin madyūsèŋ lwaḥ talaga wulakan śūnya kasĕnĕt,
wĕnaŋ sāmbĕk niŋ swāmi tariman apan tan hana mulat*

:593:\:85:\:3:. kalīṅanyālaḥ māsku maṛĕka nihan dak paṛĕkakĕn,
paran maṙmmantāsuṅṣut aṛĕṅu miṅè tan pamituhu,
paṅantī paṅkwan saŋ praƀu hila hila ŋ duhꝁa siwuhĕn,
Apan māskw āpèt pèt hayu pahayu budđinta ri sira*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:594:\:86:\:1:. nāhan liŋ saŋ sunandāmiṛĕsĕpakĕn i tiṅkaḥ narāṙyya pratīpa,
paŧya ‌wruḥ sopapattīṅgita nikaŋ ucap akṛĕp kĕna priḥ narèndra,
yāṅdè tan saṅśayè twas nira ri ḍatĕṅa rakryan suputrī kisapwan,
kady aṅhyaŋ motusan wallaƀa mamagĕhakĕn tan wuruŋ niŋ swakāṙyya*

:595:\:86:\:2:. rakryan putrī miṅè tan wawaṛĕṅĕḥ apa tan tṛpti rakwè narèndra,
saŋ nāŧa ‌wruḥ sira n tan kinahaṛĕpan ikaŋ budđi maṅkin prapañca,
Āśāƀūtānulis kètaka raṣa kakawin pöḥ nikaŋ rāga tībra,
tambā niŋ kèraṅan tan winadal i liḍaḥ iŋ kāma nāhan raṣanya*

<nawahaṙṣa> ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓

:596:\:87:\:1:. Ibu tan paꝑala pwa ŋ amalaṙ i hayunta sĕḍĕṅta rarè,
syapa māsku kadi ṅhulun aṅurati rāga lawan turida,
katunan lĕpihan kita kinirimakĕnku karaṣkwi i kita,
tĕka riŋ kararan pwa kita mapa tiki n sahajāpi lupa*

:597:\:87:\:2:. sĕḍĕŋ iŋ pabĕlaḥ turida kinĕkĕsanku kitèŋ lĕpihan,
makasāđana kuṅkw aṅiṅĕt iṅĕt i rūmta lanā n pinalar,
Aṅadĕg pwa kitèŋ puḍak araras inastwakĕn iŋ ƀramara,
winaliṅku kitāŋ liṅa puji puji yan ratu niŋ kusuma*

:598:\:87:\:3:. saŋ apiṇḍa wukiṙ ṅhulun ajaṙ ajarè kita muṅgwa sadā,
tarukāṅkwi i hayunta pamiṣayana rāga sĕḍĕṅkw alulut,
licinèŋ śayanākw anusupa ri hulĕsta suganđa miṅiŋ,
sipi māsku suꝁaṅku katuruna ri soṙ i tĕṅahta rari*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:599:\:88:\:1:. nāhan dè śrī narèndrākakawina maṅani twas nirè jro drawāṅras,
ndātan tiṅhal muwaḥ riŋ nṛpawaraduhitā kèwalèraŋ tumuṅkul,
māṙyy āśāƀūta sāmpun pinĕgat ira lulut kuŋ nirè śrī suputrī,
hètunya n tan wijil luḥ nira pamaḍĕm irèŋ rāgabahnī dalĕm twas*

:600:\:88:\:2:. sāmpun māliḥ sudèwī kasusu laku nirāṅĕñcuḥ ĕñcuḥ kaṅèlan,
ndan tiṅhal saŋ susènāṅiriṅakĕn aṅamĕṙ tan wĕnaŋ sāḥ amaṇḍĕŋ,
kady ādandan kisapwan yan alihan asilāhyūn amaṅkwè sudèwī,
haṙṣāgyā gyān anuṅṣuŋ riŋ ujaṙ akakawin lwiṙ katonèŋ palambaŋ*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:601:\:89:\:1:. rakryan saŋ pinunagyakĕnku śaraṇāśraya tumuluṅa kiṅkiŋ i ṅhulun,
Aṅlū māsku kisapwan i ṅhulun aluṅguha kita yayi haywa saṅśaya,
t asy āsiḥ kita māsihè kawi guṇaṅku palaṙ amalĕsèŋ karāṣikan,
lambā kapraƀun i ṅhulun kita rumaṅkĕpana saꝑala yogya tuṅgalĕn*

:602:\:89:\:2:. maṅkè n prāpta ni māsku tambay iŋ anon wwaŋ ahayu kadi dèwakanyakā,
yan riŋ śūnya katĕmwananta saha ƀūṣaṇa maṅĕnĕsa tan parowaṅa,
byaktānĕṅgaha dèwatī kalĕmahān‌ ṅhulun iri kita dūra saṅśayā,
Āpan dè ni hayunta yogya kita māsku panadinakĕna n pinaṅkwakĕn*

:603:\:89:\:3:. paṅkwankw ību paranti niŋ wwaŋ anukĕṙ nukĕṙ aṅĕsaḥ ĕsaḥ pinaṅkwakĕn,
śīṙṇna syuḥ lĕṅĕn i ṅhulun pinakarantunan i kuku niŋ èpu tan panūt,
tan pamwas jaja ni ṅhulun wahu waras linawad i panĕpak niŋ aṅṛĕṅiḥ,
lagy èmö pipi ni ṅhulun saƀa saƀā ni waja niŋ anulak winèḥ sĕpaḥ*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:604:\:90:\:1:. sojaṙ saŋ nāŧa kady āṅalapana kasusuk niŋ kĕnèŋ rāgapāśa,
kady ānambāna kiṅkiŋ niŋ amalaku suwal kèwĕhan kāladèśa,
sākṣāt sambat niŋ onĕŋ kinirimakĕn apèt pèt manis dè ni kuṅnya,
mambö rūm niŋ katuṙwwan winuṅu ni jarumanyānĕkākĕn wilāpa*

:605:\:90:\:2:. tatkāla śrī suputrī sapawulatan aṅantī haṛĕp saŋ susènā,
tan kantun saŋ sunandā maṛĕk ataña tĕhĕṙ sopacārātalaṅkup,
rakryan sāmpun kita ‌wruḥ ri narapati mapāmbĕkta māsku n patĕmwa,
Āpan saŋ nāŧa sākṣāt madana midĕṙ amèt hyaŋ ratī riŋ kaḍatwan*

:606:\:90:\:3:. yadyastun māsku sidđāṅhaturakĕna hayuntèŋ kisapwan narèndra,
ṅkānèŋ gĕṅgā kitāmèna mahās ahasa riŋ nūsa śūnyè tĕṅahnya,
mwaŋ yan rakryan marèŋ wṛndawana taman irānopamèŋ laṅwa laṅwan,
Akwèḥ ƀuktinta ramyāmaṛĕkana yamunā lālanākuwwa kuwwa*

:607:\:90:\:4:. rakryan putrī tan èṅĕḥ sira kinĕdĕ kĕdö yan paniwyè narèndra,
siṅgiḥ rakwa n rarā suṇṭi masĕmu lĕṅa suṇṭy ākalis dè nirāmbĕk,
ndan budđi śrī susènā kadi pulut atĕguḥ tan lumèṙ dè nirāhyun,
saṅkṣèpanya ndi tan sidđa kapalikĕtana śrī suputrī narèndra*

:608:\:90:\:5:. luṅhā lampaḥ sudèwī narapati kawĕkas kèraṅan tan tinoliḥ,
kady agriŋ nora rakwāṅinaki laṅu laṅun yan mulat riŋ sĕṛĕḥ wwaḥ,
rakryan putrī jugānuṅgayap i hati nirātyanta riŋ priṅga wiṣṭi,
maṅkin ƀrāntāṅikĕt ƀāṣa panalimuṙ irè tībra niŋ rāga tikṣṇa*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:609:\:91:\:1:. dyaḥ maḥ luṅṣuran i ṅhulun pasuṅa ni ṅhulun iri kita māsku taṅgapĕn,
siñjaŋ siñjaṅa rakryan iŋ paṅaraṅan ri huwus iŋ anulis pralāpita,
göŋ ny āsihku ri māsku yogya suwalĕn‌ ṅhulun amalaku luṅṣuran tapiḥ,
donyèbū pinakātmarakṣa n amĕṛĕnkw abasahana tĕhĕṙ pamèra luḥ*

:610:\:91:\:2:. rakryan saŋ hinaṛĕp haṛĕpku śaraṇāśraya mulata ri rāga ni ṅhulun,
tan sènuṅṣiṙ adoḥ manahta salawasku tĕka ri kita moǥa tan liniŋ,
ṅhiŋ gānyā hana kāsihanta ḍatu ḍatwa kahulunana tan sahè kita,
yèkī pañjiṅanaṅkwa nitya saparan‌ ṅhulun aṅucap ucap lawan kita*

:611:\:91:\:3:. nāhan ƀāṣa nira n tiniṅgalakĕn iŋ paṅaraṅan i layat suputrikā,
mantĕn duhꝁa nirāṣamun turida rāga ni manaḥ ira tan tinūtakĕn,
śrī hèmāṅgada kabwatan kuŋ i ḍatĕŋ nṛpawaraduhitā marè sira,
wwāgan moǥa gumanty amukti lara rāga niyata sira tan kinahyunan*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓

:612:\:92:\:1:. śrī dèwīndumatī ḍatĕŋ sira ri saŋ sāmpun kaciṙyyan‌ smara,
Èwĕḥ tan kahiḍĕp haṛĕp nira lawan tan hyūn irè saŋ praƀu,
ndān èman wĕkasan kataṙkan i kalis ny ambĕk nira n tan rimaŋ,
Aṅhiŋ piŋ rwa mulat kapiŋ rwa sahajātuṅtuŋ tikĕl niŋ halis*

:613:\:92:\:2:. sāmpun waspada doḥ i rāga nira tan tuṅgal panononana,
suṅṣut suṅṣut ira n kinon maṛĕka lèn tiṅhal nirāṅṛĕṅwani,
Ākārèṅgita niŋ manaḥ saha wijil niŋ śabda norākadi,
Ahyun ka‌wruhana n tan ahyun ika kaprajñān irāpèt wiwal*

:614:\:92:\:3:. tan ‌wruḥ śrī naranāŧa yan tan ahaṛĕp rakryan suputrī sira,
Aṅgĕṅgöŋ kamadan tṛṇāṅkura hiḍĕp saŋ nāŧa riŋ wwaŋ kabèḥ,
hamham paṙccaya dè ni rūpa nira tĕkwan śakti wānīŋ raṇa,
kĕdw ākuŋ makasoŋ laṙônĕŋ ira yan pojaṙ waśākon marā*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:615:\:93:\:1:. saŋ sākṣāt‌ smarakanyakā saŋ anarīra ri hati saŋ amiṇḍa riŋ hiḍĕp,
budđiṅkw ālal aṅantyakĕn siha ni māskw ahuyaŋ ajaruman pralāpita,
maṅkè pwā tĕka tan wawaŋ maṛĕk awaṙṇna kĕna guṇa miṅè kitāriris,
rakryan haywa kakanta māsku sinaranta kalalaḥ ibu rāga ni ṅhulun*

:616:\:93:\:2:. saṇḍaŋ ƀakta samotusankw apuyĕŋ an layat alisuḥ amèt rarāhayu,
ndātan poliḥ aṅèl aṅulwan aṅawètan aṅidĕri kaḍatwan iŋ musuḥ,
maṅkè pwa n hana māskw arūm pakawayaŋ wayaṅĕn amĕṛĕn iŋ pasaṅga 
man,
tan pātmā raṣa kapṛĕman saśayanānĕkĕnakĕna śarīra ni ṅhulun*

:617:\:93:\:3:. nāhan dè naranāŧa mojaṙ awuyuŋ sira wĕkasan adoḥ suputrikā,
śrī putrī katibān ujaṙ haji tan èṅĕḥ apuji sira yan tuhan tuhan,
Ājñālaṅǥana yogya daṇḍan apa tan hana sahuṙ ira pakṣa māliha,
simbantĕn haji molihāmiđi balik sira kawiđi dinaṇḍa niŋ‌ smara*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓

:618:\:94:\:1:. sakwèḥ saŋ maṛĕk uttamottama wiwal munduṙ paḍāmid miṅè,
Aṅhèman ri narèndra yan sira tan antuk śrī suputrī mulat,
mwaŋ‌ strī strī paricārikā paḍa humuŋ maṅyogyanī saŋ praƀu,
ḍyam tèkī wĕkasan tuhun hana mulat yan saŋ sunandāṅucap*

:619:\:94:\:2:. rakryan tiṅhalanātpada nṛĕpati sākṣāt ṣaṭpadāmèt sĕkar,
maṅhèṙ hèṙ i dalĕm taman makapaṅanty antyan kucup niŋ mĕnur,
maṅkè n mūṙ aṅaliḥ cumuṇḍuk i widaṙƀāpakṣa tan mantuka,
Āpan maṙmma nira n ḍatĕŋ kita kaṛĕṅw an paṅjraḥ iŋ campaka*

:620:\:94:\:3:. śrī hèmāṅgada laṅwa laṅwan asana ndātan mĕkaṙ kābunan,
saṅṣāra kṣaya saṅṣayāluru lumè dè niŋ‌ smarāꝁyāpanas,
hèman māsku kucup ni budđi nira yan tan sanmatan kāsihan,
ṅhiŋ gānya n mĕkara n kitāṅlawada māskw āpan gĕṛĕḥ niŋ kapat*

:621:\:94:\:4:. wwantĕn rājya nirè kaliṅga kita yogya hyaŋ hyaṅanyāhalĕp,
tĕkwan paṙśwa nikaŋ mahèndragiri hètunya n kadīndrālaya,
gĕntĕṙ ny ampuhan iŋ mahodađi kaṛĕṅw āgĕnturan tan pĕgat,
Aṅhiŋ donya mamuṅwa saŋ praƀu lawan māsku n katuṙwwān apöm*

:622:\:94:\:5:. rakryan tan kasasaṙ hayunta kawawè saŋ nāŧa hèmāṅgada,
Āpan budđi nirābĕnĕṙ tan aruṣit ‌wruḥ ry ambĕk iŋ dug rimaŋ,
hĕnwanta n maṛĕkè kisapwan ira kèwalya ṅhulun tan saha,
yèkī don i manĕhta mājara ri māṙgganta n suꝁāsaṅgama*

:623:\:94:\:6:. Aṅhiŋ yogya siwinta tan patatalan trus tuñjuŋ iŋ kapraƀun,
prajñā wany anulus bisāṅaji đanuṙwwèdāđika ‌wruḥ nira,
yan riŋ kīṙtty aniwāṙyya śudđa hana soṙ niŋ candrawimbākucĕm,
tustus niŋ ratu śakti digjaya sĕkaṙ tajy aṅkuran‌ kṣatriya*

:624:\:94:\:7:. nāhan dè niŋ amèt manis niŋ aṅucap mambö juruḥ kābunan,
Antuk niŋ maṅalap manis ni kakawin saŋ wṛḍđa wṛdđīŋ laṅö,
ndātan paṅgarit aṙdđa tan ṛĕsĕp i budđi śrī narèndrātmajā,
luṅhā ‌wruḥ tumuluy sira n kinĕḍapan dè saŋ sunandāṅaliḥ*

:625:\:94:\:8:. śrī hèmāṅgada kāri kèraṅan akiṅkiŋ tan wĕnaŋ sāhasa,
maṅgāmora makilya kilyana tumūtè śrī narèndrātmajā,
