saŋ hyaŋ manmaŧa duṣṭa tan rwa tĕlu pat rowaŋ nirāśālara,
yèkī hètu nirāṅikĕt raṣa wilāpāṅras raṣanyè hati*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:626:\:95:\:1:. maṅko pwāntĕnku dèntāmbĕk atiśaya dahat kèwalāṅgöŋ kaputṙyyan,
budđintāpyak madèŋ haṙṣa tan akuŋ iŋ akuŋ saṅṣayāpy āwalèpa,
dèntāwèḥ rāga tan popama kadi ginawè lĕṅlĕṅāku n tumiṅhal,
māyā muṅgw iŋ cṛĕmin lwiṙtta riŋ apa wĕnaṅaṅkwāṅisapwè tuwuhta*

:627:\:95:\:2:. saŋ lwīṙ aṙccāṅaraŋ byakta pan ulaha ni māskwi i ṅhulun yan pamaṅkwa,
saŋ lwiṙ dèwī tulis tan wuruṅa kasarikāku n marè pamṛĕmanta,
saŋ lwiṙ wwè niŋ samudrāṅaraṅakĕn i manahku n surud sihta māsku,
saŋ tuṅtuŋ ni rwi niŋ kètaka kari kacarik twaskwi i luṅhānta maṅko*

<basantatilaka> – – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓

:628:\:96:\:1:. nāhan manis ni paṅikĕt nira rāgacihna,
śṛṅgāra rāṣika pinöm atĕmaḥ wilāpa,
muṅgw ī dalĕm hati ginūḋa raras raraṣnya,
pinrāṙŧanākĕn ira mĕtwa mĕnè n papaṅgiḥ*

:629:\:96:\:2:. saŋ lwiṙ hyaŋ iŋ jalada kāṅinan iŋ basanta,
ndātan panis nisi huyaŋ ni manaḥ niŋ onĕŋ,
luṅhā lawan riris i budđi nirè narèndra,
saŋ nāŧa kāri tĕlĕs i dṛĕs i luḥ nirāṅdyus*

:630:\:96:\:3:. byātīta saŋ praƀu narèndraṣutā wiwakṣan,
dolāyamāna ri turuŋ ni manaḥ nirèṣi,
luṅhāmiliḥ miliḥ i jalwa nirè narèndra,
himpĕṙ sĕkaṙ midĕṙ amèt ƀramarè kuwuṅnya*

:631:\:96:\:4:. sāmpun ḍatĕŋ sira ri sanmuꝁa saŋ narèndra,
śrī pāṇḍya haṙṣa kadi tan rāt ira n tumiṅhal,
runtuḥ lĕbuṙ manaḥ irāṣĕmu rāgabahni,
lwiṙ mās hanèŋ muṣa wawaŋ drawa dè niŋ apwī*

:632:\:96:\:5:. saŋ pāṇḍya siṅhapuruṣākṛti rāgaśatru,
śrī putrikāciri wĕdi n para riŋ paḍöman,
söḥ budđi sattwa naranāŧa paḍāwṛĕg awri,
kèṇḍit manaḥ nira lawan kuŋ irè dalĕm twas*

:633:\:96:\:6:. sāmpun pĕtĕŋ twas ira söḥ turidāṅawèśa,
Aṅhiŋ hinèṙ siliḥ asiḥ naranāŧaputrī,
Āpan katon muꝁa nirāṣĕmu śītaraśmi,
yèkī nimitta nira mojaṙ amanwa manwa*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:634:\:97:\:1:. ṅkè siṅhāsana māskw aluṅguha paran karaṇa niŋ aṅadĕg baṅun wiwal,
rākantālawas aṅṛĕṅö ri hayu rakryan ika karaṇa ni ṅhulun ḍatĕŋ,
tĕkwan śrī naranāŧa ƀoja maṅutus ḍatĕṅa ri sĕḍĕŋ iŋ swayambara,
nāhan taŋ karas èsi ƀāṣa pahulaṅkwa ri kita yayi hantusākĕna*

:635:\:97:\:2:. ‌wruḥ ku n tan paṅĕnoha kuṅku ri kitāpan ahayu sakadaŋ lawan ratiḥ,
tuṅgal rakwa raraṣta riŋ muꝁa lawan ṛĕsĕp i raras i māsku riŋ pupū,
rāgaṅkw ību hanèŋ tĕṅahta kapipis lara turida kinölwa riŋ susu,
lampūn kapṛĕma riŋ pasaṅgaman i paṅhapit i wĕtis i māsku ri ṅhulun*

<basantatilaka> – – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓

:636:\:98:\:1:. sojaṙ narāđipati tan palawan manisnya,
maṅgiṣṭa śiṣṭa mari śiṣṭa sinorakĕnya,
lwiṙ tan mađu ŋ mađu tinaṇḍiṅakĕn yayān sor,
lambā manis manis ikaŋ gula tan panaṅkĕp*

:637:\:98:\:2:. śrī putrikā sira mulat ri haṛĕp narèndra,
ndātan kapūhan apa tan hana paṅgaritnya,
mogākalis manaḥ irāṣĕmu tan panaṅgĕl,
kady adwa tiṅhal ira kèwala tan papiṅṙwwa*

:638:\:98:\:3:. do doḥ i budđi nira niścaya saŋ sunandā,
śrī pāṇḍya tiṅhal ira kady aṅutus maṅĕdwa,
ndan saŋ kinon ira bisāṅupacāra śabda,
mojaṙ tuhun pali palin ya tĕkapnya mojar*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:639:\:99:\:1:. nāhan śrī naranāŧa pāṇḍya sira yogya paṅayatan i māsku riŋ hayu,
hèman rūmta yatan pagĕgwan i manis manis ira n aṅisapw aṅolakĕn,
Aṅhiŋ samƀawa rakwaṅöbana huyaṅta saꝑala paṛĕkĕnta riŋ tilam,
siŋ sojaṙ haji yan rahasya raṣan iŋ śayana kĕmitananta cupwana*

:640:\:99:\:2:. yadyastun kita māsku n āmĕŋ amĕṅèŋ tuha rawa kalawan narèśwara,
byaktānaṅśaya cakrawāka dadi mānuṣa maṭika ṭikan mariŋ ḍarat,
mwaŋ yan kaṙwwa narèndra māsku mahāsèŋ pasisi mĕgila riŋ wwaŋ iŋ pasir,
byaktānĕṅgaha dèwa niŋ miŧuna rāśi mĕtu haṛĕp ahimya himyana*

:641:\:99:\:3:. Atyantèŋ kalaṅön lĕyĕp winulatan patĕmu ni lĕṅĕŋ iŋ pasiṙ wukir,
ndan dūrāmaḍanè laṅö ni patĕmunta matĕmu kalawan narèśwara,
yadyāpin paḍa riŋ laṅö pisaniṅū kadi raraṣa ni māskw asaṅgama,
ṅhiŋ gānyāmaḍanè raraṣta raras iŋ rati madana n akālihan hulĕs*

<mālinī> ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:642:\:100:\:1:. nahan ucapan ikāpèt pèt manis tan pamandi,
kadi ṛĕsĕpa raṣanyè budđi rakryan suputrī,
kunaŋ apa tan ikāṅdè haṙṣa riŋ haṙṣa niŋ lèn,
wiꝑala kadi manis niŋ twak yan iŋ madyasakta*

:643:\:100:\:2:. narapatitanayāṅliḥ tan sahuṙ lwiṙ tulis mās,
ṛĕṅu nira paṅadèśan yan tan aṅgāmituhwa,
kalalu laku nirāṅdoḥ mūṙ lawan saŋ sunandā,
nṛpati kawĕkas ākuŋ śīǥra māwak wilāpa*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:644:\:101:\:1:. rakryan saŋ kĕna rāga tībra kaka rakryan aṅuwatana haywa saṅśaya,
hrū saŋ hyaŋ madanè hatinta dahutĕṅkwa bĕbĕdĕn i taṅanku hĕmbana,
ṅhiŋ jampyanta karāṣikanku n amĕkul gaṛĕgĕtĕn amijĕt mijĕt susu,
romantājumĕn i ṅhulun sadakanaṅkwa n anĕsĕpi laṭinta riŋ tilam*

:645:\:101:\:2:. kocap māsku wicakṣaṇôṇḍahagi yogya panagara bisāmaṅun lulut,
ṅkè ta dyaḥ mata ni ṅhulun sipatananta pĕnĕdĕn usapanta riŋ pusuḥ,
yan kālanta pinaṅkwakĕn wwaya jajaṅku rari siku sikunta yan cala,
kuṅta mwaŋ turidaṅku pādwakĕna māsku patitisana luḥ maran rapĕt*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:646:\:102:\:1:. nahan tĕmahān iŋ prapañca ni manaḥ nṛpati wahu lipuṙ linaṅwakĕn,
hanāmbĕk ira mantukāmruda tuhun mawaraha rumuhun ri saŋ praƀu,
katon ujara niŋ mulat ri sira tan pamahāyu kadi budđi niŋ rarè,
ya hètu nira tan wawaŋ muliḥ aṅantyakĕn i huwusa niŋ swayambara*

:647:\:102:\:2:. byatīta ri sĕḍĕŋ nira n mari rimaŋ tucapa sahana niŋ wwaŋ iŋ saƀā,
manahnya paḍa pakṣapāta ri narèndraṣuta tan ahaṛĕp ri saŋ praƀu,
paḍāśraŋ aṅucap ry uliḥ nṛpasutā ‌wruḥ i haṛĕpa nirèri saŋ haja,
Alap ta wus amaḥ nahan liŋ ikanāṅgĕtĕm asahuran atṙyy aṅadwakĕn*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:648:\:103:\:1:. rāga śrī naranāŧaputra masĕwö kadi kayu ragas iŋ labuḥ kapat,
Osik budđi nirè ḍatĕŋ nṛpasutā winaliŋ ira tĕkākisapwana,
Agyāwèha sĕpaḥ sakè waja siliḥ suwala guyu panaṙka niŋ mulat,
bwat śṛṅgāra dahat panāntwa nira maṙmma raṣa nika ṛĕsĕp rinĕṅwakĕn*

:649:\:103:\:2:. ṅkè rakryan pakisapwan onĕŋ alawas‌ ṅhulun ibu saŋ apiṇḍa nīrada,
saŋ saṅhub ni lulutku saŋ patĕṙ i kuṅku kilat i pĕtĕŋ i twas i ṅhulun,
saŋ ṛĕm niŋ turidāṅalaḥ siḥ apuput huyaŋ amĕkasakĕn putĕk hati,
saŋ truḥ truḥ ni laṅöṅku mukṣa hiniḍĕp kinisapu sahajātĕmaḥ riris*

:650:\:103:\:3:. donkw aṅlitlita roma rakryan anapak napaka hayu ni māsku riŋ tilam,
Āpan tan hana lèn pramāṇa ri raraṣta n aṅaraŋ aṅisapwakĕn puḍak,
māskwi induŋ huniṅan‌ ṅhulun ri manis iŋ mata saraṣija kābunan mađu,
suṅṣuŋ rāga tĕṅaḥ purihta kalawan pipi taḍaha ni luhta pintanĕn*

:651:\:103:\:4:. paṅkwankw ību wĕtĕḥ turuŋ pinakapaṅṛĕṅihan iŋ aṅĕsaḥ pinaṅkwakĕn,
tapwan kāni lĕṅĕnku dè ni kuku niŋ hinari hari miṅè kinolakĕn,
mwaŋ tapwan katĕpak jajaṅku kalawan pipi tĕkap iŋ aṛĕs kinèwala,
ṅhiŋ rakryan karaṇanya n èmwa ragĕta mwaŋ anuluṅa manĕmbu nĕmbura*

<wisaṙjjita> – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓

:652:\:104:\:1:. ṅkè saŋ apiṇḍa nirātmaka tinĕmahākĕn maṇi rājasutā,
tan hana ṅūni dĕlāha kadi kita sujanma suśīla wagĕd,
saŋ dadi janma sakèŋ taya taya kadi rakryan arūm anulus,
māsku śaśāṅkawimāna karika kita maṅdadi maṙmma dahat*

:653:\:104:\:2:. Aṅgriṅi simbali rakryan amaraṣana moǥa tĕkāṅlarani,
dyahku nihan tuluṅĕn‌ ṅhulun uwatana kāraṇa niŋ waraṣa,
griŋ kĕna rāga laraṅkw aṅinak inaki mĕṅgĕp atīs apanas,
māsku mataŋ yan akaṙ pipi guliga tĕṅaḥ palakun ri kita*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:654:\:105:\:1:. nāhan dè saŋ Ajāṅucap mĕtu raras ni kataruṇan irāṅhiḍĕp‌ smara,
mambö tuṙwwan i paṅkwan aṅharas i paṅlawad iŋ ahayu riŋ pasaṅgaman,
kady aṅṛĕṅwa ṛĕṅiḥ lawan paṅĕsaḥ iŋ kinisapu raṣa niŋ wwaŋ aṅṛĕṅö,
śrī dèwīndumatī pwa muṣṭi niŋ akuŋ kapana sira n aṅiṣṭya mintara*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:655:\:106:\:1:. Ujaṙ saŋ Aja waṙṇna waṙṣa tumibānĕkarakĕn asanāṅṛĕṅö gĕṛĕḥ,
Aśoka ḍinĕḍĕṙ sawaŋ nṛpasutā wahu kasiram alūŋ apādapa,
wawaŋ sĕkaṙ irānĕḍĕŋ ƀramara tan hana wani mara kèwalātilar,
Apan saŋ Aja rakwa tan wuruŋ aṅol aṅaṛĕkana mĕnè n pamaṅkwakĕn*

:656:\:106:\:2:. narèndratanayāwĕnĕs mulat i rūpa saŋ Aja wawaŋ agriŋ aṅlayuŋ,
kasambĕt i manis manis ni luṅid iŋ mata saraṣija kèṅgutan halis,
huwus ‌wruḥ i manis nira n kasarik iŋ lituhayu suƀagèŋ swayĕmbara,
ya kāraṇa nirāhaṛĕp maṛĕka paṅkun uwat uwatanèŋ sĕpaḥ sarik*

:657:\:106:\:3:. sawèt ni pamanas nikaŋ madanabahni ri hati nira maṅkin aṅlarè,
tinaṙka nira rājaputra dadi niŋ‌ smara saŋ Aja marèŋ swayĕmbara,
muwaḥ saŋ Aja saṅṣayānaha nahā mulat i hayu narèndraputrikā,
ratiḥ karika sinwayĕmbarakĕn iŋ madananagara liŋ nirè hati*

:658:\:106:\:4:. sipat nṛpasutā lutuṙ kadi humèṙ i paṅusapa narèśwarātmaja,
gĕluŋ nira baṅun haṛĕp suruyanè jariji nṛpatiputra yan lukar,
Aṅṛĕs kadi haṛĕp kadĕmwanana dè saŋ Aja mata nirāṅdadak lumuḥ,
paniṅṣĕt i tapiḥ nirāṣĕmu haṛĕp lukarana ni taṅan nṛpātmaja*

:659:\:106:\:5:. waja nṛĕpatiputra kātara raraṣnya tĕka ta mamusuḥ yan iŋ laṭi,
Alal kĕtĕ kĕtĕg nirèŋ jaja lumiṇḍihana jaja narèndraputrikā,
Asaṅgraha naꝁāluṅid taṅan irāmiraḥ ahaṛĕp adun lawan susu,
tĕkèruŋ ira tan pakāla kumĕsut sĕmu sĕmu niŋ asĕṅhit iŋ pipi*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:660:\:107:\:1:. saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa tan saḥ i narèndraṣuta maṛĕk amaṅku pawwahan,
lāwan dyaḥ jayawaspa kāsiḥ ika tan saḥ i pada naranāŧaputrikā,
ndan rakwènalapan sĕḍĕṅnya n ahañaŋ tinut ika mapasaḥ madum tuhan,
tĕmbènya n sapatiṅhalan paḍa lumuḥ kawĕlas aṛĕp aluṅluṅan taṅis*

:661:\:107:\:2:. saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa mājaṙ i narèndratanaya nĕhĕṙ aṅhĕmū taṅis,
rakryan honya manĕhta tiṅhalana pun marika makaṅaran mađūdakā,
pun muṅgw ī hiriṅan maṛĕk linihaṅan wagĕd araras amaṅku pawwahan,
Aṅhiŋ pun juga tan wĕnaŋ mulat awaṙṇna lara mata n aṅölakĕn taṅis*

:662:\:107:\:3:. yadyastun nṛpaputrikā mara mĕnè humaturakĕna rūm nirè kita,
rakryan tan wĕnaŋ èdihè sira yadin sira tumĕṅĕta pun mađūdakā,
dūra n đāraka riŋ lara smara manĕhta pinasahakĕn iŋ tuhan tuhan,
ṅhiŋ maty āṅaraṅè daganta bapa tan panĕmu kahulunan sadā maṛĕk*

:663:\:107:\:4:. mwaŋ yan śrīndumatī tan aptya ri tuhanku muliha sira tan panoliha,
suṅṣut śrī naranāŧa rakwa ri manĕhta bapa maṅulanĕḥ turuŋ lipur,
byaktāṅgĕgwana sĕmpalĕn bapa manĕhta bapa kita tan awĕlas maṅaṙyyakĕn,
mātīŋ māti kināladèśa kadi kambaŋ iŋ asana sinĕmpal iŋ kapat*

:664:\:107:\:5:. nāhan liṅnya nĕhĕṙ tumuṅkul anaṅis tucapa ta panaṅis mađūdakā,
hāḥ rakryan kadi riŋ paṅipyan ahurip takari manĕ manĕhta tiṅhali,
nāhan pun mađusūdanāmwaṅi narèndraṣuta maṛĕk amaṅku pawwahan,
kĕmbĕŋ kĕmbĕŋ i luḥ nipun marahakĕn siḥ ipun arabi tan wĕnaŋ muliḥ*

:665:\:107:\:6:. maṅkè ry antuk ipun tumūt ri naranāŧatanaya baṅun aṅhuwus huwus,
tan lot‌ ṅgānya pun aṅhiḍĕp turida rāga kadi wuruṅa matya monĕṅa,
yèkā hètu nipun tĕkāhañutan aṅlalu pĕjahana dè narèśwara,
Aṅhiŋ luḥ ni manĕhta kahyuna nipun rurubakĕna lawan ṅṛĕs iŋ taṅis*

:666:\:107:\:7:. Ājñā śrī naranāŧa ṅūni ḍumawuḥ ri para panĕpi riŋ pasiṙ wukir,
An pun patyana tūt tlasĕn haḍaṅĕn iŋ hawan i hawan ipun marèŋ musuḥ,
maṅkè n tan hana patya patyana sadoṣa nipun i sĕḍĕŋ iŋ swayambara,
pun‌ ṅgānyèka dumèḥ pun ahyuna mulat mulata juga sawèt ny unĕŋ nipun*

:667:\:107:\:8:. hāḥ rakryan siha rakryan iŋ manĕ manĕḥ ṅhulun ibu pituhun‌ ṅhulun tuhan,
nāhan śrī naranāŧaputra pakisapwan ibu ri sira haywa tāwihaŋ,
Āpan yan tuna kūŋ i māsku ri sirāpa ta hamĕṅana ni ṅhulun mĕnè,
tan wanđyā mati kaṙwwa pun mađu manĕhta tuhan i huwus iŋ swayambara*

:668:\:107:\:9:. maṙmmā dè jayawaspa mojaṙ ataṅis tĕka hiṛĕŋ i narèndrakanyakā,
pantĕs pantĕs apolahan maṛĕk atakwan i manaḥ ira riŋ nṛpātmajā,
siŋ solahnya wagĕd hanan pamisusal misusal api calāṅṛĕṅiḥ ṛĕṅiḥ,
kĕdw ākon maṛĕkākisapwana nĕhĕṙ mulat aṛĕṅu waśāṅdĕlö mata*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓

:669:\:108:\:1:. sāmpun dyaḥ jayawaspa mojaṙ irikā ta dyaḥ sunandāṅucap,
rakryan tiṅhalananta māsku saŋ Ajātyantèŋ halĕp riŋ saƀā,
putra śrī raǥu potrakè haji dilīpāṅhiŋ kadaṅtāpaṛĕk,
śudđakṣatriya sūṙyyawaṅśa taruṇāṅhiŋ śakti maṅkè n raray*

:670:\:108:\:2:. waswāsĕnta halĕp nirāṅdaśaguṇè rūm niŋ tulis mās tatur,
waṙṇnākāra nirāmarājaya ri waṙṇnākāra niŋ campaka,
muṅgw ī pāda nirālawan miraḥ i kĕmbaŋ niŋ tawā kèdĕkan,
Aṅhiŋ kètaka lot pinaṅkwakĕn ira n lwiṙṇnya n wĕtistālaris*

:671:\:108:\:3:. tan sāhèŋ śarapuṣpa kènaka nirāpan lwiṙ smarāṅiṇḍarat,
mwaŋ maṅgĕgwana puṣpacāpa ri kiwa n paṅdè raras niŋ mulat,
pantĕs muṅgwa ri citta niŋ rara sujanma n sūkṣma tan pāwaka,
yogyāmaṅkwa ri māskw apan paḍa lawan dèwī ratiḥ riŋ hayu*

:672:\:108:\:4:. nāhan raśmi nikāŋ ujaṙ tĕka ṛĕsĕp ri twas narèndrātmajā,
sāmpun waspada kuŋ nirè saŋ Aja maṙmma dyaḥ sunandā suꝁa,
ndan mogāṅjrum apèt prahèlika laṅö siṅgiḥ juga n‌ strī kawi,
dènyāṅjrum raṣa guywa guywan araras‌ ndātan tĕkè jro hati*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:673:\:109:\:1:. rakryan tan sasiwinta māsku sira dè ni karakĕtan irāṅuṛĕn laṅö,
riŋ tāman sira mènduŋ ènduṅan aśoka mĕkaṙ inaṛĕkan pinaṅkwakĕn,
Aṅkĕn māsa kapat mahās mahās adoḥ sahaja majamahān karas tanaḥ,
praŋ praŋ ciṇḍaga kètakī pracacaḥ akṣara salawas irāṣiḥ iŋ ṭikā*

:674:\:109:\:2:. rakryan maṅṣula māsku saŋ ratu kabèḥ muwaḥ ibu parananta waswasĕn,
piŋ pat piŋ lima waspadākĕna raras nira waluyana haywa saṅśaya,
yadyastun sira nora kāptya ni manahta muwaḥ uwahana ŋ swayambara,
ṅkā ta dyaḥ t aduluṙ pahuṙ hurakĕnanta sira lamakananta mantuka*

:675:\:109:\:3:. nāhan dènya n amèt prahèlika laṅö raṣa kakawin anambyakĕn manis,
ndan simbantĕn adoha budđi nira maṅkin arumaḥ apulaŋ lawan‌ smara,
tan ‌wruḥ ry ambĕk irè narèndraṣuta yan sira winarahakĕn marèŋ laṅö,
tan pèndaḥ lara koluran turida rāga nira ri saŋ Ajāwuwuḥ laṅö*

:676:\:109:\:4:. ndān ambĕk saŋ Ajānahā sira ri budđya narapatisutā n tan ahyuna,
Āpan tan huniṅè halĕp niŋ asĕkaṙ taji wĕdi mulatèŋ ajoŋ kuniŋ,
tan hèp hèpĕn aniwya riŋ kadi sirāpi puji sinahuran patik haji,
riŋ siṅhāsana saŋ katiṅgal aṅaraŋ paḍa lĕṅĕŋ aṅikĕt pralāpita*

:677:\:109:\:5:. Aṅlampū saŋ Ajānahĕn turida māṙyy amalaṙ i haṛĕpā suputrikā,
Āpan tan ratu liŋ nirèṙyy awak ira praƀu tuwi sira tan kinahyunan,
Ènak riŋ wĕkasan manaḥ nira haṛĕp haṛĕpĕn amĕnaṅèŋ swayambara,
molaḥ bāhu nirè tĕṅĕn marahakĕn ri pamĕnaṅa nirèŋ swayambara*

:678:\:109:\:6:. ṅkā n jātismara putrikātutuṙ i rūpa saŋ Aja ri sĕḍĕŋ nirāpsara,
riŋ swaṙgga n pakuṛĕn lawan sira tuhun kapalaŋ alaŋ i tan siḥ iŋ wiđi,
maṅkè pwa n paḍa janma mānuṣa sirātutuṙ i siliḥ asiḥ nirālawas,
‌wruḥ mèraŋ kadi tan priyāpriya ri kāla nira n atĕmu riŋ surālaya*

:679:\:109:\:7:. kāla śrīndumatī kapāśa tĕkap iŋ lara turida ḍinaṇḍan iŋ‌ smara,
rāgāṅaṇḍĕhi sāhasāmaṛĕpĕki twas ira raṣa kapatya riŋ saƀā,
yèkā hètu nira n haṛĕp maṛĕka riŋ nṛpatanaya palaṙ sirāṣiha,
Āpan yogya pakāśrayan saꝑala paṅgajaha maḍĕmana ŋ‌ smarānala*

:680:\:109:\:8:. ratnānopama candraṣūṙyyaja kaluŋ kaluŋ ira naranāŧaputrikā,
yèka n pawwat irè narèndraṣuta rāgapahula sumĕnö marè muꝁa,
Èmbuḥ tèja nikā sĕḍĕṅnya kinaluŋ kaluṅakĕn ira riŋ nṛpātmaja,
lwiṙ dèwī ratiḥ aṅhyasi smara sira n paṅamĕṙ aṅĕnakĕn kaluŋ kaluŋ*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:681:\:110:\:1:. nṛpātmaja mulat ry awak nira suꝁāmbĕk ira n amĕnaŋ iŋ swayambara,
paḍāṅrahati cakṣuṙ ādi nira moliḥ i turida narèndraputrikā,
tĕkè muꝁa nirāpriḥ oliḥ inusap hariṅĕt ira tumus tĕkè jaja,
ginañjaṙ ira riŋ sĕṛĕḥ waja nirāṣĕmu sĕmu guyu saƀya riŋ saƀā*

:682:\:110:\:2:. para praƀu sirālarālaḥ aṛĕbut ri turida naranāŧaputrikā,
paḍānĕsĕl awak nirālaraŋ anaṇḍaŋ inucap ira duṙyyaśapraƀu,
gĕluŋ nira ruṣak murè n inalapan makuṭa nira katon paḍākucĕm,
tiḍĕm waja nirāṣamun mari lumöŋ hinilan ira sĕṛĕḥ mĕṅĕs mĕṅĕs*

<giriṣa> ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:683:\:111:\:1:. hĕnĕṅakĕna narèndra śrī putrī sira caritan,
muliḥ aṅalihi ḍampāwās dè niŋ mulat i sira,
paḍa suꝁa paḍa haṙṣānĕmwākĕn kahaṛĕp ira,
patĕmu nira winaswās dèwī dèwa piniturun*

:684:\:111:\:2:. kaka kaka nira mantĕn dènyāpèt wulat amanis,
Akusikan apĕgāpriḥ yan lampaḥ paḍa balisaḥ,
siliḥ usap i muꝁāpan rūkṣa glāna hariṅĕtĕn,
wuwuḥ i hayu nikāṅhiŋ tiṅhalnyāṛĕṅu n ahuyaŋ*

:685:\:111:\:3:. paḍahi paḍa gumĕntĕṙ muny aśraŋ śraṅan i haṛĕp,
gṛĕbĕg i laku nikaŋ wwaŋ sāmānyāṅiriŋ adulur,
ri haṛĕp i wuri lumrā sakwèḥ niŋ para pajurit,
saha curiga kaṛĕsṛĕs maṅrakṣè nṛpatanaya*

:686:\:111:\:4:. ri tĕka nira maluṅguḥ riŋ paṙyyaṅka maṇimaya,
kaka kaka para guṇḍik muṅgw ī soṙ paḍa humaṛĕp,
kadi talaga patīṙŧan sakwèḥ niŋ maṛĕk apupul,
nṛpasuta nṛpaputrī tan pèndaḥ kumuda mĕkar*

:687:\:111:\:5:. tucapa ta para taṇḍa n tan‌ sŧity ākuṭa kaṭikan,
pijĕṙ aṅarahakĕn wwaŋ siŋ yogyāṅatĕṙ atĕra,
hana sira wiku wṛdđācārī motus atawura,
Amilihi śuƀasaṅjñā mwaŋ saŋ ‌wruḥ ‌wruḥ atawura*

:688:\:111:\:6:. sĕḍĕŋ atawuṙ ahosan ginyākĕn sira huwusa,
curiŋ amaṛĕṅi ǥaṇṭārūm lālitya tan asarag,
paḍahi niŋ atawuṙ śabdanyāraśmi pūjā pujān,
mahuwusan i huwus niŋ pañcabrāhma kinĕnakĕn*

:689:\:111:\:7:. tĕlas ika ginuwantĕn śudđa ŋ mūla patawuran,
śarawa kalaśa lāwan śrāntimṛĕt paḍa sumaji,
ǥaṭa kanaka wawan tīṙŧātiṅkaḥ maṛĕk atatā,
paḍa hana pinalaṅkan salwiṙ niŋ saji humaḍaŋ*

:690:\:111:\:8:. huwus asaji pari rwaŋ saṅǥāṙppat saha pipisan,
pasikĕpan ika tan saḥ soṅgwan mwaŋ hapit ajajar,
saŋ Aja sira maluṅguḥ ṅkāna mwaŋ nṛpaduhitā,
sĕmu ni manaḥ irèraŋ yan tuṅkul baṅun aṅurit*

:691:\:111:\:9:. wiđi nṛpati paṅajyan dèwī maṅdyusa ri sira,
nṛpatanaya lawan śrī dèwī śudđa manaḥ ira,
ndan i huwus ira dinyus dyus pahyas nira kumĕñar,
kadi salaga kalahṙwwan mĕmbaŋ wāhu kajawuhan*

:692:\:111:\:10:. nṛpawaraduhitādan siñjaŋ wāhu sinalinan,
tapiḥ ira katutuṅkul maṅdè tuṅkula saŋ Aja,
dumadak amuharāśrī siŋ dodot nṛpatanaya,
siliḥ asiha nirāṅhiŋ don iŋ wastra siliḥ asiḥ*

:693:\:111:\:11:. Aŧa ri huwus irāhyas prāpta mpuṅkw aṅarahakĕn,
sira tumuluy adandan sakwèḥ niŋ maṛĕk aṅiriŋ,
I lari nira cumuṇḍuk riŋ dèwagṛĕha madulur,
dwijawara sira masyaŋ tan sāhè hiriṅan ira*

:694:\:111:\:12:. huwus ajajaṙ aluṅguḥ tapwan wanwa siliḥ asiḥ,
siniwikaraṇa dè saŋ paṇḍya brāhmaṇa matuha,
saŋ amawa kuśapāśāṅgyākĕn mādĕga ri sira,
kadi mĕbĕda sira n tan sāhātĕmwa siliḥ asiḥ*

:695:\:111:\:13:. ri sĕḍĕŋ ira tinuntun dè saŋ brāhmaṇa ri haṛĕp,
kumuliliṅi ƀaṭārāgni mwaŋ kāsiḥ ira tumūt,
dwijawara paḍa saśrī maśraŋ wèda nira humuŋ,
Aƀinawa kadi kumbaŋ moliḥ kĕmbaŋ iŋ asana*

:696:\:111:\:14:. hyaŋ Anala suꝁa haṙṣa n ton saŋ rwāṅidĕri sira,
dilaḥ ira paṅadèśan tan suṇḍè malad aṅadĕg,
nṛpawaraduhitāgyaŋ mogānoliḥ i saŋ Aja,
sĕmu ni wulat irājaṙ yan piŋ sapta sira midĕr*

:697:\:111:\:15:. muwaḥ ajajaṙ aluṅguḥ kāliḥ kāliḥ ira maṛĕk,
kĕtĕṙ i taṅan ira n wahw āpāṇigraha rumaras,
paḍa paṛĕŋ anibākĕn pūṙṇnāhūti saha samit,
śiwa sakala ƀaṭārāgni n sākṣī niŋ awiwaha*

<waṅśasŧa> ⏑– ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏑⏓

:698:\:112:\:1:. huwus mamūjā ri ƀaṭāra pāwaka,
paṛĕŋ sirānĕmbaḥ inastwakĕn jaya,
lawan sawīja n siniwi n jayèŋ raṇa,
muwaḥ pratiṣṫènaƀiwāda śāśwata*

:699:\:112:\:2:. śinaṅꝁapāṇyan sira dè mahādwija,
muwaḥ mahāpaṇḍita śaiwa sogata,
maśaṅꝁapāṇī sira lèn mahāguru,
huwus winèḥ uttamadāna dè haji*

:700:\:112:\:3:. mijil suputrī kalawan nṛpātmaja,
paḍāpatĕmwan wulat èsi manmaŧa,
haṛĕp gumuywa nṛĕpaputrikāwiraŋ,
tumuṅku tuṅkul matukup tukup tutuk*

:701:\:112:\:4:. maṛĕk ‌wruḥ ī tiṅkaḥ ikaŋ pasaṅgrahan,
hatĕp nikaŋ ḍampa winèḥ sumiṅhita,
narèndraputrāṅgĕnĕṅī suputrikā,
paṛĕŋ manuṅgaŋ wĕkasan paḍāraras*

:702:\:112:\:5:. sĕkaṙ taji śrī naranāŧaputrikā,
tiliŋ kagiṅgaŋ kalawan tutup gĕluŋ,
narèndraputrāmahājĕŋ sakè wuri,
Anĕmwakĕn lèśya suꝁāṅharas pipi*

:703:\:112:\:6:. Alakwa lakwan paripūṙṇna riŋ halĕp,
tabaŋ tabaŋ ramya kaṛĕṅw awaṅṣulan,
kiduŋ kinaṅṣyan murawanya tan humuŋ,
lalitya tan kaṙkaśa saṅṣayāraras*

:704:\:112:\:7:. mṛdaṅga sāmpun sumĕnèha paṅruhun,
hanātĕkap lèn sinamèni riŋ kiduŋ,
ṇḍĕk ĕṇḍĕkan prāya ni dè nikā muni,
lĕṅĕŋ kaṛĕṅw āsĕmu paṅgyat iŋ jawuḥ*

:705:\:112:\:8:. payuŋ putiḥ rwaṙwwa manimbaṅī sira,
paṛĕŋ lumampaḥ tan adoḥ paḍāṅadĕg,
pujut lawan jĕṅgi rarāmawāhiṛĕŋ,
baṅun graha rwa rwa paḍāṅgayaṙ wulan*

<giriṣa> ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:706:\:113:\:1:. ri huwus ira tĕkèŋ paprāṣan bwat suranagara,
sahana hana nikaŋ wwaŋ ƀakty āṅañjali ri sira,
pasaji ri sira hampyal dantāśrī sira n apupul,
kadi surapati saṅkèŋ swaṙgga mwaŋ suramahiṣī*

:707:\:113:\:2:. tucapa halĕp ikaŋ paprāṣan dug sira winaraŋ,
kadi humaraṣa wimba hyaŋ candrāṙka winulatan,
tĕka riŋ alun alun söḥ luṅṣiṙ baŋ hinatĕpakĕn,
paḍa kadi gunuŋ āpuy muntab dè niŋ aṅin adṛĕs*

:708:\:113:\:3:. raṣa bubula tĕṅaḥ niŋ rājyāpan paḍa gumĕṛĕḥ,
para ratu saha gĕṇḍiŋ goŋ rojèḥ tabĕ tabĕhan,
Apituwi para taṇḍāśraṅṣāṅan midĕṙ aritan,
saha paḍahi gumĕntĕṙ lagy atṙyy āsurak aṅawat*

:709:\:113:\:4:. para widu sĕḍĕŋ aywan saŋ taṅkil hyaŋ acarita,
paḍa gumuyu kapūhan sakwèḥ niŋ widu binisa,
hana kawatĕk ujaṙṇnya n guyw āwaṙṇna macarita,
Uḍuḥ uḍuḥ uḍuḥ āḥ āḥ hā hā hāḥ bisa dahatĕn*

:710:\:113:\:5:. sahana niŋ abañol dènyāṅguywākĕna puraci,
Aṅigĕl igĕl agĕŋ göṅan koṇṭol paḍa mĕtĕtĕŋ,
wĕlu sakĕbĕḥ agasyak‌ ndan mogāwĕdi wĕkasan,
kaguyu guyu kagöman yan prāpta ŋ wĕlu sabaṭaŋ*

:711:\:113:\:6:. pirus amiruṣi mènmèn dènyāmèt pacĕḥ acĕmĕḥ,
rabi nika bisa pantĕs dènyāƀāwaka maṅĕyĕḥ,
laki nika mulat aṅdṛĕŋ kahyun hyūn aṅuṅas uṅas,
kadi wĕḍus anut añjyan yan tĕṅhā tĕka muriṅis*

:712:\:113:\:7:. Ikaŋ amacaṅaḥ oliḥ guyw apriḥ paḍa sinurak,
tĕkap ika nini niny èlik maswāmi wĕṛĕ wĕṛĕḥ,
paḍa bisa ŋ awayaŋ wwaŋ dènyāṅguywakĕn atarik,
pacĕḥ ika kaki kaky akrak ginyat muliḥ akusa*

:713:\:113:\:8:. sahana nika pinaṅguŋ tūt padw āƀinawa katon,
paḍa gumuruḥ awantus sakwèḥ niŋ guyu gumĕtĕr,
bari bari kapacĕḥ niŋ wwaŋ ŧāni n gumuyu kĕkĕl,
patĕmu ni pasurak niŋ wwaŋ kady ampuhan apagut*

:714:\:113:\:9:. Atali tali kakulwan loṙṇnyāṛĕṅgiṅan ajajar,
raṣa ḍawuha tĕkapnya n lumpat lumpat api tibā,
milu milu para raṇḍānonton dan paḍa gigiṛĕn,
paḍa sinurak i lumpatnya n kālaḥ paḍa kawalik*

:715:\:113:\:10:. Amĕnuhi nagara ŋ wwaŋ ŧāny akwèḥ madulu dulur,
winijilakĕn ikāsiŋ saṇḍaŋ saṇḍaṅan ika mās,
wijaḥ amĕli ḍaḍaŋ saṅgiŋ calwan saha kurupuk,
Anak ika suꝁa dè niŋ tumpi mwaŋ gaja gajahan*

:716:\:113:\:11:. hana sira wiku saṅkèŋ haṙyyāhālĕpiṙ acĕpuḥ,
kasutapan ira maṅdè kwèḥ niŋ śiṣya paḍa maṛĕk,
tuhun ulaḥ ira pĕñcul siŋ siŋ ƀāwa nira kiṭuŋ,
siŋ ucapan ira baṅṣit yèkī śabda nira ṛĕṅön*

:717:\:113:\:12:. ra tapa laki kapūhan wahw ānon nagaraṣaƀā,
Aƀinawa mulat iŋ ƀogātyantāmuhara suꝁa,
kalĕwi lĕwiḥ ikaŋ koṙyy alwāgöŋ gupura nikā,
nṛpati tĕka salumbuŋ riṅgi ṅgānya tiniwikan*

:718:\:113:\:13:. nahan ucapan ira wwantĕn tèkā titiṙ ataña,
paḍa karika ŋ ujaṙ kĕto mwaŋ kori hayu nipun,
kalawan ujaṙ anĕṅgaḥ kāri mwaŋ kari liŋ ikā,
sira sumahuṙ agampil mruḥ mruḥ maṅhawag aṅucap*

:719:\:113:\:14:. kṣamakĕna bapa dèntātakwan yogya tan ahala,
tumañakĕn ikanaŋ kori mwaŋ kori pariƀaṣa,
paḍa bapa wĕnaŋ aṅgon yan tuṅgal taliṅa gajaḥ,
kalawan ujaṙ adigra mwaŋ tan padriga rahayu*

:720:\:113:\:15:. nahan ujaṙ ira baṅṣit baṅṣit tan ya cala nira,
sahana hana nikaŋ wwaŋ ŧāny atwaŋ mulati sira,
tapa tapa nira pĕñcul wwaŋ wwaŋ sākṣara maṅucap,
milu milu ta ya baṅṣit‌ ndan twaṅnyè sira liŋ ikā*

:721:\:113:\:16:. hĕnĕṅakĕna saŋ aṅdon tontonan sĕḍĕŋ amĕpĕg,
waluyana caritan śrī putrī mwaŋ nṛpatanaya,
ndan i huwus ira pinraṣprās mantuk mara ri dalĕm,
gĕṛĕḥ ikaŋ aṛĕbut praṣprāṣan maṅgyat adadakan*

:722:\:113:\:17:. kunaŋ ikaŋ aṛĕbut pènī pènī hana ri ruhur,
Uliḥ ika paḍa mūlyāpan wastrāhayu saꝑala,
binĕbĕdakĕn ikākwèḥ lèn muṅgw iŋ cĕṅĕl i gulū,
hilaŋ i cĕṅĕl ikè soṙ mwaŋ dodot nika kaṛĕbut*

:723:\:113:\:18:. nda tucapa para nāŧān sāmpun kèwwan ira kabèḥ,
paḍa mamaluyakĕn mās lāwan wastra pamisalin,
saha manis iŋ ujaṙ ndan liśya n pawwata pahula,
muliḥ i huwus irāmwit duhꝁāsĕṅhit i saŋ Aja*

:724:\:113:\:19:. muwaḥ ucapakĕna śrī putrī mwaŋ nṛpatanaya,
saŋ amaraŋ i sira strī strī wṛdđā pitu ŋ abuyut,
tuwi kadaŋ ira tan lèn riŋ sajñāhayu manulus,
Atuha tuha tinuṅgal sakwèḥ niŋ maṛĕk i sira*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:725:\:114:\:1:. bwat kāmèśwara ratna nīla winaṅun gṛha linaraṅan iŋ huwus praƀu,
lwiṙ padmāsana siṅha rūpa ni sakanya kumĕñaṙ abirū paḍākiris,
kaśraŋ dè ni sĕnö nikaŋ kanaka paṅhatĕp apituwi söḥ mađubrata,
sākṣāt rātri winĕtwan iŋ wulan awā linĕṅĕṅakĕn i śabda niŋ cucur*

:726:\:114:\:2:. ṅkā dèwī winaraŋ lawan saŋ Aja māṙ hati nira rumaras paḍāwĕnĕs,
ry antuk saŋ mamaraŋ maraŋ ri sira kāri sira kadi mađubratāsana,
maṅkè pwa n tumĕmu ŋ prayojana ni rāga nira malawas aṅhiḍĕp‌ smara,
kady āṅipy aṅisapwakĕn wulan awāmbĕk ira n aṅisapu nṛĕpātmajā*

:727:\:114:\:3:. śrī dèwīndumatī miṅè tan anumoda ri palaku ŋ asiḥ nṛpātmaja,
hèman luḥ nira maṅlĕtuḥ lĕtuhi soca nira kadi saroja kābunan,
moǥanya pwa mayat mayat halis irāṛĕṅu ṛĕṅu kaharas wawaŋ tikĕl,
tan pātmā kinisapwakĕn twas ira tan pajajamuga ṛĕmĕk sakè taṅan*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:728:\:115:\:1:. lĕṅlĕŋ niŋ lod lĕyĕp niŋ wukiṙ inayu papaṅgiḥ nirārok piniṇḍa,
kālaṅkyaŋ mwaŋ ṛĕṛĕb waṙṇna nira kadi liraŋ kāmukan saṅhub awrā,
himpĕṙ saŋ hyaŋ śaśī kĕmbaṙ apupul akĕmul truḥ truḥ iŋ kāla sanđyā,
dèwī dèwāṙdđanārīśwara patĕmu nira lwiṙ ṭikākaṙwwa kaṙwwan*

:729:\:115:\:2:. saŋ kady ānaṅga māṙyy ātanu mijil atĕmaḥ rājaputrādwitīya,
maṙmmāpèt siḥ tan imbāmĕkul aṅamĕṙ amĕṙ cumbu cumbw āṅalap sor,
sotan ta ŋ wwaŋ riris kāṅinan apĕnĕd arūm paṅhilaŋ rāgabahni,
pömpöman rāṣika lwiṙ nira paliḍaḥ iŋ èlik miṅè riŋ kisapwan*

:730:\:115:\:3:. mambö sub niŋ‌ smarāṅdè huyaŋ i hati nirāwaṙṣiḥ apriḥ raṣanya,
sumyuk taŋ rāgawaṙṣāṅapitu makĕcĕhan lagy awantö raras twas,
Atruḥ truḥ haṙṣacittāmarupuhi turidāwaḥ wahan sanmatāgöŋ,
tṛṣṇāṅumbaŋ lawan siḥ manis iŋ ujaṙ arūm saṅṣayādṛĕs hilīnya*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:731:\:116:\:1:. saŋ hyaŋ hyaŋ ni laṅöku māwak aśarīra mĕtu ri paṅawèśa niŋ‌ smara,
lwiṙ dèwī sakalānurun bĕsuṙ i ramya niŋ amĕŋ amĕŋ iŋ surālaya,
lakṣmī niŋ nagarī turuŋ matĕmahān karika kita wiśāta lālana,
saŋ sākṣāt pratimāṅaraŋ hulun anugrahana tariman aṅharas pipi*

:732:\:116:\:2:. ṅūnī kāla nikaŋ swayambara mijil kita kadi wijil iŋ niśākara,
sakwèḥ saŋ pininaŋ praƀāwa nira söḥ murub aṅabaṙ abaṙ tĕkèŋ laṅit,
rākantānwam alĕk taŧāpi kita haṙṣa tan ahaṛĕp i wīṙyya saŋ praƀu,
göŋ niŋ prihku lawan siḥ iŋ hyaŋ aṅiriŋ ri ḍawuḥ i turidanta ri ṅhulun*

:733:\:116:\:3:. maṅkè muṅgaḥ apöm waliṅku ta kataṅgamaṅakĕna pamaṅku ni ṅhulun,
sèṅĕṙku n dinĕlö ndatan tinarimāṅusapi hariṅĕt i wwit iŋ susu,
dèntāhyun kadi guywa guywan iŋ apa n ṛĕsĕpa pisaniṅū tĕkè hati,
siŋ solahku sinikwakĕnta tinĕpak hana tinama rarè pinīḍana*

:734:\:116:\:4:. nāhan dè nṛpaputra haṙṣa maṅĕnākĕn ucapan amanis priyambada,
Aṅluṅlūṅi laṅö hanan pakakawin kakawin aṅaṛĕki nṛĕpātmajā,
mogātön aṅusap jajāṅĕluk ĕluk lĕṅĕn araras amaṭya maṭyani,
pèt pèt rāga mamanwa manwa mamĕpĕṙ mĕpĕṙ ataña ri mūlya niŋ tapiḥ*

<wisaṙjjita> – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓

:735:\:117:\:1:. śrīndumatī kakĕnan wiṣa niŋ ujaṙ arūm sumusuk ri hati,
ndan kadi tan huniṅā pawulatan ira moǥa mahāpi hadè,
rwā ŋ katahā n uduhĕn brituha wilaja hètu nirāpi tulak,
rāga nirāṅulanĕḥ tuhun awĕdi kawĕs riŋ ulaḥ kawawa*

:736:\:117:\:2:. maṙmma nirāwri lanākiput awĕdi kasiṅkaba siñjaŋ ira,
tan huniṅan tinañan lara ni wĕtu ni luḥ nira niṣkaraṇa,
nora wanèḥ paran iŋ manaḥ apĕga kumöl winisik wisikan,
ṅhiŋ panamantara ri śru saŋ Aja winiwèka nirè twas ira*

:737:\:117:\:3:. sāma paran wĕnaṅānulaka ri pamĕkulnya tan èraŋ amĕl,
dāna paran ta kunaŋ wĕnaŋ anuculanè paṅagĕmnya tapiḥ,
ƀèda paran wĕnaṅanya kumawaśakĕna bwat i rāga nira,
daṇḍa jugènaka liŋ nira nĕhĕṙ anĕpak jaja sāhasika*

:738:\:117:\:4:. kāla nira n panĕpak taṅan ira kadi pādapa molaḥ alon,
mambĕt ikaŋ luṅayan kadi lurus iŋ aśoka tinūb niŋ aṅin,
tiṅhal irāṛĕṅu moǥa kadi saraṣijè tĕka niŋ ƀramara,
suṅṣut irè nṛpaputra hana kadi gula drawa dè niŋ ĕbun*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:739:\:118:\:1:. Ꜽ koŋ ƀrānta kasop i luḥ niŋ aṅaraŋ kasarik i laṭi niŋ winèḥ sĕpaḥ,
lĕṅlĕŋ dènta mulat piliḥ winawa niŋ turida sinaput iŋ hyaŋ iŋ ṭikā,
rūm niŋ śabda mamèka sambĕt i gĕluŋ kari kita pati jumput jumputi,
dèntāṅol midĕṙ iŋ tĕṅaḥ kapana yan waraṣa kadi panumpal iŋ‌ smara*

:740:\:118:\:2:. siṅgiḥ ƀrānta kakanta māsku mapa don iŋ aṅasag inawènta lĕṅlĕṅa,
twaskw apriḥ binĕbĕdta riŋ tali gĕluŋ cinucuk i luṅid iŋ matāluru,
mogāṅdè wulaṅun manista rinasan tuhu tuhu n agĕlaŋ gĕlaŋ kuniŋ,
ṅhiŋ yan rakryan aṅastwa riŋ luḥ uwatanya maraṣana ri rāga ni ṅhulun*

:741:\:118:\:3:. pintĕn māsku wuyuṅta tan hana wanèḥ pinalaṙ asiha sanmatèŋ akuŋ,
cĕp tènduŋ taha tan taṅis kahaṛĕp i ṅhulun aṅisapu jöṅta sèwaka,
luhtādṛĕs humilī pasuṅta karikā taham ibu tan ikā prayojana,
Aṅhiŋ prāṙŧana moǥa sidđa katĕkana siliḥ usapa luḥ lawan kita*

:742:\:118:\:4:. Intaṙ haywa maṛĕk paran karika donta paran iku kināṙyya niŋ maṛĕk,
tan siḥ rāga nimitta niŋ taṅis adoḥ tiki kakĕnana kapriyambadan,
lāwan tan suꝁa hètu niŋ luḥ aṅasapta ri mata tuwi tan gawè gawè,
luḥ luḥ duhꝁa luḥ i ṅhulun taṅi taṅis prihati karaṇa niŋ lanānaṅis*

:743:\:118:\:5:. nāhan dè nṛpaputrikānulak i sāhasa saŋ Aja saranta riŋ pṛĕman,
tan paṅdè wĕdi riŋ kĕdö maṛĕk aṅol nĕhĕṙ aṅaṛĕki dè nirāṅucap,
maṅkin haṙṣa rinĕṅwan aṅlalu kasuṅṣutana saŋ Aja saṅṣayāwawuḥ,
śrī putrī sira kāpĕsan ri panulak nira jaja wĕkasan sirānaṅis*

<nawahaṙṣa> ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏓

:744:\:119:\:1:. Adawa n panukĕṙ saŋ ahayu kadi tuhwa nĕhĕṙ miṅaya,
Anaṅis kadi tan patĕmahāna lulut pwa ri suṅṣut ira,
Aṅĕsaḥ kadi tan siliḥ asiha mĕnè ri huwus niŋ ulaḥ,
Anulak ri sĕpaḥ nṛpasuta kadi tan pamalakwa hĕlĕm*

:745:\:119:\:2:. Atukup taliṅāwĕdi katĕkana rūm niŋ ujaṙ kinirè,
susu tan winĕḍaṙ wĕḍaṙ awĕdi kakukwa ragĕt ragĕta,
Akĕmul kĕmul èpu ri pĕpĕsa ni mađya nira n pinĕkul,
Asaput muꝁa kady awĕdi hilaṅa rūm nira kāṛĕkana*

:746:\:119:\:3:. nṛpaputra mamaṭyakĕn i manis ira n gula rāga rinok,
ratus iŋ mađupaṙka sira guliga niŋ lara haṙṣa pinöm,
rinĕbut pinakèsi ni mata niŋ akuŋ ri dalĕm nagara,
papa dè nira tan paṅaraṅakĕna tan panibākĕna luḥ*

:747:\:119:\:4:. lĕṅĕŋ iŋ mađumāsakusuma pinakaswaśarīra nira,
paḍaŋ iŋ wulan aṅrahinakĕn alaṅö pinakāmbĕk ira,
lumĕkas pwa sirāṅhari hari kadi kāṙtttika raśmi nira,
mĕtu kady asirat sirata maṇik ujaṙ nira maṙmma dahat*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:748:\:120:\:1:. māskwi induŋ mapa ramya niŋ wulatanèŋ mata mamanis tan pawora luḥ,
tan paṅṛĕṅwa ṛĕṅiḥ lawan paṅĕsaḥ iŋ kinisapu manukĕṙ tĕkè hati,
mwaŋ tan paṅgilana n paṅol sahurana n paṅucap uƀayanāṅharas pipi,
byakta n mūra lawan śawaṅkwi ibu yadin kita mulata manuṅṣuṅèŋ guyu*

:749:\:120:\:2:. ndin wanyāku tĕkāṅisapwakĕna māsku pinaṅĕmulakĕn tĕpak jaja,
Èpu ṅwaŋ mapa tèkiŋ ènaka baśāṅaṛĕkana pinamömakĕn waja,
ṛĕskwi induŋ tumĕkākĕnāmbĕk i hayunta pinaṅagĕmakĕn naꝁāluṅid,
ṅĕs ṅösĕn mulatèŋ matāmati matī ri paṅayat i halista mamraṅa*

<kilayu> Anĕḍĕŋ – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:750:\:121:\:1:. nāhan wĕtu ni turida rāga rakryan/ Aja māwak ucapan amanis,
An sāhasa sira kahanan wĕlas ri panaṅis nṛpawaraduhitā,
Om yan humĕnĕṅa sakaṛĕŋ maṅantyakĕna rāga nira saŋ anukĕr,
saŋ hyaŋ‌ smara ri manaḥ irāṅalaḥ pisaniṅūn wĕnaṅa pihĕrana*

:751:\:121:\:2:. saŋ śrī niŋ ahayu sakaḍatwan osaḥ aṅĕliḥ kawaṛĕgan anukĕr,
wahw ālupa taṅan ira riŋ tapiḥ tuṙ ira kaṙwwa lumay akilusū,
mwaŋ puṇḍutan ira tumibā lukaṙ tali talinya paḍa tan iniwö,
Aṅlampw anaṅis aṅĕsĕsan paṅèwala narèndraṣuta tinarima*

:752:\:121:\:3:. Ambĕk saŋ Aja suꝁa girahyasĕn maṛĕk añaṅkiraṅi tan inapa,
riŋ swapna hiḍĕp ira ri tan kawāđan i paṅol nira n inĕnĕṅakĕn,
Oṅṣil taṅan ira tumamèrikaŋ kadi manuk wahu kumapu kapu,
mūṙcꞓā twas ira kawa kawān anon kadi tanaḥ sumĕlap i taliṅa*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:753:\:122:\:1:. Utpāta nṛĕpaputra riŋ śayana moǥa tĕka ri papupul nirèŋ jinĕm,
liṇḍū gumrit ikaŋ palaṅka kumĕtug pakĕtĕb iŋ aṅĕsaḥ pinaṅkwakĕn,
Olaḥ lwiṙ bubula ŋ tilam pakĕdal iŋ wĕtis amijilakĕn larap larap,
wintaŋ sūṙyya śaśaṅka nāga kagiwaŋ giwaŋ i kĕlab ikaŋ laṅit laṅit*

:754:\:122:\:2:. guntuṙ luḥ mahāwan ri lambuŋ iŋ iruŋ tumĕḍun amalapaṙ marè kapö,
kasṛĕg katrag ikaŋ payođara lanāpipit alara kawantus iŋ jaja,
lambè śīṙṇna babak laṭinya hana mātra miraḥ i tapak iŋ wajānĕsĕp,
miṅgut śṛṅga nikaŋ halis huwus apaṙwwa sana sini tikĕl mayat mayat*

<wīralalita> – ⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:755:\:123:\:1:. śrīndumatī huwus kawawa māṙ gupè kawĕnĕsan,
mĕṅgaḥ awuṅw anoliha paran tikāŋ inusapan,
siñjaŋ irāmiraḥ karuđiran tinuṅkulan ira,
kapyuhan aṅligāsidĕha hèwa riŋ nṛpasuta*

:756:\:123:\:2:. maṙmma narèndraputra mawĕlas lanāṅhari hariḥ,
liśya nirāṅgamĕl susu mahāṅusap luḥ i jaja,
kèn winirū wirū lamakan iŋ paṅol hiḍĕp ira,
cumbu wicakṣaṇāmisiki lèśya niŋ maṅaṛĕki*

:757:\:123:\:3:. śrīndumatī maṅö kadi tulis winèḥ aṅaraṅa,
waṙṇna nirākucĕm kasiṛĕman damaṙ mari lumöŋ,
kram kram i pāmbĕkan saŋ Aja wahw aǥāṣa tumitiḥ,
hètu nira n wijil kadi tapĕl turuŋ tinapihan*

<Udgatawisama>,
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓
– ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓
⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏓

:758:\:124:\:1:. dumunuŋ sirèña nira kāliḥ uwa nira kapaṅgiḥ iŋ natar,
muṅgw i patiga niŋ aśoka liman,
Akĕmit lawan kaka kakāmajaŋ wulan*

:759:\:124:\:2:. tumuluy kataṅgamaŋ anuṅṣuŋ iña nira wawaŋ mamaṅkwakĕn,
mojaṙ uwa nira maṛĕk manuluŋ,
Ibu kölakĕn‌ ṅhiŋ ika dè nikāṅlarè*

:760:\:124:\:3:. wihikan‌ ṅhulun ri lara niŋ gati kawawa tinambay iŋ priya,
soṙ ibu lara lara niŋ kawĕlad,
kasahaśraƀāga lara niŋ matāpĕpĕḥ*

:761:\:124:\:4:. Anulis ṭikā dinudutan puḍak ibu lara niŋ minaṅkana,
lwiṙ hṛĕbuk aṅalilipi ṅṛĕs ikā,
Aṅinaŋ sĕṛĕḥ lĕgĕ paḍanya riŋ pĕḍĕs*

:762:\:124:\:5:. I kapiŋ rwa niŋ gati wĕnaŋ rinĕṅihakĕn ikaŋ larāhaṅan,
yan huwus alawas apöm akulè,
Alilaŋ laranya kadi mukṣa riŋ tapiḥ*

:763:\:124:\:6:. tuhan i ṅhulun muliha rakryan alaḥ ibu waluy parèŋ jinĕm,
tolihĕn alal ira saŋ kawĕkas,
mulat iŋ lawaŋ mapaga rūmta riŋ guyu*

:764:\:124:\:7:. Araras wuwus ny uwa nirāṅlipu lipuṙ i manaḥ nṛpātmajā,
moǥa winawa nira riŋ kalaṅön,
lara niŋ hañaṙ kawawa riŋ pasaṅgaman*

:765:\:124:\:8:. sira saŋ kinon maluya tan paṅucap aṛĕṅu hèwa suṅkawa,
kāṅĕn aṅĕn ulaḥ ulaḥ saŋ Aja,
kamatolihĕn tuhun aṛĕs kapiṅṙwwana*

:766:\:124:\:9:. wĕkasan hinĕmbanakĕn iŋ kaka kaka mara riŋ pasaṅgaman,
gaṙjjita saŋ Aja sawèt niŋ alal,
mĕtu kapriyambadan i dè nirāṅucap*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:767:\:125:\:1:. yak maty āku dĕlönta māsku palalun makahawana hayunta gĕgwana,
Ūṙṇnā nūpura ƀūṣaṇanta katĕkāna tĕmahāna ni janma ni ṅhulun,
mwaŋ rup ꞓattra kaluŋ kaluŋ saha sĕkaṙ taji mijila lawan tutup gĕluŋ,
Aṅgon dènta ri kāla niŋ piniḍuḍuk mapa raṣa raṣa niŋ sinanmata*

:768:\:125:\:2:. tan hèꝑèpĕn aƀūṣaṇāpan anukĕṙ nukĕri laku pataṅkis iŋ kalè,
prāyāṅrup tĕka kaṙṇnaśūla niyatāmuhara tuna ni dè niŋ aṅṛĕṅö,
kaṇṫāṅṛĕs tĕkap iŋ kaluŋ kaluŋ ikaŋ payuŋ aṅadĕg adĕg hanèŋ adoḥ,
Ūṙṇnā wyaṙŧa lawan sĕkaṙ taji tutup gĕluŋ anĕwasakĕn bwat iŋ mulat*

<giriṣa> ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:769:\:126:\:1:. nahan ujaṙ ira mambö rāgānūta ri saŋ Aja,
lukaṙ i tapiḥ irāṣowè kèṅkab hinĕnĕṅakĕn,
wahu sumahuṙ anū dè maṅkè yan tinaña tañan,
mari luḥ ira kumĕmbĕŋ wahw āwèḥ maṅaṛĕkana*

:770:\:126:\:2:. nṛpatanaya kasĕṅkwan rāgāmaṙppĕki sumaput,
Amahāwas isi niŋ kèn sāmpun waspada kaharas,
Aṅamĕṙ amĕṙ amakpak ‌wruḥ ry ambĕk niŋ aṅĕsaha,
lwiṙ anadaki kĕnèŋ hrū maṙmmāṅrèhi tan asarag*

:771:\:126:\:3:. ri huwus ira kapiṅṙwwan saŋ śrī niŋ tulis aṅaraŋ,
lara nira mahĕli prīty āluṅluŋ hyun aṅalaya,
manaḥ ira wahu tūtūt kālap dè nṛpatanaya,
turida nira kahĕnti mwaŋ siḥ niŋ hati kapulut*

:772:\:126:\:4:. paṅusĕŋ ira ri lambè lambè tan tĕka ri hati,
panĕpak ira huwus mūṙ mukṣāṅdohi taṅan ira,
mari maṛĕṅu tumiṅhal tuṅtuŋ niŋ halis alaris,
manis i guyu nirāṅdyun ‌wruḥ giṅgaŋ wahu kasiṅī*

:773:\:126:\:5:. patĕmu nira winaswās kady anwam yumayi yayi,
saŋ ahayu sira molaḥ maṅlaḥ laḥ kumĕda kĕdal,
saŋ Aja sira sumuṅkĕm tan paṅlè kumuru kurub,
paḍa kumĕsĕk iŋ ambĕk tan kèwrān awuda wudā*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:774:\:127:\:1:. riŋ krāban kalasā mijil sira sumaṅgraha wali nira pūṙṇna tan kuraŋ,
sāmpun kèwwan irānaḍaḥ sira pĕnuḥ sama maṛĕk i sira wwaŋ uttama,
ramyātiṅkaḥ atūt paluṅguḥ ira saŋ huwus agati winèḥ akaṙwwana,
Ācārī kalawan karaṇḍan ira muꝁya pinituhu paḍa ‌wruḥ iŋ krama*

:775:\:127:\:2:. ṅkānè soṙ apupul paḍāruhuṙ iŋ ambĕk aruhu ruhuran paḍāṅaliḥ,
Èwĕḥ tan kawĕnaŋ tiniṅkaḥ aputĕk saŋ amahāyu makon atiṅkaha,
dè ni kwèhnya wiwal paḍāwyahata budđi nika puji puji n pakawwaṅan,
siŋ soṙ uṅgwan ikānĕsĕl ri saŋ aniṅkaḥ inucap ika tan ‌wruḥ iŋ krama*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:776:\:128:\:1:. wèt wèt niŋ brāhmaṇātyanta wĕkas iŋ aruhuṙ kadwijāṅśan ginöṅnya,
wèt niŋ śaiwaṙṣy aluṅgw ī nĕhĕṙ apuji kaƀasmāṅkuran mūlya dènya,
wèt niŋ bodđādwitīya n rumĕja ṛĕja kabudđāṅkuran kāraṇanya,
tan tuṅgal māṙgga niŋ kādyan asĕmu hawan iŋ muṅgaḥ iŋ paṙwwatāgra*

:777:\:128:\:2:. wwaŋ ‌wruḥ riŋ lokikācāra sĕḍĕŋ iŋ anaḍaḥ tan kawoṙ woṙ manahnya,
dènyābudđy āmanis mĕṅgĕp upaśama tinon mèwĕḥ olaḥ tiniṅkaḥ,
Aṅdoḥ tan saṅgrahèŋ uṅgwan aruhuṙ alĕmĕḥ woṛĕn iŋ tan kaśudđi,
maṅgā muṅgwèŋ asoṙ ndan yan apupul atatā sabrayārok sahāṙyyan*

:778:\:128:\:3:. guṇḍik rwaṙwwāpupul tan wĕnaŋ apasaḥ adoḥ dè ni göŋ iŋ pamitran,
kady ākaṙwwan swarūpanya paḍa paḍa siliḥ mūla tuṅgal pināliḥ,
solaḥ sèṅĕṙṇnya mogāṅinaki ri panunasnyèŋ tuhan sāri sāri,
dènyāniṅkaḥ ry awaknyāṅruhuri rinuhuran ramya sawyāpasawya*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:779:\:129:\:1:. paḍānaḍaḥ akālihan sama kinon maṛĕka suꝁa linawwa lawwakĕn,
sawaŋ hudan atöb tibèŋ bañu kĕcap niŋ apupul amaṅan rinĕṅwakĕn,
maṛĕk sahana niŋ magoṣṫi humĕnĕŋ rumasa raṣani paŧya niŋ raṣa,
tuhun kasĕṛĕtĕn jugāṅucap aminta paluṅan atĕkĕm jajāsĕgu*

:780:\:129:\:2:. lariḥ lumari tan paraṙyyan alaris ri katahapan ika n hanātulak,
surāṣira siran raṣanya suraṣāṛĕbu ṛĕbu sumĕḍaḥ kinahyunan,
maṇik pinakajaṅga tan papĕgatan kucuṙ ika kadi pañcuran juruḥ,
kilaŋ bṛĕm inalap ginanti kadi tīṙŧa mađu mamulakan sakèŋ gĕḍaḥ*

:781:\:129:\:3:. paḍālap alapan tahap sama maṛĕk wija wijaḥ awĕṝö girahyasĕn,
Apintiga hanan papiṅpat aṅigĕl katĕkan urak aganti tan bĕsur,
Ikaŋ wwaŋ atĕṛĕḥ manahnya kĕna riŋ sayub ahaṅan agasyak iŋ saƀā,
putus maṙ atĕṅö para mpu bini moǥa salaḥ ĕluk ulaḥ nirāḍakè*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:782:\:130:\:1:. strī niŋ śaiwa tan èraŋ èraŋ aṅigĕl kaguyu guyu wĕṝö wĕṝö dawā,
tan haṙṣèŋ swara niŋ mṛdaṅga salukat ṅuni ṅuni yan i gīta niŋ wanèḥ,
hètunya n paṅiduŋ wijil niŋ ajiyaḥ sahuli huliḥ ikāṅṛĕṅö ṛĕṅö,
sahtotè praŧamā kiduṅnya n aṅawat midĕm aṅujiwat ambahan tayoḥ*

:783:\:130:\:2:. ḍaŋ hadyan tumurun gumanty aṅigĕl oṅṣil aṅawak akikat rumampayak,
ṅhiŋ kahyunya kiduŋ buwun ya kiniduṅnya n aṅalik alik èndaḥ iŋ saƀā,
ramyārūm sinĕlanya gĕṇḍiŋ i tutuk kaguyu guyu ginañjaṙ iŋ lariḥ,
giḥ giḥ puŋ ri kipaḥ ḍuraŋ diniwayūḥ amamati juga dè nikāmbahan*

:784:\:130:\:3:. Èndaḥ ƀāwa nikaŋ wanèḥ saha kiduŋ midĕṙ aṅilagakĕn wwaŋ iŋ saƀā,
ndan‌ strī niŋ widu rakwa moǥa kawatĕk sawaŋ acarita dè nikāṅigĕl,
đik haḥ kaśmala nāhan ambahan ikāṅgyat anudiṅi matāṅjĕjĕk lĕmaḥ,
Aig lĕs liṅnya nĕhĕṙ muliḥ matĕlasan maṅumik umik aṅañjalīŋ tawaŋ*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:785:\:131:\:1:. samantaji tibā ŋ ḍawuḥ pitu muliḥ nṛpasuta kalawan suputrikā,
paṛĕŋ maṅadĕg iŋ nataṙ sira kabèḥ tumut aṅiriṅakĕn marè dalĕm,
paḍāmwit atatā winèḥ maṅinaṅāraṛĕm upaśama sādarāṅucap,
dwijāṅśa maduluṙ duluṙ maṅaƀiwāda para wiku maṛĕk maṅañjali*

:786:\:131:\:2:. gumanti para wālakāmuhun anĕmbaḥ inuƀaya sināntwa riŋ guyu,
Ikaŋ baṇija lot amaṅkari panambaḥ ika kawagĕdanya tan hilaŋ,
paḍāṅucap akon ahosana marèŋ jinĕm agawaya paṅhawin laras,
mulat saŋ Aja ri priyā nira nĕhĕṙ gumuyu guyu midĕm suputrikā*

:787:\:131:\:3:. Aliṅgiḥ atitiḥ pupū siliḥ usap muꝁa sira ri huwus nirādamu,
prahāsana narèndraputra manĕcĕk nĕcĕki rahi ri kĕmbaŋ iŋ hawu,
baṅun haṛĕp aminta paṅkwakĕna söŋ ni paṅawaśa ni siḥ suputrikā,
paṅa‌wruhana kèn lukaṙ kadi mahāṅiṅin iṅin i manaḥ nṛpātmaja*

<śiꝁariṇī> ⏑– – | – – – | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | – ⏑⏑|⏑⏓

:788:\:132:\:1:. suꝁāsaṇḍiŋ saṇḍiŋ samaṅinakanèŋ citta ginawè,
sĕlaŋ māain pojaṙ saŋ Aja mawaraḥ ry antuka nira,
manaḥ dèwī kagyat gyat asĕkĕl ikaŋ twas kapĕnĕtan,
kumĕmbĕŋ kĕmbĕŋ luḥ nira mijil aṅèṙttambaŋ asayut*

:789:\:132:\:2:. sĕnĕŋ yan yogyè jöṅta wawaṛĕṅĕhĕn luhku k anaṅis,
wiraṅṙwwaŋ dè niŋ tan wĕnaŋ apasaḥ i śrī narapati,
manĕḥ rakryan‌ ndi n yogya kawĕkasa tan tūta ri kita,
mataṅnya n paṅhèṙ ṅkè kahuluna kĕnaṅkwè kita sadā*

:790:\:132:\:3:. paran kahyunantè haji pisaniṅūn tan katĕkana,
tuhun budđyantāṅhèra pakatuhanĕn māsiha siwin,
yadin muṅgwèŋ siṅhāsana pakaratun yan kita haṛĕp,
katon tan tṛṣṇā śrī nṛpati palakun kapraƀun ira*

<wisaṙjjita> – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓

:791:\:133:\:1:. yogya wuwusta tuhun‌ ṅhulun ahaṛĕp aṅuṅṣira wīṙyya guṇa,
ndātan adoha sakèŋ ibu paṛĕkĕn apan sira māsiḥ anak,
göŋ i kaƀaktin iŋ apraƀu maṅipulu ri twas akon muliha,
ṅhiŋ kita māsku rumaṅkĕpana kahulunankwi i narāṙyya raǥu*

:792:\:133:\:2:. yan muliha prihawak‌ ṅhulun ibu kita kāṙyya ri jöŋ nṛpati,
tiṅhali kāsihan iŋ huwus akuṛĕn asiḥ mara tambaṅana,
yan waluyāku muwaḥ ri kita pira piraŋ tahunĕn ḍatĕṅa,
ṅhiŋ panaṅisku lawan kita linalu ri dūra nikaŋ palagan*

:793:\:133:\:3:. mwaŋ yan anuṅgaṅa riŋ raŧa lĕpasa madoha sakèŋ nagara,
brāhmaṇa sogata śaiwa ṛṣi sira ta maṅgala niŋ lumaku,
söḥ bala śūra kuraŋ hawan aṅiriŋ arampak aṅambaḥ alas,
śūnya hiḍĕpku yatan hana kita maṅisapwana minta sĕpaḥ*

<giriṣa> ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – – – | – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:794:\:134:\:1:. priya kahiḍĕp ujaṙttārūm kady āmṛta kasirat,
kunĕŋ amuhara kèpwan ry ambĕk ni ṅhulun alawas,
ya tan asiha kitānaṅṣārāpujya tinutakĕn,
syapa ta taṅisanaṅkwa ṅhiŋ matyānaṅisi tawaŋ*

:795:\:134:\:2:. ya ta karaṇa niŋ aswī yan rakryan jĕnĕka siwin,
Iwĕḥ iŋ aniwi maṅhèṙ siḥ niŋ hyaŋ ya ta tinahā,
Atilara kita luṅhātiṅgal wanwa n alalisa,
ṅhiŋ anaṅisana ri śrī ƀoja mwaŋ nṛpamahiṣī*

:796:\:134:\:3:. taham ibu taha rakryan maṙmmāsiḥ ṅhulun atuhan,
saꝑala pinakadèwī tan wwaŋ lèn kadaŋ apaṛĕk,
sapati sahuripa ṅwaŋ sakwan sèlwan adulura,
kita pinakahuripku n sèkaprāṇa siliḥ asiḥ*

:797:\:134:\:4:. manis i wacana rakryan sāmpun kagraha ri hati,
pinakapaṅanumānan ry ambĕkta n tulus asiha,
sapara parana rakryan ƀaktyākw āṅiriṅi kita,
yadin anadina lampūn matyāśānuku riŋ awak*

:798:\:134:\:5:. ṅhulun ibu wihikan yan budđyantāwĕlas asiha,
Ika karaṇa niŋ aswī māsku n rowaṅa muliha,
nṛpati raǥu katon gyā gyā ny ambĕk nira mulata,
niyata papagĕn iŋ‌ strī sāyođyā n kita ḍatĕṅa*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓

:799:\:135:\:1:. sāmpun māyu wuwus nṛpātmaja lawan dèwī nira n maṅkata,
ṅkānè wwit niŋ aśoka rambay anaḍaḥ prāpta ŋ madaṅgāṅhaḍĕp,
luṅhā ŋ kāla huwus hyaŋ aṙka sumurup sanđyā masĕṅṣĕŋ miraḥ,
mambö kasturi niŋ patuṙwwan araras kady āṅutus mañjiṅa*

:800:\:135:\:2:. Ambĕk niŋ paḍa haṙṣa sāmpun amatĕḥ riŋ rāga soluṙ lulut,
tṛṣṇèŋ saṅgama tan kawaṙṣihan apöm māywan raras riŋ pṛĕman,
yan līlā mijil iŋ nataṙ pinanasan dè niŋ‌ smarāṅras hati,
Oṅṣil tuṅtuŋ ikaŋ halis jaruman aṅgyākĕn marā riŋ tilam*

:801:\:135:\:3:. sāmpun muṅgaḥ aṅanti riŋ pasamayan saŋ hyaŋ hyaŋ iŋ pamṛĕman,
maṙmmāsiḥ paḍa dè nirāṅĕnahi rāga ‌wruḥ ri tuṅgal nira,
Aṙwwa rwan manaḍaḥ manis niŋ upadèśātyanta riŋ rāṣika,
nora ŋ saṅśaya riŋ rahasya winĕḍaṙ kāgĕm raṣanyè hati*

:802:\:135:\:4:. saŋ raśmīnayu niŋ‌ smarāṅucap ucap riŋ pamṛĕman tan bĕsur,
sèkaprāṇa sapakṣa tan wĕnaŋ adoḥ māsiḥ sađaṙmmādulur,
prajñèŋ budđi siliḥ wikalpa ri ruṣit niŋ śabda kady ācĕṅil,
paṅliṅganya n anak sināđya nira masw aswāmiƀāwèŋ tilam*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:803:\:136:\:1:. I sāmpun iŋ ulaḥ kapintiga nikaŋ ǥaṭita kawalĕsan sirāturū,
Ikaŋ hulĕs adoḥ sakè sira lanā kawadal alulunan marèŋ dagan,
hanan pawuṅu sakṣaṇālĕḥ akaraŋ hulu taṅan aharip suputrikā,
tapiḥ nira huwus lukaṙ kasarakat kahurup i basahan nṛpātmaja*

:804:\:136:\:2:. huwus kalalu dè nirāmṛĕm asuwè paḍa tan umik aṅèl asaṅgama,
Ikaŋ manuk anaṅhi riŋ ḍawuḥ ĕnĕm suꝁa muni maṅuyūyu riŋ taman,
cucuṙ taḍahasiḥ swaranya kawĕlas haṛĕp anaṅis i paṅlwaŋ iŋ wulan,
Ikaŋ mrak akakab munīŋ gupura lagy amuṅu ri sira riŋ ḍawuḥ pitu*

:805:\:136:\:3:. paḍāśraŋ aṅajīŋ kulĕm sahana niŋ manuk anarawatāguṇèriya,
parañjaṅan aṅanti riŋ gagana paŧya tumiru tiru śabda niŋ pĕkiŋ,
I soṙṇnya hana caṅkiluŋ muni laki stṙyy asĕmu mamarahi ry anak nikā,
syapèka ta kunaŋ paṅajyan ika maṅhuwusakĕn ika yan bisāṅaji*

:806:\:136:\:4:. Awuṅw ajajaṙ iŋ surambyan arahup nṛpatanaya lawan suputrikā,
Anĕṅgaḥ atis aṅharas haraṣakĕn susu saŋ ahayu maṅṛĕṅiḥ ṛĕṅiḥ,
kataṅgamaŋ aṅolakĕn saŋ Aja maṙmma maṅĕmuli nĕhĕṙ mamaṅkwakĕn,
pupū nira kasiṅgahan hulĕs i polaḥ ira kasuluhan niśākara*

:807:\:136:\:5:. samaṅkana ni göŋ i rāga nira kāliḥ aṅisapu lawan mamaṅkwakĕn,
taŧāpi sinamantaran manis i dè nira ṅucap araras prahāsana,
saŋ adyaḥ api hèwa hèwa tuhun ambĕk ira tumiliŋ iŋ karāṣikan,
nṛpātmaja mañumbu ñumbu mamibik tapiḥ ahaṛĕp i buṅkaḥ iŋ tĕṅaḥ*

:808:\:136:\:6:. ri luṅṣuṙ i tapiḥ nirārukĕt ikaŋ luṅayan asĕmu luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,
Ikaŋ gĕlaŋ ataṅkis iŋ wĕtis apiṇḍa mađukara marāhyun iŋ puḍak,
payođara lanāpipit kadi wĕdinya kaharaṣa ri tuṅtuŋ iŋ kuku,
Ikaŋ muꝁa sawaŋ wulan maṛĕk i wimba nira sĕḍĕŋ ira n sapamṛĕman*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓

:809:\:137:\:1:. maṅkin wṛdđi wijil ni rāṣika nira n paṙwwaṙwwan iŋ pamṛĕman,
nidrācumbana ta pwa nitya ginawè maṅdè suꝁè twas nira,
söṙ mambö waṅi niŋ sĕkaṙ kadi mahā mañjiŋ mamuṅw ī sira,
tan ‌wruḥ yan rahināpaḍaŋ paḍa mijil dè niŋ hṛĕbuk niŋ puḍak*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:810:\:138:\:1:. samantaji mijil hyaŋ aṙka kadi raktakumuda sumĕkaṙ sakèŋ bañu,
wulan mari lumöŋ kagöṅan ahulap sumiṛĕp awĕdi tan wĕnaŋ mulat,
tĕkèŋ grahagaṇānusup nusup aṛĕs karahinana humöt paḍākucĕm,
Ikaŋ wĕṅi huwus paḍĕm kadi hilaŋ pinĕjahan ira riŋ ḍawuḥ wwalu*

:811:\:138:\:2:. Ikaŋ ƀuwana kālapan wĕṅi baṅun jalađi karaŋ asat ḍasaṙ nika,
katon awas ikaŋ gunuŋ kadi timiṅgila makatihalaŋ paḍāṅjĕlag,
Urut saka satal kumĕṇḍĕŋ ajajaṙ paḍa paḍa kadi nāga maṅlayaŋ,
muni ŋ jalada maṅṛĕguŋ sagajamīna kasatan aṅuliŋ haṛĕp bañu*

<puṣpacāpa> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| – ⏓

:812:\:139:\:1:. ri wwit niŋ kayu pārijāta hana tīṙŧālantaran wwad kucuṙṇnya,
tūsanyānalagājajaṙ watu karaṅnyāgroŋ rinoŋ pañcuranya,
tampyak tampyakan iŋ wĕṛĕḥ pamarigi lwiṙṇnya n patap dè nikaŋ ryak,
wwainyāƀrā kadi saṙwwawaṙṇna ri sĕḍĕŋ niŋ puṣpamāyā hanè jro*

:813:\:139:\:2:. ṅkā dèwī marahup rahup sira yaŧālīlāṅuḍoḍāñawuk wwai,
tan saḥ śrī naranāŧaputra maṅĕmit lwiṙ kumbaŋ aṅrakṣa kĕmbaŋ,
‌wruḥ riŋ cāmana pītṛtaṙppaṇa satiṅkaḥ tiṅkaḥ iŋ tīṙŧayātra,
mādĕg pūṙwwamuꝁājajaṙ paṛĕŋ amūjāṅañjalī saŋ hyaŋ Aṙka*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓

:814:\:140:\:1:. mantuk śīǥra marè dalĕm humatuṙ i śrī ƀoja riŋ pamṛĕman,
Akwèḥ strī haji samƀramè tĕka nirāganty āṅucap gaṙjjita,
maṙmma śrī paramèśwarī mulat anuṅṣuŋ cumbu cumbw āṅucap,
Ī ī śrī maṇik i ṅhulun sira ḍatĕŋ kāliḥ nihan liŋ nira*

:815:\:140:\:2:. śrī dèwīndumatī paṛĕŋ sira manĕmbaḥ mwaŋ narāṙyyātmaja,
riŋ lampit hana siṅhacaṙmma humaḍaŋ kāna n pratiṣṫāraṛĕm,
saŋ nāŧa ‌wruḥ i don ira n para wawaŋ śoka drawa twas nira,
Amwit sādara sopacāra saŋ Ajānĕmbaḥ ri jöŋ saŋ praƀu*

<kilayu> Anĕḍĕŋ – – ⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑–| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏓

:816:\:141:\:1:. sĕmbaḥ niŋ aśaraṇa ri jöŋ narèndra huniṅan paṛĕk i narapati,
Amwīta muliha satatāṅriwĕg riwĕgi tan bĕsuṙ amaribini,
tan sĕṅgahĕn akalis i pāda saŋ praƀu pasaŋ kuhira pinahayu,
paṅgil wĕnaṅa dadaha riŋ raṇāṅhaṛĕpa śatrukula yan iŋ ayun*

:817:\:141:\:2:. Om ‌wruḥ ṅhulun ika mara hètu niŋ kahĕnĕṅan kapĕgan aṅucapa,
māsiḥ ṅhulun iri kita moǥa tan wĕnaŋ asiḥ karaṇa niŋ asĕkĕl,
maṅkè n mulat iri kita tan palèkan aṅĕḍap muliḥ analahasa,
wahw āpupul alal alawas tĕka pwa kita sakṣaṇa wawaŋ apasaḥ*

:818:\:141:\:3:. pintaṅkwi i kita bapa sihanta tan kapalaṅāmipila riŋ agati,
saṅkan raray uwuḥ uwuḥ ūpamānĕn iŋ ulaḥ kasiḥ aṛĕp alawas,
maṅkè n maṛĕk iri kita sanmatan kawiguṇanya tan ucap ucapĕn,
Aṅhiŋ pakadaṅan i bapaṅku tolihĕn i māsku laki pakatalin*

:819:\:141:\:4:. nwam ny ambĕk ika mĕṅĕ mĕṅö kalotakĕna dènta kajugulan ikā,
tan ‌wruhnya riŋ aṅinakanè mulat pipili dènta pituturi piṅit,
saṅkṣèpa nika kita waśa pramāṇa guṇadoṣa nika wawaṛĕṅöḥ,
yadyastun iwĕŋ iwĕṅa riŋ hulun bapa manahnya palu palu waraḥ*

:820:\:141:\:5:. Atwaŋ saŋ Aja sumahuṙ apraṇamya rumuhun saha manis iŋ ujar,
Ājñā nṛpati raṣa nirāwĕkas wĕkas akon siliḥ asiha sadā,
sāmpun kaṛĕgĕp i hati dè patik haji minuṣṭi maṅinaki hati,
ṅhiŋ gānya n apasaha ri tan siḥ iŋ wiđi haṛĕp mulata riŋ alara*

:821:\:141:\:6:. Atyanta hĕla hĕla niŋ aṅṛĕṅö wacana rakryan aṅinaki hati,
niṙwwiǥna kita bapa tĕkèŋ sināđya wĕnaŋ uṅṣiṛĕn iŋ aśaraṇa,
śānti dwijawara ri bapaṅku kèsyana tumiṙwwa narapati raǥu,
swasty astu saha tanaya dāra māsku saŋ anĕmwa jayaꝑala sadā*

:822:\:141:\:7:. mwaŋ yan pawuwuha kita ǥāra pat lima sujanma wĕka wĕka ratu,
tan doṣa tumĕkakĕna sāmbĕk iŋ wĕnaŋ amukti wiṣaya saꝑala,
ndan haywa sira ta bapa kāri dènta pakamaṅgala niŋ anakbi,
yogya n kalĕwihakĕna tan paḍan ꝑala nikāṅurati kahulunan*

:823:\:141:\:8:. tĕmbè ŋ śuƀadiwasa bapaṅku maṅkata kakanta maṅatĕrakĕna,
jyotīṣa paḍa tinañan i ṅhulun wiṅi ri kāla nira paḍa maṛĕk,
Awyāhata pawaraḥ irāpadohan atukaṙ paḍa kamasĕṅĕṛĕn,
saŋ lèkan aṅucap apagĕḥ tuwin binisa kāraṇa niŋ amituhu*

:824:\:141:\:9:. yèkī muwaḥ ucapakĕnè  bapaṅku sahajālupa kamitutuṛĕn,
dūmĕn sahana hana ni dṛwya dṛwya haji dèwata tĕka tĕkanĕn,
lāwan sahana hana nikaŋ rarè kawula rakryan aṅalapa muwaḥ,
yadyan jĕnĕka kita bapaṅku pālihĕn ikaŋ nagara kaliliran*

:825:\:141:\:10:. nāhan paṅucap ucap ira lwiṙ amṛĕta hañaṙ mĕtu siniratakĕn,
maṅdadyakĕn i suꝁa narèndraputra kalawan nṛpawaraduhitā,
kèsyan raṣa ni manis i dè nirāṅucap arūm asĕmu gula siṅī,
ƀèda mwaŋ ujaṙ amanis iŋ pralāpita namun ṛĕcĕpa raṣa nikā*

:826:\:141:\:11:. kañcit paḍa tĕka maduluṙ sirèŋ pagaḍuhan maṛĕk i narapati,
sakwèḥ ni kĕmitan ika mās maṇik pirak ikā ya tinañakĕn ira,
yèka n pamaca padadaran tĕlas pwa ya samaṅkana winijalakĕn,
kaśraḥ satĕṅaḥ i naranāŧaputra kalawan nṛpawaraduhitā*

:827:\:141:\:12:. nantĕn samĕgĕt aniga muꝁya sāra ginulaŋ halu makĕmitana,
mwaŋ dṛwya pahula naranāŧa sojaṙ i narèndra paḍa sinuṅakĕn,
lāwan muwaḥ anĕkakĕnèṙyy Ayođyanagarī tumuta ri saŋ Aja,
Āpan wĕnaŋ akun iŋ ulaḥ prayatna wĕka sāđu wĕka niŋ aniga*

:828:\:141:\:13:. dum dūman ira pira kunaŋ wilaṅnya kadi tan kawĕnaṅa wilaṅĕn,
yadyan banawa saha bahitra dūra wĕnaṅāmwata niyata sarat,
muṅgw iŋ raŧa pira pira taŋ raŧèŋ nagara hĕnti paḍa hinibĕkan,
wastrādi pinada pinadāti pādadara tan wuruŋ apan adadar*

:829:\:141:\:14:. ndātan caritan ulaḥ irānaḍaḥ ri huwus iŋ wwalu wahu ḍumawuḥ,
tan saḥ uwa nira kalawan sirèña nira muꝁya niŋ aṅiriṅakĕn,
sāmpun praṇata sira paḍāṅadĕg muliḥ i pamṛĕman ira ri dalĕm,
sakwèḥ ni hulun ira kinon madandana paḍāgarawalan ataña*

:830:\:141:\:15:. dèwī sira maṅutus aniṅka niṅkaḥ i sadṛwya nira pinahayu,
norāhala hala kalasā tinon kinajaṅan winalunan ahalĕp,
Akwèḥ papiku pikul irāpupul kawula dāsa kaliliran ira,
boṇḍan sajuru lawan ikaŋ pujut sajuru jĕṅgi sajuru humaḍaŋ*

:831:\:141:\:16:. wyāpāra sahana hana niŋ wwaŋ iŋ nagara tan hana maṅinak inak,
kady āsawuṅan asipĕt olaḥ olaḥ adamaṙ damaṙ amalaku duḥ,
cèṭī rumara rara paḍāṅasū wija wijaḥ dudu taŋ amususi,
siṅgoḥ ya humuŋ asahuran baṅun śakaṭa gumrit amuhara laṅö*

:832:\:141:\:17:. guṇḍik kaka kaka mawiwèka pahyas ikaŋ èndaha tan awanĕha,
lagy āminĕkĕti hayu tuṅgal ĕmbulana tan hana niŋ amihaṅa,
ṅhiŋ raṇḍi dadaṙ ika kabèḥ kahaywakĕna don ika pinagĕhakĕn,
dènyāmahāyu sipat ināptyakĕn pinakadaṙśana tiniru tiru*

:833:\:141:\:18:. sāmpun ǥaṭita pitu tibā putiḥ timuṙ ikāwawa rahina mijil,
Āƀā ni pawuṅu naranāŧaputra kaṛĕṅö piliḥ anuculi kèn,
dèwī kadi kahĕnĕkan aśriŋ ambĕkan irāṣahuran aṅĕsĕsan,
Ākāra ni hĕnĕŋ ira mèḥ tigaŋ paṅinaṅāwuṅu mijil adamu*

:834:\:141:\:19:. dèwī sira pinahayu hinyasan pinahawās kadi maluya rarā,
dūran wĕnaṅa paṅanumānanè huwus irāpriya luṅayan ira,
lāwan mata waja nira tan wĕnaŋ pinakaliṅga ni pasawi nira,
ṅhiŋ mājaṙ i huwus ira mèdĕman susu nirè kiwa kani kakuku*

<basantatilaka> – – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓

:835:\:142:\:1:. sāmpun sirāhyas asalin hima puṣpawaṙṣa,
dodot narèndraṣuta rakwa kilat rinĕṅga,
Āsĕṅka niŋ mulat i rūpa narèndraputrī,
putrī sakèŋ surapadānĕmu rājaputra*

:836:\:142:\:2:. prāṣāda ratnamaya muṅgw i dalĕm kaḍatwan,
ḍaŋ hyaŋ purohita sirèniriŋ iŋ pamūjā,
ǥaṇṭālaṅö đwani nikā saha pūja pūjān,
śaṅꝁa lwiṙ asyaŋ aṅuhuḥ ri narèndraputra*

:837:\:142:\:3:. sāmpun ḍatĕŋ nṛpatiputra lawan suputrī,
ganđākṣatādi humaḍaŋ kalawan niwèdya,
mañjiŋ sirè dalĕm aṅaṙppaṇakĕn pamūjā,
Amwīt i wimba haji dèwata ƀakty anĕmbaḥ*

:838:\:142:\:4:. dèwī sirāmĕkul i jöŋ nira saŋ hyaŋ aṙcca,
Aṙṇnaḥ manaḥ nira sadāṅaku rāma rèna,
glānānaṅis kasiḥ aṛĕp twas ira wyamoha,
sambat nirāmuhara luḥ pamĕlas haṛĕpnya*

:839:\:142:\:5:. Ꜽ rāma rèna kita saŋ lumaḥ iŋ kaḍatwan,
ṅūni n maṇusya kita kaṙwwa bapèbu liṅku,
maṅkè dadi hyaŋ inalĕmbana sāṙdđadèha,
hā hāḥ yayā bapa hajību hajīki liṅku*

:840:\:142:\:6:. ndā t aṅṛĕṅö bapa hajību hajī taṅisku,
pamwitku tiṅhali sumambaḥ i pādukanta,
Āḍā wĕkasku mulatī kita tèki maṅkè,
rakṣan‌ ṅhulun bapa hajību hajī paranku*

:841:\:142:\:7:. nāhan taṅis taṅis irālara wāhu mantĕn,
milw ānaṅis nṛpatiputra nĕhĕṙ tumuṅkul,
lāwan hyaŋ aṙcca pakatonan irèpu winwit,
dè niŋ śiwāmƀa ri muꝁāsĕmu luḥ drawādṛĕs*

:842:\:142:\:8:. sāmpun mijil nṛpatiputra lawan suputrī,
prāptè narèndra mahiṣī tumuluy sirāṅliŋ,
kĕmbĕŋ ni luḥ nira panuṅṣuŋ irè suputrī,
dè niŋ sĕkĕl sapaṅucap nira tan sꝑuṭāsṛĕt*

:843:\:142:\:9:. māskw ību haywa kita tan praṇatā suƀakti,
I swāmi rakryan apan uttamarājaputra,
Āsiŋ sakahyun ira tūtakĕnanta māsku,
yèkā patibrata ṅaranya pakabratanta*

:844:\:142:\:10:. mwaŋ haywa māsku paṅayāya karājaputṙyyan,
lāwan hayunta wiꝑala n pakapaṅhaḍanta,
tan kwèḥ ni māsta makapaṅgajahanta māsku,
kakṣatriyanta maniwību pakātmarakṣa*

:845:\:142:\:11:. lāwan muwaḥ saŋ Aja haywa bapaṅkw atiṅgal,
I śrī narèndraduhitā paḍa wastu māsku,
riŋ rūpa sampĕlaḥ awaṙṇna sĕkaṙ pināliḥ,
prāṇanta tuṅgalakĕnanta maran tan imbā*

:846:\:142:\:12:. tan kètaka ŋ puḍak adoha ri ṣaṭpadanya,
tan ṣaṭpada ŋ ƀramara sāha sakè puḍaknya,
tan putrikā sarika yan taya rājaputra,
tan rājaputra kita yan taya rājaputrī*

:847:\:142:\:13:. nā liŋ narèndramahiṣī n panaṅis sumuṅkĕm,
I śrī narèndraduhitā pinĕkul siniṅṣĕt,
Akwèḥ mulat kapitaṅis ri narèndraputrī,
Āpan wĕkas nira katon ri widaṙƀarājya*

:848:\:142:\:14:. Èmbuḥ taṅis ri pataṅis taṅisan suputrī,
dè niŋ swawanđu nira söḥ atuluŋ bwat iŋ luḥ,
prāptāmalandani pirak maṇi wastu mūlya,
lèn taŋ sĕṛĕḥ kinajaṅan saha modakādi*

<dođakawṛtta> – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏓

:849:\:143:\:1:. śrī nṛpaputra lawan nṛpaputrī,
Amwit anĕmbaḥ i jöŋ mahādèwī,
maṙyy ataṅis taṅisan paḍa līlā,
śèṣa ni luḥ nira mātra kumĕmbĕŋ*

:850:\:143:\:2:. maṙmma dahat paṅucap mahādèwī,
Om bapa saŋ makapunpunana ŋ rāt,
sora samāpta para praƀu dènta,
śrī raǥu māsku tirunta jayèŋ praŋ*

:851:\:143:\:3:. śrīndumatību huripku kitāntĕn,
moǥa katĕmwa suꝁanta dadi strī,
rowaṅa rakryan/ Ajāsisihan siḥ,
tuṅgalĕn apriya riŋ nṛpaputra*

:852:\:143:\:4:. sāmpun ira n paṅucap mahādèwī,
śrīndumatī kalawan nṛpaputra,
mādĕg inumbalan iŋ paricārī,
maṅkat awaṙṇna śaśāṅka kamèǥan*

:853:\:143:\:5:. kīṙṇna tikaŋ pamikul  pikul akwèḥ,
dènya lumampaḥ arampak apaṇṭa,
nora jaruḥ wihikan ri duluṙṇnya,
yogya katiṅhalanāpan atiṅkaḥ*

:854:\:143:\:6:. maṅkana taŋ raŧa nora kagiṇḍal,
mèww iwu lampaḥ ikādĕdĕṙ adṛĕs,
dṛwya narèndraṣutā winawanya,
mās maṇi lèn rajatādi suwastra*

:855:\:143:\:7:. salwiṙ ikaŋ paḍahīŋ nagarāśraŋ,
ramya tĕkapnya hanan sinamèni,
lèn masarag makapaṅhaḍa göṅnya,
lwiṙ kĕtug iŋ lĕwu dènya gumĕntĕr*

:856:\:143:\:8:. śrīndumatī siwuhĕn sira luṅhā,
dè ni lulut nira riŋ nṛpadèwī,
lūḥ ira tan pĕgat adṛĕs awantu,
śrī nṛpaputra kaṅèlan amèri*

:857:\:143:\:9:. muṅgw irikaŋ kapiṅan sira kāliḥ,
ramya katonan irāpan awèlā,
lwiṙ kawĕlad twas ikaŋ wwaŋ aniñjo,
ƀakti mamakpak aṅañjali māsiḥ*

:858:\:143:\:10:. maṙmma nira n mari sukṣĕka rañca,
rūm saŋ Ajāṅhari haṙyy aṅalap sor,
mwaŋ jayawaspa wicakṣaṇa tan saḥ,
māṙyy aputĕk sira rakwa tumon ya*

:859:\:143:\:11:. strī ri dalĕm nagarāṛĕja pantĕs,
mātus atus paḍa maṙmma raraṣnya,
kocap anampikakĕn sĕkaṙ aṅjraḥ,
milw aṅiriŋ ri narèśwaraputrī*

:860:\:143:\:12:. kādƀuta lampaḥ iraŋ nṛpaputrī,
dè ni halĕp para guṇḍik atiṅkaḥ,
wastra nikā paḍa raṇḍi sapaṇṭa,
lwiṙ kusumānĕḍĕŋ iŋ pratimāsa*

:861:\:143:\:13:. śrī naranāŧa tumūt saha mantrī,
söḥ aṅiriŋ paḍa śūra wanīŋ praŋ,
mèww iwu lakṣa sahaśra kumĕṇḍĕŋ,
lwiṙ paṅawak nikaŋ antaka sākṣāt*

:862:\:143:\:14:. śrī naranāŧasutā sira śoka,
sis kamatolihĕn iŋ nṛpadèwī,
wāhu lipuṙ tumuluy sira monaŋ,
luḥ nira lāgi kumĕmbĕŋ asowè*

:863:\:143:\:15:. sāmpun ira n lĕpas iŋ kuṭa wètan,
toliḥ ikaŋ nagarāṣĕpi tistis,
kaywan ikā manirāṅaway aśriŋ,
kady aṅutus maluyè sira kāliḥ*

:864:\:143:\:16:. ramya nikaŋ kahawan sawaḥ alwā,
maṅdadi ƀasma daminya tinunwan,
ṣaṭpada muṅgw i sĕkaṙ ni wuruṅnya,
lwiṙ kawi māsiḥ aǥāra daridra*

:865:\:143:\:17:. ndan sadawā ni hĕnu nira ramya,
sontĕn ikaŋ jawuḥ adṛĕs asowè,
śīǥra pucuk ni tĕkinya tumūwuḥ,
waṙṇna nikā kadi campaka siṅṣal*

<wisaṙjjita> – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓

:866:\:144:\:1:. kīṙṇna katon wijil iŋ laru laru kumukus kadi tan lĕwasa,
haṙṣa sirèña nira mwaŋ uwa nira riwönya katon aṅĕliḥ,
mwaŋ para guṇḍik amupw awurahan aṛĕbut paḍa budđi rarè,
śrīndumatī maṛĕk iŋ nṛpasuta suꝁa haṙṣa sirāmawani*

:867:\:144:\:2:. hyaŋ rawi tumraŋ ikaŋ walaŋ aṅariŋ ariŋ makamūla ŋ atis,
cumbw i rabinya maṛĕk nĕhĕṙ aṅĕpĕṙ uninya kaṛĕṅw araras,
strīnya kumöl inaras haras anarima solaḥ ulaḥ niŋ akuŋ,
saŋ rwa mulat maṛĕn ahyun aṅalapa tumon i wilāsa nikā*

:868:\:144:\:3:. moǥa jĕnĕk sira dè ni paṅaraman ikaŋ bañu wāhu ḍatĕŋ,
katkat aliwran amèt walaŋ asira siran kalawan dadali,
Aṅlĕṅĕṅi twas irèka ta karaṇa nirāṣṛĕt alon lumaku,
lālana lagy anĕpĕṙ nĕpĕri sĕkaṙ arūm kadi mitra kadaŋ*

:869:\:144:\:4:. lampaḥ irātut ayun tinutakĕn iŋ aṅin saha mèǥa ṛĕmĕŋ,
lwiṙ makadoṣa laṅö nira sahasa manĕmpal aśoka liman,
hinṛĕt i kĕmbaŋ ikaŋ gaḍuŋ anĕḍĕŋ analyani budđi nira,
riŋ wĕkasan dinudut ni karas ira nimitta nira n lumaku*

:870:\:144:\:5:. lwaḥ laraṅan kahalintaṅan asat apirak pirakan gumĕlar,
waḥ kayu mās ri tĕpinya salak apupul awwaḥ atöb anĕḍĕŋ,
nista nika n sugiḥ iŋ kalĕṅĕṅan atĕṅö tuwi tan papaḍa,
wwatnya katiṅgal adoḥ anĕmu maru hĕnū pamĕnĕṙ mĕnĕran*

:871:\:144:\:6:. piṅgiṙ ikaŋ pagagan harata hara hara n pamuraŋ muraṅan,
luñcip ikaŋ rwi kulampis i pagĕṙ ika waṙṇna tanaḥ kinikir,
wwaḥ ni saganya baṅun mata hañaṙ asipat pinuyuṙ puyuran,
daṅdaṅan aṅgarit iŋ wĕtis aniru kuriñjĕm umuṅgw i pipi*

:872:\:144:\:7:. sīma kawaṅśan alas juraŋ anasarakĕn sinĕpĕṙ sĕpĕran,
saṅkawilanya mañaṇḍĕt i ruṣit i hĕnūnya lawan wadara,
mĕṅgĕp arūm araras gaḍuŋ ika katĕkan tuha milw amilĕt,
budđi nikā wilut aṅduhuṅakĕn apituwy aḍaḍap wwaŋ agöŋ*

<jagadnāŧa> ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:873:\:145:\:1:. taṅèḥ yan ucapĕn kalaṅwan i hĕnū nira kadi nawanāṭya niŋ kawi,
wimūṙcꞓa para guṇḍik aṅṛĕṅi ṛĕṅiḥ para kaka kaka śoka kaṅlihan,
katuhwan iŋ apa n tan apriha sukunya wahu lumaku lakw adoḥ dahat,
sirèña nira lèn uwā nira paḍākĕsĕl awak ira muṅgu riŋ raŧa*

:874:\:145:\:2:. I tan wĕnaŋ ikā lumampaḥ awĕḍak suku binĕbĕd ikèŋ kajaṙ kajar,
baṅun surawađū paḍādarupa kady anapaka gagana n tiniṅhalan,
tuhun suꝁa manahnya riŋ wĕkasan èṅgal asĕmu guyu māri suṅkawa,
Ikaŋ magiliṅan kajātaka paḍāmawa giliṅan inājña mamwata*

:875:\:145:\:3:. tigaŋ wĕṅi sirāṅinĕp nṛpati mamwit i saŋ Aja lawan nṛpātmajā,
I pāntaran ikaŋ wukiṙ hiṅan irāṅatĕrakĕn i narèśwarātmajā,
maluy sira lawan gajāśwa raŧa tan hana hiḍĕp ira wanya wāđakā,
narèndratanayānaṅis nṛpatiputra salahasa tumon kamānuṣan*

:876:\:145:\:4:. muwaḥ nṛpatiputra maṅkat aṅusī pakulĕmana nira wwaŋ iŋ pasir,
karaŋ karaṅan èndaḥ èndaḥ alaṅö hinaturakĕn ikā lawan sayub,
paḍānrik aṅinum twak iŋ pasisi saŋ watĕk/ Aja karuhun nṛpātmaja,
ƀaṭāra baruṇāṅaliḥ nagara rūpa nira wahu mijil sakèŋ tasik*

:877:\:145:\:5:. riŋ èñjiŋ i wijil hyaŋ aṙka sira maṅkat aduluṙ ahawan gunuŋ gunuŋ,
huwus tĕka sirèrikaŋ pĕkĕn agöŋ sĕḍĕŋ amĕpĕg ikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ pĕkĕn,
Ikaŋ baṇija saṅśayānaha nahā ri patukara narèśwarātmaja,
lawan sahana saŋ watĕk ratu kabèḥ rumĕbuta ri narèndraputrikā*

:878:\:145:\:6:. mpu rāma humatuṙ marè saŋ Aja sādara tĕkap ika mojaṙ apṛĕgi,
tuhanku bapa sugya tan ‌wruha bapaṅku ri hana nira saŋ watĕk ratu,
ry uliḥ nira sakèŋ swayĕmbara paḍāpupul amaṛĕki dèśa duṙggama,
kunaŋ bapa panaṙka naṙka ni manĕhta kadi rumĕbutè suputrikā*

:879:\:145:\:7:. putus mara lĕbā nikaŋ tĕgal ayun palapat alas alas gunuŋ gunuŋ,
taŧāpi paḍa söḥ kinuwwan arupĕk wĕkasan asalĕsĕk tĕkèŋ juraŋ,
dudū sawĕṅi saṅṣayāwuwuḥ ikaŋ gaja raŧa saha sañjatāsinaŋ,
mataṅnya bapa yatna yatna tuhan i ṅhulun apupula haywa wismṛti*

:880:\:145:\:8:. nahan wuwus ikā nṛpātmaja wawaŋ sumahuṙ asĕmu siṅha kātara,
mpu rāma tak anāgatākwi iriya yadyan awuwuha muwaḥ samaṅkana,
muwaḥ yadin amèta daitya saha dānawa pakaśaraṇanya riŋ raṇa,
hadè raǥusutāku tak sy Aja ṅaranya yak atakuta riŋ samaṅkana*

:881:\:145:\:9:. samantaji ḍatĕŋ hulun nṛpatiputra sahana nikaŋ aṅruhun ruhun,
kanin rujit awaknya maṅhaturakĕn śiraḥ apan arujit nĕhĕṙ murud,
ya tājaṙ i narèndraputra saha cihna ṛĕsĕp i hati dè nikāṅucap,
Alap ta wus amaḥ nahan liŋ ikanaŋ wani wani karuhun nṛpātmaja*

:882:\:145:\:10:. I sāmpun ira muṅgaḥ iŋ raŧa tumūt nṛpawaraduhitā hanè wuri,
pasaṅǥa ni surak watĕk raǥusutāmaji taliṅa nikaŋ wwaŋ aṅṛĕṅö,
linūd i kĕtug iŋ gubaṙ saha garantuŋ uni nika kaṛĕṅw aṅalw alö,
Ikaŋ wwaŋ apĕkĕn pĕkĕn gumuruḥ awṛĕg inawaran i dūta niŋ musuḥ*

<mèǥawitānā> ⏑⏑– |⏑⏑– |⏑⏑– | ⏓

:883:\:146:\:1:. tucapa ŋ kahawan paḍa yatna,
wihikan ri manaḥ para nāŧa,
sahasāṅṛĕbutè nṛpaputrī,
saŋ Aja prihĕn iŋ raṇamađya*

:884:\:146:\:2:. juru sāmya ḍatĕŋ paṅatagnya,
I samāṅjuru lèn para duhwan,
paḍa samƀrama maṙmma paḍāgya,
Anabĕḥ kukulan makapĕṇṭok*

:885:\:146:\:3:. pamajānwam anaṇḍaŋ agasyak,
wahu wahw akuṛĕn paḍa māsiḥ,
kamĕnanya lumakwa masaṇḍiŋ,
hana budđi nikāmwit akāṙyya*

:886:\:146:\:4:. juru tuṅgul añumbw i rabinya,
Ibu puñcawali n pĕjaha ṅwaŋ,
pĕraṅĕn ri jajaṅku kitāntĕn,
mila liŋ ni rabinya tan aṅgā*

:887:\:146:\:5:. widu milw ahaṛĕp tumutāpraŋ,
wĕdi wĕdy aṅabuk prawalanya,
I hilaŋ ni galahnya salaḥ ṅgwan,
tinañākĕn ikè pagaḍaynya*

:888:\:146:\:6:. saŋ ibu nya paran di galahku,
hana riŋ paḍaṅan ya hikā ya,
Aŋ usĕn laku t āsaḥ iri ŋ lwaḥ,
mata maḥ laku hè pira dohè*

:889:\:146:\:7:. ndi wahosku paran di wahosku,
mbruta pèt‌ ndi pamètana siŋ sī,
syapa ta ‌wruha takwanakĕn sī,
Aḥ aḥ aḥ sy apĕṅiŋ kadi wāni*

:890:\:146:\:8:. Alupāku paran pwa katiṅgal,
ri sĕḍĕṅta siliḥ galaḥ oliḥ,
kawĕkas ni wĕtis ni lawanta,
si ḍulīka paṅènak uwanya*

:891:\:146:\:9:. Atutuṙ wĕkasan sy aku maṅkè,
pañukilku hapū maḥ asaḥ ñèn,
mapa yan guruwindakĕnanta,
paṅupaḥ tĕlu mās aḍug induŋ*

:892:\:146:\:10:. ndi juluk julukuṅku dalampat,
hana riŋ lwaḥ anakta si maṅdyus,
A dĕlit ny anak iŋ wani riŋ praŋ,
baribin pa ya tan tuhu hāḥ ñwak*

:893:\:146:\:11:. ndwa sĕṛĕḥ ndi ta polihanaṅkwa,
ndi pupuk ni hucu n kinaṅĕṅkwa,
maḥ alap haḍug ību taluhnya,
ndwa kamal ḍiḍikan hibu rakryan*

:894:\:146:\:12:. laku t aṅkat amaḥ bĕkĕlanta,
ndwa ta sī mapa liṅta malīya,
ndwa ta sī mapa hāḥ hapi tan ‌wruḥ,
ndwa ta sī si putiḥ pisanè wus*

:895:\:146:\:13:. ya tikā paṅucap si jaṛĕmpu,
Aṅadĕg ya maṅundurakĕn wwaŋ,
gumadā wĕsi tèki galahnya,
pinikulnya nĕhĕṙ mĕtu aig lĕs*

:896:\:146:\:14:. para sāmya paḍāpṛĕgi maṅkat,
muni goṅnya lawan paḍahinya,
saha sañjata söḥ ri tĕgalnya,
papupulnya salakṣa sinākĕn*

:897:\:146:\:15:. tĕka śīǥra ri jöŋ nṛpaputra,
sira muṅgw irikaŋ raŧa ratna,
I katon ira dènya madandan,
humatuṙ saha tuṅgul anĕmbaḥ*

:898:\:146:\:16:. sĕmu haṙṣa sirè para sāmya,
kadi wanwa tĕkap nira n aṅliŋ,
Uƀayè panunasnya macatwa,
paḍa maṅdaśamāsa catunya*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:899:\:147:\:1:. śīǥrādandan kinon dè saŋ Aja maṛĕka lumrā katon sañjatanya,
Āpan prāpta ŋ musuḥ sāhasa waragaŋ ikā krūra tan paṅgalaŋ twas,
sakwèḥ niŋ śūra śūra ŋ watĕk/ Aja kumutug söŋ ikaŋ krođabahni,
gut gūtĕn tan panaṅgĕl tṛṇa hiḍĕp ira riŋ sañjatākṛĕp lumaṅkuŋ*

:900:\:147:\:2:. sakwèḥ niŋ‌ strī makādi nṛĕpawaraduhitā muṅgu riŋ dèśa duṙgga,
mwaŋ salwiṙ niŋ raŧāmwat pahula haji lawan dṛwya rakryan suputrī,
līlānon tan tinon śrī nṛpawaraduhitā dè nikaŋ kaywa kaywan,
tĕkwan salwā nikaŋ papraṅana kalihatan koṅkulan tan pawiǥna*

:901:\:147:\:3:. mojaṙ saŋ mambaŋ iŋ śrī raǥusuta bapa haywāta tan yatna yatna,
haywècꞓāpan musuhtāṅdaśaguṇa ri wilaṅtèŋ mahāpadmasanꝁya,
loṙ kulwan wètan akwèḥ tumut i paṅuliliŋ niŋ gunuŋ söḥ lumaṅkuŋ,
wadwāntāṅhiŋ wijilnya n paṅayat ayat i göŋ niŋ praƀāwanta riŋ praŋ*

:902:\:147:\:4:. ndā nahan śrī mahārāja magađapati kady ānĕṅaḥ riŋ samudra,
Āpan sāmantarājākĕmit i sira lawan rājaputra prawīra,
ratnāyw aywan lawan mās raŧa nira kumĕñaṙ katraṅan dè hyaŋ aṙka,
śwètākārāhalĕp ꞓattra nira kadi halĕp niŋ wulan tan kamèǥan*

:903:\:147:\:5:. paṙṇnaḥ kulwan saŋ Aṅgāđipati kadi kilat niŋ truḥ iŋ kāla sanđyā,
dè niŋ saṙwwāstra muṅgw ī hiriṅan ira pĕtĕŋ lwiṙ hudan tan pamèǥa,
lāwan mātaṅga mèww īwu kadi gunuŋ apuy dè ni ṛĕṅganya kumram,
Aṅlīlānuṅgaŋ iŋ ratnaraŧa sira hanè wwit nikaŋ pārijāta*

:904:\:147:\:6:. nāhan taŋ bāṇa sālas kadi sinaliwaḥ iŋ campakāṅjraḥ sĕkaṙṇnya,
Akwèḥ wīrāṅṛĕṛĕb‌ ṅkāna saha gaja turaṅgāwakīww īwu lakṣa,
honyè wwit niŋ susantĕn raŧa kanaka rinĕṅgan maṇī hīrabajra,
Uṅgwan śṙyy āwantināŧādƀuta bapa kadi digdāha niŋ kāla sanđyā*

:905:\:147:\:7:. ndaḥ nāhan śrī pratīpāṅadĕg amawa laras riŋ raŧāṅdandani hrū,
Akwèḥ wadwā nirātumpuk awuwuḥ i haṛĕp maṅṛĕgĕp sañjatanya,
lwiṙ priŋ sālas galaḥ niŋ prajurit ira wahosnyānamaṙ mèǥa mĕṇḍuŋ,
maṅdè ṛĕs niŋ tumiṅhal raṅin i bala nira n lwiṙ gĕlap tan pawaṙṣa*

:906:\:147:\:8:. lamban loṙ saŋ susènā saha bala kadi siṅhāsigāsiṅhanāda,
salwiṙ niŋ sañjatālas nira pinakaguhā rūpa niŋ hastiṛĕṅga,
wyāǥrāṅjuṙww āpupul tiṅkaḥ i bala nira muṅgw ī haṛĕp sāra śūra,
budđinyāsiŋ musuḥ kèwala dĕmakĕn ikā pawwatanyè narèndra*

:907:\:147:\:9:. nā saŋ hèmāṅgadāḍĕm sawatĕk ira kabèḥ riŋ kĕpuḥ rambay akṛĕp,
tan pèndaḥ rākṣasa mwaŋ bala nira kadi daityāṅuhuḥ sāri sāri,
solahnya n kādƀutāsañjata baḍama lawan laṇḍĕsanya n pamöki,
Agyāmūkèŋ musuḥ sāsinĕsĕb ika turuŋ matya laṅgan ya rahnya*

:908:\:147:\:10:. paṙṇnaḥ wètan walū mwaŋ karamayan aṅurambat marèŋ siṅkṣapāgöŋ,
saŋ pāṇḍyāṅhöb kaṛĕsṛĕs kagiri giri baṅun rāja ƀūtātirodra,
wadwā pèkāsĕmu prèta hana kadi piśācālapā raḥ paḍāṅhruk,
Agyā gyān apraṅāgyāṅrujaka hati nikaŋ śūra sāmpun pinökan*

:909:\:147:\:11:. nā liŋ saŋ mambaŋ ojaṙ saŋ Aja mijil ikaŋ budđi kakṣatriyāṅśan,
siṅgiḥ kwèḥ niŋ musuḥ liṅta kadi jalađi bahny atrigañcāṅgaluntaŋ,
ndātan waŋ mātra wĕdy āku dan irika kabèḥ mon patambĕḥ samāna,
siṅhāṅantī guhā byūha nika surupi wūk hĕntyakĕn hīnaśakti*

:910:\:147:\:12:. nāhan liŋ saŋ narāṙyyātmaja kadi sinaṅa twas nirāṣĕṅhit apriḥ,
tan saḥ saŋ mambaŋ āpan maṛĕk añamarani mwaŋ kawi ḍaṇḍanīti,
siṅgiḥ yan putra niŋ śakti saŋ Aja katĕṅĕṙ krūraṣiṅhāwamāna,
Agyāmūkèŋ musuḥ duṣṭa kamadan ika śīṙṇnan marapwan panĕmbaḥ*

:911:\:147:\:13:. sākṣāt hyaŋ niŋ đanuṙwwèda saŋ Aja sakala n pāwak iŋ đaṙmmayudđa,
raktākārākiris wastra nira kilat i sub niŋ praŋ aśriŋ larapnya,
saṅkèŋ swaṙggānurun cāmara nira kumĕlab roma niŋ saṙwwakadga,
saṅhub niŋ sañjatāḍĕm pinakapayuŋ irāntuk niŋ aṅdaṇḍa śatru*

:912:\:147:\:14:. hyaŋ hyaŋ niŋ tuṅgaṅan sāraŧi nira wĕka niŋ sidđi sāmbĕknya sidđa,
ratnènādyūta dè hyaŋ rawi raŧa nira tan manda manda praƀānya,
śudđākārāputiḥ roma ni kuda nira pöḥ niŋ praƀā niŋ śaśāṅka,
rwaŋ lakṣa ŋ sūṙyyabadđađwaja nira piturun saŋ hyaŋ āditya sèwu*

:913:\:147:\:15:. Akwèḥ sāmantaputrāṅiriŋ i sira paḍātuṅgalan saṙggacāpa,
pantĕs lwiṙ hyaŋ hyaŋ iŋ sañjata tĕka rumaras māṙ twas iŋ śatru dènya,
sèwu kwèhnyānwam anwam ‌wruḥ akuda kudan iŋ papraṅan wīraputra,
jihwā niŋ mṛtyu sākṣāt đwaja nira dumilaḥ rājasiṅhāmaṛĕmpu*

:914:\:147:\:16:. wīra prajñā juru dyaḥ nira sama sama ganđaṙwwa dènyāmawāmbĕk,
Ilwèlwanyānwam  anwam saṅaŋ iwu taruṇānaknya mantrī narèndra,
Apriḥ riŋ praŋ sujanmāraŧa raŧan apupul tan saḥ iŋ waṅśa sālas,
wālāṙkākāra sākṣāt lwiṙ ika n aruṇamèǥa đwajanya pradīpta*

:915:\:147:\:17:. sakwèḥ kwèḥ niŋ rarè jro wani hañaṙ anapuk sañjatāgyāmrihèŋ praŋ,
rwaŋ lakṣa kwèhnya mĕttāṅuhuḥ aṅayam ayam śatru mwaŋ dèwa daitya,
Anwam ‌wruḥ riŋ đanuṙwwèda juru nika huwus kāku siṅhanya riŋ praŋ,
dèwāṅgānèka tuṅgulnya saṅaŋ iwu kadīndrādi milwāmukèŋ praŋ*

:916:\:147:\:18:. Ambĕk niŋ dāsa śūrāpraṅa rumuhun apan kāsatan pwa ŋ hatinya,
mattā wīṙyyāṅuhuḥ göŋ ni kamanan ika riŋ praŋ murub tan pahīṅan,
miṅṣoṙ mĕntas mariŋ tuṅgaṅan apan ahuyaŋ kwèhnya sèwwaṙwwudāḍĕm,
mātaṅganyāpupul mwaŋ đwaja nika dumilaḥ citramèǥākilat mās*

:917:\:147:\:19:. saŋ juṙww ājābala rwaŋ prayuta pinakasènāpati prāṇa niŋ praŋ,
kapwādandan rukuḥ mās kawaca minaṇikan lwiṙ samudrāgni muntab,
wadwāṅjuṙww apramèyāraŧa sayuta gajahnyātatā sèwu lakṣa,
lākānèka đwajanya n pracalita kadi bahnī sĕḍĕŋ niŋ yugānta*

:918:\:147:\:20:. mantrī rwaŋ lakṣa sāmpun ginĕlaṙ i hiriṅan bāhudaṇḍāṅgakāra,
lèn tèkaŋ pādarakṣa prakaṭa kadi tasik rwaŋ puluḥ duṙgga niŋ praŋ,
Aṙppat muṅgw ī tĕṅaḥ śrī nṛpasuta muꝁa niŋ siṅha śāṙddūla śakti,
kady āgastyāṅuyup sāgara wunuhan ikaŋ byūha sāmpun tiniṅkaḥ*

<wisaṙjjita> – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓

:919:\:148:\:1:. Aṙppat ikaŋ waragaŋ sahasa siliḥ usī paḍa nora wĕdi,
siŋ sakasambut ikaŋ pinakagada gadānya paḍāmurulu,
Umban aliwran arok ṛĕmĕk iŋ awaŋ awaŋ kapagut kawaluy,
dukduk ikā kadi saṙppa pakan aṅin anèka hanèŋ gagana*

:920:\:148:\:2:. wwaŋ bahulātuha milw ajurit alara tĕṇḍas ikā ginutuk,
Ꜽ putu liṅnya nihan laku walĕsi gutuk buru dèmu pisuḥ,
ndi n wĕnaŋ aṅgutukāṅrahana tan uƀayāku putu prihawak,
dwal putu dèmu palakwan i katigawĕlas tĕṅahè laku ta*

:921:\:148:\:3:. brāhmaṇa wany apuliḥ galaḥ apupul aḍĕm pinurugnya ṛĕbaḥ,
tan ‌wruḥ awèda kuraŋ kuraŋ aji makapaṅhaḍa timbul ikā,
kèpwan ikaŋ musuḥ amraṅa paḍa wĕdi yan raḥ ikā mijila,
ṅhiŋ pamĕdinya pulut pulutan ika ta hètu nikā malayū*

<basantatilaka> – – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓

:922:\:149:\:1:. nya ŋ sogatānwam ajurit kĕna tan dwa bĕntar,
mojaṙ kutiknya ḍuḥ uḍuḥ pukulun laranya,
yèka n mijil para cĕṅĕlnya nĕhĕṙ sinuṇḍaŋ,
kadyaṅgan iŋ ǥaṭa ṛĕmĕk tika yan panaṇḍĕm*

:923:\:149:\:2:. śaiwāpuliḥ kĕna pilis wulaṅun kajuṅkĕl,
mitrānuluŋ‌ mpu mapa tèku manahta maṅko,
Èṅĕt‌ ṅhulun ri kita ƀāgya tasim yan èṅĕt,
strī ni ṅhulun kita tulakṣaya ko hadèki*

:924:\:149:\:3:. nā liŋ nira mpu tucapa ŋ prajurit siliḥ praŋ,
Ārok rinok awuṙ awuṙ paḍa tan wri rātnya,
tèg tog ḍaḍap nika bubul ginalaḥ tinaṅkis,
ḍöhak musuhnya sinuḍatnya pĕjaḥ kasoran*

:925:\:149:\:4:. gĕntöṙ i śabda ni gubaṙṇnya baṅun siliḥ pṛĕp,
kady ācakĕp đwani nikaŋ kukulan kaṛĕsṛĕs,
kaṅṣinya lāgi manaḥ ambĕk iŋ ajriḥ iŋ praŋ,
moṅmoṅan aṅgyat anamaṙ macan aśriŋ oliḥ*

:926:\:149:\:5:. wadwā nṛpātmaja tumampuhakĕn gadānya,
rwaŋ lakṣa tan kuraŋ asĕṅhit asiṅhanāda,
Akwèḥ tikĕl tikĕl igā ni lawanya ṛĕmpuḥ,
Aṅṙwwaŋ pulūḥ uliḥ ikā ri patuṅgalanya*

:927:\:149:\:6:. wīrānapuk raṅin apiṇḍa sahaśra wṛnda,
mèww īwu koṭi pagalahnya paṛĕŋ tumampuḥ,
gĕk ǥoṙ ṛĕbaḥ wiꝑala siŋ kinayuhnya runtuḥ,
sawṛĕnda māti ginalaḥ sawanèḥ pinökan*

:928:\:149:\:7:. sèwwaṙwwudāmana manaḥ mwaŋ ikāŋ agaṇḍi,
tandaṅnya tan dwa kinawĕdyan apan kaṛĕsṛĕs,
hrūnyānrik iŋ gagana söḥ kadi mèǥa mĕṇḍuŋ,
saṙ cĕb tibāṅĕnani siŋ kĕna tan pasāra*

:929:\:149:\:8:. wadwā narèndra malayū sawatĕk watĕknya,
pèka prawīra kĕna tan dwa yaya praŋ aṅrok,
kombak linūd awalikan kumĕlab đwajanya,
himpĕṙ nadī kinĕbuṙ iŋ gaja sèwu lakṣa*

:930:\:149:\:9:. ƀātriṅśa lakṣa ŋ apuliḥ kalulun kawaṅṣul,
kālaḥ tibā siliḥ idĕk sinĕsĕb pinökan,
ṛĕmpak tikĕl wiꝑala salwiṙ i sañjatanya,
lwiṙ kaywa kaywan asipattra ṛĕbaḥ kaliṇḍwan*

:931:\:149:\:10:. wadwā narèśwara inatyan irèŋ kasiṅhan,
śakti prawīra parapök i musuḥ yan iŋ praŋ,
yèkāpuliḥ tan awĕdī ripubāṇawaṙṣa,
wany ānusup tĕpĕt amūk makasoŋ ḍaḍapnya*

:932:\:149:\:11:. kagyat balā nṛpatiputra maluy tinaṅkis,
Akwèḥ an amriha tawan tiki tan kagöman,
mĕṅgĕp kadi jriḥ akikib malayū tan adṛĕs,
munduṙ yayā bala narèśwara duṙbbalālwaŋ*

:933:\:149:\:12:. tan jriḥ bala nṛĕpati đaiṙyya sahāƀimāna,
Apraŋ karuŋ paḍa tumiṅgalakĕn ḍaḍapnya,
dè niŋ siliḥ pĕḍĕk arok wĕkasan siliḥ pṛĕp,
bĕk tĕg hĕhĕḥ kahĕnĕkan jriḥ ikaŋ lumumpat*

:934:\:149:\:13:. Awrālayū bala narèndraṣutāwṛĕg awrin,
śakti prawīra kapana n kĕna pakṣa pakṣan,
hamham tĕkāṅamaḥ amaḥ bala saŋ narèndra,
Apyak tĕkapnya n aṅucap tuhu siṅha riŋ praŋ*

:935:\:149:\:14:. Ꜽ koŋ watĕk raǥusuta priḥ awakmu maṅko,
haywāpraŋ unduṙ aŧawā paṅaliḥ para ṅkè,
Āpan ya tan hana sihankwa ri kāsy asihmu,
kāton pĕjahmu pususĕṅkwa ri sañjataṅku*

:936:\:149:\:15:. nā liŋ nikāmutuŋ aṅĕmbuli tan panaṅgĕl,
kwèhnyāpramèya kadi sāgara tan papiṅgir,
maṙmmanya wāni sahasāmraŋ amūk tumiṇḍiḥ,
dukduk panaḥ kadi hudan ya ta paṅhaṛĕpnya*

:937:\:149:\:16:. Aṅwèhi sañjata humuŋ gumuruḥ suraknya,
Aṅrok atambĕḥ i haṛĕp kumucup đwajanya,
Akwèḥ pĕjaḥ tan awĕdī pati maṅkin èmbuḥ,
lwiṙ laṙwwa laṙwwan aṛĕbut damaṙ alwaŋ èmbuḥ*

:938:\:149:\:17:. krūrāpuliḥ bala narèndraṣutāmuk amriḥ,
munduṙ bala nṛĕpati śīǥra muwaḥ tumampuḥ,
Ènak siliḥ galaḥ apan paḍa wāni wāni,
söḥ sāhasāṅuḍik uḍik praŋ ikā siliḥ sob*

:939:\:149:\:18:. Ènak marāpraŋ arukĕt paḍa nora mundur,
rwaŋ yojana ŋ paƀaratan paḍa söḥ gajāśwa,
sāmpun ṛĕbaḥ wukiṙ anaknya watunya kabwaŋ,
Akwèḥ juraŋ mari juraŋ wĕkasan kahinya*

:940:\:149:\:19:. ṅkānè ruhuṙ gunuŋ ikaŋ praŋ arok siliḥ sob,
Apraŋ sumĕṅka tumurun paḍa rota rodra,
ṛĕp tan katon hanan awās tĕkap iŋ himāwrā,
ramyātulis praŋ ika konĕŋ unĕŋ tinonton*

:941:\:149:\:20:. brāhmaṙṣi śèwa sugatādi ri soṙ anonton,
mwaŋ wwaŋ jriḥ iŋ raṇa huwus katuhan wayahnya,
kwèhnyātatānudiṅi haṙṣa nĕhĕṙ tumĕṅhā,
Akrak paḍātri gumuruḥ ri paṅadwakĕnya*

:942:\:149:\:21:. rīyūk ṛĕbaḥ kidul alaḥ rinĕbut sinökan,
rīyūk ṛĕbaḥ muwaḥ alaḥ kasĕsöḥ ikaŋ lor,
rīyūk ṛĕbaḥ muwaḥ ikaŋ kidul alwaŋ akwèḥ,
rīyūk ṛĕbaḥ pinĕgatan wĕdi wök ikaŋ lor*

:943:\:149:\:22:. Āḥ uḥ piraŋ juru muwaḥ saka loṙ tumandaŋ,
rīyūk ṛĕbaḥ kidul alaḥ binurunya kagyat,
kady ānutuḥ kalapa dènya mamöki tĕṇḍas,
nā liŋ nikā hana ta lèn aṅutū kapūhan*

:944:\:149:\:23:. śīṙṇna ŋ samaṇḍala samaṇḍala konduran syuḥ,
Awṛĕg paḍāṅhili sira mpu tĕkèŋ kaninyan,
Aprakprakan di ta kaki hyaŋ ujaṙ nini hyaŋ,
putrī nikā kabuṛĕṅèk buṛĕṅèk tinaṅguŋ*

:945:\:149:\:24:. sāmpun tĕkè ruhuṙ iŋ agra muwaḥ paḍāwṛĕg,
wwaŋ wṛdđa wṛdđa guru niny aṅuhuḥ sakè sor,
pāran pinawṛĕgakĕn ā mapa liŋ kaki hyaŋ,
wikw āñaruk wiṣaya rakwa nimitta niŋ wṛĕg*

:946:\:149:\:25:. lāwan turun patapan ĕmbuli haywa mundur,
Ambĕk ṅwaŋ iŋ kaguru ninyan alaḥ padandan,
ṅwaŋ pwātuhālaḥ alaḥ ĕmpu buyut ta lampaḥ,
nā liŋ nini mpu kabalik wĕdi wök kaki mpu*

:947:\:149:\:26:. wīrāpraŋ iŋ tĕgal ayun paḍa wāni wāni,
kontab maṅontabakĕn amraŋ amūk añakra,
kèdĕṙ paḍākuliliṅan gumuluŋ raŧanya,
lwiṙ nāga moliḥ amĕbĕd gaja matta sālas*

:948:\:149:\:27:. Ènak dahat praŋ ika kādƀuta riŋ triloka,
Āpan katuhwan atĕwĕk tĕwĕkan paḍākris,
lèn taŋ siliḥ tujaḥ amatṛĕm amajra maṅduk,
bāhunya runtuḥ asakit trus aṅĕmbak ĕmbak*

:949:\:149:\:28:. sojaṙṇnya kātara nĕhĕṙ marahup rahup raḥ,
hāmaḥ śiraḥ hurupa jīwamu haywa tājriḥ,
haywādwa ƀoḥ ndya ta śiraḥ mata maḥ ndya jīwa,
bwat kaprawīran iki tan dadi miŧyawāda*

:950:\:149:\:29:. nā liŋ nikā tucapa śabda ri dè nikāpraŋ,
pyak byuṙ kĕpuk kĕtĕlĕbuk kĕḍĕpĕk kĕtug tog,
cèŋ has tĕhap tĕhap aḍuḥ gĕdĕbĕg ḍĕhak syok,
caṙccab lĕbik bĕk aḍu göŋ gumĕcik gĕlĕmpöŋ*

:951:\:149:\:30:. nāhan taŋ ĕlwan asĕluṙ kaṛĕṅö kaṛĕsṛĕs,
maṅdè ƀayānaka pasaṅǥa nikā gumĕntĕr,
lèn taŋ mahātiśaya rodra paṅalw alönya,
wīrāṅgĕtĕm nĕhĕṙ aṅohan i mèhnya matya*

<wisaṙjjita> – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏓

:952:\:150:\:1:. śrī magađāđipa sāhasa mijil aƀimāna nirèŋ palagan,
nāgamayāstra laras nira sĕḍĕŋ inayat ƀramita ŋ pṛŧiwī,
göŋ swara niŋ tali dè ny aṅin ika kumusuḥ mĕtu kātatakut,
hrū nika kādƀuta kātara gunuŋ ahĕlaṙ warakadga murub*

:953:\:150:\:2:. prajwalitāgni cucuknya kagiri giri đūma dilahnya murub,
sèk gumuruḥ paṅawaknya kumisik amĕgat jaladèŋ gagana,
boṙ kumutug śara bajra saŋ Aja kumĕtug lĕpas aṅdwiguṇa,
tèg tumibā ŋ wihagācala mati pinanaḥ makĕbĕt kĕbĕtan*

<jagadđita> – – – | ⏑⏑– | ⏑– ⏑| ⏑⏑– | ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| – ⏑– | ⏑⏓

:954:\:151:\:1:. muntab krođa saŋ Aṅganāŧa kadi bahni maṅaraman i puñcak iŋ wukir,
ṅkānè kūwara niŋ raŧāmahāyu lañciṅan ira pinisit siniṅṣĕtan,
hrū lāwan laras adwitīya sinamāđy amijilakĕna saṙwwasañjata,
wuntw īkaŋ gaganāntarāla tĕkap iŋ panaḥ atip atĕtĕl turuŋ tibā*

:955:\:151:\:2:. dèwanyāwurahan tĕkāṅamaḥ amaḥ haṛĕp amususa riŋ nṛĕpātmaja,
lwiṙ mèǥodaya māǥamāsa sumaput pĕtĕŋ alimunan aṅhudan hawu,
saŋ hyaŋ bāywanala pracaṇḍa pamanaḥ nṛpatanaya dumèḥ kawaṅṣula,
bĕk gĕk toṙ cĕṛĕcĕb tibèŋ bala narèśwara makasulayaḥ kawaṅṣulan*

:956:\:151:\:3:. śaktīŋ praŋ saŋ Awantināŧa sira mṛtyu sakala yan i mađya niŋ musuḥ,
maṅgĕḥ budđi nirāpuliḥ nĕhĕṙ aṅakw amĕjahana narèśwarātmaja,
rahasyāntya nikaŋ kaśaktin inayat nira mĕtu ŋ ayuđāgnipaṙwwata,
boṙ muṅgw iŋ gaganāntarāla paḍa yatna bala saŋ Aja kèbĕkan panas*

:957:\:151:\:4:. tan kèwran saŋ Ajāpan adƀuta kaśaktin ira tumiru śakti saŋ raǥu,
ṛĕp mārāđana pañcabāyu mĕtu kātaratara gumĕṛĕḥ magĕnturan,
kabwaŋ taŋ śara paṙwwatāgni kadi handaru sayuta dilahnya riŋ laṅit,
ƀuṙ tog söŋ pṛĕkĕtĕk nahan swara nikāmĕkasi hurip i mađya niŋ tasik*

:958:\:151:\:5:. maṅṣö sāhasa tan surud saŋ Anupāđipati manaḥ ira n wanīŋ raṇa,
paṅhrik niŋ kuda lèn grit iŋ raŧa kaṛĕṅw asĕluṙ i hiriṅan hanè haṛĕp,
pakrak niŋ balasaṅǥa maṅgyat aṅasut ri bala saŋ Aja wāni kāmbulan,
tèg tok lwiṙ garuḍāḍahĕm kĕtug ikaŋ gubaṙ asahuran apratiđwani*

:959:\:151:\:6:. sampunya n lumĕpas panaḥ saŋ Anupāđipa kadi ruga ŋ aṇḍamaṇḍala,
pātālasŧa samāpta nāga lĕkĕṙ iŋ ƀuwana rumĕbuti nṛĕpātmaja,
porot boṙ dumilaḥ mara ŋ wiṣa sinĕmburakĕn ika hanātĕmaḥ kukus,
byuṙ laṙ lĕs paḍa mukṣa dè ni kuku saŋ garuḍa wahu minuṣṭi riŋ laras*

<śragđara> – – – | – ⏑– | – ⏑⏑| ⏑⏑⏑| ⏑– – | ⏑– – | ⏑– ⏓

:960:\:152:\:1:. krođāmbĕk saŋ susènā saha bala sumaput kātarāṣiṅhanāda,
haṙṣa n ton saŋ narāṙyyātmaja pinakamusuḥ kèwalānuṅga nuṅgal,
hrū hrū śaktīŋ daṅū söḥ linĕpasakĕn irātaṅkis akrak kaṛĕsṛĕs,
Āpan pakṣy āhĕlaṙ sañjata kadi garuḍānèka sèww aṙwwudāhöm*

:961:\:152:\:2:. sumyaŋ sumyak hĕlaṙṇnya n kinirigakĕn ikāǥāṣa muntab dilahnya,
sumyuk tan kāwaran dṛĕsnya kadi dinukakĕn yan tumandaŋ sakèŋ doḥ,
kāṇḍĕg katṛĕn dinuk dè saŋ Aja linud irèŋ cakra puṅgĕl gulūnya,
pèrat sok rahnya saṅkèŋ ḍaḍa nika kawutaḥ mṛĕm tibādoḥ gumĕntĕr*

:962:\:152:\:3:. ṅhiŋ saŋ hèmāṅgadāmriḥ mriḥ apuliḥ i luyuk saŋ susènā katampĕk,
sāmpun kèmpun sinimpĕn bala saŋ Aja paḍa krūra kèdran kawuṅkus,
syuḥ tan sārā sa hèmāṅgada mati tinĕḍak bĕntaṙ alwaŋ salakṣa,
kāṙyy aṅlīlā narèndrāmanahakĕn irikaŋ sāgarātyanta rodra*

:963:\:152:\:4:. śīǥra rwabnyāṅgaluntaŋ gaganacara lĕpas māmpuhan matrigañca,
lĕmboranyāṅlayaŋ kāƀinawa kadi gunuŋ sèwu māliḥ marampak,
sumyūk adṛĕs tumĕmpuḥ ri saŋ Aja kawaluy dè ni göŋ niŋ kaśaktin,
mawṛĕg luṅhāstra dè hyaŋ baruṇasuta kaṛĕsnya n hilaŋ tan paśèṣa*

:964:\:152:\:5:. saŋ pāṇḍyāmaḥ gunuŋ sāhasa tĕka rumahāb dè ni göŋ niŋ kamānan,
sākṣāt guntuṙ sakèŋ paṙwwata tumurun atūt lwaḥ juraŋ duṙggamājro,
mātaṅga mwaŋ raŧa lwiṙ watu gumuluŋ apan tan paraṙyyan lakunya,
krođāmĕṇṭaŋ laras saŋ praƀu mamanahakĕn bahni saṅkèŋ samudra*

:965:\:152:\:6:. lumrā riŋ dik widik tèja nika saha panasnyāṅgĕsĕŋ saṙwwawṛkṣa,
sakwèḥ niŋ mèǥa mĕṇḍuŋ pinaṅan ika huwus hĕnti lāwan gĕlapnya,
lwiṙ jihwānya ŋ mahāmṛtyu dumilata narèndrātmajātyanta rodra,
saŋ hyaŋ kālāgni muṅgw ī naraca saŋ Aja maṙmmanya mātīŋ raṇāṅga*

<basantatilaka> – – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑– ⏑| ⏑– ⏑| – ⏓

:966:\:153:\:1:. saŋ pāṇḍya soṙ titiḥ alaḥ malayū tinaṅkis,
wadwā nirālara hilaŋ kahalāwṛĕg alwaŋ,
Āpan siliḥ praŋ aṛĕbut hawan ahrit èwĕḥ,
wadwā nṛpātmaja maluy sakaṛĕŋ maraṙyyan*

:967:\:153:\:2:. saŋ saptarāja sumahāb saha ƀṛtyamantrī,
sāmpun sirāṅhabĕtakĕn đwaja śīǥra maṅkat,
saṙ sök prawīra gumuruḥ kadi sāgara rwab,
lwiṙ siṅha sāṙwwuda paḍākrak asiṅhanāda*

:968:\:153:\:3:. wīrātyan iŋ wani hinatyan inĕṇḍĕm ĕṇḍĕm,
Agyāpraŋ aṅgĕtĕm atön maṅusap lĕṅĕnya,
mwaŋ saṙwwasañjata nikā milu haṙṣa riŋ praŋ,
paṅliṅganāṅiṅis iṅis kumĕñaṙ wajanya*

:969:\:153:\:4:. hamham tĕkāmanaḥ añakra bubak sakāmbaḥ,
rodrāmupak cĕṅĕl amūk aṛĕbut kasiṅhan,
lèn taŋ paḍāpapatihan kuḍuwak paḍākrè,
saṅhāra kātĕkan i rūpa nika n kaṛĕsṛĕs*

:970:\:153:\:5:. śūrāmĕṛĕḥ kadi surat tĕkap iŋ kaśūran,
kontanya kādƀuta sahaśra kuwuŋ kuwuṅnya,
Aśraŋ kĕtug ni panutugnya ḍaḍap gumĕntĕr,
